44002006	Yana aka bo daka emina , bato batitana banɛnɛ mɛnɛ , na bayegebana bou , cina bo bakaka moto na moto , a kɔpi ende mɛnɛ .
44002007	Ibo bakamoa na dilese mɛnɛ , na babalana bo , Ikani ! Bato baya babalaka , bo basusu te bato baGalile ?
44002008	Oko boa , ekaka so moto na moto monɔkɔ monde mɛnɛ cina nda ?
44002009	Iso te BaPalutia , BaMadai , BaElama , na bato baya badonga a Mɛsɔpɔtamia , Yuda , Kapadokia , Ponto , Asia ,
44002010	Pelugia , Pampuha , Ejipito , na makota maLibia oho a dɔngɔ diKulene , na bato baya badonga oho Loma , na BaYuda na bapakano baya bahekoa Bayuda ;
44002011	BaKulete na BaAlabia ; na bokaka bato bamina baya batɔndɔkɔ mijɔ miNjambe mibokamoa a kɔpi jisu bɛnɛ .
44002012	Ibo basusu bakamoa na dilese , na badaka koko na mokakwano ; babalana bo , Cina emina edi bo ?
44002013	Bakina batongo ko basɛkɛ oko bosɛkɛ , na babala bo , Balangoi na vino eyene .
44002014	Pɛtɛlo adaka na babwɛnji batongo domi-na-omɔci , na yo angɔ , adipoa monɔkɔ monde , na abala na bu bo , Ino bami baYuda , na no basusu baYelusalema , hokeani mojɔ mobalaka mbi , na eingeani mojɔ mu .
44002015	Ibaba balangoiti nongo o alɛkɛ no . Boni . Edi oko neuf heures ehuma pɛ .
44002016	Mojɔ mu modi oko mojɔ mobala motɔndɔi Yoele bo ,
44002017	Njambe abalaka bo , Mbi nasopabi Mwembo mombi Ai bato basusu a masu masuka . Banabami banu na banabali banu bapabí biseko ; Menga manu banɛbi mijɔ a njɔti , Na basuku banu batɔbí njɔti .
44002018	Mbi nasopabí Mwembo mombi ai bakɔmɛli bambi bami , na Bakɔmɛli bambi bali a masu mamina , na bapabi biseko .
44002019	Nanejabí mijɔ mibokamoa ta busa , Na bimbete a ngondo ya nase , Oko makia , na mosa , na modidi momosa .
44002020	Modika-busa mohindabí , Na songe abongoabí makia , Oko busa bua boKumu bodoakini , Busa bonɛnɛ boekumu .
44002021	Na modabí bo moto na moto yona obeaka a kombe eKumu ahelabí .
44002022	Ino bami baYisalaele , hokeani mijɔ mi . Ojehakani mojɔ moYesu oNasaleta . Njambe aneja no bo ahɔ moto omina a tei enu , oko na bimbete na mindumba mikɔ Njambe na nde a boso bonu .
44002023	Ino ko omotombani na omowejani a mole-mobokea na mɔmɔ mabato babe . Njambe ajeba a bobanga mɛnɛ bo badi bomokaba ; mojɔ momina modaka oko a mokano monde .
44002024	Njambe ko amocingoa a mbɔci jibogwa , na amongɔjɔ , mojɔ bo bogwa boidaka na ngulu a bomopea na bosusu .
44002025	Mojɔ bo Dawidi abala mojɔ monde bo , Mbi nanɛkɛ Kumu ombi a boso bombi masu masusu ; Mojɔ bo adi a dɔngɔ dimbi diebɔ ebami bo ambilimejae mbi .
44002026	Molema mombi mosepaka a mojɔ momina , na monɔkɔ mombi modi na enanga ; Mojɔ motongo koko , — mokuku mombi môyeyoa a esika enjingo .
44002027	Cina bo otakina mwembo mombi a esika ebogwa , Na otajima bo Yona Mosɛnɔke owɛ apɔe .
44002028	Onejaini njea jibomɔ , Na molema mombi môda na sepi botɔ , mojɔ bo wɛ odi na mbi .
44002029	Baninga , kinani nabale na nu a bohu a mojɔ motata osu Dawidi .
44002030	Iyo agwa na bamopusea ; esɛmɔ ende edi oko na su busa bu . Iyo adaka motɔndɔi , na ajebaka bo Njambe amosakea mosako bo abakee okina mwana’nde a mongbɛlɛngɔ mobokumu bonde .
44002031	Iyo abala boa a mojɔ moMasiya . Anɛ na atɔndɔ mojɔ mobongɔ boMasiya a bogwa , yana abala yo bo atayeyoa a esika ebagwake , na bo mokuku monde motapɔ .
44002032	Oko boa Njambe amongɔjɔ , oko Yesu yo mɛnɛ . Iso basusu bodi banjɛnɛki bamojɔ momina .
44002033	Oko boa , adi yo na ekumu a dɔngɔ diebɔ ebami eNjambe , na asi yo Mwembo Mosɛnɔke ai Sango , o akina yo sako , amosopi ai so , o anɛkɛ no na akaka no .
44002034	Mojɔ bo Dawidi aikwea a Diko yo mɛnɛ . Iyo ko abala bo , Kumu abali na Kumu ombi bo , Da ya a ebɔ embi ebami ,
44002035	Oko adi mbi pɛ bopeta dumba soki jiwɛ a cina jibibota biwɛ .
44002036	Oko boa , bato basusu badenga diYisalaele babwani bojeba bo Njambe abakea Yesu bo adae Kumu na Masiya , oko yona owa ’ no a mole-mobokea .
44002037	Bikenge bimina bibandea oko a milema , na babala na Pɛtɛlo na babwɛnji batongo bo , Baninga , êkɔ so ndeni ?
44002038	Pɛtɛlo abala na bubo , Hekojani milema minu , na batisamani ino basusu a kombe eYesu Masiya , a mojɔ moboyɛ bojibe jinu , nongo osɛni epeeli eMwembo Mosɛnɔke .
44002039	Sako ye edi ai no bɛnɛ , na bana banu , na bato basusu baya badi bohali pongono , oko bato basusu babeaka Kumu Njambe osu ai yo .
44002040	Pɛtɛlo abatɔndɔ mijɔ mitongo minɛnɛ , na abaleha bo , Ciani elulu ye engulumake !
44002041	Oko boa baya bajima mwako monde babatisama . Busa bomina , etango ebacingami ehɛ na bato koto jisato .
44002042	Ibo badaka na bingi enɛnɛ a mojɔ mobokoja bobabwɛnji , na bakatana na molema momɔci a bobuka molɛmbɛ na a mojɔ mobo’nga .
44002043	Bato basusu badaka na bɔ a mojɔ mobimbete na mindumba mikɔkɔ babwɛnji .
44002044	Bato basusu baya bajimaka bakatana bopele , na bakabana leka pongono .
44002045	Bangɛjɛ ndako na leka lobu , na bakaba likonja na bato batongo o adaka moto na moto na taka .
44002046	Baikputoa bokwea a tempelo busa na busa na molema momɔci . Babukaka molɛmbɛ a ndako-ndako , na bayakaka mia oko na sepi na bowi a milema .
44002047	Basakoaka Njambe , na badaka na gala epele a tei ebato bangando . Njambe anɛngɛja Denga busa na busa oko na bato baya bahelaka .
44003001	Pɛtɛlo na Yoane bakɛ a tempelo a ehole ebo’nga , oko atrois heures .
44003002	Okina momi adaka ena yona obotama mondɔke . Bamotombaka bo bamosambee masu masusu a modipe motempelo mua modaka na kombe Esɛngɔ ; na angaka likonja ai bato baya bakweaka a tempelo .
44003003	Yana anɛ yo bo Pɛtɛlo na Yoane bakɛkɛ akwee a tempelo , aba’nga likonja .
44003004	Pɛtɛlo na Yoane bamonja ngbɛ ; na Pɛtɛlo abala bo , Anja so !
44003005	Iyo abanja boa , mojɔ bo adaka na njingo bo bamopɛ ekina eka .
44003006	Pɛtɛlo ko abala bo , Mbi napeliti nongo likonja , pɛpɛ flanka , pɛpɛ pata ; endele ko , mbi napaka wɛ oko lia lipeli mbi ; a kombe eYesu Masiya oNasaleta , dala !
44003007	Amopea na ebɔ ebami , amongɔjɔ , na yo asɔ ngulu bokpa a mako na a gaga .
44003008	Ama mema , apimboa , abanga bodala , na akwea na bu a tempelo oko na bosakoa ai Njambe .
44003009	Bato basusu bangando bamonɛ akadale na akasakoe Njambe .
44003010	Bamombetea , na bajeba bo adi oko moto yona omaka da a modipe motempelo a mojɔ molinga ; na bakamoa na bayegebana cina emojɔ mokɔɔmɔ na nde .
44003011	Iyo ko aipala bokina Pɛtɛlo na Yoane , na bato basusu bapota , na batitana a Eseba eSɔlɔmɔ .
44003012	Yana anɛ Pɛtɛlo mojɔ momina , abala na bato bo , Ino bami baYisalaele , okamoakani a mojɔ momoto yo cina eye ? onjakani so ngbɛ mojɔ moye ? Olɛkɛni bo so bodalejai moto yoyo na ejimeli na ngulu esu bɛnɛ ?
44003013	Njambe oAbalayama na oIsaka na oYakobo , Njambe obatata basu akumejai Mwana’nde Yesu . Ino omopani a mɔmɔ maPilato , na omolonani a boso bonde , yana ajima Pilato bo amocingoe .
44003014	Olonani Yona Mosɛnɔkɛ , Yona oBodongo , na ohɔni bo bacingoe mobengo ai no .
44003015	Owani Kumu oBomɔ ; Njambe ko amongɔjɔ a bogwa , na so bodi banjɛnɛki bamojɔ momina .
44003016	Edi oko kombe ende yena epi moto yoyo ngulu , cina eejimeli a kombe ende ; omonɛkɛni na omojebakani no bɛnɛ . Edi oko ejimeli ai Yesu yena epi moto yoyo mokuku monjilake a boso bonu basusu .
44003017	Baninga , mbi najebaka bo okɔni mojɔ momina a libumi linu , no bɛnɛ na bakumu banu pongono .
44003018	Njambe ko ajebeja mojɔ momina eyou na minɔkɔ mibatɔndɔi basusu , bo Masiya onde adi bodingoa ; na mojɔ momina mongami boa .
44003019	Oko boa toma jasani dosa ; toma hekojani milema , bo jibe jinu jihakoame , bo Kumu alomee no masu mabomɔ boyene ,
44003020	na alome Masiya yona ohɛngɛmɛ a mojɔ monu , oko Yesu .
44003021	Iyo ko adi boyeyoa oho Diko oko a ehole ebohɔngeja ngando jisusu . Njambe atɔndɔ mojɔ momina ehele mɛnɛ na minɔkɔ mibatɔndɔi bande basɛnɔke .
44003022	Mose yo mɛnɛ abala bo , Kumu Njambe adi bongɔjɔ motɔndɔi ai no a tei ebaninga banu , o adi mbi . Toma hokeani mijɔ misusu mibalabi yo na nu .
44003023	Moto na moto yona olonabí bohokea motɔndɔi omina adi bogwa a tei ebato .
44003024	Samwele , na batɔndɔi basusu batongo baya badoa ngɔngɔ jinde , na babwɛnji koko , bajebeja mojɔ momasu mama .
44003025	Ino odini bana babatɔndɔi , basangoli baMokongo mobakea Njambe na batata banu , yana abala yo na Abalayama bo , Makota masusu mangondo majongoamabí a mojɔ mobana bawɛ .
44003026	Njambe angɔjɔ Mwana’nde , na amolomea boso ai no a bojongoa no , na a bobuleja no basusu a jibe jinu .
44004001	Nganga , na mosuku otempelo , na Basadoki , bamea oko yana abalaka Pɛtɛlo na Yoane na bato .
44004002	Ibo badaka na kɛlɛ , cina bo babwɛnji bakojaka bato , na batɔndɔkɔ mojɔ mobongɔ boYesu a bogwa .
44004003	Babapea na baba’sa ta blɔkɔ , bo bambe ehuma , mojɔ bo busa boma dipa .
44004004	Bato banɛnɛ ko baya baka mwako momina bajima . Etango ebami edaka isa koto jitano na dea .
44004005	Yana ahoa busa , babolea likita libakumu , na basuku bangando , na basɔni , a Yelusalema .
44004006	Ana , mosuku onganga adaka ena , na Kayapa , na Yoane , na Alesandele , na bato basusu badenga dimosuku onganga .
44004007	Bameja Pɛtɛlo na Yoane a boso bobu , na babahɔjɔ bo , Ino okɔini mojɔ mu na nguliu enda , na a kombe enda ?
44004008	Pɛtɛlo aluma oko na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke , na abala na bu bo , Ino bakumu bangando na basuku ,
44004009	opalakani bokokeleja so busa bu a mojɔ moelomu epele eboheleja moto yo a yogo , oko moto mondɔke .
44004010	Toma cingeani no basusu , na bato basusu baYisalaele pongono , bo moto yoyo adi a boso bonu edɛye na mokuku mopele , oko a mojɔ mokombe eYesu Masiya oNasaleta , oko yona owa no a mole-mobokea ; Njambe ko amongɔjɔ a bogwa .
44004011	Iyo adi litai lilona no bayoi , na lidi edɛye litai limogbukusu .
44004012	Pɛpɛ nongo okina otongo odi boheleja ; mojɔ bo botahela nongo na ekina kombe etongo a tei ebato ya nase , oko kombe emina pɛ .
44004013	Ibo bakamoa oko bokamoa yana anɛ bo bogale boPɛtɛlo na Yoane ; mojɔ bo bajebaka bo badi oko bato baelomu pɛ , pɛpɛ nongo ejebeli enɛnɛ emikanda . A mojɔ momina bacingea bo bama cingama oko na Yesu .
44004014	Na anɛkɛ bo moto yona oma hela a yogo a boso bobu , baisɔmbeja nongo ekenge .
44004015	Oko boa babatɔndɔ bo bamane a likita , bo babalane mojɔ momina .
44004016	Babala bo , Êkɔ so na bato bamina ndeni ? Bato basusu baYelusalema bajebaka bo bakɔi mondumba monɛnɛ , na so bɛnɛ bobwaniti bongana mojɔ momina .
44004017	Bopele bo bobakanee , na bobalembe bo batabala koko na moto a kombe emina , mojɔ mosaka hɛ a tei ebato .
44004018	Oko boa , bababea na baba-lemba na bopipo bo batabala , na batakoja koko a kombe eYesu .
44004019	Pɛtɛlo na Yoane ko babasɔmbeja bo , A boso boNjambe , iso bobwani bohokea nda , isa Njambe , isa no ? Sambejani no bɛnɛ .
44004020	Mojɔ bo so botahɔnɔkɔ boda bogo a mojɔ mongando jinɛ so na jika so .
44004021	Babakanea koko na babacingoa ; bato basusu basakoaka Njambe a mojɔ momondumba momina ; oko boa baihɔnɔ bokɔ na bu nongo mojɔ , oko a mojɔ mobato bangando .
44004022	Mojɔ bo momi omina yona ohela a yogo adaka na bianga domi-inɛi na dea .
44004023	Ama bo cingoama , ba’mi kɛ oko ai bina’bu , na babatɔndɔ mijɔ misusu mibala nganga na basuku .
44004024	Yana aka bo , basakoa Njambe na molema momɔci bo , Kumu oDiko na oNase , wɛ oyoa Diko na Nase , na madiba-mamukwa , na leka losusu lua lodi a bisika bimina .
44004025	Na obala na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke oko na monɔkɔ motata osu Dawidi , mokɔmɛli owɛ ; obala bo , Makota madi na ejoki , Na bato bangando badumbaka ndungu jingasa mojɔ moye ?
44004026	Bakumu bangondo badi na mosɛlingo mobila , Na bakonji batitani , A bona na Kumu na Masiya onde .
44004027	Soti mɛnɛ , batitana a ngando ye a bona na Yesu Mwana owɛ mosɛnɔke yona ohɛngɛ wɛ , — oko Elode , na Pontio Pilato , na bato bamakota matongo , na bato baYisalaele pongono .
44004028	Oko boa bangameja ngando jisusu jikana wɛ eyou na ngulu na bowɛi bowɛ .
44004029	Edɛye Kumu , ika rnijɔ mikaneaka bo . Pa bakɔmɛli bawɛ bogale bonɛnɛ bo botɔndɔe mwako mowɛ .
44004030	Ninoja ebɔ ewɛ a bosengoa , na a bokɔ bimbete na mindumba a kombe eYesu Mwana owɛ mosɛnɔke .
44004031	Aseja bo bo’nga , ndako edaka bo baboli ekumana oko bokumana . Ibo basusu baluma na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke , na batɔndɔ Mwako moNjambe na bogale .
44004032	Bato basusu baya bajima , kanga banɛnɛ mɛnɛ , badaka na molema momɔci na mwembo momɔci . Pɛpɛ nongo moto obala bo leka londe lodaka ai yo mɛnɛ ; bakabana leka losusu .
44004033	Babwɛnji batɔndɔ mwako mobongɔ boYesu a bogwa na kpaci enɛnɛ , na monganji moNjambe monɛnɛ modaka na bu .
44004034	Pɛpɛ nongo moto obu odaka na taka , cina bo baya badaka na gbie isa ndako , bajingɛjɛ , badoa na likonja lileka longɛjɛ bo ,
44004035	na balisambea a bibota bibabwɛnji . Oko boa moto na moto asɔ libondo lia libwana na taka ende .
44004036	Okina MoLewi pongono , kombe ende Yosepa , ( Babwɛnji bamobakea kombe etongo Balanaba . Cina ekombe emina edi Mwana oEleho , ) moto oKupulio ,
44004037	angɛjɛ gbie ende , adoa na likonja limina , na alisambea a bibota bibabwɛnji .
44005001	Okina momi , kombe ende Anania , na mwali onde Sapila , bangɛjɛ gbie .
44005002	Iyo ko abomba ekenge elikonja , oko na mojimo momwali onde . Adoa na ekenge etongo , na alisambea a bibota bibabwɛnji .
44005003	Pɛtɛlo ko abala bo , Anania , Satana alumejai molema mowɛ bo okosee Mwembo Mosɛnɔke , na bo obombe ekenge elikonja ligbie mojɔ moye ?
44005004	Adaka wɛ pɛ bopeta ngɛjɛ gbie , edaka oko ai wɛ ; na yana angɛjɛi wɛ gbie , likonja lidaki oko likonja liwɛ bo okɔe o apalaki wɛ . Oko boa , olɛi a molema mowɛ bo okɔe mojɔ momina cina eye ? Wɛ okosei Njambe , te bato .
44005005	Anania , ama yo ka bikenge bimina , ami kwa oko nase , ami gwa oko bogwa . Na bato basusu baya baka mojɔ momina baluluma na bɔ .
44005006	Menga ko badoa , bamodinga , bamotomba na bamopusea .
44005007	Yana anɔ isa heures jisato na dea , mwali onde adoa , pɛ nongo bojeba mojɔ momina .
44005008	Na Pɛtɛlo abala na nde bo , Tɔndɔ mbi isa ongɛjɛini gbie na bobuno bu ? Iyo asɔmbeja bo , Ee , oko bobuno bomina .
44005009	Pɛtɛlo abala na nde bo , Ino odumbini ndungu bo omekeni Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mojɔ moye ? Hokea ! Bibota bibato baya bapusei muma’wɛ bidi ya a monɔkɔ mondako , na bâtomba wɛ pongono .
44005010	Iyo akwa bokpa a bibota binde , na agwa oko bogwa . Yana akwea menga , bamotana oko mogo , bamotomba na bamopusea a dɔngɔ dimuma nde .
44005011	Bato basusu baDenga , na bato basusu batongo baya baka mojɔ momina , badaka na bɔ bonɛnɛ mɛnɛ .
44005012	Babwɛnji bakɔkɔ bimbete na mindumba minɛnɛ a boso bobato . Batitanaka na molema momɔci a Eseba eSɔlɔmɔ .
44005013	Bato batongo badaka na bɔ a bocingama na bu ; bato bangando ko basepaka na bu bou mɛnɛ .
44005014	Na etango ebato baya bajimea Kumu ehɛ oko bohɛ , banɛnɛ mɛnɛ , na bami na bali pongono .
44005015	Bamejaka bato babego a macilinga , na babasambeaka a bisambe na matɔkɔ mabu , na njingo bo Pɛtɛlo akanɔ , esie ende ekunde bakina babu .
44005016	Na bato banɛnɛ badonga a ngando jitongo jia jidaka mbuci , a bodoa a Yelusalema na babego , na bato baya badingoaka na miembo mibe ; na bahela kanga basusu mɛnɛ .
44005017	Mosuku onganga , na bato basusu baya badaka bacingi na nde ( oko bato baejimeli eBaSadoki ) badaka na likaka linɛnɛ a mojɔ momina .
44005018	Bato bamina bangɔ , bapea babwɛnji , na babasa ta blɔkɔ engando .
44005019	Obwɛnji ko oKumu adipoa midipe miblɔkɔ na bulu , abameja sokolu , na abala bo ,
44005020	Kɛni , imani mema oko oho a tempelo , tɔndɔni bato mwako mosusu moBomɔ .
44005021	Ibo baka mojɔ momina , na bakwea a tempelo ehuma mɛnɛ , na babanga bokoja . Yana atitana mosuku onganga na bato bande , babolea likita libajuji , na basuku baYisalaele , na baloma ndɔsɔ ebabwɛnji a blɔkɔ .
44005022	Bapolisi baya bakɛ baibatana a blɔkɔ ; oko boa bahula oko na bwɛnji bomina .
44005023	Babala bo , Iso botani ndako eblɔkɔ ebaki bopele mɛnɛ , na basinjili badaki ba’mi ta midipe ; adipoi so ko modipe , botaniti nongo moto a tei .
44005024	Yana aka mosuku otempelo , na basuku banganga mojɔ momina , badaka na bokamoa bonɛnɛ , pɛ bocingea nongo cina emina .
44005025	Okina moto adoa a ehole emina , na abala na bu bo , Ikani ! Bami basabi no ta blɔkɔ badi oko oho a tempelo , na bakojaka bato .
44005026	Oko boa , kapitɛni akɛ na bapolisi na abapea , te na sanga ko , mojɔ bo badaka na bɔ , isa bato badi boba’la matai .
44005027	Bahula na bu , na babameja a boso bolikita . Mosuku onganga abanga bobakokeleja .
44005028	Abala bo , Iso boilemba no na mobeko mopipo mɛnɛ bo otakojani koko a kombe emina ? Anjani edɛye ko ; olumejaini Yelusalema na bokoja bonu , na opalakani bobakea lindo jimakia mamoto omina oko ai so .
44005029	Pɛtɛlo na babwɛnji batongo basɔmbeja bo , Na Njambe , na bato , iso bodi bosuma gbo oko Njambe .
44005030	Njambe obasangwa’su angɔjɔ Yesu yana amobakea no a mole na omowani .
44005031	Njambe ko amokumeja a ebɔ ende ebami , Kumu na Moheleja , a mojɔ mobohekoja milema miYisalaele na boyɛ jibe jibu .
44005032	Iso bodi banjɛnɛki bangando jimina , na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke pongono , mua mopaka Njambe ai baya bamosumaka .
44005033	Yana aka bo bikenge bimina , bakɛnjɔ kɛnjɔ enɛnɛ , na badaka na posa bo babawoe .
44005034	Okina MoPalusi ko angɔ a tei elikita , kombe ende Gamaliele . Iyo adaka mokoja oMibeko , na adaka na gala epele a tei ebato basusu , na apa monɔkɔ bo bamanejae babwɛnji mweka .
44005035	Abala na likita bo , Ino bami baYisalaele , toma nganjamani na mojɔ mokanaka no bokɔ na bato ba .
44005036	Mojɔ bo Teuda adoa , te nongo ehele , na ajimeja bato bo adi okina kumu . Na bato bacingama na nde isa mikama minɛi na dea . Bamowa yo mɛnɛ , na bato basusu baya bacingama na nde bacia na basamboa .
44005037	Okina otongo koko , Yuda oGalile , angɔ ngɔngɔ jinde , oko a ehole elangaka bo etango ebato , na alɛngɛ bakma bato ai yo . Iyo agwa pongono , na bato basusu baya bacingama na nde banangana oko bonangana .
44005038	A mojɔ momina , mbi nalehaka no bo otakɔni na bato ba nongo mojɔ ; kinani badae . Cina bo , isa mojɔ mumu , isa elomu yeye edi oko mojɔ mobato pɛ , edi bodimoa .
44005039	Isa ko modi mojɔ moNjambe , ino otahɔnɔkɔni bomogbokeja ; toma nganjamani bo osaka ’ nani na Njambe yo mɛnɛ .
44005040	Bajima mojɔ mobala yo . Babea babwɛnji , babatueja , bababekea bo batabala koko a kombe eYesu , na babacingoa .
44005041	Babwɛnji bamana a likita , na badaka na sepi mojɔ bo babwana bosɔ ekumu ebosamboa a mojɔ mokombe emina .
44005042	Bakoja busa na busa a tempelo na a ndako , na batɔndɔ Mwako Mopele moYesu Masiya , pɛ nongo bokina .
44006001	Etango ebacingami ehɛkɛ oko bohɛ a masu mamina . BaYuda ko baya babalaka kɔpi eBaEla badaka na manungunungu a mojɔ moBaEbele , cina bo bali babu babogwa baisɔkɔ libondo libipeeli busa na busa .
44006002	Babwɛnji domi-na-babae babolea likita libacingami ; babala na bu bo , Iso bobwaniti bokina mwako moNjambe botɔndɔ a bokɔ elomu emesa .
44006003	Baninga , dukani bami sambo a tei enu , bato bagala epele baya balumi na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke na bowɛi , bo bobapɛ elomu emina .
44006004	Iso ko bodi bosahɛngɛ oko a mojɔ mobo’nga na elomu eMwako Mopele .
44006005	Bato basusu bajima mojɔ momina ; na bahɔ Sɛtɛpano , moto oejimeli yona oluma na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke . Bahɔ koko Pilipo na Pulokɔlɔ , Nikanola na Timona , Palamena na Nikola , mocingami oAntiokia .
44006006	Babameja a boso bobabwɛnji , baya ba’nga Njambe , na babakea mɔmɔ ai bo .
44006007	Mwako moNjambe monangana . Etango ebacingami ehɛ bou mɛnɛ a Yelusalema , na nganga banɛnɛ bahekoa a ejimeli emina na lisuma .
44006008	Sɛtɛpano aluma na ngulu na monganji , na akɔkɔ bimbete na mindumba a tei ebato .
44006009	Bakina bato ko babanga boboma kitɛ na Sɛtɛpano , oko bato basinagoge eBikomba , na BaKulene , na BaKilikia , na BaAsia .
44006010	Ibo ko bagboka na bowɛi bonde , mojɔ bo yo abalaka oko na Mwembo .
44006011	A mojɔ momina , bajimeja bakina bato na poloso bo babale bo , Iso bomo’ki yana abali yo bikenge bibosambolu a mojɔ moMose na a mojɔ moNjambe .
44006012	Oko boa bakeja bato kɛlɛ , na basuku na basɔni pongono . Ibo badoa , bamopea , na bakɛ na nde a esambi .
44006013	Bameja batati babokosea baya babala bo , Moto yoyo t’akinake bobala mijɔ mibosambolu a mojɔ moesika ye esɛnɔke , na Mibeko pongono .
44006014	Iso bomo’ki yana abali yo bo Yesu , yona oNasaleta , adi bobuka esika ye , na bobeja mijɔ misɔ so ai Mose .
44006015	Bato basusu baya badaka a esambi banjaka Sɛtɛpano linjenje , na banɛ boso bonde o boso boobwɛnji oDiko .
44007001	Mosuku onganga abala bo , Mijɔ mi midi soti ?
44007002	Sɛtɛpano asɔmbeja bo , Baninga na basango , hokeani ! Njambe oekumu asaboloja ai tata osu Abalayama yana adaka yo a Mesopotamia , oko apetakini kɛ a Alana .
44007003	Abala na nde bo , Donga ya a esika yeye . Kina bato bawɛ mɛnɛ a bokɛ a ngondo etongo . Mbi mɛnɛ nadi boneja wɛ esika emina .
44007004	Oko boa yo adonga a ngondo eKaladai , na akɛ adae a Alana . Yana agwa sangwa’nde , Njambe amodongeja a esika emina , bo adoe a ngondo ye edi no edɛye .
44007005	Endele ko , aimopa nongo mokpɔtɔ a ngondo ye esu , pɛpɛ nongo esimbo emɔci . Yana adaka yo ngasa , pɛpɛ mwana , Njambe amokinea sako bo ngondo ye edae oko ai yo na bana bande .
44007006	Njambe abala koko na nde bo bana bande badi boyeyoa a ekina ngondo etongo , bo badi boda a libuli oho , na bo badi boda na minɔngɔ bianga mikama minɛi .
44007007	Njambe abala koko bo , Mbi nâsambeja bato baya bâbapika babuli . Ngɔngɔ jimina ko , badi bomana a bohu , na bâkɔmɛ mbi a esika ye .
44007008	Njambe abakea na Abalayama mokongo mobolena-ganda . Oko boa , yana abota yo Isaka , Abalayama amolena ganda a busa bobomwambe . Isaka abota Yakobo , na Yakobo abota batata domi-na-babae .
44007009	Batata bamina bangɛjɛ Yosepa a Ejipito , oko a mojɔ molikaka .
44007010	Njambe ko adaka na nde , na amoheleja a minɔngɔ minde misusu . Amopa koko bowɛi , na amokɔ monganji a boso boPalo kumu oEjipito . Iyo abakea Yosepa gouverneur oEjipito , na amopa kpaci a ndako ende esusu .
44007011	Linjale lidoa linɛnɛ a makota masusu maEjipito na Kanana , jɔɔlɔ enɛnɛ mɛnɛ . Batata basu baiboloja nongo leka loboyaka .
44007012	Yakobo ko aka bo ndongo jidaka a Ejipito , na aloma batata basu oho , — ehole eboso yena .
44007013	Yana asɔmbɔ bo koko oho , Yosepa ajebeja bananango bo yo adi mwangwa’bu . Oko boa mojɔ mombota eYosepa moboloa ai Palo .
44007014	Yosepa aloma ndɔsɔ esangwa’nde Yakobo na denga dinde disusu , bato macinda masato na domi na bato batano .
44007015	Oko boa Yakobo akɛ a Ejipito na agwa oho , na batata basu pongono .
44007016	Babatomba na babapusea a Sekeme , oko a esɛmɔ ema somba Abalayama na likonja ai bana baAmola .
44007017	Yana abatama ehole ebongameja sako ekina Njambe na Abalayama , bato basu bahɛ bou mɛnɛ a Ejipito .
44007018	Okina otongo adaka kumu a ehole emina , yona oijeba mojɔ moYosepa .
44007019	Kumu omina akɔ poloso na bato basu , anɔngeja batata basu , na adumba mobeko bo badumbe bana babu bakɛkɛlɛkɛ bo batahela .
44007020	Mose ahotama a ehole emina , mwana obomwenga mɛnɛ a boso boNjambe . Bamobanea songe basato a ndako esangwa’nde .
44007021	Yana amomeja bo sokolu , mwamwali oPalo amoboloja , na amobɔkɔ o mwana’nde mɛnɛ .
44007022	Bakoja Mose mijɔ misusu mibowɛi boEjipito , na adaka moto monɛnɛ a mojɔ moebaeli ende na bilomu binde .
44007023	Yana adaka yo na bianga domi-inɛi , akana bo akɛe a bonja bato bande mɛnɛ , bana baYisalaele .
44007024	Iyo anɛ okina obu na monɔngɔ na amokakela . Awa moto oEjipito , na aheleja yona odaka na monɔngɔ .
44007025	Iyo alɛ bo bato bande mɛnɛ badi bocingea bo Njambe adi bobaheleja na ebɔ ende . Ibo ko baicingea .
44007026	Ahoa koko busa , atana bakina babu baya bawanaka , na akwea bosiili . Abala bo , Ino bami , ino bananange jibato , okɔkɔni mojɔ mu mobe cina eye ?
44007027	Moto ko yona oma banga mojɔ na motuteano monde , amolona na abala na nde bo , Obakei wɛ kumu na juji osu nda ?
44007028	Opalaka bowa mbi o awabi wɛ MoEjipito mɔkɔ ?
44007029	Mose acia oko bocia a mojɔ moekenge emina . Akɛ adae a likota liMidiana , na abota bana-bami babae oho .
44007030	Yana asia bianga domi-inɛi , obwɛnji oDiko asaboloja ai yo a lipumba limole mua mongoa mosa , oho a lisobe liMono moSinai .
44007031	Yana anɛ Mose mojɔ momina , akamoa bou . Abatama yo ko a bokokeleja mojɔ , Kumu abala na nde bo ,
44007032	Mbi nadi Njambe obatata bawɛ ; Njambe oAbalayama , oIsaka , na oYakobo . Mose aluluma na bɔ , pɛ bohɔnɔ bonja .
44007033	Kumu abala na nde bo , Ihwa sapata a bibota biwɛ , mojɔ bo esika edi wɛ edi mokpɔtɔ mosɛnɔke .
44007034	Mbi nanɛkɛ soti monɔngɔ mobato bambi a Ejipito . Nakaka mibemo mibu , na natiti ya bo nabahelejae . Edɛye , doa , nâloma wɛ a Ejipito .
44007035	Oko boa Njambe aloma Mose bo adae kumu , na juji , na moheleja , oko na ngulu eebɔ eobwɛnji oDiko yona osaboloja ai yo a lipumba , — oko Mose oma bo lona boso yana abala ’ bo bo , Obakei wɛ kumu na juji osu nda ?
44007036	Iyo abamaneja a Ejipito . Akɔ mindumba na bimbete bianga domi-inɛi a Ejipito , a Madiba Makpetu , na a lisobe .
44007037	Mose omina adi oko yona obala na BaYisalaele bo , Njambe adi bongɔjɔ motɔndɔi ai no a tei ebaninga banu , o adi mbi .
44007038	Iyo adaka koko a likita a lisobe , na adaka na obwɛnji oDiko yana abala yo na batata basu a Mono moSinai . Iyo asɔ koko bikenge bibomɔ a bopa so .
44007039	Batata basu ko baipala bomosuma . Bamolona oko bolona , na milema mibu mihekoa a Ejipito .
44007040	Babala na Alona bo , Lua banjambe a mojɔ mosu , bo badale a boso bosu . Mojɔ bo , yo Mose yona omaneja so a Ejipito — botajebaka nongo mojɔ mua mokwi na nde .
44007041	Balua mwana-ngɔmbɔ a masu mamina , bawa masiko a bopeja elimo emina , na badaka na sepi a mojɔ moeka ekɔ bo na mɔmɔ mabu bɛnɛ .
44007042	Njambe ko ababulɛ , na abakina bo basakoe njɔtɔ baDiko , o adi mosɔnɔ a mokanda mobatɔndɔi bo , lno bato baYisalaele , owani tito a bopeja mbi masiko , Bianga domi-inɛi a lisobe ?
44007043	Otombani oko Etondo ebosakoa eMɔlɔka , Na njɔtɔ onjambe onu Lepana , Na bilimo bilua no a mojɔ mobosakoa . A mojɔ momina , mbi nâdongeja no oho a suka eBabilo .
44007044	Batata basu badaka na Etondo etati a lisobe . Iyona obala na Mose amobekea bo ayoe Etondo oko na elimo ema yo nɛ .
44007045	Yana acieja Njambe makota a boso bobatata basu , batomba Etondo emina , bakwea na Yosua a esika ebapakano , na eyeyoa na bu oko a ehole eDawidi .
44007046	Njambe asepa na Dawidi . Iyo anga Njambe njea bo abolojae esika eboda a mojɔ moNjambe oYakobo .
44007047	Edaka Sɔlɔmɔ ko yona oyoa ndako ende .
44007048	Endele ko , Yona oBonɔ t’adake a ndako jiyoaka bato na mɔmɔ . Motɔndɔi abala bo ,
44007049	Busa bodi ngɛndɛ embi ; Ngondo edi egboto a bobakea bibota bimbi . Kumu abalaka bo , Odini boyoa ndako embi na ye ? Esika eliheme limbi edi jɔ ?
44007050	Ebɔ embi mɛnɛ eikɔ leka lu losusu ?
44007051	Ino bato bamelo mipipo ! Balena no ganda , bailena no ko a milema na a matoi . Ino oswianakani na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke bihole bisusu , o akɔ batata banu .
44007052	Batata banu baikputoa bodingoja batɔndɔi basusu . Bawa batɔndɔi baya batɔndɔ eyou bo Yona Mosɛnɔke adi bodoa ngɔngɔ . Ino ko odini bakabi na bawoi bande ,
44007053	oko no baya basɔ Mibeko a mɔmɔ mababwɛnji baDiko , pɛ ko bomisuma .
44007054	Yana aka bo bikenge bimina , bakɛnjɔ kɛnjɔ enɛnɛ a milema mibu , na bamokɔ bikɛɛlɛ bimino .
44007055	Sɛtɛpano ko aluma na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke , akahoa miso diko , anɛ ekumu eNjamhe , na anɛ Yesu yona odaka ami mema a ebɔ ebami eNjambe .
44007056	Na abala bo , Anjani ! Mbi nanɛkɛ Diko bwase , na Mwana ’ Moto adi ami a ebɔ ebami eNjambe .
44007057	Ibo baditea matoi mabu , babekoa na bopipo , na bapota ai yo na mokano momɔci .
44007058	Bamogbula a sokolu engando , na bamola matai . Banjɛnɛki bakina bisenja bibu a bibota bimwenga omɔci , kombe ende Saula .
44007059	Yana alaka bo Sɛtɛpano matai , yo anga bo , Kumu Yesu , asɔ mwembo mombi .
44007060	Atita na magbunda , na abekoa na bopipo bo , Kumu , pɛ bobakea lindo emojɔ mu ai bo . Ama yo bala boa , ami hwɛ oko bohwɛ . Na Saula ajima mojɔ mobogwa bondo .
44008001	Bato baDenga diYelusalema babanga bonɛ monɔngɔ monɛnɛ a busa bomina , na banangana bo basusu a Yuda na Samalia . Badika a Yelusalema oko babwɛnji pɛ .
44008002	Bato baejimeli bapusea Sɛtɛpano , na bamoyea eyeeli enɛnɛ .
44008003	Saula ko anɔngeja Denga . Akweaka a ndako na ndako , na apeaka bami na bali bo abasɛ ta blɔkɔ .
44008004	Bato baya banangana batɔndɔ mwako a bisika bisusu .
44008005	Pilipo akɛ a ekina ngando eSamalia , na abatɔndɔ Mwako moMasiya .
44008006	Yana aka bo , na yana anɛ bo bimbete bikɔkɔ Pilipo , bahokea mijɔ mibalaka yo na molema momɔci .
44008007	Mojɔ bo bato banɛnɛ bahela a miembo mibe ; miembo mibe mimana na bobekoa na bogboma ; bandɔke na bamitɛngu bahela koko banɛnɛ .
44008008	Na sepi edaka enɛnɛ a ngando emina .
44008009	Okina momi adaka a ngando emina , kombe ende Simona . Iyo adaka nganga obole . Akamojaka bato baSamalia , na abajimeja bo adaka moto monɛnɛ .
44008010	Bato basusu bahokeaka moto omina , bato banɛnɛnɛ na bato bakɛkɛlɛkɛ pongono . Babala bo , Moto yo adi Ngulu eNjambe yena edi na kombe Enɛnɛ .
44008011	Bamojimea , mojɔ bo abakamojaka ehole eyai na mijɔ mibole bonde .
44008012	Yana ko ajima bo Mwako Mopele moBokumu boNjambe mua motɔndɔkɔ Pilipo , na mojɔ mokombe eYesu Masiya , babatisama , na bami na bali pongono .
44008013	Simona yo mɛnɛ ajima pongono , na abatisama . Aikina nongo Pilipo , na akamoa bou a mojɔ mobimbete na mindumba mikɔkɔ yo .
44008014	Yana aka babwɛnji a Yelusalema bo bato baSamalia basɔ Ebaeli eNjambe , babalomea Pɛtɛlo na Yoane .
44008015	Ibo bakɛ oho na ba’nga a mojɔ mobu , bo basɛ Mwembo Mosɛnɔke .
44008016	Mojɔ bo Mwembo Mosɛnɔke moipaka sopea ai bo . Bama batisama oko a kombe eKumu Yesu pɛ .
44008017	Babwɛnji bababakea mɔmɔ , na basɔ Mwembo Mosɛnɔke .
44008018	Yana anɛ Simona bo basɔ Mwembo Mosɛnɔke oko na bobakea bomɔmɔ mababwɛnji , yo apala bo abapɛ likonja .
44008019	Abala na bu bo , Pani mbi kpaci emina pongono , bo nakabakea mɔmɔ ai moto , asɛ Mwembo Mosɛnɔke .
44008020	Pɛtɛlo amosɔmbeja bo , Yɛ likonja liwɛ ligwɛ , na wɛ mɛnɛ pongono , — wɛ yona odingaka bo odi bosomba epeeli eNjambe na likonja !
44008021	Wɛ opeliti nongo libondo limojɔ mu , pɛpɛ nongo mweka ; mojɔ bo molema mowɛ moditi bojo a miso maNjambe .
44008022	Hekoja molema mowɛ a mojɔ mobobe bowɛ ; ingɔɔnɔ Njambe , isa abwani bokina bobe bobolɛ bomolema mowɛ .
44008023	Mojɔ bo mbi nanɛkɛ bo odi a njɔngɔ na boyo , na a mbɔci jibobe .
44008024	Simona asɔmbeja bo , Ingɔɔnɔni Kumu a mojɔ mombi , bo nitanɛ nongo mijɔ mibali no .
44008025	Ama bo tata tnojɔ moKumu , na ama bo tɔndɔ Mwako moKumu , ba’mi hula oko a Yelusalema , na bakatɔndɔe Mwako Mopele a ngando jinɛnɛ jiSamalia .
44008026	Obwɛnji oKtunu abala na Pilipo bo , Angɔ ; kɛ oho a sudo , a njea eYelusalema na Gaza , oko njea elisohe .
44008027	Iyo angɔ , akɛ oho , na atana okina mosuku oEtiopia yona odaka na kpaci enɛnɛ a bokumu boKandake , kumu-mwali oEtiopia , na adaka mobanei olikonja linde lisusu .
44008028	Iyo ama kɛ a Yelusalema a bosakoa Njambe , na adaka a njea elihule .
44008029	Mwembo mobala na Pilipo bo , Kɛ acingame na lijangi dia .
44008030	Pilipo apota ai moto omina , na amoka akalange mokanda momotɔndɔi Yisaya . Amohɔjɔ bo , Ocingeaka mojɔ molangaka wɛ ?
44008031	Iyo amosɔmbeja bo , Moto amiti neja mbi njea nadi bocingea na ye ? Abea Pilipo bo akonde a boda na nde .
44008032	Esika edaka yo akalange edaka oko ye , Bakɛ na nde o ekɔmɛli ebata bo bamowoe . Mwana-bata adi emimi a boso bomoto yona omolenaka ngungi ; Iyo koko boa ; aidipoa nongo monɔkɔ monde .
44008033	Iyo asamboa , na bamolona esambi esoti Odi botɔndɔ mojɔ mombota ende nda ? Mojɔ bo basukeja mohelo monde ya nase .
44008034	Moto omina abala na Pilipo bo , Mbi nahɔjɔkɔ wɛ lihɔjɔ . Motɔndɔi abalaka a mojɔ monda ? isa a mojɔ monde mɛnɛ , isa moto otongo ?
44008035	Pilipo adipoa monɔkɔ monde , atomba bosɔnɔ bomina , na abanga bomotɔndɔ Mwako Mopele moYesu .
44008036	Akɛkɛ bo a njea emina , bamea a ekina ediba . Mosuku omina abala bo , Anja madiba ! Mbi nabwaniti bobatisama ?
44008037	Pilipo abala bo , Isa ojimaka na molema mowɛ mosusu , obwani .
44008038	Iyo apa monɔkɔ bo bamejae lijangi . Batitea a madiba ibo basusu babae , Pilipo na mosuku pongono , na Pilipo amobatisa .
44008039	Aduboa bo a madiba , Mwembo moKumu motomba Pilipo , na mosuku omina aimonɛ koko . Iyo akɛ oko a njea ende na sepi .
44008040	Pilipo ko adaka a Asoto ; akanɔne a ngando na ngando a botɔndɔ Mwako Mopele , na amea boa a Kaisalia .
44009001	Saula aikina bokanea bacingami baKumu bo abawoe . Iyo akɛ ai mosuku onganga
44009002	na amonga mikanda a mojɔ mosinagoge jiDamaseke , bo akaboloja bato baNjea emina oho , adi bohula na bu a mbɔci a Yelusalema , isa bami isa bali .
44009003	Abatama yo na Damaseke , oko yana adalaka yo a njea , bohu bonɛnɛ bodonga bundumo oho Diko , na bongɛngɛ a esika edaka yo .
44009004	Iyo akwa ta kpɔtɔ , na aka kɔpi ekabale na nde bo , Saula , Saula , onɔngejaka mbi mojɔ moye ?
44009005	Iyo asɔmbeja bo , Wɛ nda , Kumu ? Kumu abala bo , Mbi nadi Yesu , nâ wɛ onɔngejaka oko mbi .
44009006	Angɔ ko . Kɛ oho a ngando , na odi boka oho mojɔ mobwani wɛ bokɔ .
44009007	Bami baya bamopakaka a njea badaka o bimimi ; baka kɔpi , pɛ ko bonɛ nongo moto .
44009008	Saula angɔ a kpɔtɔ ; adipoa yo miso ko , ainɛ nongo eka . Oko boa bamopea ebɔ na bamolɔndɔ boa a Damaseke .
44009009	Adaka masu masato pɛ bonɛ na miso , pɛ boyaka , pɛ bomwaka .
44009010	Okina mocingami adaka a Damaseke , kombe ende Anania . Kumu amobea a njɔti bo , Anania . Iyo ’ ɛ bo , Kumu , mbi yona !
44009011	Na Kumu abala na nde bo , Angɔ , kɛ oho a licilinga lia lidi na kombe Litangboake , oko a ndako eYuda , na duka moto ena yona odi na kombe Saula , moto oTalusia .
44009012	Iyo angaka edɛye ; na ani moto a njɔti , kombe ende Anania , akakwee na akabakee mɔmɔ ai yo bo asɛ koko njɛnɛ ende .
44009013	Anania asɔmbeja bo , Kumu , mbi nakaka bato banɛnɛ bakabale a mojɔ momoto omina , na a mojɔ mobobe bokɔkɔ yo ai bato bawɛ oho Yelusalema .
44009014	Na adoi ya na kpaci ebasuku banganga bo apee bato basusu baya bangaka a kombe ewɛ .
44009015	Kumu ko abala na nde bo , Kɛ . Mbi nahɔi moto omina bo ajebejae kombe embi ai bapakano , ai bakumu , na ai bana baYisalaele .
44009016	Na mbi nadi bomoneja bo adi bodingoa bou mɛnɛ a mojɔ mokombe embi .
44009017	Anania akɛ na akwea a ndako emina . Abakea mɔmɔ ai Saula , abala na nde bo , Mwangwa’mbi Saula , Kumu Yesu yona osanejabi ai wɛ yana adalakabi wɛ a njea , alomi mbi bo osɛ koko njɛnɛ ewɛ , na bo olume na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke .
44009018	Oko a ehole emina , leka o poso jiswi , lokwa a miso mande , na asɔ koko njɛnɛ ende . Angɔ na abatisama ,
44009019	na yana ayaka yo dia asɔ ngulu . Saula ayeyoa makina masu na bacingami baya badaka a Damaseke .
44009020	Na abanga botɔndɔ bokpa a smagoge bo Yesu adi Mwana ’ Njambe .
44009021	Bato basusu baya bamoka bakamoa . Babala bo , Moto yo , te yona onɔngejaka bato oho Yelusalema , oko bato baya basembaka kombe emina ? Na adoiti ya a bopea bato , bo akɛe na bu a mbɔci ai basuku banganga ?
44009022	Saula ko aluma na ngulu , na agegeaneja BaYuda baya badaka a Damaseke , na aneja na soti bo Yesu adi Masiya .
44009023	Yana anɔ masu manɛnɛ , BaYuda badumba ndungu bo bamowoe .
44009024	Saula ko aka mwako mondungu ebu . Ibo bamoseaka na bulu na moi a midipe mimongba mongando bo bamowoe .
44009025	Bacingami ko babea Saula bokina busa na bulu , bamonɔjɔ a mongba , na bamosoloja a tei eekɔlɔ .
44009026	Yana amea yo a Yelusalema , Saula akenga bocingama na bato baDenga . Ibo ko bamobanga oko bobanga . Baijima nongo bo adi mocingami .
44009027	Balanaba ko amosɔ , na akɛ na nde ai babwɛnji . Iyo abajebaja mojɔ moSaula , bo ama nɛ Kumu a njea , na bo Kumu ama bala na nde . Abajebeja koko bo Saula ama tɔndɔ Mwako Mopele na eci a kombe eYesu a Damaseke .
44009028	Oko boa Saula akwea a tei ebu , na akɛkɛ adale na bu a Yelusalema .
44009029	Atondo koko Mwako Mopele na eci enɛnɛ a kombe eKumu . Abalaka koko na BaYuda baya badaka na kɔpi eBaEla , na abomaka na bu kitɛ . Ibo ko badaka oko na posa bo bamowoe .
44009030	Yana aka bacingami mojɔ momina , bamoloma a Talusia , na bamosukeja a njea a Kaisalia .
44009031	Denga didaka na bowi a ehole emina , a ngondo eYuda , na Galile , na Samalia , na limbilima . Denga didaka na lisuma ai Kumu , na dinɛngɛ a mojɔ mongulu eMwembo Mosɛnɔke .
44009032	Pɛtɛlo adala a bisika bisusu a bonja bato baDenga . Oko boa akɛ ai bato baDenga baya badaka a Luda .
44009033	Atana okina moto oho , kombe ende Enea . Iyo amaka sama na yogo bianga bomwambe , na adaka mondɔke .
44009034	Pɛtɛlo abala na nde bo , Enea ; Yesu Masiya ahelejaka wɛ a yogo . Angɔ ; kolea esambe ewɛ ! Iyo angɔ bokpa mɛnɛ .
44009035	Bato basusu baLuda na Salona bamonɛ , na bahekoa ai Kumu .
44009036	Okina mocingami adaka a Yopa , kombe ende Tabita . ( Cina ekombe emina edi Dɔkasi . ) Mwali omina adaka na bingi enɛnɛ a mojɔ mobilomu bipele , na akɔkɔ bato monganji bou mɛnɛ .
44009037	Iyo akɔnɔ yogo a masu mamina , na agwa . Bamososa , na bamosambea a ekenge endako a mboba ediko .
44009038	Yana aka bacingami bo Pɛtɛlo adi oho Luda ( mojɔ bo Luda edi na Yopa hulelu ) haloma bami babae a ndɔsɔ ende , na bamongɔɔnɔ bo adoe bokpa .
44009039	Oko boa Pɛtɛlo angɔ na akɛ na bu . Yana amea yo , bakɛ na nde a ekenge endako a mboba ediko . Bali-babogwa basusu badaka ena na bamoyeaka . Ibo baneja Pɛtɛlo kasaka na lɔpu jima kɔ Dɔkasi , yana adaka yo a tei ebu .
44009040	Pɛtɛlo ko abameja basusu sokolu . Atita na magbunda , na anga Njambe . Ahekoa a dɔngɔ dinjemba na abala bo , Tabita , angɔ ! Iyo adipoa miso , na yana anɛ yo Pɛtɛlo , angɔ na ada na mobondo .
44009041	Pɛtɛlo amopea ebɔ na amongɔjɔ . Abea bato baDenga na balibabogwa , na abaneja bo adi mɔ .
44009042	Bato basusu baYopa baka mojɔ momina , na bakina babu banɛnɛ bajimea Kumu .
44009043	Pɛtɛlo ayeyoa mweka a Yopa , a ndako eSimona , moto yona obɔngejaka biobo bitito .
44010001	Okina momi adaka a Kaisalia , kombe ende Kɔlunelio . Iyo adaka kapitɛni obasoda baItalia .
44010002	Adaka moto oejimeli na lisuma ai Njambe , yo mɛnɛ na bato basusu badenga dinde . Adaka na liikabo ai bato , na angaka Njambe bihole hisusu .
44010003	Bokina busa , yo anɛ obwɛnji oNjambe a njɔti , bohu mɛnɛ . Obwɛnji akwea na abala na nde bo , Kɔlunelio !
44010004	Iyo amonja oko na bɔ bonɛnɛ , na abala bo , Kumu , mojɔ modi bo ? Obwɛnji amosɔmbeja bo , Njambe t’abosake nongo ma’nga mawɛ na likabo liwɛ .
44010005	Edɛye ko , toma loma ndɔsɔ emoto oho Yopa , kombe ende Simona .
44010006	Adi a ndako eSimona , moto yona obɔngejaka biobo bitito . Ndako ende edi a mbongu .
44010007	Yana amana obwɛnji yona obala na nde , Kɔlunelio abea bakɔmɛli bande babae , na soda omɔci oejimeli yona omopakaka bihole bisusu .
44010008	Abajebeja mojɔ mosusu , na abaloma a Yopa .
44010009	Yana ahoa husa , badaka oko a njea . Pɛtɛlo awea a mboba ediko endako a ehole emidi a mojɔ mobo’nga , oko yana abengeaka bo ngando .
44010010	Iyo adaka na nja , na adaka na posa bo ayake ekina eka . Yana ko akaleaka bo mia , yo atɔ njɔti .
44010011	Anɛ Diko bwase , na likina libɔkɛ likatite . Lidaka o esenja enɛnɛ yena epeama a matoka manɛi a mojɔ mobosoloja .
44010012	Na tito badaka a tei , tungu jisusu , na tito babolanda na mbulu badiko pongono .
44010013	Aka kɔpi ekabale na nde bo , Pɛtɛlo , angɔ ! Iwa na yaka .
44010014	Pɛtɛlo ko abala bo , Kumu , pɛpɛ nongo mweka ! Mbi nayakakini nongo eka ebe isa eka ebokia .
44010015	Aka koko kɔpi emina bo , Isa Njambe asɛnojai eka , wɛ obwaniti boenyamoa .
44010016	Moda boa bihole bisato , na libɔkɛ lisɔmbɔ koko oho Diko .
44010017	Pɛtɛlo aduka cina enjɔti emina oko na mokakwano a molema monde ; na bato baKɔlunelio baya badukaka ndako eSimona , bamea a monɔkɔ mondako oko a ehole emina .
44010018	Ibo babea a bohɔjɔ isa Simona yona odi na kombe Pɛtɛlo adi ena .
44010019	Na yana alɛkɛ Pɛtɛlo a mojɔ monjɔti , Mwembo mobala na nde bo , Ika , bami basato badukaka wɛ .
44010020	Ima , tita oho nase na kɛ na bu ; yɛ bokakwana , mojɔ bo mbi nabalomi .
44010021	Pɛtɛlo atita , na abala na bato bamina bo , Mbi yona ; odukakani oko mbi . Odoini mojɔ moye ?
44010022	Ibo basɔmbeja bo , Okina kapitɛni obasoda , kombe ende Kɔlunelio , asɔbi bwɛnji ai obwɛnji oDiko bo alome ndɔsɔ ewɛ a bosɔ eleho ewɛ ; yo adi moto oyongi epele , asumaka Njambe , na adi na gala epele a tei eBaYuda basusu .
44010023	Oko boa Pɛtɛlo abasɔ a ndako bo babwɛe ena . Ahoa busa , angɔ na akɛ na bu , na bakma bato baDenga diYopa babapaka a njea .
44010024	Ahoa koko busa , bamea a Kaisalia . Kɔlunelio abanjaka , na abolea bina’nde na denga dinde disusu .
44010025	Yana akwea Pɛtɛlo , Kɔlunelio amosɔ , akwa a bibota binde na amosakoa .
44010026	Pɛtɛlo ko amongɔjɔ , abala bo , Ima mema . Mbi nadi oko moto pɛ .
44010027	Abalaka yo boa , akwea a tei na atana bato banɛnɛ baboli .
44010028	Abala na bu bo , Ino ojebakani bo MoYuda adi na mobeko bo atakatana na moto ombota etongo , na atakwea nongo a ndako ende . Njambe ko anejai mbi bo nabwaniti bonyamoa nongo moto , pɛ bolona moto o eka ebokia .
44010029	Oko boa alomejabi no mbi , mbi nadoi , pɛ boboma nongo kitɛ . Edɛye ko nahɔjɔkɔ no cina elomabi no ndɔsɔ embi .
44010030	Kɔlunelio abala bo , Masu manɔbi manɛi , oko a ehole yeye , mbi nadakabi a bonga a ndako embi a ehole trois heures . Bundumo , moto yona odaka na bisenja bibolailiai amabi a boso bombi .
44010031	Iyo abalabi bo , Kɔlunelio , Njambe atabosaka monganji mowɛ , na aki bonga bowɛ .
44010032	Lomeja Simona Pɛtɛlo yona odi oho Yopa , a ndako eSimona nganga obiobo a dɔngɔ dimbongu .
44010033	Oko boa mbi nalomejabi wɛ bokpa , na adoi wɛ , okɔi mojɔ mopele . Edɛye so basusu bodi ya a boso boNjambe , a boka ngando jisusu jisi wɛ ai Njambe , bo obale na su .
44010034	Pɛtɛlo adipoa monɔkɔ na abala bo , Soti mɛnɛ , mbi nacingeaka bo bato basusu badi amɛci a boso boNjambe .
44010035	Iyo asepaka na moto na moto yona omosumaka na odi na ekɔmɛli ebodongo , a makota masusu .
44010036	Njambe aloma bwɛnji bonde ai bana baYisalaele , oko Mwako Mopele mobowi , na Yesu Masiya yona odi Kumu obato basusu .
44010037	Ojebakani no bɛnɛ mojɔ mua mobanga a Galile na bokoja boYoane a mojɔ mobatisimo , na monangana a Yuda esusu .
44010038	Njambe asuoa Yesu oNasaleta Mwembo Mosɛnɔke na ngulu pongono . Na yo akɛ akadale a ngando na ngando a bokɔ bilomu bipele , na a boheleja bato basusu baya badingoaka na Satana , mojɔ bo Njambe adaka na nde .
44010039	Iso bodi banjɛnɛki bangando jisusu jikɔ yo a Iikota li BaYuda na a Yelusalema . Ibo bamobakea a mole na bamowa .
44010040	Njambe ko amongɔjɔ a bogwa a busa bomasato , na ajima bo aboloe ai bato na bohu mɛnɛ ;
44010041	te bato basusu ko , oko banjɛnɛki bama yo hɔ boso , oko so bɛnɛ . Mojɔ bo yana angɔ yo a bogwa , iso boyaka na bomwaka na nde .
44010042	Na abekea so bo botɔndɔe bato Mwako Mopele , na bo bojebejae bato bo Njambe ahɔ oko yo pɛ a boda juji obato , babomɔ na bagwake pongono .
44010043	Batɔndɔi basusu badi batati bande , na batɔndɔkɔ bo moto na moto yona omojimeaka asɔkɔ boyɛ bojibe a kombe ende .
44010044	Amaka bala Pɛtɛlo bikenge bimina , Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mo’mi kwa oko ai bato basusu baya bahokeaka mwako .
44010045	Oko boa epeeli eMwembo Mosɛnɔke esopea ai bapakano pongono ; na bato baejimeli baya badoa na Pɛtɛlo bakamoa bou mɛnɛ a mojɔ momina , mojɔ bo ’ bo bɛnɛ badaka BaYuda .
44010046	Baka koko bato bamina bakabale na kɔpi jitongotongo na bakakumejae Njambe .
44010047	Na Pɛtɛlo abala bo , Bato ba ba’si Mwembo Mosɛnɔke o asɔ so bɛnɛ ; odi bolemba bo batabatisama a Inadiba nda ?
44010048	Iyo ababekea bo babatisame a kombe eYesu Masiya . Na bamongɔɔnɔ bo ayeyoe na bu makina masu .
44011001	Babwɛnji na bacingami a likota liYuda baka bo bapakano basɔ Ebaeli eNjambe .
44011002	Oko boa , yana asɔmbɔ Pɛtɛlo a Yelusalema , bato balibondo libolena-ganda basoa na nde .
44011003	Babala na nde bo , Wɛ okwea a ndako jibapakano na oyaka na bu mojɔ moye ?
44011004	Pɛtɛlo abala na bu , na abacingea mojɔ mosusu .
44011005	Abala bo , Adaka mbi a bonga a ngando kombe Yopa , natɔ njɔti na nanɛ mojɔ mu . Ekina eka ehula Diko , o ekɔmɛli eesenja enɛnɛ yena epeama a matoka masusu manɛi , na emea oko ai mbi .
44011006	Nalongotoana eka emina bo naesisoe , na nanɛ tito bangondo , tito baesika , tito babolanda , na mbulu badiko .
44011007	Naka koko kɔpi ekabale na mbi bo , Pɛtɛlo , angɔ ! iwa na yaka .
44011008	Mbi ko nabala bo , Kumu , pɛpɛ nongo mweka , mojɔ bo mbi nayakakini eka ebe isa eka ebokia .
44011009	Kɔpi ko ehula koko Diko bo , Isa Njambe asɛnojai eka , wɛ obwaniti boenyamoa .
44011010	Modaka boa bihole bisato , na leka losusu losɔmbɔ oho Diko .
44011011	Oko a ehole emina , bami basato baya bama donga a Kaisalia na bwɛnji ai mbi , ba’mi mea oko a ndako edaka mbi .
44011012	Mwembo motɔndɔ mbi bo nakɛe na bu , pɛ bokakwana nongo . Baninga ba basamano bapaka mbi a njea pongono , na bomea a ndako emoto omina .
44011013	Iyo atɔndɔ mbi bo anɛ obwɛnji oDiko a ndako ende yona obala na nde bo , Loma ndɔsɔ eSimona , kombe ende etongo Pɛtɛlo ; adi a Yopa .
44011014	Iyo adi botɔndɔ wɛ mwako mobobeleja , wɛ mɛnɛ na bato bawɛ basusu .
44011015	Na abenga mbi bobala na bu , Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mokwa ai bo , o ama mo kwa ai so a bobanga .
44011016	A ehole emina , mbi nalɛ ekenge ema bala Kumu bo , Yoane abatisa a madiba ; ino ko ôbatisamani a Mwembo Mosɛnɔke .
44011017	Oko boa , isa Njambe abapi epeeli epa yo so , yana ajimea so Kumu Yesu Masiya , mbi nabwani bomolemba ?
44011018	Yana aka bo mojɔ momina , bayɛyɔ oko boyɛyɔ . Bakumeja Njambe na babala bo , Njambe ajimi bo bapakano pongono bahekojae milema bo basɛ bomɔ .
44011019	Bato baya banangana a mojɔ momonɔngɔ mua mobanga na Sɛtɛpano , bakɛ a Poinike na Kupulio na Antiokia , na batɔndɔ Mwako Mopele oko ai BaYuda pɛ .
44011020	Bakina babu ko , bami baKupulio na Kulene , yana amea bo a Antiokia , babala na BaEla pongono , na babatɔndɔ Mwako Mopele moKumu Yesu .
44011021	Ebɔ eKumu edaka na bu ; bato banɛnɛ bajima na bahekoa ai Kumu .
44011022	Bato baDenga diYelusalema baka mojɔ momina , na baloma Balanaba a Antiokia .
44011023	Amea yo oho , na anɛ yo monganji moNjambe , asepa a mojɔ momina . Iyo aleha bo basusu bo basabekee , na bo bacingame na Yesu na lingbangba .
44011024	Balanaba adaka moto mopele ; aluma na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke , na ejimeli ; na bato banɛnɛ mɛnɛ bacingama na Kumu .
44011025	A mojɔ momina , Balanaba akɛ ndɔsɔ eSaula oho Talusia .
44011026	Yana amoboloja yo , ahula na nde a Antiokia . Batitana na Denga , na bakoja bato banɛnɛ yanga esusu . Bato babanga bobakea bacingami kombe BaKlisto oko a Antiokia .
44011027	Bakina batɔndɔi badonga a Yelusalema , na bamea a Antiokia a masu mamina .
44011028	Okina obu angɔ , kombe ende Agabo ; na yo apa eseko oko na Mwembo bo linjaele linɛnɛ likɛkɛ adoe a ngondo esusu . Mojɔ momina mokwa ngɔngɔ , a masu makumu Kulaudio .
44011029	A mojɔ momina , bacingami bajima bo balome toma a bokɔmeja baninga baya badaka a Yuda , moto na moto o abwana yo bokɔ .
44011030	Bakɔ boa , na baeloma ai basuku baDenga oko na Balanaba na Saula .
44012001	Kumu Elode abanga bonɔngeja bakina bato baDenga a ehole emina .
44012002	Awa Yakobo , mwanange ’ Yoane na mopamba .
44012003	Na yana anɛ yo bo BaYuda basepaka na mojɔ momina , apea koko Pɛtɛlo , oko a masu maMilɛmbɛ mia mipeliti lipetu .
44012004	Apea yo Pɛtɛlo , amo’sa ta blɔkɔ na ahɛngɛ basoda domi-na-basamano bo bamosɛnjɛle , bato banɛi banɛi . Mokano monde modaka bo amomejae a boso bobato ngɔngɔ jiKola-eBonɔ .
44012005	Oko boa babanea Pɛtɛlo a blɔkɔ . Bato baDenga ko bangɔɔnɔ Njambe na bingi a mojɔ monde .
44012006	Yana akanaka Elode bo amejae Pɛtɛlo a boso bobato ehuma , Pɛtɛlo adaka ahwɛli na bniu bomina a tei ebasoda babae . Bama kanda yo na minyɔlɔ mibae , na basinjili badaka a boso bomodipe a bosɛnjɛlɛ blɔkɔ .
44012007	Obwɛnji oKumu ko adoa , na bohu bohoja kasho ende ; aboma Pɛtɛlo a panje bo amosisojae , na abala bo , Angɔ bokpa ! Na minyɔlɔ mia midaka a makalo mande midonga .
44012008	Obwɛnji abala na nde bo , Kanda kamba ewɛ , lwa sapata jiwɛ . Akɔ yo boa , obwɛnji abala na nde bo , Lwa kasaka ewɛ na susa mbi .
44012009	Iyo amana na amosusa , pɛ ko bojeba isa mojɔ mokɔkɔ obwɛnji modi soti ; alɛkɛ oko bo ati njɔti .
44012010	Banɔ sinjili oboso na yona obabae , na bamea a modipe monɛnɛ moebende mua moyɛyɛkɛ ngando . Modipe momina modipoama oko bodipoama boa . Bamana sokolu , badala a licilinga na obwɛnji amokina bokpa .
44012011	Yana abanga Pɛtɛlo bocingea mojɔ , abala bo , Najebaka na soti edɛye bo Kumu alomi obwɛnji onde bo ahelejae mbi a ebɔ eElode , na a mijɔ misusu mikanaka BaYuda .
44012012	Ama yo lɛ mojɔ momina , ami ko kɛ oko a ndako eMalia nange ’ Yoane , yona odaka na kombe etongo Malako . Bato banɛnɛ badaka baboli ena , na bangaka .
44012013	Pɛtɛlo aboma monɔkɔ mondako , na okina moseka , kombe ende Loda , adoa a bodipoa .
44012014	Iyo ko , yana ambetea yo monɔkɔ moPɛtɛlo , aidipoa nongo modipe ; apota na sepi enɛnɛ a tei endako , na atɔndɔ bato bo Pɛtɛlo adaka ami a monɔkɔ mondako .
44012015	Ibo babala na nde bo , Odi na lilale ! Iyo ko abala na bopipo mɛnɛ bo mojɔ modi soti . Ibo babala bo , Edi obwɛnji onde .
44012016	Pɛtɛlo ko aikina boboma , na yana adipoa bo , bamonɛ na bakamoa bou mɛnɛ .
44012017	Pɛtɛlo ahɛhɛ ebɔ bo badae bogo , na abatɔndɔ mojɔ mosusu , bo Kumu amomaneja a blɔkɔ . Abala koko bo , Jebejani Yakobo na baninga mojɔ mu . Oko boa adonga ena , na akɛ a esika etongo .
44012018	Ahoa busa , basoda badaka na mokakwano monɛnɛ a mojɔ moPɛtɛlo .
44012019	Elode amoduka , pɛ ko bomoboloja . Akokeleja basinjili , na abekea bo babawoe . Ngɔngɔ jimina , adonga a Yuda , na akɛ a Kaisalia a boyeyoa oho .
44012020	Elode adaka na bato baTula na Sidona mojɔ monɛnɛ . Ibo ko bambɛjɛ molema moBalasito mosuku ondako ekumu , na badoa ai Elode na molema momɔci a bobakea mokongo na nde , mojɔ bo mia mangando jibu mahulaka a makota makumu .
44012021	Oko boa Elode alwa molilo monde mokumu bokina busa , ada a ngɛndɛ , na abapa eleho .
44012022	Na bato babekoa bo , Monɔkɔ moNjambe , te nongo monɔkɔ momoto !
44012023	Obwɛnji oKumu ko amoboma bokpa , mojɔ bo yo aikumeja Njambe ; mboa bamoyaka na agwa .
44012024	Ebaeli eNjambe ko enangana , na ehɛ oko bohɛ .
44012025	Balanaba na Saula , asieja bo elomu ebu , bahula a Yelusalema ; na Yoane , yona odaka na kombe etongo Malako , abapaka a njea .
44013001	Bakina batɔndɔi na bakoja badaka a Denga diAntiokia ; Balanaba na Simeona Nigela ; Lukio , moto oKulene , na Manae ( bamobɔkɔ na kumu Elode a bwɛngɛ bobu ) na Saula .
44013002	Yana akɔmɛkɛ bo Kumu na bosakoa na bokia bodia , Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mobala bo , Hɛngɛni ai mbi Balanaba na Saula a mojɔ moelomu ebahɔi mbi .
44013003	Oko boa yana akia bo koko , na yana anga bo , bababakea mɔmɔ na babaloma .
44013004	Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mobaloma boa na bakɛ a Sɛlukia . Batamba a masua a esika emina , na bakɛ a Kupulio .
44013005	Asɛmɛ bo a Salami , batɔndɔ Mwako moNjambe a sinagoge jiBaYuda . Yoane abakɔmeja koko .
44013006	Badala a mosanga mosusu , bamea a Papo , na batana okina nganga obole a ngando emina . Iyo adaka MoYuda , motɔndɔi obokosea , kombe ende Balayesu .
44013007	Adaka a esika egouverneur , Selugio Paulo , moto obowɛi . Iyo Selugio Paulo alomeja Balanaba na Saula , mojɔ bo adaka na posa bo ake Mwako moNjambe .
44013008	Iyo Elima ko , nganga obole , ( cina ekombe ende oko yena ) abalona na bopipo , na ameka bopangoa gouverneur bo atajima .
44013009	Saula ( kombe ende etongo Paulo ) aluma na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke , amonja linjenje lipipo ,
44013010	abala na nde bo , Wɛ moto oepulu na bokosea ; wɛ mwana ’ Satana yona odi na mijɔ misusu mibodongo oko soki , otakina bongulumeja njea jitangboake jiKumu ?
44013011	Ika , ebɔ eKumu edi a diko diwɛ edɛye ; miso mawɛ madi bogwa , na ôtanɛ nongo modika-busa ekina ehole . A ehole emina , lidudu lihindo limohua , na yo acimacima a boduka moto bo amolɔndɔe na ebɔ .
44013012	Iyo gouverneur , yana anɛ yo mojɔ momina , ajima oko bojima ; adaka oko na bokamoa a mojɔ mobokoja boKumu .
44013013	Paulo na bina’nde batamba a masua a Papo , na bakɛ a Pelege a likota liPampulia . Yoane abakina a esika emina , na asɔmbɔ a Yelusalema .
44013014	Badonga a Pelege , na bamea a Antiokia a likota liPisidia . Bakwea a sinagoge a busa boSabata na bada .
44013015	Asieja bo bolanga Mibeko na mokanda mobatɔndɔi , basuku basinagoge baba-lomea monɔkɔ bo , Baninga , isa odini na ekina eleho a mojɔ mobato , balani .
44013016	Oko boa Paulo angɔ , ahɛhɛ ebɔ ende na abala bo , Ino bami baYisalaele , na no baya basumaka Njambe , hokeani .
44013017	Njambe oBaYisalaele ahɔ batata basu ; akɔ bo bato basu badae bato banɛnɛ yana adaka bo a Ejipito , na abameja a ngondo emina na ebɔ epipo .
44013018	Ababanea a lisobe bianga domi-inɛi .
44013019	Agbokeja makota sambo a Kanana , na abapa ngondo ebu o lisango .
44013020	Yana anɔ bianga mikama minɛi na domi-itano , abapa sambi , oko a ehole emotɔndɔi Samwele .
44013021	Ibo ko bapala bo badae na kumu , na Njambe abapa Saula , mwana ’ Kisi , moto ombota eBenyamina . Iyo adaka kumu bianga domi-inɛi .
44013022	Njambe amodongeja , na abakea Dawidi bo adae kumu obu . Njambe abala a mojɔ moDawidi bo , Mbi nabolojai Dawidi mwana ’ Yisai ; molema mombi mosepaka na nde ; yo âkɔ ngando jisusu jipalaka mbi .
44013023	Njambe angɔjɔ Moheleja a mojɔ moYisalaele , oko Yesu ombota eDawidi , o ama yo kina sako .
44013024	Adaka yo pɛ bopeta doa ko , Yoane atɔndɔ Bato baYisalaele mwako mobobatisa cina ebohekoja bomilema .
44013025	Yoane yo mɛnɛ , yana ameaka yo a suka eelomu ende , abajebeja bo , Mbi naditi yona olɛkɛ no . Ikani ko , yo akɛkɛ adoe ngɔngɔ jimbi , na mbi nitabɔngɔ bo nacingoe sapata jinde .
44013026	Baninga , bana baAbalayama , na no basusu baya basumaka Njambe , mwako mu mobohela molomami oko ai no .
44013027	Mojɔ bo , bato baYelusalema na bakumu babu baimombetea , na baicingea mijɔ mibala batɔndɔi mia milangaka bo masu masusu maSabata ; na yana amodumba bo , bangameja mijɔ mimina .
44013028	Nongo adaka bo pɛ bonɛ mojɔ na nde mua mobwana na mokindo mobogwa , ba ngɔɔnɔ Pilato bo amowejae .
44013029	Oko boa , yana angameja bo mijɔ misusu mia misɔnɔmɔ a mojɔ monde , bamotiteja a mole na bamosa ta esɛmɔ .
44013030	Njambe ko amongɔjɔ a bogwa .
44013031	Na asaneja masu manɛnɛ ai bato baya badonga na nde a Galile , na badoa na nde a Yelusalema ; ibo badi edɛye batati bande ai bato .
44013032	Oko boa so bodoi ai no na Mwako Mopele bo , sako esɔ batata basu ai Njambe ,
44013033	yo angameja sako emina ai so bana babu yana angɔjɔ yo Yesu . Mojɔ momina mosɔnɔmɔ koko a yembo ebibae bo , Wɛ odi Mwana ’ mbi ; naboti wɛ busa bu .
44013034	Na abala koko a mojɔ mobongɔ bonde a bogwa , bo atasɔmbɔ koko a bopɔ ; abala bo , Mbi nâpa wɛ majongoa masɛnɔke masoti maDawidi .
44013035	A mojɔ momina , abalaka a yembo etongo bo , Ôtakina yona owɛ mosɛnɔke bo apɔe .
44013036	Dawidi apɔ ; mojɔ bo ama yo kɔmɛ mbota ende o akana Njambe , ami hwɛ oko bohwɛ , na bamopusea a dɔngɔ dibasangwa’nde .
44013037	Iyona ongɔjɔ Njambe ko aipɔ nongo .
44013038	Oko boa baninga , toma jebani bo bwɛnji boboyɛ bojibe bodi ai no oko a mojɔ moto omina .
44013039	A tei ende , moto na moto yona ojimaka acingoami a ngando jisusu , mojɔ bo Mibeko miMose miditi na ngulu a bocingoa no a ngando jimina .
44013040	A mojɔ momina , toma nganjamani bo mojɔ mobala batɔndɔi mosaka ngama na nu , bo ;
44013041	Ikani , no bato babosɛtɔ ; kamoani na dimoani ; Mojɔ bo mbi nadi bokɔ mokina mojɔ a masu manu ; Moto akajebeja no mojɔ momina , otajimani .
44013042	Yana amana bo , bato babangɔɔnɔ bo batɔndɔe koko mwako momina a busa boSabata botongo .
44013043	Na yana anangana likita , bakina BaYuda banɛnɛ , na bato banɛnɛ baya bama hekoa a ejimeli eBaYuda , bacingama na Paulo na Balanaba . Ibo babala na bu , na babaleha bo bayeyoe a monganji moNjambe .
44013044	Edika mweka pɛ bo bato basusu bangando batitana a busa boSabata bongɔngɔ a boka mwako moNjambe .
44013045	BaYuda ko , yana anɛ bo emumu enɛnɛ ebato , badaka na likaka linɛnɛ . Bakpɛngɔlɔ bibaeli biPaulo bo biditi soti , na bamololea .
44013046	Paulo na Balanaba ko babala na bu na eci bo , Ebɔngi bo so bopete tɔndɔ no mwako moNjambe soti ; edɛye ko , olonini mwako momina , na ojimakani no bɛnɛ bo obɔngitini bosɔ bomɔ bua bodi na bosusu ; oko boa so bodi bohekoa ai bapakano .
44013047	Mojɔ bo mobeko moKumu ai so modi bo , Mbi nahɛngɛ wɛ bo odae bohu bomakota , Bo suka engondo mɛnɛ esɛ boheleja oko na wɛ .
44013048	Bapakano basepa yana aka bo mojɔ momina , na bakumeja Ebaeli eKumu . Na basusu bajima baya bama hɔmɔ a mojɔ mobomɔ bua bodi oko na bosusu .
44013049	Na Ebaeli eKumu enangana a likota dia lisusu .
44013050	BaYuda ko bapangoa bali baejimeli , bali baesako epele , na basuku bangando pongono , na bakeja bato kɛlɛ , bo banɔngejae Paulo na Balanaba , na bababengana a ngando ebu .
44013051	Ibo bahakoa dutu dibibota bibu a boso bobu , na bakɛ a Ikonia .
44013052	Na bacingami baluma na sepi na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke .
44014001	Adaka bo a Ikoma , bakwea bo babae a sinagoge eBaYuda , na bato banɛnɛ mɛnɛ bajima a mojɔ momwako mobu , na BaYuda na BaEla pongono .
44014002	BaYuda ko baya balona bojima , bakeja bapakano kɛlɛ na balumeja milema mibu na bokosea a mojɔ mobaninga .
44014003	Bayeyoa ko a Ikonia , na batɔndɔ mwako moKumu na eci . Kumu angameja Ebaeli emonganji monde na bimbete na mindumba na mɔmɔ mabu .
44014004	Bato bangando ko badaka na bobɔtɔ . Likina libondo lidaka a dɔngɔ diBaYuda , na libondo litongo a dɔngɔ dibabwɛnji .
44014005	Oko boa , bakina bapakano , na BaYuda , na basuku babu , bakana bo babanɔngejae , na bo babamae matai .
44014006	Paulo na Balanaba ko baka mojɔ momina , na bacia a Lusetulia na Delube , ngando jiLukaonia , na a bisika bitongo oho ,
44014007	na batɔndɔ Mwako Mopele oho .
44014008	Okina momi adaka a Lusetulia yona obotama na mako mago , pɛ bongɔ , pɛ bodala .
44014009	Momi omina ahokeaka Paulo yana atɔndɔkɔ yo mwako . Paulo acingea bo adaka na ejimeli a bohela a yogo ende .
44014010	Oko boa yo amonja linjenje , na abala na nde bo , Ima mema na mako mawɛ mɛnɛ . Iyo angɔ oko bongɔ , na abanga bodala .
44014011	Yana anɛ emumu ebato mojɔ mokɔ Paulo , babala na kɔpi ebu eIkonia bo , Banjambe batiti ya ai so na elimo ebato .
44014012	Babakea Balanaba kombe Zeu , na babakea Paulo kombe Ɛlɛmɛ , cina bo yo adaka na bɛtɛ ebobala .
44014013	A mojɔ momina , nganga otempelo eZeu yena edaka a sokolu engando , adoa na ngɔmbɔ baya balwaka makongo mafulɛlɛ , a modipe momongba mongando . Iyo na bato bangando Pongono , bapala bo babawejae tito o masiko .
44014014	Yana ko aka babwɛnji Balanaba na Paulo mojɔ momina , ba’la bisenja bibu , bakwea a ndanda ebato , na babekoa bo ,
44014015	Ino bami , okɔkɔni mojɔ mu cina eye ? Iso bodi oko bato pɛ , o adi no bɛnɛ . Milema misu na nu midi oko amɛci . Iso bodoi ai no na Mwako Mopele bo okineni ngando ji jingasangasa , a bohekoa ai Njambe obomɔ , yona oyoa Diko na nase , na madiba-mamukwa , na leka losusu lua lodi ena .
44014016	Bosoboso yo akina makota masusu bo badale a njea jipalaka bo .
44014017	Iyo ko aitaka nongo motati . Mojɔ bo yo adaka mobɔkɔli onu . Akɔkɔ bopele , alomaka no mbua badiko , na bididi bibikpeteli bileka , na alumejaka milema minu na sepi .
44014018	Nongo abala bo boa , edika mweka pɛ bo bato bangando babawejae tito o masiko .
44014019	Bakina BaYuda ko baAntiokia na Ikonia badoa . Ibo bapangoa bato , ba’la Paulo matai , na bamokpakula a sokolu engando , mojɔ bo balɛkɛ bo adi mogo .
44014020	Bacingami ko bamohika , angɔ koko , na ahula a ngando . Yana ahoa busa , akɛ na Balanaba a Delube .
44014021	Batɔndɔ Mwako Mopele a ngando emina , na bakina bato banɛnɛ bajima . Ngɔngɔ jimina , bahula koko a Lusetulia , a Ikoma , na a Antiokia .
44014022	Bambilimeja milema mibacigami , na babaleha bo bayeyoe a ejimeli . Babatɔndɔ koko bo bodi bokwea a Bokumu boNjambe oko na minɔngɔ minɛnɛ .
44014023	Bahɔ basuku a Menga masusu ; ba’nga oko na ekia edia , na babakina a mɔmɔ maKumu ojimeaka bo .
44014024	Banɔ a tei elikota liPisidia , na bamea a Pampulia .
44014025	Aseja bo mwako botɔndɔ a Pelugia , bakɛ a Atalia .
44014026	Batamba a masua a ngando emina a bohula a Antiokia . Mojɔ bo bama hɛngɛmɛ a monganji moNjambe a ngando emina , a mojɔ moelomu enɛnɛ emaka bo kɔ .
44014027	Yana amea bo , babolea likita liDenga , na babatɔndɔ ngando jisusu jima kɔ Njambe na bu , na bo ama dipoa njea eejimeli ai bapakano .
44015001	Bakina bato badonga a Yelusalema , na bakoja bato baDenga bo , Bamiti lena no ganda o adumbea Mose mobeko , otahelani .
44015002	Paulo na Balanaba baboma na bu kitɛ enɛnɛ , na basoana na bu . Oko boa , bato baDenga bajima bo Paulo na Balanaba na bakina babu bɛnɛ bakɛe a Yelusalema , a bolena mojɔ momina na babwɛnji na basuku baDenga .
44015003	Bato baDenga babasukeja a njea . Badalaa njea ePoinike na Samalia , na batɔndɔ baninga basusu bo bapakano bahekoa ai Njambe . Ibo basepa bou mɛnɛ na mojɔ momina .
44015004	Amea bo a Yelusalema , bato baDenga , na babwɛnji , na basuku baDenga babasɔ bopele . Batɔndɔ ngando jisusu jima kɔ Njambe na bu .
44015005	Bakina bacingami ko baya badaka a libondo liBaPalusi , bangɔ na babala bo , Bato bamina babwani bosɔ embete ebolenaganda , na badi bosɔ eleho bo basume Mibeko miMose .
44015006	Babwɛnji na basuku baDenga batitana a bolɛ mojɔ momina .
44015007	Babomana kitɛ enɛnɛ . Pɛtɛlo ko angɔ ngɔngɔ , na abala na bu bo , Baninga , ojebakani bo Njambe ahɔ okina onu eyou , bo bapakano badi boka Mwako Mopele oko a monɔkɔ mombi mɛnɛ , bo bajime .
44015008	Njambe yona ojebaka milema mibato anejai bapakano monganji monde , na abapi Mwembo Mosɛnɔke o akɔ yo ai so bɛnɛ .
44015009	Isona bo bodi oko amɛci a boso bonde , na yo asɛnojai milema mibu a mojɔ moejimeli .
44015010	Oko boa , odingeakani Njambe mojɔ moye ? Opalakani bobakea muna a mabɛkɛ mabacingami , na so bɛnɛ na basangwa’su boihɔnɔ muna momina ?
44015011	Iso bojimaka bo bodi bohela oko a mojɔ momonganji moKumu , iso na ho oko njea emɔci .
44015012	Bato basusu balikita bayɛyɔ bogo . Bahokea Paulo na Balanaba yana abalaka bo a mojɔ mobimbete na mindumba mikɔ Njambe na bu a tei ebapakano .
44015013	Asieja bo bobala , Yakobo asɔmbeja bo , Baninga , hokeani mbi .
44015014	Simona acingea so bo Njambe adoi ai bapakano ehole eboso , bo ahɔe bato a tei ebu a mojɔ mokombe ende .
44015015	Bikenge bibatɔndɔi bidi koko na cina emina , mojɔ bo mosɔnɔmɔ bo ,
44015016	Mbi nâhula ngɔngɔ jimina . A bongɔjɔ koko etondo eDawidi yena ekwi . Ebehi esusu ; mbi ko naengɔjɔ koko ,
44015017	Bo bato batongo baya badi a ngondo baduke Kumu , Na bapakano basusu pongono , mojɔ bo kombe embi edi ai bo .
44015018	Kumu abali boa . Iyo akɔi ngando jimina , Na ajeba ngando jimina eyou .
44015019	A mojɔ momina , mbi najimaka bo ebɔngiti bo bopukejae bapakano baya bahekoi ai Njambe .
44015020	Bopele bo bobasɔnee mokanda bo bakie ngando jisusu jia jicingi na bosakoa bobanjambe babokosea , na bɔɔli , na tito baya bagwa na mocibano , na makia .
44015021	Mojɔ bo bato balangaka mikanda miMose a sinagoge masu masusu maSabata . Mose adi na bato a ngando jisusu baya batɔndɔkɔ mijɔ minde , na edaka koko boa a bilulu biehele mɛnɛ .
44015022	Oko boa , babwɛnji , na basuku baDenga , na bato basusu baDenga , bajima bo bahɔe bakina babu , a boloma oho Antiokia na Paulo na Balanaba . Bahɔ Yuda ( kombe ende etongo Balasaba ) na Sila , bato baesako epele a tei ebaninga .
44015023	Basɔnɔ mokanda mu na babapa : Njɛbɛ esu babwɛnji , na basuku baDenga , na baninga , ai no baninga bamakota baya badi a Antiokia , a Silia , na Kilikia .
44015024	Iso boka bo bakina bato basu bakɛ oho ai no , na banɔngeja no , na bakeja no mokakwano a milema . Baikɛ nongo na kpaci esu .
44015025	A mojɔ momina , iso botitani , na bojimi so basusu bo bohɔe hakina bato basu , na bobalome oho na bina’su Paulo na Balanaba ,
44015026	baya bapi njupi a mojɔ mokombe eKumu osu Yesu Masiya .
44015027	Oko boa , bolomi Yuda na Sila baya badi botɔndɔ no ngando ji na minɔkɔ mibu bɛnɛ .
44015028	Mojɔ bo Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mojimi , na so koko , bo botabakea muna motongo ai no , oko mijɔ mia mibwani na nu na soti .
44015029	Toma kiani tito bamasiko ai banjambe babokosea , na makia , na tito baya bagwaka na mocibano , na bɔɔli . Okasangbindeani a mojɔ mongando jimina , ôkɔni bopele . Dikani bopele .
44015030	Oko boa baloma bato bamina , na bo bakɛ a Antiokia . Babolea likita liDenga , na babapa mokanda momina .
44015031	Ama bo langa mokanda , ba’mi ko sepa oko na eleho emina .
44015032	Yuda na Sila badaka batɔndɔi . Ibo baleha baninga na bikenge binɛnɛ , na babapingeja .
44015033	Bayeyoa mweka , na bato baDenga babasɔmbeja na bowi ai baya babaloma .
44015034	Sila ko ajima bo adikae .
44015035	Paulo na Balanaba na bakina batongo pongono , bayeyoa a Antiokia a bokoja na botɔndɔ mwako moKumu .
44015036	Yana anɔ makina masu , Paulo abala na Balanaba bo , Kɔ so bosɔmbe koko a ngando jisusu jikɛ so boso a botɔndɔ mwako moKumu , bo bonje ekɔmɛli ebu .
44015037	Balanaba apala bo Yoane ( kombe ende etongo Malako ) abapakae .
44015038	Paulo ko alɛ bo babwaniti bo tomba moto yona oma sika a njea a Pampulia , na aikɛ na bu a elomu .
44015039	Oko boa badaka na mosoo , na babɔtɔnɔ a mojɔ momina . Balanaba atomba Malako , atamba na nde a masua bo bakɛ a Kupulio .
44015040	Paulo ko ahɔ Sila , na akɛ na nde ; na bato baDenga babajongoa bo monganji moKumu modae na bu .
44015041	Akɛ a makota maSilia na Kilikia , na apingeja Menga .
44016001	Paulo amea a Delube na Lusetulia . Okina mocingami adaka ena , kombe ende Timoteo , ngwa’nde MoYuda , sangwa’nde MoEla .
44016002	Iyo adaka na gala epele a tei ebaninga baLusetulia na baIkonia .
44016003	Paulo apala bo Timoteo amopakae a mɔngɔ monde ; oko boa amotomba na amoleneja ganda a mojɔ moBaYuda baya badaka a bisika bimina ; mojɔ bo bajeba bo basusu bo sangwa’nde adaka MoEla .
44016004	Akɛ bo a ngando na ngando a njea ebu , bajebeja bacingami ngando jijima babwɛnji na basuku baDenga a Yelusalema , bo basume ngando jimina .
44016005	Oko boa Menga mambilima a ejimeli , na etango ebacingami ehɛ husa na husa .
44016006	Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mobalemba bo batatɔndɔ Mwako Mopele a Asia ; oko boa bakɛ a makota maPelugia na Galatia .
44016007	Yana amea bo a Musia , bakenga bokɛ a Bitunia ; Mwembo moYesu ko mobalemba bo batakɛ .
44016008	Oko boa , banɔ Musia na bakɛ a Toloa .
44016009	Na Paulo atɔ njɔti na bulu na anɛ momi oMakedonia . Iyo adaka ami , na amongɔɔnɔko bo , Leka jɔnɔ a Makedonia a bokɔmeja so .
44016010	Anɛ yo mojɔ momina , iso bomeka bokɛ bokpa a Makedonia , mojɔ bo bojima bo Njambe abeaka so a botɔndɔ Mwako Mopele oho .
44016011	Botamba a masua a Toloa na bokɛ bojo a Samotulake . Yana ahoa busa bokɛ a Neapoli .
44016012	Angɔ so ena , bokɛ a Pilipoi , ngando eboso edɔngɔ dimina diMakedoma , na kingili eBaLoma . Boyeyoa makina masu a ngando emina .
44016013	A busa boSabata , bomana a modipe momongba mongando na bokɛ a ekina ediba , mojɔ bo bodaka na njingo bo esika ebonga edaka oho . Boda na mbondo oko ena , na bobala na bakina bali baya batitana a esika emina .
44016014	Okina obu adaka mwali ongando kombe Twatila , kombe ende mɛnɛ Ludia . Iyo akɔkɔ bwasa na bisenja bikpetu bibobuno bonɛnɛ . Adaka mosakoi oNjambe , na ahokea so . Kumu adipoa molema monde ho alɛe mijɔ mibalaka Paulo .
44016015	Yana abatisama yo na denga dinde pongono , angɔɔnɔ so bo , Okajimani na soti bo mbi nadi na ejimeli ai Kumu , doani a ndako embi a boda ena . Ahɛjɛ bingi na so bojima .
44016016	Yana akɛkɛ so a esika ebonga , bosongana na moseka omɔci , mobuli , yona odaka nganga oketa . Baswa bande badihaka likonja linɛnɛ a mojɔ mobiseko binde .
44016017	Iyo adoa ngɔngɔ jisu na Paulo , na abekoa bo , Bato baba badi bakɔmɛli baNjambe oBonɔ , na banejaka no njea emohelo .
44016018	Iyo akɔ hoa masu manɛnɛ . Paulo apukaka a mojɔ momina , na ahekoa , ahala na mwembo bo , Mbi nabekeaka wɛ a kombe eYesu Masiya bo omane ai yo ; na mwembo momana oko bomana a ehole emina .
44016019	Yana anɛ haswa bande bo njingo ebu elikonja esia , bapea Paulo na Sila , na babagbula ai basuku bangando a jando .
44016020	Ibo bakɛ na bu ai bajuji , na babala bo , Bato ba badi BaYuda baya babejaka ngando esu .
44016021	Bakojaka bikina bikɔmɛli bitongo bia bibɔngiti na su BaLoma a bojima na bokɔ .
44016022	Bato bangando koko bahɛjɛ daka enɛnɛ a mojɔ mobu . Oko boa bajuji babahweja hisenja na babatueja pimbo .
44016023	Asieja bo bobatua , baba’sa ta blɔkɔ , na baleha kɔmisɛlɛ ohlɔkɔ bo ahabanee bopele .
44016024	Asɔ yo eleho emina , aba’sa ta kasho , na asa bibota bibu ta misɔngɔ .
44016025	Paulo na Sila ba’ngaka na bambaka njembo na bulu tei , na bato bablɔkɔ babahokeaka .
44016026	Bojonga bongondo bodoa bundumo , bonɛnɛ mɛnɛ , na ndako eblɔkɔ ekumana oko a eyoeli ecina . Midipe misusu midipoama bokpa , na minyɔlɔ mibato basusu bablɔkɔ mitwea oko botwea .
44016027	Kɔmisɛlɛ oblɔkɔ asisoa , na yana anɛ yo midipe miblɔkɔ bwase , ahwa abɛnɛ onde na akɔ bo asawoe , mojɔ bo alɛkɛ bo bato bablɔkɔ bacia .
44016028	Paulo ko abekoa na bopipo bo , Yɛ bosakɔ mojɔ mobe boa , cina bo bodi ya so basusu .
44016029	Iyo abea bo badoe na paka . Akwea a tei bokpa , na asadumba a boso boPaulo na Sila , oko na bɔ na mongongoma .
44016030	Abameja sokolu , na abala na bn bo , Baswa bambi , êkɔ mbi ndeni bo nahele ?
44016031	Ibo babala bo , Jimea Kumu Yesu na ôhela , wɛ mɛnɛ na bato bandako ewɛ .
44016032	Bamotɔndɔ Mwako Mopele moKumu , na bato basusu baya badaka a ndako ende .
44016033	Iyo abatomba a ehole emina na hulu , asosa mapipi mabu , na abatisama bokpa , yo mɛnɛ na bato bande basusu .
44016034	Abakweja koko a ndako ende na abapa mia . Adaka na sepi enɛnɛ , na bato bande pongono , mojɔ bo ajima Njambe .
44016035	Yana ahoa busa , bajuji baloma basoda na monɔkɔ bo , Cingoa bato bamina .
44016036	Kɔmisɛlɛ oblɔkɔ akɛ na bwɛnji bomina ai Paulo . Abala bo , Bajuji balomi monɔkɔ bo bocingoe no . Oko boa , imanani na yanani na bowi .
44016037	Paulo ko abala na bu bo , Batui so a boso bobato , pɛ nongo bopeta sambeja so , oko so baya badi BaLoma , na basi so ta blɔkɔ . Edɛye ko bapalaka bo bamejae so a libombi ? Pɛpɛ nongo mweka . Bopele bo badoe bo bɛnɛ a bocingoa so .
44016038	Basoda bajebeja bajuji mojɔ momina . Iyana aka bajuji bo badi BaLoma , badaka na bɔ .
44016039	Oko boa badoa bo babagɔmbejae . Babameja ta blɔkɔ , na babangɔɔnɔ bo badonge a ngando emina .
44016040	Ibo bamana a blɔkɔ , na bakɛ a ndako eLudia . Iyana anɛnɛ bo na baninga , babaleha na bayana .
44017001	Banɔ a tei emakota maAmpipoli na Apolonia , na bamea a Tɛsalɔnike . Sinagoge eBaYuda edaka a esika emina .
44017002	Paulo akwea a smagoge o akɔkɔ yo bihole bisusu . Aboma na bu kitɛ a mojɔ mongando jiMisɔnɔ .
44017003	Abaneja cina eMisɔnɔ , na angameja bo Masiya abwana bodingoa bo angɔe a bogwa . Abala koko bo , Iyo Yesu , oko yona otɔndɔkɔ mbi no , adi Masiya .
44017004	Bakina babu bajima , na bacingama na Paulo na Sila . Bato banɛnɛ baBaEla baya bajimaka Njambe , na bakina bali , basuku bangando , bacingama na bu pongono .
44017005	BaYuda ko badaka na likaka . Ibo babea bakina bami babe bangando . Batitaneja koko bato kanga banɛnɛ mɛnɛ , na bahɛjɛ wokowoko enɛnɛ a ngando . Bahika ndako eYasona , na baduka njea a bomeja Paulo na Sila a boso bobato .
44017006	Baibaboloja ko ; oko boa bapea Yasona na bakina bato baDenga , na bakɛ na bu ai bakumu bangando . Babekoa bo , Bato ba babejai ngondo esusu , na bamei oko ya .
44017007	Yasona aba’si a ndako ende ; batasumaka nongo mibeko miKaisala , na babalaka bo okina Kumu otongo adi , kombe ende Yesu .
44017008	Bato bangando na bakumu badaka na mokakwano yana aka bo bikenge bimina ;
44017009	na bajima bo bacingoe Yasona na bo batongo , oko yana apa bo mikando .
44017010	Bacingami baloma Paulo na Sila bokpa a Belea na bulu . Yana amea bo oho , bakwea a sinagoge e BaYuda .
44017011	BaYuda bamina badaka na ekɔmɛli epele mɛnɛ , te nongo na yena eBaYuda baTɛsalɔnike . Babokea Mwako Mopele na posa enɛnɛ , na balanga Mokanda moNjambe busa na busa a bojeba isa ngando jimina jidi boa soti .
44017012	Oko boa , bakina babu banɛnɛ bajima ; bakina BaEla bajima pongono , na bali banɛnɛ baBaEla baesako epele .
44017013	Yana aka BaYuda baTɛsalɔnike bo Paulo atɔndɔkɔ Mwako moNjambe a Belea pongono , bakɛ oho a bopangoa bato , na a bokeja bato kɛlɛ .
44017014	A mojɔ momina , bacingami bayaneja Paulo a njea emadiba-mamukwa ; Sila na Timoteo ko badika oko ena .
44017015	Bato baya basukeja Paulo bamopaka oko a Atena ; basɔ bwɛnji ai Sila na Timoteo bo badoe ai Paulo bokpa , na basɔmbɔ .
44017016	Yana ambaka Paulo bo a Atena , molema monde mopukaka yana anɛkɛ yo ngando na bilimo botɔ .
44017017	Abala na BaYuda a sinagoge , na bato batongo baya bajimaka Njambe . Na abala busa na busa na bato batana yo a jando .
44017018	Bakina bato babowɛi , BaEpikulo na BaSotoiko , basoola na nde . Bakina babu babala bo , Moto yo obibalabala apalaka bobala bo ? Bakina batongo babala bo , Adi o motɔndɔi obanjambe batongotongo ; mojɔ bo abatɔndɔ Mwako moYesu , na mojɔ mobongɔ a bogwa .
44017019	Oko boa bamobea , na bakɛ na nde a Mono moAleo , na babala bo , Iso bopalaka bojebe mojɔ mu moyene mokojaka wɛ .
44017020	Mojɔ bo bopakiti ka mijɔ mibokamoa mibalaka wɛ , na bopalaka bocingee mijɔ mimina .
44017021	( Bato basusu baAtena , na bakɛndɛli bangando emina , badaka oko na posa emɔci pɛ , — oko bobala na boka mokina mojɔ moyene . )
44017022	Oko boa , Paulo ama a ndanda elibanda liAleo , na abala bo , Ino bami baAtena , mbi nanɛkɛ bo odini na ejimeli ai banjambe bou mɛnɛ .
44017023	Mojɔ bo , akɛki mbi adale , na anjaki mbi leka losakoaka no , nabolojai litumbu limɔci lia lidi na mosɔnɔ mu ; AI NJAMBE YONA ODI SO PE BOJEBA . Omosakoakani pɛ nongo bomojeba . Oko boa mbi natɔndɔkɔ no mojɔ monde .
44017024	Njambe adi Kumu oDiko na nase . Iyo akɔ ngondo na leka losusu lua lodi ena . Iyo t’adake a tempelo jipikaka bato na mɔmɔ .
44017025	Editi nongo elomu emɔmɔ mabato yena edi bomokɔmɛ . Iyo t’atakake nongo eka , mojɔ bo yo mɛnɛ apaka bato basusu bomɔ , na mohuli , na leka losusu .
44017026	Iyo akɔ makota masusu na botina bomɔci bo badae a bisika bisusu bingondo . Akolea mojɔ mobianga , na mwɛ jibisika bibu .
44017027	Iyo akɔ boa bo baduke Njambe , na njingo bo bamoduke na bocimacima bo bamobolojae , mojɔ bo adi na su mbuci mɛnɛ .
44017028	Mojɔ bo bomɔ bosu bodi a tei ende . Bodalaka , na bodi a tei ende . Bakina basɔni banu bɛnɛ babala bo , Iso bodi bana bande .
44017029	Oko boa , isa bodi bana baNjambe , ebɔngiti bo bolɛe bo Njambe adi na elimo ewɔlɔ , isa palata , isa litai , — leka loluaka bato na bowɛi na bɛtɛ ebu .
44017030	Njambe adipa miso mande a mojɔ mongando jiehole elibumi limina . Edɛye ko abekeaka bato basusu a ngondo esusu bo bahekojae milema mihu .
44017031	Mojɔ bo , yo ahɛngɛ bokina busa a bosambeja ngondo , esambi ebojo , oko na moto oma yo hɔ . Na angɔjɔ moto omina a bogwa , a boneja So bo mojɔ momina modi soti .
44017032	Yana aka bo mojɔ mobongɔ bobagwake , bakina basɛkɛ oko bosɛkɛ . Batongo ko babala bo , Bodi boka wɛ koko a mojɔ momina .
44017033	Oko boa Paulo abakina .
44017034	Bakina bami ko bacingama na nde na bajima . Okina obu adaka Dionusio , moto olikita liBaAleo , na mwali omɔci kombe ende Damali , na bakina batongo pongono .
44018001	Ngɔngɔ jimina , Paulo adonga a Atena , na akɛ a Kolinto .
44018002	Atana okina MoYuda oho , kombe ende Akwila , moto oPonto . Iyo na mwali onde Pilisila bama donga a Italia , cina emobeko modumba Kulaudio bo BaYuda basusu badonge a Loma . Apanda na bu limbaci ,
44018003	na ada a ndako ebu , mojɔ bo elomu ende na elomu ebu edaka amɛci ; bakɔkɔ bisenja bipipo bihema , na bakɔ elomu ebu oko ena .
44018004	Paulo apa bileho a smagoge a masu maSabata masusu , a bojimeja BaYuda na BaEla pongono .
44018005	Yana ahula Sila na Timoteo a Makedonia , Paulo atɔndɔ Mwako Mopele na hingi enɛnɛ , na ajebeja BaYuda bo Yesu adi Masiya .
44018006	Ibo ko badaka na nde soki , na bamotangola oko botangola . Oko boa yo ahɛhɛ hisenja binde , abala na bu bo , Yɛ makia manu madae a melo minu bɛnɛ ; mbi naditi na lindo jimina . Edɛye , mbi nadi bokɛ oko ai bapakano .
44018007	Abakina boa , na akɛ a ndako emoto , kombe ende Tito Yuseto ; moto omina adaka na lisuma ai Njambe , na ndako ende etutea smagoge .
44018008	Kulusipo , mosuku osinagoge , na bato bandako ende basusu , bajimea Kumu . BaKolinto koko banɛnɛ baya baka Paulo bajima na babatisama .
44018009	Kumu abala na Paulo a njɔti na bulu bo , Yɛ bobanga ; bala oko bobala , pɛ boda bogo .
44018010	Mbi nadi na wɛ ; pɛpɛ nongo moto odi bobakea ebɔ ai wɛ a bobeneja wɛ , mojɔ bo mbi nadi na bato banɛnɛ a ngando ye .
44018011	Oko boa ayeyoa ena yanga emɔci na songe basamano , a bokoja bato Ebaeli eNjambe .
44018012	Yana adaka Galio gouverneur eAkaya , BaYuda basusu bangɔ na bapea Paulo , na bakɛ na nde a esambi .
44018013	Babala bo , Moto yoyo alabojaka bato bo basakoe Njambe na njea yena ebɔngiti na Mibeko .
44018014	Paulo adipoa monɔkɔ monde a bobala ; Galio ko abala na BaYuda a ehole emina bo , Ino BaYuda , akɔki no doa na mokina mojɔ soti , mokina mojɔ mobe , ka nabwani bohokea no .
44018015	Edi ko oko kitɛ a mojɔ mobikenge , na kombe , na Mibeko minu ; anjani mojɔ momina no bɛnɛ ; mbi naloni bosambeja ngando jimina .
44018016	Na ababengana a esambi .
44018017	Ibo basusu bapea Sosotene , mowɛi osinagoge , na bamotua a boso bondako eesambi . Galio ko ailɛ nongo mojɔ momina .
44018018	Paulo ayeyoa koko masu manɛnɛ a Kolinto . Yana aseana yo na bacingami ngɔngɔ , atamba a masua na Pilisila na Akwila , na akɛ a Silia . Adaka yo a Kenkulea , alena swe jinde a mojɔ moekina bɛli .
44018019	Yana asɛmɛ bo a Ɛpɛsɔ , yo abakina oko ena . Iyo ko akwea yo mɛnɛ a sinagoge na aboma kitɛ na BaYuda .
44018020	Ibo bamonga bo ayeyoe na bu ; yo ko aijima .
44018021	Abala na bu bo , Njambe akajima , nadi bohula koko ai no . Aseana na bu boa na atamba a masua a Ɛpɛsɔ .
44018022	Asɛmɛ yo a Kaisalia , aduboa , abɛjɛ bato baDenga na anɔ oko a Antiokia .
44018023	Ayeyoa Paulo mweka a Antiokia , angɔ koko , na akɛ a ngando na ngando a makota maGalatia na Pelugia , na ambilimeja bacingami basusu .
44018024	Okina MoYuda adoa a Ɛpɛsɔ , kombe ende Apolo , moto oAlesandaha . Iyo adaka na bɛtɛ ebobala , na ajeba mokanda moNjambe na bopele mɛnɛ .
44018025	Iyo ama koa njea eKumu ; atɔndɔ na akoja mijɔ miYesu na bingi enɛnɛ a molema monde . Iyo ko ajeba oko batisimo eYoane pɛ .
44018026	Abanga botɔndɔ mwako na eci a sinagoge . Pilisila na Akwila ko , yana amoka bo , bamotomba na bamocingea yo njea eNjambe na soti .
44018027	Yana akana yo bo akɛe a Akaya , bato baDenga bamokɔmeja , na basɔnea bacingami oho mokanda bo bamosɛ bopele . Amea yo oho , akɔmeja bou mɛnɛ bato baya bama jima oko na monganji moNjambe ,
44018028	mojɔ bo agbokeja BaYuda na bibaeli binde a boso bobato basusu , na abaneja a Mokanda moNjambe bo Yesu adi Masiya .
44019001	Yana adaka Apolo a Kolinto , Paulo asieja mɔngɔ monde a molaba moAsia na amea a Ɛpɛsɔ .
44019002	Atana bakina bacingami a ngando emina , na abahɔjɔ bo , Yana ajima no , osɔni Mwembo Mosɛnɔke ? Bamosɔmbeja bo , Ngasa , iso boipaka ka bo Mwembo Mosɛnɔke modi .
44019003	Iyo abala na bu bo , Obatisamani na batisimo enda ? Bamosɔmbeja bo , Oko batisimo eYoane .
44019004	Paulo abala bo , Yoane abatisa na batisimo a mojɔ mobohekoja bomolema , na atɔndɔ bato bo bajimee yona odi bodoa ngɔngɔ jinde , oko Yesu .
44019005	Aka bo mojɔ momina , babatisama a kombe eKumu Yesu .
44019006	Na yana abakea Paulo mɔmɔ mande ai bo , Mwembo Mosɛnɔke motita ai bo , babanga bobala na kɔpi jitongo , na bapa biseko .
44019007	Badaka bato domi-na-babae .
44019008	Paulo akwea a sinagoge na abala na eci . Atɔndɔ mwako moBokumu boNjambe songe basato , na ameka bojimeja baya bamohokeaka .
44019009	Bakina babu badaka na kitɛ enɛnɛ , na melo mipipo , na bapɔmbeja Njea eKumu a boso bobato . Oko boa yo abakina , abea bacingami , na akoja busa na busa a ndako ekalasi eTulano .
44019010	Akɔ boa bianga bisusu bibae , na bato basusu baAsia baka mwako moKumu , na BaYuda na BaEla pongono .
44019011	Njambe akɔ mindumba mibokamoa na mɔmɔ maPaulo .
44019012	A mojɔ momina , bato babɛnjɛ mokuku monde na matambala na bisenja , na yana abakea bo leka lomina ai bato babego , bahela a bego bibu , na miembo mibe mimana ai bo pongono .
44019013	Bakina BaYuda ko , bakɛndɛli , badaka nganga jiketa . Ibo bameka bomeja miembo mibe ai bato a kombe eKumu Yesu . Babala bo , Mbi nabekeaka wɛ a kombe eYesu yona otɔndɔkɔ Paulo .
44019014	Badaka boa bami sambo , bana baMoyuda kombe ende Sekewa , mosuku onganga .
44019015	Mwembo mobe ko mobasɔmbeja bo , Najebaka Yesu , nambeteaka Paulo , ino ko banda ?
