44019016	Na momi yona odaka na mwembo mobe abapea , abadumba , abatua ; babena pola , na bacia a ndako emina oko mbundu .
44019017	BaYuda basusu , na BaEla basusu , baya badaka a Ɛpɛsɔ baka mojɔ momina , na badaka na bɔ . Na gala ekombe eYesu ehɛ oko bohɛ .
44019018	Bato banɛnɛ baya bajima badoa , na batɔndɔ ngando jibe jima bo kɔ .
44019019	Na bato banɛnɛ baya bakɔkɔ elomu edemba badoa na mikanda mibu , na bamitumba a boso bobato . Bobuno bomikanda mimina bodaka pata koto domi-itano .
44019020	Oko boa Ebaeli eKumu enangana na ngulu na ndangasa .
44019021	Yana asia ngando jimina , Paulo akana a molema bo akɛe a Yelusalema a njea eMakedonia na Akaya . Abala bo , Nâpeta kɛ oho na ngɔngɔ nadi bokɛ a Loma pongono .
44019022	Aloma bakɔmeja bande babae a Makedonia , oko Timoteo na Elaseto , na ayeyoa koko mweka a Asia .
44019023	A ehole emina ko , mokina mojɔ monɛnɛ mokwa a cina eejimeli ai Kumu .
44019024	Okina nganga oliboma , kombe ende Demetulio , aluaka bilimo bitempelo eDiana na palata . Basali bande badihaka likonja linɛnɛ a mojɔ moelomu emina .
44019025	Iyo abolea bato bamina , na basali batongo pongono baya bakɔkɔ elomu emina . Abala na bu bo , Ino bami , ojebakani bo likonja lisu licingi na elomu ye .
44019026	Edɛye ko onɛkɛni na okakani bo yo Paulo alɛngi na alabojai bato banɛnɛ , iya a Ɛpɛsɔ , na a bisika bitongo biAsia pongono . Iyo akojaka bo banjambe baluaka bato na mɔmɔ baditi banjambe basoti .
44019027	A mojɔ momina , elomu esu edi bobeha ; te elomu esu pɛ ; tempelo enjambe monɛnɛ Diana edi bodika ngasa . Bato bamosakoaka a Asia esusu , na a ngondo esusu , na ekumu ende edi bosamboa oko bosamboa .
44019028	Bikenge bimina bibakeja kɛlɛ enɛnɛ , na babekoa bo , Diana oBaƐpɛsɔ adi monɛnɛ !
44019029	Ngando esusu ejoka na wokowoko . Bapea Gayo na Alisitaluko , pakali jiPaulo , bato baMakedonia , na bato basusu bakɛ mbango a libanda limakou .
44019030	Paulo apala bo amane a boso bobato , bacingami ko baijima .
44019031	Bakina bina’nde batongo , basuku baAsia , bamolomea monɔkɔ , na bamongɔɔnɔ bo atakɛ a libanda limakou .
44019032	Bakina bato babekoa mojɔ momɔci , bakma oko mojɔ motongo . Emumu esusu edaka oko na wokowoko pɛ , na bato banɛnɛ baijeba nongo cina etitana bo .
44019033	BaYuda balinda Alesandele , na bakina bamomeja a boso bobato . Alesandele ahɛhɛ ebɔ ende na akenga bobala .
44019034	Yana anɛ bato bo adi MoYuda , bahɛjɛ daka enɛnɛ mɛnɛ , na babekoa na monɔkɔ momɔci heures jibae bo , Diana oBaƐpɛsɔ adi monɛnɛ !
44019035	Mosɔni ongando ko agɔmbeja emumu , na abala bo , lno bami baƐpɛsɔ , bato basusu bajebaka bo ngando eƐpɛsɔ edi mobanei otempelo eDiana na elimo ende yena ehula diko .
44019036	Mojɔ momina modi soti , pɛ kitɛ . Oko boa toma dani bogo ; t’okɔeni oko mojɔ na kɛnjɔ .
44019037	Odoini na bato bamina jɔnɔ , na babejaiti nongo tempelo , na batasɛkɛkɛ nongo njambe osu .
44019038	Oko boa , isa Demetulio na basali bande badi na moto mojɔ , esambi edi ya na bajuji pongono , na babwani bosambeja mojɔ moto na moto .
44019039	Isa odini na mokina mojɔ motongo , babwani bolena mojɔ momina a likita lingando .
44019040	Soti mɛnɛ , iso bobwani bonɛ mojɔ cina ewokowoko ye busa bu . Mojɔ bo emumu ye etitani ya ngasa , pɛpɛ nongo cina esoti .
44019041	Abala yo boa , ayaneja bato oko boyaneja .
44020001	Iyana asia wokowoko emina , Paulo abolea bato baDenga . Abaleha , aseana na hu , na adonga ena bo akɛe a Makedonia .
44020002	Adala a makota maMakedonia , na apa bacingami bileho binɛnɛ . Ngɔngɔ jimina , akɛ a ngondo eEla .
44020003	Ayeyoa oho songe basato , na akana bo atambe a masua a bokɛ a Silia . BaYuda ko badumba ndungu a mojɔ monde . A mojɔ momina , ajima bo asɔmbe a njea eMakedonia .
44020004	Bato ba bamopaka a njea oko a Asia ; Sopatulo , moto oBelea , mwana ’ Pulo ; Alisitaluko na Sekundo , bato baTɛsalɔnike ; Gayo , moto oDelube , na Timoteo ; Tukiko na Tulopino , bato baAsia .
44020005	Ibo basua boso na ba’mba so a Toloa .
44020006	Yana asia masu maMilɛmbɛ mia mipeliti lipetu , botamba a masua a Pilipoi . Bohwɛ a njea masu matano , na bobatana yana asɛmɛ so a Toloa . Bohwɛ masu sambo a esika emina .
44020007	Botitana a busa boNjambe a bobuka molɛmbɛ . Paulo abaleha , mojɔ bo adaka na mokano a bongɔ ena ehuma . Abala ekoka mɛnɛ , oko a tei ebulu .
44020008	Paka jidaka jinɛnɛ a ekenge endako etitana so a mboba ediko .
44020009	Okina mwenga , kombe ende Eutuko , adaka na mobondo a likina lininisa , na yo ahwɛ hiɔ . Adaka diko a mboba ejisato , na yana ayeyoa Paulo a bobala , adinda a hiɔ , akwa nase , na bamondoa oko mogo .
44020010	Paulo atita nase , asasunea a diko dinde , amodinga na mɔmɔ mande , na abala bo , Yɛni bobanga ! Adi oko mɔ .
44020011	Asɔmbɔ koko diko , abuka molɛmbɛ , ayaka , na abala koko ekoka , oko a ehole ehoa busa , na ayana .
44020012	A mojɔ momwenga ko , bakɛ na nde oko mɔ , na milema mibu migɔmbɔ .
44020013	Iso bosua boso a masua , na botamba a bokɛ a Aso . Mokano mosu modaka bo Paulo atambe na su a esika emina , mojɔ bo yo ajima bo akɛe oho na njea engondo .
44020014	Oko boa , yana atana so Paulo a Aso , atamba na su , na bokɛ a Mitulene .
44020015	Angɔ so ena , na yana ahoa busa , boyɛli Kio . Ahoa koko busa , bosɛmɛ a Samo . Ahoa koko busa bosɛmɛ a Mileto .
44020016	Paulo adaka na mokano bo anɔe Ɛpɛsɔ oko bonɔ , mojɔ bo aipalaka boyeyoa koko a Asia . Apalaka bo akɛe pɛlɛpɛlɛ , bo adae a Yelusalema a busa boDomi-itano isa adi bohɔnɔ .
44020017	Amea yo a Mileto , aloma ndɔsɔ ebasuku baDenga diƐpɛsɔ .
44020018	Yana amea bo , Paulo abala na bu bo , lno ojebakani ekɔmɛli embi a tei enu bihole bisusu , donga a busa boduboa mbi a Asia .
44020019	Nakɔmɛkɛ Kumu na lisuma lmɛnɛ na mbisoli pongono , cina eminɔngɔ minɛ mbi na ndungu jiBaYuda .
44020020	Ojebakani bo naidimboa botɔndɔ no ngando jia jibwana na nu . Nakojaka no a matitana , na a ndako na ndako pongono .
44020021	Nalehaka BaYuda na BaEla pongono bo bahekoe ai Njambe na ejimeli ai Kumu osu Yesu Masiya .
44020022	Anjani edɛye ; mbi nakɛkɛ a Yelusalema oko a mbɔci jiMwembo , pɛ bojeba mijɔ mia mimbaka mbi oho .
44020023	Mwembo Mosɛnɔke ko mojebejaka mbi a ngando na ngando bo minyɔlɔ na minɔngɔ mimbakani oho .
44020024	Mhi ko nalɛkɛ bo mohelo mombi modi eka engasa mɛnɛ ; moditi nongo na yumu a miso mambi . Posa embi edi oko bo namee a suka enjea embi , bo nasiejae elomu esɔ mbi ai Kumu Yesu , elomu ebotɔndɔ Mwako Mopele momonganji moNjambe .
44020025	Mbi nadala a bisika na bisika a tei enu , a botɔndɔ Mwako Mopele moBokumu boNjambe , na edɛye najebaka bo pɛpɛ nongo okina onu odi bonɛ boso bombi na ikina .
44020026	A mojɔ momina , mbi natɔndɔkɔ no a bohu busa bu , bo iindo jimakia manu jicingiti na mbi .
44020027	Mojɔ bo natɔndɔ no mokano moNjambe mosusu mɛnɛ , pɛ bobomba mokina mojɔ .
44020028	Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mohɔ no habanei babwela a bobɔkɔ Denga diNjambe dia disikoa yo na makia mande mɛnɛ . A mojɔ momina toma sabaneani no bɛnɛ , na baneani bwela bosusu pongono .
44020029	Najebaka bo mbi nakayana , swa babila badi bokwea a tei enu a bobeja bwela .
44020030	Na bato badi bongɔ a tei enu bɛnɛ a bokoja mijɔ mibokosea , na bâlaboja bacingami .
44020031	Oko boa toma nganjamani . Pɛ bobosani bo mbi naingwa boleha no basusu na mbisoli , mabulu na mei , bianga bisusu bisato .
44020032	Edɛye nakmaka no a mɔmɔ maNjambe na ebaeli emonganji monde . Iyo adi na ngulu a bombilimeja no , na adi bopa no lisango linu a tei ebato basusu baya bahɛngɛmɛ ai yo .
44020033	Mbi naimboaka likonja linu , isa wɔlɔ , isa palata , isa bisenia .
44020034	Ojebakani no bɛnɛ bo nakɔkɔ elomu na mɔmɔ mambi mɛnɛ , bo nadihe leka lua lobwanaka na mbi na baya badaka na mbi .
44020035	Mbi naneja no na ngando ji jisusu bo bobwani bokɔ elomu boa , a bokɔmeja bayɛmbu , na pɛ bobosa nongo bikenge bibala Kumu Yesu bo , Na bopa na bosɔ , enɔi na bopele oko bopa .
44020036	Asieja yo bobala mijɔ mimina , atita na magbunda , na anga Njambe a tei ebu basusu .
44020037	Ibo basusu bayea bio , badinga Paulo malɔbɔ na bamobia .
44020038	Na wa ebu egbasoa cina eekenge ema yo bala , bo batanɛ koko boso bonde na ikina . Ngɔngɔ jimina bamopaka a njea oko a masua .
44021001	Aseana so na bu , botamba a masua , na bokɛ bojo oko a Kosa . Yana ahoa busa , bosɛmɛ a Lodo ; angɔ so ena , bomea a Patala .
44021002	Botana masua ena maya makanaka boleka oho Piinike . Oko boa botamba a masua mamina na bokɛ .
44021003	Anɛ so mosanga kombe Kupulio , bomokina a dɔngɔ diebɔ ebali , na bonɔ oko a Silia . Bosɛmɛ a Tula , mojɔ bo masua madaka na leka a mojɔ mongando emina .
44021004	Botana bacingami ena , na boyeyoa na bu masu sambo . Ibo babala na Paulo oko na Mwembo bo atakɛ a Yelusalema .
44021005	Yana asia masu masu a esika emina , bongɔ koko a bokɛ a njea esu . Ibo basusu badoa a bosukeja so a njea . Bodonga a ngando , na yana amea so a mbongu , botita na magbunda , na bonga Njambe .
44021006	Aseana so na bu , botamba koko a masua , na bo basɔmbɔ a ngando .
44021007	Angɔ so a Tula , bosɛmɛ a Potolemai , na mɔngɔ mosu a madiba-mamukwa mosia boa .
44021008	Ahoa busa , bongɔ ena na bomea a Kaisalia . Bokwea a ndako ePilipo , motɔndɔi oMwako Mopele , na boda na nde . Iyo adaka okina obasuku baDenga sambo .
44021009	Adaka na bana-bali banɛi ; baipaka jeba nongo momi , na bapaka biseko .
44021010	Ayeyoa so ena makina masu , okina motɔndɔi , kombe ende Agabo , ahula a Yuda na atana so ena .
44021011	Iyo atomba kamba ePaulo , na amokanda mɔmɔ na mako . Abala bo , Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mobalaka bo BaYuda badi bokanda moswa okamba ye mbɔci boa a Yelusalema , na bâmopa a mɔmɔ mabapakano .
44021012	Aka so mojɔ momina , iso na bacingami bangando emina bongɔɔnɔ Paulo bo atakɛ a Yelusalema .
44021013	Paulo ko asɔmbeja bo , Oyeakani na ombɛjɛkɛni molema mombi mojɔ moye ? Mbi nadi na mosɛlingo , te a mojɔ mombɔci pɛ ; nadi koko na mosɛlingo a mojɔ mobogwa pongono a Yelusalema , a mojɔ mokombe eKumu Yesu .
44021014	Aipala bohokea so . Oko boa bokina bobala na ekenge ye , Yɛ modae o apalaka Kumu .
44021015	Yana asia masu mamina , bokanda leka losu na bokɛ a Yelusalema .
44021016	Bakina baemgami baKaisalia bapaka so a njea , a boneja so ndako eMenasona , bo bohwɛe a esika ende . Iyo adaka mocingami moyou , moto oKupulio .
44021017	Amea so a Yelusalema , bato baDenga basɔ so na sepi .
44021018	Yana ahoa busa , Paulo akɛ na su ai Yakobo , na basuku baDenga basusu badaka ena .
44021019	Paulo ababɛjɛ njɛbɛ , na abatɔndɔ ngando jisusu jima kɔ Njambe a tei ebapakano a mojɔ moelomu ende .
44021020	Ibo basakoa Njambe yana aka bo mojɔ momina , na babala na Paulo bo , Moninga , onɛkɛ bo BaYuda bajimaka pongono , koto na koto , na ibo basusu badi na bingi a mojɔ moMibeko .
44021021	Ibo ko bakaka bo wɛ okojaka BaYuda baya badi a makota mabapakano bo bakine ngando jiMose . Bakaka bo obalaka bo babwaniti bolena bana babu ganda , na bo bakme bikɔmɛli bibatata .
44021022	A mojɔ momina , iso bôkɔ bo ? Badi boka soti bo omei ya . Bopele bo okɔe oko mojɔ mobalaka so na wɛ .
44021023	Bodi na bato banɛi ya baya babɛli bɛli .
44021024	Cingama na bu bo osasɛnojae na bu , na ôbapa likonja a bonwɛ swɛ jibu . Oko boa badi bojeba bo ngando jikaka bo a mojɔ mowɛ jidi oko bokosea . Badi bojima koko bo ekɔmɛli ewɛ edi na lisuma a Mibeko .
44021025	A mojɔ mobapakano baya bajimaka , iso bolena mojɔ momina eyou , na bosɔnɔ mokanda bo bakie tito bamasiko bakabaka bato ai banjambe babokosea , na makia , na tito baya bagwaka na mocibano , na bɔɔli .
44021026	Oko boa , yana ahoa busa , Paulo akɛ na bato bamina , asasɛnoja , na akwea na bu a tempelo bo ajebejae ehole ebosukeja masu mabosɛnoja , na a bopa epeeli a mojɔ mobu basusu .
44021027	A suka emasu mamina sambo , BaYuda baAsia batana Paulo a tempelo . Bakeja bato basusu kɛlɛ a mojɔ momina , na bapea Paulo .
44021028	Babekoa bo , Bami baYisalaele , kɔmejani so ! Anjani moto yoyo ; akojaka bato a bisika bisusu bo balone bato basu , na Mibeko , na esika yeye pongono . Mojɔ motongo koko , akwejai BaEla a tempelo , na asambojai esika ye esɛnɔke .
44021029	( Cina bo bama nɛ Tulopmo , moto oƐpɛsɔ , yona opakaka Paulo , na badingaka bo Paulo amokweja a tempelo . )
44021030	Ejoki edaka a ngando esusu , na bato basusu badoa mobonda , na bapea Paulo . Bamogbula sokolu na badipa midipe mitempelo .
44021031	Yana adukaka bo njea bo bamowoe , kapitɛni obasoda aka bo ngando esusu eYelusalema edi na wokowoko .
44021032	Oko boa yo abea basaloja na basoda bokpa , na apota na bu oho adaka bato . Yana anɛ bo kapitɛni na basoda , bakina botua Paulo .
44021033	Kapitɛni adoa , amotembea , na apa monɔkɔ bo bamokande na minyɔlɔ mibae . Ahɔjɔ koko kombe ende na mojɔ moma yo kɔ .
44021034	Bato baemumu ko babekoa , bakina mojɔ momɔci , batongo mojɔ motongo . Oko boa yo aihɔnɔ bokokeleja mojɔ na soti cina edaka , na apa monɔkɔ bo bakɛe na nde a esika ebasoda .
44021035	Amea yo a ebutelo , basoda bamolwa oko bolwa cina ekɛnjɔ ebato ;
44021036	mojɔ bo engbondo ebato edaka ngɔngɔ jinde na babekoaka bo , Mowani !
44021037	Yana abenga bo bokwea na Paulo a tei endako ebasoda , yo abala na kapitɛni bo , Napalaka nabale na wɛ mokina mojɔ . Kapitɛni asɔmbeja bo , Wɛ okaka kɔpi eBaEla ?
44021038	Wɛ , te MoEjipito yona ongɔjɔ bato bila oko na masu ma , na akɛ a lisobe na bilombe koto jinɛi ?
44021039	Paulo abala bo , Mbi nadi MoYuda , moto oTalusia oho Kilikia . Mbi nadi sɔmi ongando enɛnɛ . Kinani nabale na bato .
44021040	Ajima yo bo Paulo abale , yo ama a ebutelo , ahɛhɛ ehɔ ende ai bato . Ibo bayɛyɔ bowi , na abanga bobala na bu a kɔpi eBaEbele bo .
44022001	Baninga na basangwa ’ mbi , hokeani bikenge bimbi bo nasalongejae a boso bonu .
44022002	Yana aka bato bo abalaka na bu na monɔkɔ moBaEbele , badaka kanga bogo mɛnɛ . Iyo abala bo ,
44022003	Mbi nadi MoYuda ; nabotama a Talusia oho Kihkia . Babɔkɔni ko a ngando yeye ; nakoa Mibeko mibatata na bopipo mɛnɛ a bibota biGamliele . Nadaka na bingi enɛnɛ ai Njambe o adi no basusu busa bu .
44022004	Mbi nanɔngeja bato baNjea ye ; napea bami na bali , na naba’sa ta blɔkɔ bo bagwɛ .
44022005	Mosuku onganga , na basuku basusu bangando , babwani botɔndɔ bo mojɔ momina modi soti . Ibo bapani mikanda ai bato baDamaseke , bo nakɛe oho a bopea bato , a bohula na bu a mbɔci a Yelusalema a mojɔ mobosamba .
44022006	Adalaka mbi a njea , nabenga Damaseke , na bokina bohu bonɛnɛ bohojani bundumo boa , bua bodonga oho Diko .
44022007	Mbi nakwa oko a kpɔtɔ , na naka kɔpi ekabale na mbi bo , Saula , Saula , onɔngejaka mbi mojɔ moye ?
44022008	Mbi nasɔmbeja bo , Kumu , wɛ nda ? Na yo abala na mbi bo , Mbi nadi Yesu oNasaleta na wɛ onɔngejaka oko mbi .
44022009	Bato baya bapakaka mbi banɛ bohu bomina soti ; baika ko kɔpi ende yona obalaka na mbi .
44022010	Oko boa mbi nabala bo , Kumu , êkɔ mbi ndeni ? Na Kumu abala na mbi bo , Angɔ , kɛ oho a Damaseke , na odi boka oho mojɔ moelomu esusu yena ehɛngɛmɛ ai wɛ bo okɔe .
44022011	Miso mambi ko magwa a mojɔ mobolailai bobohu bomina ; baya bapakaka mbi bapeani ebɔ , na namea a Damaseke boa .
44022012	Okina momi , kombe ende Anania , adoa ai mbi . Iyo adaka na lisuma linɛnɛ a Mibeko , na adaka na gala epele a tei eBaYuda bangando emina .
44022013	Iyo ama a dɔngɔ dimbi , abala na mbi bo , Moninga Saula , asɔ koko njɛnɛ ewɛ . Bokpa mɛnɛ , mbi nasɔ njɛnɛ embi , na namonɛ na miso .
44022014	Iyo abala na mbi bo , Njambe obasangwa’su ahɔi wɛ bo ojebe mokano monde , bo onɛe Yona oBodongo , na bo oke ekenge emonɔkɔ monde .
44022015	Mojɔ bo , wɛ odi boda motati onde ai bato basusu , a botɔndɔ ngando jisusu jini wɛ na jiki wɛ .
44022016	Embaka wɛ edɛye ndeni ? Angɔ , batisama , na sɛnoa a jibe jiwɛ , na ingɔɔnɔ a kombe eKumu .
44022017	Ahula mbi a Yelusalema , natɔ njɔti yana angaka mbi a tempelo .
44022018	Nanɛ Kumu ; na yo abala na mbi bo , Donga ya a Yelusalema bokpa , mojɔ bo batajima mwako motɔndɔkɔ wɛ a mojɔ mombi .
44022019	Mbi nasɔmbeja bo , Kumu , bajebaka bo bɛnɛ bo mbi natueja bato , na nasa bato a blɔkɔ baya bajimea wɛ a sinagoge jisusu .
44022020	Yana asopa bo makia mamotati owɛ Sɛtɛpano , mbi nadaka ena pongono ; mbi mɛnɛ najima mojɔ momina , na nabanea bisenja bibato baya bamowa .
44022021	Na Kumu abala na mbi bo , Kɛ ; mbi nadi boloma wɛ bohali ai bapakano .
44022022	Bato bahokea Paulo . Yana abala yo ko ekenge emina , babekoa bo , Dongeja moto omina a ngondo ! Abɔngiti bohela !
44022023	Abekoa bo boa , bahwa bisenja bibu na bamɛsɛ mopunji a diko .
44022024	Kapitɛni apa monɔkɔ bo bakwejae Paulo a ndako ebasoda , na bamotue a bojeba cina emojɔ mobalaka bato a mojɔ monde .
44022025	Bakanda Paulo na kamba , na yo abala nasalajon yona odaka ena bo , Odini na kpaci a botua MoLoma pimbo , pɛ bopeta mosambeja ?
44022026	Aka yo ekenge emina , salajon akɛ ajebejae kapitɛni bo , Okanaka bokɔ bo ? Moto omina adi MoLoma .
44022027	Kapitɛni adoa , abala na Paulo bo , Tɔndɔ mbi ; wɛ odi MoLoma ?
44022028	Paulo ajima , Ee . Kapitɛni abala bo , Mbi nasomba bosɔmi bombi na likonja linɛnɛ . Paulo amosɔmbeja bo , Mbi ko nabotama oko sɔmi .
44022029	A mojɔ momina , baya badaka na mosɛlingo bo batue Paulo bamokina bokpa . Kapitɛni pongono , yana acingea yo bo Paulo adi MoLoma , adaka na bɔ , mojɔ bo ama mokanda yo mbɔci .
44022030	Yana ahoa busa , yo apala bo ajebe cina emojɔ mobalaka BaYuda a mojɔ moPaulo , na acingoa Paulo . Abolea likita libasuku na nganga , akɛ na Paulo , na amomeja a boso bobu .
44023001	Paulo anja likita linjenje ; abala na bu bo , Baninga , molema mombi motadumbaka mbi a mojɔ moekɔmɛli embi masu masusu a miso maNjambe .
44023002	Anania , mosuku Onganga , abala na bato baya badaka na nde hulelu bo bamobome a monɔkɔ .
44023003	Na Paulo abala na nde bo , Njambe âboma wɛ ; wɛ etutu epu ! Odi ya a bosambeja mbi cina eMibeko , na osopaka Mibeko wɛ mɛnɛ yana apaka wɛ monɔkɔ bo babome mbi .
44023004	Baya badaka na nde hulelu babala bo , Ololeaka nganga monɛnɛ oNjambe boa mojɔ moye ?
44023005	Paulo asɔmbeja bo , Baninga , mbi najebiti bo yo adi nganga monɛnɛ ; mojɔ bo mosɔnɔmɔ bo , T’obale oko mojɔ mobe na mosuku obato bawɛ .
44023006	Paulo ko acingea bo likina libondo lilikita lidi na BaSadoki , na libondo litongo oko na BaPalusi . Oko boa yo abekoa bo , Baniga , mbi nadi MoPalusi , mwana oMoPalusi . Nadi a esambi a mojɔ monjingo ebongɔ bobagwake .
44023007	Abala yo boa , BaPalusi na BaSadoki babomana kitɛ enɛnɛ , na likita lidaka na bobɔtɔ .
44023008	Mojɔ bo BaSadoki babalaka bo bagwake batangɔ , bo babwɛnji baDiko baditi , na bo miembo miditi . BaPalusi ko bajimaka ngando ji jisusu .
44023009	Oko boa daka edaka enɛnɛ . Bakina basɔni balibondo liBaPalusi bangɔ na babala bo , Iso botanɛkɛ nongo mojɔ na moto yoyo ; isa mokina mwembo kako obwɛnji oDiko abali na nde ?
44023010	Wokowoko ehɛ enɛnɛ , na kapitɛni adaka na bɔ isa badi bolakaka Paulo oko bolakaka . A mojɔ momina , abea basoda bo bamomanejae sokolu , na bakɛ na nde a ndako ebasoda .
44023011	Kumu adoa ai Paulo na bulu bomina , ama a dɔngɔ dinde na abala na nde bo , Da na eci . Otɔndɔi mwako mombi a Yelusalema ; odi botɔndɔ koko boa a Loma .
44023012	Yana ahoabusa , BaYuda badumba ndungu , nababɛlɛ bɛli bo batayaka na batamwaka eka oko bapetakini wa Paulo .
44023013	Baya badumba ndungu emina badaka bato macinda mabae na cika .
44023014	Ibo bakɛ ai basuku banganga na ai basuku bangando , na babala na bu bo , Iso bobɛli bɛli epipo bo botayaka nongo eka oko bowakini Paulo .
44023015	Oko boa , no na bajuji toma jebejani kapitɛni bo adoe na Paulo ya adi no , oko na mokalo bo opalakani bo okokelejaeni mojɔ monde na bopele mɛnɛ . Iso ko bosɛlingoi bo bomowoe a njea .
44023016	Mwana ongɛnɛ ePaulo ko aka mojɔ mondungu emina , na yo akɛ a ndako ebasoda bo ajebejae Paulo .
44023017	Paulo abea salajon , abala na nde bo , Kɛ na mwamomi yo ai kapitɛni ; apalaka amotɔndɔe mokina mojɔ .
44023018	Oko boa salajon atomba mwamomi omina na akɛ na nde ai kapitɛni . Abala na nde bo , Paulo , moto opeabi so , abei mbi na angi mbi bo nadoe na mwamomi yo ai wɛ . Adi na mokina mojɔ a botɔndɔ wɛ .
44023019	Kapitɛni amopea ebɔ , asua na nde mweka na amohɔjɔ bo , Mojɔ mopalaka wɛ bojebeja mbi modi bo ?
44023020	Iyo asɔmbeja bo , BaYuda badumbi ndungu bo ba’nge wɛ a bodoa na Paulo puma a likita libasuku , oko na mokalo bo bapalaka bokokejejae mojɔ monde bopele .
44023021	T’ojime oko mojɔ momina , cina bo bakina babu , isa macinda mabae na dea , bamoseaka a njea , na babɛli bɛli bo batayaka na bata-mwaka oko bamowakini ; mosɛlingo mobu mobwani , na bambaka oko mojimo mowɛ .
44023022	Kapitɛni abekea mwamomi bo atabala nongo na moto mojɔ moma yo bala na nde , na amoyaneja .
44023023	Abea basalajon bande babae , abala na bu bo , Sɛlingoani basoda mikama mibae , basoda bapunda domi-sambo , na basoda bamakɔngɔ mikama mibae bo bakɛe a Kaisalia a neuf heures na bulu .
44023024	Sɛlingoani koko punda a mojɔ moPaulo bo amee ai gouverneur na bopele mɛnɛ .
44023025	Asɔnɔ koko mokanda mu . —
44023026	Kulaudio Lusia ai Pelike , gouverneur oekumu enɛnɛ , njɛbɛ !
44023027	BaYuda bapeabi moto yo na bapakabi mowa . Mbi ko nameabi na basoda bo namohelejae , mojɔ bo nakabi bo adi MoLoma .
44023028	Mbi napalakabi bojeba cina emojɔ modakabi bo na nde ; oko boa nakɛbi na nde a likita libasuku babu .
44023029	Nanɛbi bo badi na nde mokina mojɔ moMibeko mibu bɛnɛ ; aikɔ nongo mojɔ mua mobwani na mokindo mobogwa isa na blɔkɔ .
44023030	Aki mbi ko bo BaYuda badumbi ndungu a mojɔ momoto omina , namolomi ai wɛ bokpa . Nabali koko na bato baya badi na nde mojɔ , bo bamejae mojɔ momina ai wɛ mɛnɛ .
44023031	Basoda batomba Paulo o ama bo sɔ monɔkɔ ; bakɛ na nde na bulu na bamea a Antipatulo .
44023032	Ahoa busa , basoda-bapunda badala koko na nde , na bo batongo basɔmbɔ a ndako ebasoda .
44023033	Amea bo a Kaisalia , bapa gouverneur mokanda , na bamoneja Paulo .
44023034	Iyo alanga mokanda na ahɔjɔ Paulo kombe elikota linde .
44023035	Yana aka yo bo adi moto oKilikia , abala bo , Bato bakamea baya badi na wɛ mojɔ , nadi boka mojɔ mowɛ . Na apa monɔkɔ bo bamobanee a lopango loElode .
44024001	Iyana anɔ masu matano , Anania , mosuku onganga , amea na bakina basuku bangando , na okina nganga oMibeko pongono , kombe ende Teletulo . Ibo batɔndɔ gouverneur mojɔ moPaulo .
44024002	Yana abea bo Paulo , Teletulo abanga bobala mojɔ monde bo , Pelike , wɛ kumu yona onɔi na bopele , iso bosepaka cina ebowi bonɛnɛ bua bodi a tei esu a mojɔ mowɛ . Wɛ obaneaka likota lisu , na libɔngi oko a mojɔ mowɛ ;
44024003	na so bodi na sepi enɛnɛ a mojɔ momina .
44024004	Nitapalaka bo nanɔngejae wɛ ; endele ko , nangɔɔnkɔ wɛ bɔ oke bikina bikenge bisu oko na monganji monɛnɛ .
44024005	Iso bonɛkɛ bo moto yoyo apukejaka bato bou mɛnɛ . Alindaka BaYuda a ngondo esusu oko a bona pɛ . Adi koko mosuku obu baya badi na kombe BaNasaleta .
44024006	Iyo ameka bobeja tempelo pongono na so bomopea . Mokano mosu modaka bo bomosambejae cina eMibeko misu ;
44024007	Lusia ko , kapitɛni obasoda , adoa na amohwa ta mɔmɔ masu na hopipo mɛnɛ .
44024008	Na apa monɔkɔ bo baya badi na nde mojɔ badoe ai wɛ mɛnɛ . Okamokokeleja odi boka wɛ mɛnɛ mijɔ minɛnɛ mimoto omina mia mibalaka so .
44024009	Bayuda batongo badaka na monɔkɔ momina momɔci , na bajima bo modi boa .
44024010	Gouverneur angɔjɔ ebɔ bo Paulo abale . Paulo asɔmbeja bo , Ajebaka mbi bo wɛ odi juji olikota di bianga bmɛnɛ , nadi na sepi a bobala bo nasalongejae .
44024011	Okakokeleja , odi bojeba bo mbi nadoa a Yelusalema a bosakoa , masu monɔi oko domi-na-mabae pɛ .
44024012	Baitana bo nasoa na moto mosoo , isa bo nalindaka bato a bona , nongo a tempelo , isa a sinagoge , isa a ngando .
44024013	Na babwaniti bongameja nongo ngando jibalaka bo a mojɔ mombi .
44024014	Mbi najimaka a boso bowɛ bo nasakoaka Njambe obasangwa’su oko na njea ebeaka bo Bobɔtɔ . Najimaka mijɔ misusu mia misɔnɔmɔ a Mibeko , na a mikanda mibatɔndɔi .
44024015	Njingo embi ai Njambe edi oko njingo ebu , bo bapele na babe badi bongɔ a bogwa .
44024016	A mojɔ momina , mbi nakɔkɔ na bingi bihole bisusu bo molema mombi motada na mojɔ , isa a boso boNjambe , isa a boso bobato .
44024017	Ama mbi yeyoa bohali bianga binɛnɛ , nami doa oko a bokɔ bato balikota limbi monganji , na a bopa bipeeli .
44024018	Bakina BaYuda ko baAsia batana mbi a tempelo , pɛpɛ nongo ekina ekia , pɛpɛ koko embamba ebato isa mogbomegbome .
44024019	Isa bato bamina badi na mbi mokina mojɔ , babwani boma ya a boso bowɛ a bobala mojɔ momina .
44024020	Pɛ mojɔ , kina bato baya badi jɔno bajebejae wɛ isa badumba mbi na mokina mojɔ mobe yana asamba mbi a likita libasuku .
44024021	Isa modi oko mu , bo mbi nama , na nabekoa a tei ebu bo , Mbi nasambaka busa bu a mojɔ mobongɔ bobagwake .
44024022	Pelike ajebaka na bopele mɛnɛ mojɔ moejimeli emina . Oko boa yo asɔmbeja Paulo ; abala bo , Kapitɛni Lusia akadoa , nadi bolena mojɔ mowɛ .
44024023	Apa salajon monɔkɔ bo abanee Paulo bopele , na amokɔ mokina monganji , na ajima bo bato bande bamokɔmejae .
44024024	Yana anɔ makina masu , Pelike adoa na mwali onde Dulusila yona odaka MoYuda , na alomeja Paulo . Aka mwako motɔndɔ yo a mojɔ moejimeli ai Masiya Yesu .
44024025	Yana alehaka yo a mojɔ mobodongo na bosangbindea na esambi ebodoa , Pelike adaka na bɔ . Abala na Paulo bo , Peta kɛ edɛye ; ekina ndɔndɔ , nakaboloja njea , nadi bobea wɛ .
44024026	Adaka koko na njingo bo Paulo amopɛ likonja . Oko boa amolomejaka mandɛli-mandɛli bo babalane .
44024027	Bianga bibae bisia boa , na Pelukio Peseto asangoa na Pelike . Na Pelike akina Paulo oko a blɔkɔ , cina bo apalaka bo adae na gala epele a tei eBaYuda .
44025001	Peseto , abanga yo elomu ende , ayeyoa a Kaisalia oko masu masato pɛ , na akɛ a Yelusalema .
44025002	Basuku banganga na basuku baBaYuda bamojebeja mojɔ moPaulo .
44025003	Bamoleha na bamongɔɔnɔ bo abakɔe monganji mu — oko bo alome ndɔsɔ ePaulo bo adoe a Yelusalema , mojɔ bo basɛlingoa bo bamosee a njea bo bamowoe .
44025004	Peseto ko asɔmbeja bo Paulo adi bodika a blɔkɔ a Kaisalia , na bo yo mɛnɛ adi bosɔmbɔ oho bokpa .
44025005	Abala koko bo , Bopele bo bakina basuku banu bakɛe na mbi oho , bo bamejae mojɔ momoto omina , isa adi na mojɔ soti .
44025006	Ayeyoa na bu masu bomwambe isa domi a tei ebu , na asɔmbɔ koko a Kaisalia . Aboa busa , ada a mongbɛlɛngɔ moesambi , na aloma ndɔsɔ ePaulo .
44025007	Yana adoa yo , BaYuda baya badonga a Yelusalema bamohika na balanga mijɔ minde mibe minɛnɛ . Endele ko , baibwana bongameja mijɔ mimina .
44025008	Paulo abala bo asalongejae ; abala bo , Mbi naisopa nongo mobeko moBaYuda , isa motempelo , isa moKaisala .
44025009	Peseto ko apala bo asepejae BaYuda , na ahɔjɔ Paulo bo , Opalaka bokɛ a Yelusalema a bosamba na mbi a mojɔ mongando jimina ?
44025010	Paulo asɔmbeja bo , Mbi nami a boso bomongbɛlɛngɔ moesambi eKaisala ; nabwani bosamba oko ya . Ojebaka na bopele mɛnɛ bo mbi naikɔ nongo bobe ai BaYuda .
44025011	Isa nadi moto mobe , isa nakɔ mokina mojɔ mua mobwani na mokindo mobogwa , nitalona bogwa . Na isa ngando jibalaka bo a mojɔ mombi jidi oko bokosea pɛ , pɛpɛ nongo moto odi na kpaci a bopa mbi a mɔmɔ mabu . Mbi napalaka nasambe na Kaisala mɛnɛ .
44025012	Peseto abala mojɔ momina na likita libajuji , na asɔmbeja Paulo bo , Opalaka bosamba na Kaisala ; odi bokɛ oko ai Kaisala .
44025013	Anɔ makina masu , kumu Agulipa na Bɛlɛnike bamea a Kaisalia a bobɛjɛ Peseto njɛbɛ .
44025014	Bayeyoa ena makina masu , na Peseto atɔndɔ kumu mojɔ moPaulo . Abala bo , Pelike akina momi omɔci ya a blɔkɔ .
44025015	Yana adaka mbi a Yelusalema , basuku banganga na basuku baBaYuda bameja mojɔ monde , na bapala bo namodumbe .
44025016	Mbi nabasɔmbeja bo BaLoma te badumbake moto oko yo apeta kini yɛyɛ bato baya bamokambaka , bo abwani bosalongeja a mijɔ mibalaka bo .
44025017	Oko boa bahula na mbi ya , na mbi naimba nongo ekoka . Yana ahoa busa , nada a mongbɛlɛngɔ moesambi , na naloma ndɔsɔ emoto omina .
44025018	Bakambi bande bama , na baimeja nongo mijɔ mibe milɛkɛ mbi .
44025019	Baboma na nde oko kitɛ a mojɔ moejimeli ebu , na a mojɔ mookina moto kombe ende Yesu yona ogwa ; Paulo ko abala bo adi oko mɔ .
44025020	Adaka mbi na mokakwano a bokokeleja ngando jimina , namohɔjɔ isa apalaka akɛe a bosamba a mojɔ mongando jimina oho .
44025021	Paulo ko angɔɔnɔ bo mojɔ monde mokɛe a esambi eKaisala . Oko boa mbi napa monɔkɔ bo bamobanee ya , bo namolome ai Kaisala .
44025022	Agulipa abala na Peseto bo , Mbi nadi na posa bo nake moto omina mbi mɛnɛ . Peseto asɔmbeja bo , Odi bomoka puma .
44025023	Yana ahoa busa , Agulipa na Bɛlɛnike badoa na ekumu enɛnɛ , na bakwea a ndako eesambi na bakapitɛni , na basuku bangando pongono . Peseto apa monɔkɔ bo badoe na Paulo .
44025024	Peseto abala bo , Kumu Agulipa , na no bami basusu baya batitani na su ya , anjani moto yo . BaYuda banɛnɛ bangɔɔnɔ mbi a mojɔ monde , oho Yelusalema na ya pongono , na bahekoa bo ebɔngiti bo ahele .
44025025	Mbi ko nanɛ bo aikɔ nongo mojɔ mua mobwani na mokindo mobogwa . Iyo mɛnɛ ko apala bo akɛe ai Kaisala , na mbi najima bo namolome .
44025026	Endele ko , naditi na mojɔ mosoti a bosɔnea kumu ombi . Oko boa namobei ya a boso bonu , na boso bowɛ kumu Agulipa , na njingo bo bokamokokeleja , bodae na mokina mojɔ a bosɔnɔ .
44025027	Mojɔ bo , nalɛkɛ bo bokaloma moto oblɔkɔ ngasa , pɛ botɔndɔ mojɔ monde , etabɔngɔ nongo mweka .
44026001	Agulipa abala na Paulo bo , Obwani botata tati ewɛ edɛye . Paulo animoja ebɔ , na atata na bikenge bi .
44026002	Kumu Agulipa , mbi nadi na sepi busa bu , bo nasalongejae a boso bowɛ a ngando jisusu jibalaka BaYuda a mojɔ mombi .
44026003	Wɛ olandoa na bikɔmɛli na mijɔ miBaYuda . Oko boa nangɔɔnɔkɔ wɛ bo otangwa bohokea mbi .
44026004	BaYuda basusu bajebaka moda mombi , donga oko a bwɛngɛ bombi , a likota limbi mɛnɛ , na a Yelusalema .
44026005	Bakajima bo babale , bajeba eyou bo mbi nadaka moto oBaPalusi , baya banɔi na bingi a mojɔ moMibeko misu .
44026006	Mbi nadi ya edɛye a esambi a mojɔ monjingo esako ekinea Njambe batata basu .
44026007	Mbota jisu domi-na-jibae bakɔmɛkɛ Njambe na bulu na moi , oko na njingo bo basangoe sako emina . Ee kumu , BaYuda badi na mbi mojɔ oko na cina enjingo emina .
44026008	Okina onu abwaniti bojima bo Njambe angɔjɔkɔ bagwake mojɔ moye ?
44026009	Mbi mɛnɛ najima ehele bo nakɔe mijɔ minɛnɛ oko na lisoki a kombe eYesu oNasaleta .
44026010	Nakɔ boa a Yelusalema . Nasa bato baMasiya banɛnɛ a blɔkɔ , oko na kpaci ebasuku banganga . Na yana abawa bo , mbi najima mojɔ momina pongono .
44026011	Nabadingoja bihole binɛnɛ a sinagoge jisusu ; nakenga koko na bopipo bo basambojae Njambe na bibaeli bibu . Nabanɔngeja oko a ngando jitongo bohali , cina ekɛlɛ embi enɛnɛ ai bo .
44026012	Oko boa nakɛ a Damaseke na kpaci ebasuku banganga , oko a mojɔ momina .
44026013	Ee kumu ombi , yana adaka mbi a njea a ehole emidi , nanɛ bohu bonɛnɛ boDiko bua bonɔ modika-busa na bolailai . Bongɛngɛ a mɔngɔ mambi masusu , na bato baya badalaka na mbi a njea .
44026014	Iso basusu bokwa a kpɔtɔ , na mbi naka monɔkɔ mokabale na mbi a LiEbele bo , Saula , Saula , onɔngejaka mbi mojɔ moye ? Okalakimea na mosongo ôbena .
44026015	Mbi nasɔmbeja bo , Kumu , wɛ nda ? Kumu abala bo , Mbi nadi Yesu , na wɛ onɔngejaka oko mbi .
44026016	Angɔ ko ; ima mema . Mbi nadoi ai wɛ , bo nahɔe wɛ mokɔmɛli na motati ongando jini wɛ na jîneja mbi wɛ ngɔngɔ .
44026017	Mbi nâheleja wɛ ai bato bawɛ na ai bapakano , na nalomaka wɛ oko ai ho
44026018	a bodipoa miso mabu , bo badonge a modidi , a bomana a bohu , bo bakine ngulu eSatana a bodoa ai Njambe , a bosɔ boyɛ bojibe jibu cina eejimeli ai mbi , na a bosɔ lisango a tei ebasɛnɔke .
44026019	Oko boa , kumu Agulipa , mbi nailona bosuma mojɔ moDiko monɛ mbi .
44026020	Natɔndɔ bato baDamaseke , na a Yelusalema , na a makota masusu maYuda , na natɔndɔ koko bapakano bo bajase dosa na bahekoe ai Njambe , na bo bangamejae bohekoa hobu oko na bikɔmɛli bipele .
44026021	BaYuda bapea mbi a tempelo , na bameka boweja mbi oko a mojɔ momina .
44026022	Njambe ko akɔmeja mbi masu masusu oko a busa bu ; na nami ya a botondɔ bato bakɛkɛ na bato banɛnɛnɛ ngando jibala Mose na batɔndɔi bo jidi bokwa ngɔngɔ , pɛpɛ mojɔ motongo ;
44026023	oko bo Masiya abwani bodingoa , bo angɔe boso a tei ebagwake , na bo atɔndɔe mwako mobohu ai bato basu na a makota matongo .
44026024	Abalaka yo boa bo asalongejae , Peseto abekoa bo , Paulo , odi na lilale ! Mijɔ minɛnɛ mikoa wɛ milabojaka wɛ oko bolaboja .
44026025	Paulo asɔmbeja bo , Peseto oekumu enɛnɛ ; mbi naditi nongo na lilale . Mijɔ mibalaka mbi midi soti mɛnɛ , te nongo ebalabala .
44026026	Kumu Agulipa ajebaka ngando jimina , na mbi nabalaka na nde a bohu . Ngando jimina jiikɔmɔ a libombi na mbi nalɛkɛ bo ajebaka jisusu .
44026027	Kumu Agulipa , ojimaka batɔndɔi ? Mbi najebaka bo ojimaka .
44026028	Agulipa abala na Paulo bo , Edikai mweka pɛ bo ohekojae mbi moto oMasiya !
44026029	Paulo asɔmbeja bo , Mbi nangaka Njambe bo , isa edɛye isa ngɔngɔ , bato basusu baya bakaka mbi busa bu badae o adi mbi , na wɛ mɛnɛ pongono , — te na minyɔlɔ mi ko !
44026030	Kumu Agulipa angɔ , na gouverneur na Bɛlɛnike pongono , na baya badaka na bu a esika emina , na bamana
44026031	Ibo babalana bo , Moto omina aikɔ nongo mojɔ mua mobwani na mokindo mobogwa isa na blɔkɔ .
44026032	Na Agulipa abala na Peseto bo , Eipeta da bo apalaka asambe na Kaisala , ka moto omina abwani bocingoama .
44027001	Yana ajima ’ bo bo botambe a masua a bokɛ a Italia , bakina Paulo na bato batongo bablɔkɔ a mɔmɔ maJulio , kapitɛni okompani eAuguseto .
44027002	Atamba so a masua maAdalamite , bokɛ oko na njingo ebosɛmɛ a ngando jia jidaka a dɔngɔ diAsia . Alisataluko , moto oTɛsalɔnike , ngando eMakedonia , apaka so .
44027003	Ahoa busa , bosɛmɛ a Sidonia . Julio akɔ Paulo monganji , na ajima bo boduboe ai bina’nde bo bamokɔmejae .
44027004	Angɔ so ena , bonɔ a dɔngɔ ditongo dimosanga kombe Kupulio , mojɔ bo pwea edongaka a dɔngɔ dikɛkɛ so .

44027006	Kapitɛni obasoda atana masua maAlesandalia a ngando emina maya makɛkɛ a Italia , na atambeja so a masua mamina .
44027007	Bodala bopɛtɛ-bopɛtɛ makina masu , na bomea a Kinido oko na kpɔkɔsɔ . Pwea esɔmbeja so oko bosɔmbeja a esika emina , na bonɔ sangɔngɔ jiKulete a dɔngɔ diSalamona .

44027009	Masɔ manɔ boa manɛnɛ . Ehole ebikia esia , na mɔngɔ momadiba-mamukwa modaka na njupi . A mojɔ momina , Paulo aleha bato bo ,
44027010	Ino bami , mbi nanɛkɛ bo mɔngɔ mu modi bodaloa . Iso bodi bopa njupi enɛnɛ , te nongo a mojɔ momasua na leka pɛ , oko a mojɔ mosu bɛnɛ koko .

44027012	Mbongu emina eidaka epele a boyeyoa ena a edidi epio . Oko boa bato banɛnɛ bajima bo bongɔe ena , na njingo ebomea a Poinike , ngando eKulete , a boyeyoa ena a edidi epio ; mojɔ bo mbongu emina eyɛyɛ nord-est na sud-est .
44027013	Ekina pwea eyɛmbu edonga a dɔngɔ disudo . Oko boa balɛ bo mɔngɔ mobu modi bobɔngɔ . Bangɔjɔ longo , na banɔ a dɔngɔ diKulete , hulelu mɛnɛ na mosanga .
44027014	Ngɔngɔ mweka ko , mopomba monɛnɛ modoa ; kombe emopomba momina Yulukulu .
44027015	Boihɔnɔ bonɔ a njea esu , mojɔ bo masna mabasoa na pwea oko bobasoa . A mojɔ momina , boihɔnɔ bokɔ eka , na bolindama boa .
44027016	Bonɔ a dɔngɔ dimokina mosanga mokɛkɛ , kombe Kauda . Bokɔ elomu epipo mɛnɛ a boheleja ebei emasua .
44027017	Boengɔjɔ na boekweja a tei emasua . Ngɔngɔ jimina , banɔjɔ singa cina emasua a bodinga masua . Badaka na bɔ bo basaka bakama a jɛlɔ jiSaluti . A mojɔ momina , basoloja bisenja bimasua , na bolindama oko bolindama .
44027018	Yana ahoa busa , bojengajengaka na mopomba , na babanga bodumba leka lotombaka masua a madiba .
44027019	Anɔ koko masu mabae , batomba leka lomasua na mɔmɔ mabu bɛnɛ , na balodumba a madiba .
44027020	Bodaka masu manɛnɛ , pɛ bonɛ nongo modika-busa isa njɔtɔ . Mopomba modaka mopipo mɛnɛ , na boidaka na njingo ebohela .
44027021	Badaka masu manɛnɛ pɛ boyaka eka . A mojɔ momina , Paulo angɔ a tei ebu , na abala na bu bo , lno bami ; akɔki no hokea mhi , na akɔki no yeyoa a Kulete , ka bopiti nongo njupi , na leka lonamiti boa .
44027022	Edɛye ko mbi nalehaka no ho otitejaeni milema minu , mojɔ bo ôhelani no basusu . Masua ko madi bogwa .
44027023	Mbi nadi moto oNjambe . Namokɔmɛkɛ , na obwɛnji onde amai hulelu na mbi na bulu bu .
44027024	Abali na mbi bo , Paulo , yɛ bobanga ! Wɛ odi bo’ma a boso boKaisala . Na hokea ; Njambe api wɛ bato basusu baya badi na wɛ a masua .
44027025	Ino bami , titejani milema minu , mojɔ bo mbi nadi na ejimeli ai Njambe bo mojɔ mobali yo na mbi modi boda oko boa .
44027026	Endele ko , bodi bobakama a mokina mosanga .
44027027	Iso bojengajengaka boa a madiba-mamukwa maAdalia . A busa bodomi-na-inɛi ko , oko na bulu tei , bato bamasua badaka na bolɛ bo bobatei na ekina esika .
44027028	Adumba bo pɔndɔ , banɛ bo madiba madaka na ndinda , mabɔkɔ domi-na-matano .
44027029	Badaka na bɔ isa bodi bobakama a matai . Oko boa badumba longo jinɛi a madiba a mbolo engɔngɔ , oko na posa bo busa bohoe .
44027030	Basali bamasua ko bameka bocia masua . Basoloja ebei a madiba na mokalo bo bapalaka batitejae longo a mbolo eboso .
44027031	Paulo ko abala na kapitɛni obasoda , na basoda pongono bo , Bato bamina bamiti da a masua , ino otahelani nongo .
44027032	Oko boa basoda balena mikpulu bo ebei ekwɛ nase .
44027033	Yana abenga busa bohoa , Paulo angɔɔnɔ bato basusu bo bayake dia . Abala bo , Ombakani edɛye na mokakwano masu domi-na-manɛi , pɛpɛ dia , pɛ boyaka nongo eka .
44027034	Mbi nangɔɔnɔkɔ no bo oyakeni dikina dia edɛye a bopa no ngulu ; mojɔ bo pɛpɛ nongo moswe momɔci momelo minu modi bogwa .
44027035	Ama yo bala boa , ami tomba oko molɛmbɛ , asakoa Njambe a boso bobu basusu , abuka molɛmbɛ na abanga boyaka .
44027036	Oko boa milema mibu basusu mitita , na bayaka koko dia .
44027037	Bodaka a masua bato mikama mibae na domi-sambo na bato basamano .
44027038	Yana aseja bo boyaka bopele , badumba ndongo a madiba-mamukwa a bohahaneja masua .
44027039	Yana ahoa husa haimbetea nongo ngondo . Banɛ ko likina libɔngu na eboma epele , na bajima bo bameke bosɛmeja masua a esika emina .
44027040	Bacingoa singa jilongo , na bajikina a madiba-mamukwa . Bakanda koko minyɔlɔ miyenda , bangɔjɔ esenja enɛnɛ emasua a mojɔ mopwea , na babenga mbongu .
44027041	Bamea ko a ekina esika yena eidaka na mbɛngɛ , na masua mabakama oko bobakama . Mbolo eboso ebakama , na mbolo engɔngɔ ebanga bobukea a mojɔ momula mopipo .
44027042	Basoda badaka na mokano bo bawoe bato bablɔkɔ , bo batasadumba a madiba a bocia .
44027043	Kapitɛni obasoda ko adaka na posa bo abanee Paulo bopele , na aijima mojɔ momina . Apa monɔkɔ bo baya bajebaka madiba basadumbe a madiba boso , bo babenge ngondo ,

44028001	Apa so njupi boa , boka bo mosanga momina modi na kombe Melita .
44028002	Bato bangando babonjea so na bopele mɛnɛ . Batokana mosa monɛnɛ , na basɔ so bopele , mojɔ bo mbua abanga bokwa , na pio edaka enɛnɛ .

44028006	Ibo ko bamonja , mojɔ bo badingaka bo mokuku monde modi boBaala , isa bo adi bokwa gbu , oko mogo . Ba’mba ekoka , na banɛ bo aditi nongo na epeko . A mojɔ momina balɛ mokina mojɔ motongo , na babala bo adi okina njambe .
44028007	Kumu omosanga , kombe ende Pubulio , asɔ so bopele , na akɔ so monganji masu masato . Gbie jinde jidaka hulelu na esika emina .

44028020	Oko boa napalaki bonɛnɛ na nu , bo nabale na nu mojɔ momina ; cina bo nadi a monyɔlɔ mu oko a mojɔ monjingo eYisalaele .

44028024	Bakina babu bajima mijɔ mibala yo ; batongo ko baijima .
44028025	Oko boa baidaka na molema momɔci , na bayana boa . Paulo ko abala na bu ekenge ye ; Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mobala na basangwa’su na soti na monɔkɔ momotɔndɔi Yisaya bo ,
44028026	Kɛ ai bata ba ; bala bo , Ô’kani na matoi soti , otacingeani ko ; Ônjani na miso soti , otanɛni ko .
44028027	Mojɔ bo milema mibato ba midi mipipo ; Matoi mabu madi na bohoka , Na hadipi miso mabu , Bo batanɛ na miso , na bata’ka na matoi , Bo batacingea a milema mibu , Basaka hekoa ai mbi bo nababelejae .

44028030	Paulo ahwɛ a ndako emina hianga bisusu bibae , na asɔkɔ bato basusu baya badoaka ai yo .
44028031	Atɔndɔkɔ mwako moBokumu boNjambe , akojaka ngando jiKumu Yesu Masiya na eci enɛnɛ , pɛpɛ nongo moto omosia .
45001001	Mbi Paulo nadi mobuli oYesu Masiya . Nabeama bo nadae obwɛnji ; nahɛngɛmɛ a mojɔ moMwako Mopele moNjambe

45001009	Mbi nakɔmɛkɛ Njambe na mwembo mombi a elomu eMwako Mopele moMwana’nde , na yo adi motati ombi bo nalangaka kombe jinu a ma’nga mambi bihole bisusu .
45001010	Nangɔɔnɔkɔ Njambe bo nabolojae njea ekina ehole epele a bodoa ai no , isa bolulea bonde bodi boa .
45001011	Mojɔ bo nadi na posa a bo’nɛnɛ na nu , bo napɛ no ekina epeeli emwembo a bombilimeja no .
45001012	Nakada a tei enu bodi bopingejana , mbi a mojɔ moejimeli enu , ino a mojɔ moejimeli embi .
45001013	Baninga , napalaka najebejae no bo nadaka na mokano mobodoa oho ai no bihole binɛnɛ , bo nadae na likina lituna a tei enu o adi mbi na lituna a makota matongo ; nanɛkini ko njea .
45001014	Nadi na nongo ai BaEla na ai bapakano pongono , ai bato babowɛi na ai bato balibumi pongono .
45001015	A mojɔ momina , nadi na posa bo natɔndɔe Mwako Mopele ai no pongono baya badi a Loma .
45001016	Mbi naditi nongo na sɔni a mojɔ moMwako Mopele , mojɔ bo modi ngulu eNjambe a boheleja moto na moto yona ojimaka , MoYuda boso , na MoEla pongono .
45001017	Bodongo boNjambe boboloi a tei eMwako Mopele , banga oko na ejimeli , suka oko na ejimeli , o adi mosɔnɔ bo , Moto obodongo ahela oko a mojɔ moejimeli .
45001018	Njambe aneja kɛlɛ ende , na edonga oho Diko a mojɔ mobosɛtɔ na bobe bobato , mojɔ bo bobe bobu bobindanejaka Soti .
45001019	Mojɔ bo ejebeli eNjambe edi bohu a miso mabu ; Njambe yo mɛnɛ abaneja .
45001020	Leka lokɔ yo oko a bobanga bongondo lobolojaka ai so mijɔ minde mibombamake , na ngulu ende yena etasia , na bonjambe bonde . Oko boa bapeliti nongo mokalo .
45001021	Ibo ko , yana ajeba bo Njambe , baimokumeja o Njambe , na baimosakoa . Bahekoa a ngando jingasangasa , na milema mibu miyebe mihinda oko bohinda .
45001022	Basakumeja na bowɛi bobu , na bakindoa oko bigegele .
45001023	Basɔmbɔtɔnɔ ekumu eNjambe yona oditi nongo na bogwa , na bilimo bimoto obogwa , na mbulu , na tito , na mboa babolanda .
45001024	A mojɔ momina , Njambe abakinea a bosɛtɔ bomilema mibu bɛnɛ , bo basambojae mikuku mibu a tei ebu bɛnɛ .
45001025	Mojɔ bo , balona Soti eNjambe a bojima mojɔ mobokosea ; basakoa na bakɔmɛ leka lokɔ Moyoeli , te nongo yo mɛnɛ , yona odi na bojongoa oko na bosusu . Amen .
45001026	A mojɔ momina Njambe abakinea a posa jibosambolu . Bali babu bakina elomu yena ebwana na mikuku mibu a mojɔ mongando jia jibɔngiti na mokuku .
45001027	Bami koko boa — bakina mojɔ momomi na mwali , na bangoa na posa oko ai bami ; na bakɔ mijɔ mibosambolu , bami na bami , na basɔ mokindo mua mobwana na bobe bobu a mikuku mibu bɛnɛ .
45001028	Balɛ bo babwani bosɛtoja Njambe ; oko boa Njambe abakina o babuli bamilema mibu mibokosea , bo badae na bikɔmɛli bia bibɔngiti .
45001029	Baluma na bobe tungu jisusu , na bosɛtɔ , na mbengea , na libwano ; likaka oko botɔ , na bowa , na miano , na epulu , na lisoki , na malɔngi .
45001030	Bato baminɔkɔ mibe , baloni baNjambe , bato babiloli , bato bajala na egbo ; balɛkɛ oko mijɔ mibe pɛ , na bapeliti lisuma ai baboti babu ,
45001031	pɛpɛ bocingea , pɛpɛ lisuma a mibeko , pɛ epaeli , pɛ nongo wa .
45001032	Bajebaka mobeko moNjambe bo baya badi na bikɔmɛli bimina babwani oko na bogwa ; endele ko , bakɔkɔ ngando jimina bo bɛnɛ , na basepanaka na bato baya badi na bikɔmɛli bimina .
45002001	Oko boa opeliti mokalo , wɛ moto yona osambejaka otongo . Mojɔ bo okasambeja moto otongo , osadumbaka wɛ mɛnɛ , cina bo , wɛ yona osambejaka okɔkɔ ngando jimina wɛ mɛnɛ .
45002002	Iso bojebaka bo bato bakakɔ ngando jimina , Njambe abasambejaka na soti mɛnɛ .
45002003	Wɛ moto yona osambejaka bato baya bakɔkɔ ngando jimina , na okɔkɔ boa wɛ mɛnɛ , odingaka bo odi bocia esambi eNjambe ?
45002004	Isa osɛtojaka monganji monde monɛnɛ , na lingbangba linde , na yongi ende ? Otajebaka bo monganji moNjambe mobeaka wɛ a bohekoja molema ?
45002005	Esambi eNjambe esoti êboloa a busa bokɛnjɔ , na wɛ ohɛjɛkɛ na ohɛngɛkɛ kɛnjɔ ai wɛ mɛnɛ a busa bomina , cina ebaso ewɛ , na molema mowɛ mua mopeliti nongo dosa .
45002006	Mojɔ bo yo adi bokaba ai moto na moto libondo lia libwani na bikɔmɛli binde ;
45002007	adi bopa bomɔ bua bodi na bosusu ai bato baya badi na lingbangba a bikɔmɛli bipele , baya badukaka ekumu , na lisuma , na bomɔ bua bodi na bosusu .
45002008	Bato ko baya badi na miano , baya balonaka Soti na basumaka oko bobe , badi bonɛ kɛnjɔ na likundu .
45002009	Moto na moto yona okɔkɔ bobɛ adi bonɛ jɔɔlɔ na molɔbɔ , MoYuda boso na MoEla pongono .
45002010	Ekumu ko , na sepi , na bowi jihɛngɛmɛ ai moto na moto yona okɔkɔ bopele , MoYuda boso na MoEla pongono .
45002011	Mojɔ bo bato basusu badi amɛci a boso boNjambe .
45002012	Bato basusu baya bapeliti Mibeko na bakɔkɔ bobe , bâgwa koko boa , pɛpɛ Mibeko . Bato ko baya badi na Mibeko , na bakɔkɔ bobe , bâsamba oko na Mibeko .
45002013	Mojɔ bo balongaka a miso maNjambe , te nongo baya bakaka Mibeko , oko baya basumaka Mibeko .
45002014	Bapakano bapeliti Mibeko ; endele ko bakɔkɔ ngando jibekeaka Mibeko na bolɛ bobu bɛnɛ ; oko boa , nongo adi bo pɛ Mibeko , badi na Mibeko a tei ebu .
45002015	Mojɔ momina monejaka so bo ngando jibekeaka Mibeko iisɔnɔmɔ a milema mibu . Bolɛ bobu bodi koko motati ; na malɛ mabu mabadumbaka isa mabalongejaka .
45002016	Mojɔ mu modabi bohu a busa bosambejabí Njambe mijɔ mibombamake mibato , oko na Masiya Yesu ; mwako mombi modi oko boa .
45002017	Wɛ yona obalaka bo odi MoYuda , ejimeli ewɛ edi oko a Mibeko , na osakumejaka a mojɔ moNjambe .
45002018	Ojebaka bolulea bonde , na obɔkɔ ngando jipele , mojɔ bo ohokea hokoja boMibeko .
45002019	Ojimaka na soti bo obwani boneja njea ai bato baya bagwa miso , na bo odi bohu ai baya badi a modidi ,
45002020	molehi ai balaboake , na mokoja obana , mojɔ bo obolojai mokuku moejebeli na Soti a tei eMibeko .
45002021	Oko boa , wɛ yona okojaka batongo , otasakoja wɛ mɛnɛ ? Okatɔndɔ mwako , olembaka bato bo bata’ba ; wɛ mɛnɛ ko oditi na liba ?
45002022	Wɛ yona olembaka bato bo bata’ngɛ bɔɔli , ongɛkɛ bɔɔli wɛ mɛnɛ ? Wɛ yona olonaka bilimo , opunjaka tempelo ?
45002023	Wɛ yona osakumejaka a mojɔ moMibeko , asopaka wɛ Mibeko , otasambojaka Njambe ?
45002024	Mojɔ bo mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Kombe eNjambe esamboi a tei ebapakano a mojɔ monu .
45002025	Isa osumaka Mibeko , bolena boganda bodi na cina soti . Isa ko osopaka Mibeko , bolena bowɛ boganda bodi oko ngasa mɛnɛ .
45002026	Oko boa isa Mwea asumaka bokoja boMibeko , yo atabwana na wɛ molenake , nongo adi yo oko Mwea ?
45002027	Oko boa baya bapeliti embete ebolena ganda a mikuku , na basumaka Mibeko , badi bodumba no baya badi na mokanda moMibeko , na bolena boganda , na basopaka Mibeko .
45002028	Odi MoYuda , te yona odi na embete eMoYuda a mokuku ; bolena boganda bosoti bocingiti na mokuku , na boditi mojɔ mosokolu .
45002029	Moto adi MoYuda , isa adi MoYuda a tei ; bolena boganda bosoti bodi mojɔ momolema na momwembo , te nongo momokuku ; bodi a mojɔ moesako eNjambe te a mojɔ momoto .
45003001	Oko boa MoYuda adi boso bobato batongo ? Bolena boganda bodi na cina ? Ee , bou mɛnɛ .
45003002	Mojɔ moboso modi oko mu ; Njambe abapa Misɔnɔ a mojɔ mobobanea .
45003003	Isa bakina babu baijima , sako eNjambe edi bokputoa a mojɔ mokitɛ ebu ?
45003004	Pɛpɛ nongo mweka ! Nongo adi bato basusu bakosei , Njambe atakputoja ebaeli ende ; mojɔ bo mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Bo olonge na bibaeli biwɛ , Na ogbokejae yana asambaka wɛ .
45003005	Bobe bosu bonejaka bodongo boNjambe a bohu . Oko boa , Njambe akakɛnjɔ na su , bodi bobala bo alongiti ? ( Nabalaka na monɔkɔ momoto . )
45003006	Pɛpɛ nongo mweka ! Ekada boa , Njambe adi bosambeja ngondo o bo ?
45003007	Na isa Soti eNjambe eboloaka a bohu a mojɔ mobokosea bombi , na ekumu ende ehɛkɛ boa , nadi bosamba o moto mobe mojɔ moye ?
45003008	Ekada boa , bobwaniti bokɔ bobe bo bopele boboloe ? Mojɔ bo bakina bato badɔkɔ so , na batɔndɔkɔ na bokosea bo so bobalaka boa . Bato bamina babwani bodumbama soti .
45003009	Oko boa nde ? Iso BaYuda bodi na Iikina lilonga ? Pɛpɛ nongo mweka ! Mojɔ bo bonejai boso bo bato basusu boya badi a libuli libobe , BaYuda na BaEla pongono .
45003010	Mosɔnɔmɔ koko bo , Moto obodongo aditi , pɛpɛ nongo omɔci .
45003011	Pɛpɛ nongo moto ocingeaka ; Pɛpɛ nongo moto odukaka Njambe .
45003012	Bato basusu bapengoi ; balaboi kanga basusu mɛnɛ na molema momɔci . Pɛpɛ nongo moto okɔkɔ bopele , pɛpɛ nongo omɔci .
45003013	Bikoolo bibu bidi oko esɛmɔ yena edi bwase ; Biemi bibu bidi oko na bokosea . Ngɛngɛ elibate edi cina jibiposo biminɔkɔ mibu .
45003014	Minɔkɔ mibu milutni na masingi na biloli .
45003015	Bapotaka mbango a bosopa makia .
45003016	Mɔlɛ mabu madi oko bowa na bobeja .
45003017	Batajebaka nongo njea ebowi .
45003018	Miso mabu matabangaka nongo Njambe .
45003019	Bojebaka bo bikenge bibalaka Mibeko bidi oko a mojɔ mobato baya badi cina jiMibeko . Oko boa pɛpɛ nongo monɔkɔ modi bosalongeja , na ngondo esusu edi bojima kpaci eNjambe a bosambeja .
45003020	Mojɔ bo pɛpɛ nongo moto odi bolonga a miso mande cina ebilomu biMibeko ; Mibeko mipaka oko ejebeli ebobe .
45003021	Edɛye ko bodongo boNjambe boboloi na njea etongo , te nongo na Mibeko . Endele ko , Mibeko na batɔndɔi badi batati babodongo boNjambe ,
45003022	oko bodongo boNjambe ai bato basusu baya baji-maka , na cina eejimeli ai Yesu Masiya . Bato basusu badi amɛci ,
45003023	mojɔ bo bato basusu mɛnɛ bakɔ bobe ; pɛpɛ nongo moto omɔci omea a mwɛngi moekumu eNjambe .
45003024	Balongaka ko na monganji moNjambe o epeeli , a mojɔ molisiko lia lidi a tei eYesu Masiya .
45003025	Njambe amoloma bo adae lisiko a mojɔ momakia mande , ai baya bajimaka . Oko boa Njambe aneja bodongo bonde , mojɔ bo akina jibe jia jikɔɔmɔ ehele , pɛ bosambeja .
45003026	Akɔ boa a boneja so a ehole ye , bo adi na bodongo yo mɛnɛ , na bo alongejaka moto yona odi na ejimeli ai Yesu .
45003027	Oko boa moto adi bosakumeja na ye ? Abwaniti bosakumeja ; mojɔ moye ? A mojɔ mobilomu ? Ngasa , oko a mojɔ moejimeli pɛ .
45003028	Mojɔ bo , iso bojebaka bo moto adi bolonga oko a mojɔ moejimeli , te nongo a mojɔ mobilomu biMibeko .
45003029	Njambe adi Njambe oBaYuda pɛ ? Aditi Njambe obapakano pongono ? Ee , adi Njambe obu pongono .
45003030	Njambe adi oko omɔci . Adi bolongeja babolena-ganda a mojɔ moejimeli ebu , na baya bapeliti embete ebolena-ganda a mojɔ moejimeli ebu .
45003031	Oko boa , bodi bodumba Mibeko a mojɔ moejimeli ? Pɛpɛ nongo mweka ; bopingejaka Mibeko oko bopingeja .
45004001	Oko boa bodi bobala bo , a mojɔ moAbalayama yona odi tata osu a njea emokuku ?
45004002	Isa Abalayama alonga a mojɔ mobilomu , abwana bosakumeja na mojɔ momina , te a boso boNjambe ko .
45004003	Misɔnɔ ibalaka bo ? Mibalaka bo Abalayama ajima Njambe , na ejimeli emina elangama ai yo o bodongo .
45004004	Moto akakɔ elomu , likonja lisɔkɔ yo liditi epeeli ; abwani bosɔ likonja limina .
45004005	Endele ko , moto akada na ejimeli ai Njambe yona longejaka bato babe , alongaka a mojɔ moejimeli ende , te a mojɔ moelomu ekɔkɔ yo .
45004006	Dawidi pongono ajongoaka moto olongejaka Njambe , te nongo cina ebilomu .
45004007	Abala bo , Bojongoa ai bato baya basɔ boyɛ bojibe jibu , na mabunga mabu makundama .
45004008	Bojongoa ai moto , — Kumu akada pɛ bolanga koko bobe bonde o nongo .
45004009	Bojongoa bomina ko bodi oko ai bato babolena ganda pɛ , isa ai bato bamwea pongono ? Mojɔ bo bobalaka bo ejimeli eAbalayama elangama ai yo o bodongo .
45004010	Edaka boa mojɔ moye ? Edaka boa yana adaka yo pɛ bopeta lenama ganda isa ngɔngɔ ? Te nongo ngɔngɔ , oko yana adaka yo pɛ bopeta lenama ganda .
45004011	Iyo asɔ mojɔ mobolena ganda o embete , a boneja bo amaka da na bodongo yana adaka yo pɛ bopeta lenama ganda . A mojɔ momina yo adi tata obato basusu baya bajimaka , na badi na bodongo a miso maNjambe a njea emina , nongo adi bo pɛ bolenama ganda .
45004012	Oko boa pongono , adi tata obato babolena ganda baya baditi na bolena boganda pɛ , mojɔ bo badalaka a njea eejimeli eAbalayama tata osu , yena esɔ yo yana adaka yo pɛ bopeta lenama ganda .
45004013	Abalayama aisɔ sako elisango lingondo ai yo mɛnɛ na bana bande a mojɔ moMibeko , oko a mojɔ mobodongo boejimeli .
45004014	Mojɔ bo isa basangoli badi oko baya bajimaka Mibeko , ejimeli edi eka engasa , na sako ebɔngiti .
45004015	Suka eMibeko edi kɛnjɔ ; endele ko , isa Mibeko miditi , bosopa boMibeko boditi .
45004016	Mojɔ mosusu mocingi oko na ejimeli pɛ . Oko boa koko , sako emina edi mojɔ momonganji moNjambe , na edi ai bana basusu baAbalayama — te nongo ai baya bajimaka Mibeko pɛ , oko ai baya badi na ejimeli eAbalayama ; mojɔ bo , yo adi tata osu basusu .
45004017	Mosɔnɔmɔ koko bo , Mbi nakɔi wɛ tata omakota manɛnɛ . Adi tata osu a miso maNjambe yona ojimea yo , oko Njambe yona opaka bomɔ ai bagwake , na abeaka leka lua loditi , bo lodae .
45004018	Abalayama , yana adaka yo pɛ njingo , ajima ko oko na njingo bo adi boda tata omakota manɛnɛ , o ama yo sɔ sako bo , Bana bawɛ badi boda boa .
45004019	Yana alɛ yo bo mokuku monde modi o mogo , ( mojɔ bo adaka na bianga mokama na dea ) na yana alɛ yo bo Sala adi motete , ejimeli ende eimbɛ nongo .
45004020	Aidaka nongo na mokakwano a mojɔ mosako eNjambe ; ejimeli ende emopa ngulu , na akumeja Njambe
45004021	mojɔ bo ajima na soti mɛnɛ bo Njambe adi bokɔ mojɔ mobala yo .
45004022	A mojɔ momina , ejimeli ende elangama ai yo o bodongo .
45004023	Bikenge bimina ko , — Elangama ai yo — biisɔnɔmɔ a mojɔ moAbalayama pɛ .
45004024	Bisɔnɔmɔ a mojɔ mosu pongono . Bodongo bolangama koko ai so baya bajimeaka yona ongɔjɔ Yesu Kumu osu a bogwa ,
45004025	oko Yesu yona ogwa a mojɔ mojibe jisu , na angɔ a bogwa a bolongeja so .
45005001	Oko boa , adi so na lilonga a mojɔ moejimeli , bodi na bowi a tei esu na Njambe , a mojɔ moKumu osu Yesu Masiya .
45005002	Iso bodi bambilimake a monganji mu moNjambe ; bonɛ njea ebokwea a monganji momina oko a mojɔ monde ; na bodi na sepi a mojɔ monjingo esu ebosɔ ekumu eNjambe .
45005003	Mojɔ motongo koko , bosepaka a tei eminɔngɔ misu . Bojebaka bo monɔngɔ mobotaka lingbangba ;
45005004	lingbangba libotaka ekɔmɛli esoti ; ekɔmɛli esoti ebotaka njingo .
45005005	Njingo etakputoa nongo , mojɔ bo ngɛnjɔ eNjambe esopei a tei emilema misu , oko na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mosɔ so .
45005006	Mojɔ bo , Masiya agwea baya baijeba Njambe a ehole yena ebwana , oko yana adaka so pɛpɛ ngulu .
45005007	Odi bogwea moto otongo nda , nongo akada moto obodongo ? Isa okina adi bojima bo agwɛ a mojɔ momoto mopele .
45005008	Njambe ko anejaka ngɛnjɔ ende ai so oko na mojɔ mu ; — Masiya agwea so yana adaka so oko bato babe .
45005009	Oko boa , bolongi edɛye a mojɔ momakia mande , na yo mɛnɛ adi boheleja so na soti a kɛlɛ eNjambe .
45005010	Isa bogwa boMwana ’ Njambe bodaka mokongo mobosiili bosu na Njambe , yana adaka so na Njambe soki ; esingaiti bomɔ bonde ! Adi so na bosiili bomina , bomɔ bonde bodi boheleja so .
45005011	Mojɔ motongo koko ; sepi esu edi oko ai Njambe , a mojɔ moKumu osu Yesu Masiya yona okwea bosiili a mojɔ mosu .
45005012	Oko boa , bobe bokwea a ngondo na moto omɔci , na bogwa bokwea a mojɔ mobobe . A mojɔ momina , bogwa bonangana ai bato basusu , mojɔ bo bato basusu bakɔ bobe .
45005013	Bobe bodaka a ngondo oko Mibeko mipetakini da . Isa Mibeko ko miditi , lindo jiditi koko .
45005014	Bogwa bodaka na kpaci a ngondo , donga oko a ehole eAdama oko a ehole eMose , kpaci ai bato baya baikɔ bobe o ama kɔ Adama , yona odaka elimo eyona odaka na sako ebodoa .
45005015	Bobe bodi tungu emɔci ; epeeli emonganji ko edi tungu etongo . Mojɔ bo , isa bato banɛnɛ bagwa cina ebobe bomoto omɔci , monganji moNjambe , na epeeli emonganji emoto omɔci , oko Yesu Masiya , ehɛ a mojɔ mobato banɛnɛ .
45005016	Epeeli emonganji edi tungu emɔci ; suka ebobe bomoto omɔci ko edi mojɔ motongo . Mojɔ bo bosambeja bobobe bomoto omɔci bosia na bodumba ; epeeli emonganji ko yena elongejaka so , edi a mojɔ mojibe jinɛnɛ .
45005017	Isa bogwa bosɔ bokumu ai moto omɔci a mojɔ mobobe bonde , baya basɔkɔ monganji moNjambe oko na bonɛtɔ , na epeeli ebodongo , badi bosɔ bokumu bobomɔ a mojɔ momoto omɔci koko , oko Yesu Masiya .
45005018	Oko boa koko , suka ebobe bomoto omɔci edaka bodumba a mojɔ mobato basusu , na suka eelomu emɔci ebodongo emoto omɔci edi lilonga na bomɔ a mojɔ mobato basusu .
45005019	Mojɔ bo isa bato banɛnɛ badi na lindo a mojɔ molipanga limoto omɔci , iboa koko bato banɛnɛ badi bolonga a mojɔ molisuma limoto omɔci .
45005020	Yana adoa Mibeko , lindo jihɛ oko bohɛ . Bohe bodaka bonɛnɛ soti ; monganji moNjambe ko monɔ .
45005021	A mojɔ momina , o adaka bobe na bokumu bobogwa , monganji moNjambe modi boda na bokumu bobomɔ oko na bosusu , a mojɔ moYesu Masiya Kumu osu .
45006001	Oko boa bodi bobala bo ? Bodi boyeyoa a bobe bo monganji moNjambe mohɛe ai so ?
45006002	Pɛpɛ nongo mweka . Iso bogwi a bobe ; oko boa bobwaniti boda koko a tei ebobe .
45006003	Otajebakani bo so basusu baya babatisama a tei eMasiya Yesu , bobatisama a tei ebogwa bonde .
45006004	Yana abatisama so , bopuseama na nde a tei ebogwa , bo bodae na ekɔmɛli ebomɔ boyene o angɔjɔmɔ Masiya a bogwa na ekumu eSango .
45006005	Mojɔ bo , isa bokatani na nde a tei ebogwa bonde , bodi bokatana koko na nde a njea ebongɔ bonde a bogwa .
45006006	Bojebaka bo moto osu moyou abakeama na nde a mole-mo-bokea , bo mokuku mobobe mogwɛ , na a bocingoa so a libuli libobe .
45006007	Mojɔ bo , isa moto agwi , bobe boditi koko na kpaci ai yo .
45006008	Na isa bogwi na Masiya , bojimaka bo bodi bohela na nde .
45006009	Mojɔ bo bojebaka bo , angɔ Masiya a bogwa , ataya gwa . Bogwa boditi koko na kpaci ai yo .
45006010	Iyo agwa , na bogwa bonde bodaka oko ehole emɔci pɛ a mojɔ mobobe . Edɛye ko , adi mɔ ; na bomɔ bonde bodi oko ai Njambe .
45006011	Oko boa , toma jimani bo ino odini bagwake a bobe , na bo odini na bomɔ boNjambe a tei eMasiya Yesu .
45006012	T’ojimeni oko bo bobe bodae na bokumu a mikuku minu mia midi bogwa . T’osumeni oko posa jimokuku .
45006013	T’opejaeni oko binama binu a bokɔ bobe . Odini bato baya badaka bagwake , na ohelani koko . Oko boa , sapejani ai Njambe ; hɛngɛni binama binu ai Njambe a bokɔ ngando jipele .
45006014	Bobe botada koko moswa’nu , mojɔ bo oditini cina ciMibeko ; odini oko cina emonganji moNjambe .
45006015	Oko boa , isa monganji moNjambe modi na kpaci ai so , na Mibeko pɛpɛ nongo kpaci , bobwani bokɔ bobe ? Pɛpɛ nongo mweka !
45006016	Okasumani moto , okasapejani ai moto , otajebakani bo odini babuli bamoswa omina ? Isa odini babuli babobe , suka edi oko bogwa ; isa odini babuli balisuma , suka edi oko bodongo .
45006017	Mbi nasakoaka Njambe mojɔ bo osumakani edɛye bokoja bosɔ no boso na milema minu boya , oko no baya badaka boso babuli babobe .
45006018	Asikoama no a bobe , odini edɛye babuli babodongo .
45006019	Mbi nabalaka na monɔkɔ momoto , mojɔ bo odini na bwɛmbu a munu . Toma pejani binama binu o babuli babodongo na bosɛnɔ , o apeja no boso binama binu bo bidae babuli babosɔtɔ na bobe bua bonɔi .
45006020	Yana adaka no babuli babobe , oidakani a libuli libodongo .
45006021	Edɛye ko , odini na sɔni a mojɔ mongando jimina . Ndese enu edaka bo ? Mojɔ bo suka engando jimina edi bogwa .
45006022	Edɛye ko osikoamini a bobe , na odini babuli baNjambe . Mbuma jibotaka no jidi oko bosɛnɔ , na suka emina edi oko bomɔ bua bodi na bosusu .
45006023	Mojɔ bo ndese ebobe edi bogwa . Epeeli ko epaka Njambe bopa edi bomɔ bua bodi na bosusu a tei eMasiya Yesu Kumu osu .
45007001	Baninga , otajebakani bo Mibeko midi na kpaci ai moto oko yana adi yo mɔ . ( Nabalaka na bato baya bajebaka Mibeko . )
45007002	Oko boa , mwali akalongana na momi , akatani na muma’nde a mojɔ moMibeko , oko a bogwa bomuma’nde . Muma’nde ko akagwa , mobeko mobolongana na muma’nde moditi koko na kpaci ai yo .
45007003	Mwali omina ko akakɛ ai momi otongo oko muma’nde mɛnɛ agwakini , adi mwali obɔɔli . Muma’nde ko akagwa , mobeko mobolongana bomina moditi koko na kpaci ai yo ; na akalongana na momi otongo aditi nongo moto obɔɔli .
45007004	Baninga , mojɔ monu modi koko boa ; Mibeko miditi na kpaci ai no , mojɔ bo ogwani na mokuku moMasiya , bo okataneni na okina otongo , oko na yona ongɔjɔmɔ a bogwa , bo so bobote mbuma a mojɔ moNjambe .
45007005	Adaka so cina jikpaci jimunu , Mibeko misisoja posa jisu jibe jia jidaka na ngulu a tei ebinama bisu ; na mbuma jibota so jidaka a mojɔ mobogwa .
45007006	Edɛye ko , Mibeko miditi koko na kpaci ai so ; bodaka a mbɔci jiMibeko , na bogwa bo bokɔe elomu esu na bomɔ boyene boMwembo , te a njea eMibeko miyou mimokanda .
45007007	Cina emina edi bo ? Mibeko midi mibe ? Pɛpɛ nongo mweka . Endele ko , mbi najeba bobe oko a mojɔ moMibeko . Eipeta da bo Mibeko mibala bo , T’odae oko na mbengea , ka naijeba nongo bo mbengea edi .
45007008	Oko boa bobe boboloja njea a mojɔ moMibeko , na bosisoja posa jisusu jibe a tei embi . Bobe oko ngasa , pɛpɛ Mibeko , bodi oko bogwake .
45007009	Yana adaka mbi , pɛpɛ nongo Mibeko , nadaka mɔ ; yana ko adoa Mibeko , bobe bosɔ ngulu , na mbi nagwa .
45007010	Mibeko mia midaka na sako ebomɔ miwa mbi oko bowa .
45007011	Mojɔ bo bobe boboloja njea a mojɔ moMibeko , bokosea mbi na mowa mbi oko na Mibeko .
45007012	Oko boa Mibeko midi misɛnɔke ; na eleho edi esɛnɔke na bojo na epele .
45007013	Mojɔ mua mopele modaka ai mbi oko bogwa ? Pɛpɛ nongo mweka . Bobe ko botomba mojɔ mopele a boweja mbi . Oko boa ekɔmɛli ebobe eboloa na soti , na bobe bogbasoa a mojɔ moMibeko .
45007014	Bojebaka bo Mibeko micingi na Mwembo ; mbi ko nadi moto omunu a mbɔci jibobe .
45007015	Te nacingeake ekɔmɛli embi mɛnɛ . Nakapala bokɔ mokina mojɔ , nitakɔkɔ mojɔ momina ; na nakalona mokina mojɔ , nakɔkɔ mojɔ momina .
45007016	Oko boa , nakalona mokina mojɔ , na nakakɔ mojɔ momina , najimaka bo Mobeko modi mopele .
45007017	A mojɔ momina , ekɔmɛli embi ecingiti na mbi mɛnɛ ; ecingi oko na bobe bua bodi a tei embi .
45007018	Mojɔ bo , najebaka bo pɛpɛ nongo mojɔ mopele modi a tei embi , oko a tei emunu mombi . Nadi na bolulea bo nakɔe bopele , pɛ ko bohɔnɔ bokɔ boa .
45007019	Te nakɔke bopele bopalaka mbi bokɔ , na nakɔkɔ bobe bolonaka mbi .
45007020	Nakakɔ mua molonaka mbi , editi mbi mɛnɛ yona okɔkɔ boa , oko bobe bua bodi a tei embi .
45007021	Oko boa , mojɔ monɛkɛ mbi moMobeko modi oko mu ; — nakapala bokɔ bopele , bobe bodi na mbi .
45007022	Mbi nasepaka na Mibeko miNjambe a tei emolema mombi ;
45007023	endele ko , nanɛkɛ bo mobeko motongo modi a tei ebinama bimbi , mua monaka na bolɛ bomolema mombi , na mopeaka mbi njango a libuli limobeko mobobe bua bodi a tei ebinama bimbi .
45007024	Mbi moto ojɔɔlɔ soti ! Odi boheleja mbi a mokuku mu mobogwa nda ?
45007025	Oko Njambe ; a mojɔ moYesu Masiya Kumu osu ; bosakoa ai yo ! Oko boa mbi mɛnɛ nasumaka Mibeko miNjambe na molema mombi ; nasumaka ko mobeko mobobe na munu mombi .
45008001	Bodumba boditi koko edɛye a mojɔ mobato baya badi a tei eMasiya Yesu .
45008002	Mojɔ bo mobeko moMwembo mosikoa mbi a mobeko mobobe na mobogwa .
45008003	Mojɔ bo Njambe aloma Mwana’nde mɛnɛ a mojɔ mobobe , o ekua emunu mobobe , a bodumba bobe a munu . Mibeko miibwana bokɔ boa a mojɔ moboyɛmbu bomunu .
45008004	Akɔ boa bo bocingoame a Mibeko , oko so baya badalaka a njea eMwembo , te nongo njea emunu .
45008005	Mojɔ bo baya badalaka a njea emunu balɛkɛ oko ngando jimunu ; ibo ko baya badalaka a njea eMwembo balɛkɛ oko ngando jiMwembo .
45008006	Molema momoto mokasusa njea emunu , suka edi oko bogwa ; molema ko mokasusa njea eMwembo , njea emina edi njea ebomɔ na bowi .
45008007	Mojɔ bo molema mua mosusaka njea emunu modi na Njambe soki ; motasumaka Mibeko miNjambe mojɔ bo moditi na ngulu a bokɔ boa .
45008008	Na baya basusaka njea emunu batahɔnɔkɔ bosepeja Njambe .
45008009	Ino ko oditini bato bamunu ; odini oko bato baMwembo , isa Mwembo moNjambe modi a tei enu soti . Moto amiti da na Mwembo moMasiya a tei ende , aditi moto onde .
45008010	Masiya ko akada a tei enu , miembo minu midi mɔ a mojɔ mobodongo , nongo adi mokuku eka ego a mojɔ mobobe .
45008011	Isa Mwembo monde yona ongɔjɔ Yesu a bogwa modi a tei enu , yona ongɔjɔ Masiya Yesu a bogwa adi bopa no bomɔ a mikuku minu mibogwa , oko na Mwembo monde mua modi a tei enu .
45008012	Oko boa baninga , boditi na nongo a munu bo bosuse njea emunu .
45008013	Mojɔ bo okasusani njea emunu odini bogwa . Okawejani ko bikɔmɛli bimokuku na ngulu eMwembo , ôdani na bomɔ .
45008014	Mojɔ bo bana baNjambe badi oko baya basusaka njea eMwembo moNjambe .
45008015	Ino ositini mwembo molibuli bo osumeni a mojɔ mobɔ ; osini oko mwembo molisango ; na bosembaka , Aba ! Sesa ! oko na mwembo momina .
45008016	Na Mwembo mɛnɛ motataka na miembo misu bo bodi bana baNjambe .
45008017	Isa bodi bana , bodi koko sangoli , sangoli jiNjambe , na bosangoanaka na Masiya . Bokadingoa na nde , bodi bokuma na nde pongono .
45008018	Mbi najimaka bo minɔngɔ miehole ye , na ekumu yena êboloa ai so ngɔngɔ , misangiti nongo mweka .
45008019	Mojɔ bo ngondo esusu embaka na tɛndɛ bo bana baNjambe baboloe .
45008020	Ngondo edaka a libuli lingando jingasangasa , te na bolulea bonde mɛnɛ , oko na bolulea bonde yona oekina boa ,
45008021	na njingo bo leka losusu lokɔ Njambe locingoame a libuli libopɔ , a bosangoa ekumu ebosɔmi bobana baNjambe .
45008022	Bojebaka bo ngondo esusu ebemaka na bipeko bilibota oko edɛye .
45008023	Te leka lokɔ Njambe pɛ , oko so bɛnɛ baya bajui mbuma jiboso jiMwembo , bobemaka a tei esu yana ambaka so lisiko limikuku misu , oko bosɔmi bosu .
45008024	Iso bobela oko na njingo emina . Bokada na njingo eeka , na bokanɛ eka etnina , njingo editi koko . Moto ambaka na njingo eka epeli yo ?
45008025	Bokada na njingo ko a mojɔ moeka edi so pɛ bonɛ , bombaka eka emina na lingbangba .
45008026	Oko boa pongono , Mwembo mokɔmejaka so yana adi so na bwɛmbu ; te bojebake bo’nga bua bobwani na su ; Mwembo ko mongɔɔnɔkɔ a mojɔ mosu na mibemo mia miditi a kɔpi emoto .
45008027	Iyona osisoaka milema mibato ajebaka mokano moMwembo , mojɔ bo Mwembo mongɔɔnɔkɔ a mojɔ mobasɛnɔke oko na bolulea boNjambe .
45008028	Bato bakapala Njambe , bakabeama na mokano monde , ngando jisusu jikɔkɔ yo jidi a mojɔ mobopele bobu .
45008029	Mojɔ bo ajeba bosoboso baya badi boda bato bande . Akolea eyou bo badae na elimo eMwana’nde , bo yo adae Mwana-sɔmi a tei ebananango banɛnɛ .
45008030	Abahɛngɛ oko a mojɔ momina , na ahabea . Ababea na abalongeja . Abalongeja na abakumeja .
45008031	Cina emina edi bo ? Edi oko bo , Isa Njambe adi na su , odi bolona so nda ?
45008032	Iyo aijuma Mwana’nde mɛnɛ ; amopa a mojɔ mosu basusu . Oko boa , atabakea a epeeli ende , epeeli eleka losusu ? Njambe akahɔ bato , odi bolanga bobe bobu nda ? Njambe alongejaka .
45008033	
45008034	Odi bodumba nda ? Oko Masiya yona ogwa , yona ongɔ a bogwa , na adi edɛye a ebɔ ebami eNjambe , na angɔɔnɔkɔ amojɔ mosu .
45008035	Odi bobɔteja so na ngɛnjɔ eMasiya nda ? Isa bodingoa , isa jɔɔlɔ , isa monɔngɔ , isa nja , isa mbundu , isa njupi , isa likɔngɔ ?
45008036	Mojɔ bo mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Bodi a bogwa busa bosusu a mojɔ mowɛ ; Banjaka so o bata baya bahɛngɛmɛ a bogwa .
45008037	Pɛpɛ . Iso bogbokejaka a tei engando ji jisusu na bopipo mɛnɛ , oko na yo yona opalaka so .
45008038	Mbi najebaka na soti bo pɛpɛ nongo eka emɔci ekɔ Njambe edi na ngulu a bobɔteja so na ngɛnjɔ eNjambe yena edi a tei eMasiya Yesu Kumu osu ,
45008039	isa bogwa , isa bomɔ , isa babwɛnji baDiko , isa makumu , isa ngando jia jidi edɛye , isa ngando jia jikɛkɛ adoe , isa ngulu oho Diko isa ya nase , isa ekina eka etongo .
45009001	Mbi nabalaka mojɔ mosoti a tei eMasiya . Nitakoseaka . Molema mombi mojimaka na mbi a tei eMwembo Mosɛnɔke
45009002	bo nadi na jɔɔlɔ enɛnɛ a molema mobi .
45009003	Mojɔ bo posa embi edi bo nalakejamembi mɛnɛ , na bo nabɔtɔne na Masiya , a mojɔ mobaninga bambi baya badi na mbi mbota emɔci .
45009004	Ibo badi BaYisalaele . Lisango libu lidi oko bosɔmi , na ekumu , na mikongo , na mibeko , na bosakoa , na sako .
45009005	Batata badi oko batata babu , na Masiya amana a mbota ebu . Bojongoa ai Njambe yona onɔi basusu , oko na bosusa . Amen .
45009006	Ebaeli eNjambe ko etakputoa . Mojɔ bo bato basusu baya babotama a Yisalaele baditi bana baYisalaele .
45009007	Na bato basusu baya badi bambota eAbalayama baditi bana bande . Mojɔ bo sako edi bo , Bana bawɛ bada bambota eIsaka .
45009008	Cina emina edi bo bana baNjambe baditi nongo baya babotama na bato ; badi bana bande na soti oko sangoli jindikeja .
45009009	Bikenge bisako bidi oko bi , Mbi nâhula a edidi ye , na Sala âbota mwana momi .
45009010	Te yo pɛ ; Lebeka alwa demi koko boa na tata osu Isaka .
45009011	Na yana adaka bana pɛ bopeta botama , yana adaka bo pɛ bopeta kɔ bopele isa bobe , yo asɔ sako bo , Mosuku âda mokɔmɛli ombakɛli onde ,
45009012	bo ekɔmɛli eNjambe ebohɔ bato edi boyeyoa , te a mojɔ mobilomu bibu , oko a mojɔ mobobea bonde .
45009013	Mosɔnɔmɔ boa pongono bo , Napalaki Yakobo ; nalonaki Esau .
45009014	Ekada boa , bodi bobala bo Njambe aditi bojo ? Pɛpɛ nongo mweka .
45009015	Mojɔ bo Njambe abala na Mose bo , Nakajima bo nakee bato wa , nadi boba’kea wa . Nakajima bo nadae na molema moyɛmbu ai bato , nadi boda na molema moyɛmbu ai bo .
45009016	Oko boa mojɔ mosusu mocingi na monganji moNjambe , te nongo na bolulea bomoto , isa na bingi emoto .
45009017	Ekenge yena ebalama na Palo esɔnɔmɔ bo , Mbi nangɔjɔi wɛ bo nanejae ndangasa embi oko na wɛ , bo gala ekombe embi etunde a ngondo esusu .
45009018	Oko boa Njambe akeaka moto wa oko akajima bo amokee wa , na akapala bopingeja molema momoto akɔkɔ boa .
45009019	A mojɔ momina , odi bobala na mbi bo , Isa modi boa , abakeaka lindo ai so mojɔ moye ? Odi bogbokeja bolulea bonde nda ?
45009020	Wɛ ko , wɛ moto , odi nda ? Wɛ obwani boboma kitɛ na Njambe ? Teni edi bobala na mobomi oteni bo , Okɔi mbi boa mojɔ moye ?
45009021	Mobomi aditi moswa ’ libali ? Akapala , adi botomba ekenge elibali bo abome na ekina teni a mojɔ moelomu eekumu , na teni etongo a mojɔ moelomu engasa .
45009022	Bodi bobala bo , isa Njambe , nongo apalaka yo boneja kɛlɛ ende na bojebeja so bo adi na ndangasa , adi oko na lingbangba lmɛnɛ ai baya bamokejaka kɛlɛ , baya babwani oko na likundu linde ?
45009023	Isa apalaka boneja ekumu ende yena enɔi , ai baya bamokejaka wa ? mojɔ bo abahɔ ehele a mojɔ moekumu , oko so ;
45009024	mojɔ bo abobei , te a tei eBaYuda pɛ , oko a tei ebapakano pongono .
45009025	Abala boa a mokanda moOsea bo , Baidaka bato bambi ; mbi ko nâbabea bato bambi . Nâda na epaeli ai yona osɔkini epaeli .
45009026	Na bâsɔ kombe ebana baNjambe obomɔ , oko a esika eka bo ekenge bo , Ino oditini bato bambi .
45009027	Yisaya pongono abala a mojɔ moYisalaele bo , Nongo etango ebana baYisalaele ekada o mbume jimadiba-mamukwa , Badi bohela oko eketa pɛ .
45009028	Mojɔ bo Kumu ângameja ebaeli ende a ngondo Oko na bopipo na pɛlɛpɛlɛ .
45009029	Na Yisaya abala koko bo , Eipeta da bo Kumu omandundu madiko akinea so bakina bana , Ka so na Sɔdɔmɔ bodi amɛci , Na bobwani oko na Gomola .
45009030	Cina emina edi bo ? Edi oko bo , bapakano baisusa njea ebodongo ; ba’si ko bodongo , oko bodongo bua bocingi na ejimeli .
45009031	BaYisalaele ko baya baduka bodongo a njea eMibeko mibodongo , bakputoi , pɛ bobwana na Mibeko mimina .
45009032	Mojɔ moye ? Mojɔ bo baduka bodongo a njea ebilomu bibu bɛnɛ , te nongo a njea eejimeli . Basaka libaku oko a litai lia lisakejaka bato .
45009033	Mojɔ momina mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Anjani ; mbi nasambeaka iitai a Siona a bosakeja bato , Litai linɛnɛnɛ a bobadumba . Endele ko , yona omojimeaka atasamboa nongo .
45010001	Baninga , posa emolema mombi , na bonga bombi ai Njambe bodi oko a mojɔ mobu , bo bahele .
45010002	Najimaka bo badi na bingi ai Njambe ; bingi emina ko editi na bocingea .
45010003	Baduka njea ebu bɛnɛ ebodongo , mojɔ bo baimbetea njea ebodongo boNjambe , na baijima bodongo bonde .
45010004	Mojɔ bo Masiya adi suka eMibeko , bo moto na moto yona ojimaka adae na bodongo .
45010005	Mose asɔnɔ bo moto yona okɔkɔ bilomu bibodongo bua bocingi na Mibeko , adi bohela a mojɔ momina .
45010006	Cina ebodongo bua bocingi na ejimeli edi bo , T’obale oko a molema mowɛ bo , Odi bowea oho Diko nda ? ( a botiteja Masiya nase ) ;
45010007	isa , Odi botita a ebubondo nda ? ( a bohuleja Masiya a bogwa ) .
45010008	Pɛpɛ ; bodongo boejimeli bobalaka bo , Ebaeli ebati na wɛ ; edi oko a monɔkɔ mowɛ , na a tei emolema mowɛ . Ebaeli emina edi oko mwako moejimeli motɔndɔkɔ so .
45010009	Okatata na monɔkɔ mowɛ bo Yesu adi Kumu , na okajima a molema mowɛ bo Njambe amongɔjɔ a bogwa , ôhela .
45010010	Mojɔ bo moto ajimaka na molema , na alongaka boa ; atataka na monɔkɔ na ahelaka boa .
45010011	Misɔnɔ mibalaka bo , Pɛpɛ nongo moto yona omojineaka odi bosamboa .
45010012	Mojɔ bo BaYuda na BaEla badi amɛci . Kumu omɔci adi Kumu obu basusu , na likabo linde iibwani na bato basusu baya bamongɔɔnɔkɔ .
45010013	Mojɔ bo moto na moto yona ongɔɔnɔkɔ a kombe eKumu âhela .
45010014	Isa bamojimeakini ko , badi bomongɔɔnɔ na ye ? Isa bakakini mwako monde , badi bomojimea na ye ? Isa motɔndɔi aditi , badi boka na ye ?
45010015	Na bato bamiti lomama , badi botɔndɔ mwako na ye ? Mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Baya batɔndɔkɔ Mwako Mopele — bibota bibu esɛngɔ !
45010016	Bato basusu ko baibokea Mwako Mopele . Mojɔ bo Yisaya abalaka bo , Kumu , ojimi mwako mosu nda ?
45010017	Oko boa bato bamiti ka , batada na ejimeli , na badi boka oko na Mwako Mopele moMasiya .
45010018	Mbi ko nahɔjɔkɔ bo , Baika ? Ee , baka soti . Ngondo esusu eka kɔpi ebu ; Mwako mobu momea oko a suka engondo .
45010019	Nahɔjɔkɔ koko bo , BaYisalaele baicingea ? Ehele mɛnɛ Mose abala bo , Mbi nadi bokeja no likaka a mojɔ molikota lia lidi ngasa ; Nadi bokeja no kɛlɛ a mojɔ molikota lia lipeliti bocingea .
45010020	Ngɔngɔ jinde , Yisaya abala na eci bo , Ibaya baiduka mbi babolojai mbi ; Nasabolojai ai baya baihɔjɔkɔ mbi .
45010021	A mojɔ moYisalaele ko , abala bo , Mbi naninojai mɔmɔ mambi busa bosusu Ai bato balipanga baya bapeliti lisuma .
45011001	A mojɔ momina , mbi nahɔjɔkɔ isa Njambe aloni bato bande ? Pɛpɛ nongo mweka ! Mbi nadi MoYisalaele mbi mɛnɛ ; nadi mwana oAbalayama , moto ohkota liBenyamina .
45011002	Njambe alomti nongo bato bande , mojɔ bo ajeba eyou bo badi bato bande . Otaje-bakani mojɔ moElia mua modi a Misɔnɔ ? Iyo anga Njambe a bodumba Yisalaele bo ,
45011003	Kumu , bawoi batɔndɔi bawɛ . Babuki matumbu mawɛ . Mbi nadikai oko mbi buki pɛ , na badukakani bo bawoe mbi .
45011004	Njambe ko amosɔmbeja bo ? Abala bo , Mbi nadikai na bato bami koto sambo baya baisumana nongo a boso boBaala .
45011005	Eketa edikai koko edɛye , bahɔmɔke bamonganji moNjambe .
45011006	Bohɔ bomina bodi a mojɔ momonganji moNjambe , te nongo a mojɔ mobilomu . Eipeta da boa , ka monganji moNjambe moditi monganji mosoti .
45011007	Cina emina edi bo ? Edi bo BaYisalaele baduka mokina mojɔ , pɛ ko bomoboloja . Bahɔmɔke ko bamoholoja , na milema mibu batongo mipinga oko bopinga .
45011008	Mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Njambe abapi mwembo mongbungbuma , Miso maya mapeliti njɛnɛ , Na matoi maya mapehti njoki , Oko a busa bu .
45011009	Dawidi pongono abala bo , Kina kola ebu edae likimba na elambo ai bo , Libaku a mojɔ mobosaka , bo basɛ ndese ebu .
45011010	Kina miso mabu mambimbine bo bata’nɛ , Na ngundubaneja mikɔngɔ mibu na bosusu .
45011011	Oko boa mbi nahɔjɔkɔ isa basaka libaku bo bakwɛ ? Pɛpɛ nongo mweka . Njea ebohela ko ehoa ai bapakano oko a mojɔ mobokwa bobu , a bokeja bo likaka .
45011012	Oko boa , isa ngondo ebɔngi a mojɔ mobokwa bobu , na isa bapakano basɔ lisango a mojɔ molibunga libu , esingaiti na bohula bobu !
45011013	Mbi yona odi obwɛnji ai bapakano , natɔndɔkɔ no bapakano bo nakumejaka elomu embi
45011014	oko na njingo bo nakejae bato bambi BaYuda likaka , a boheleja bakina babu .
45011015	Mojɔ bo , isa bosiili bongondo bocingi na bɔbɔtɔ bobu , bohula bobu bodi boda bomɔ a tei ebagwake .
45011016	Isa mbuma eboso edi esɛnɔke , mbuma jisusu jidi jisɛnɔke . Isa monjeli modi mosɛnɔke , bitape bimole bidi koko bisɛnɔke .
45011017	Bikina bitape ko bikatɛndɔmɔ , na wɛ olive oesika okakatana na mole a esika edaka bitape bimina , odi bokatana na cina emole , na odi bosɔ ngulu emole moolive .
45011018	Pɛ bosakumeja ko na bitape bimina . Okada na jala , pɛ bobosa bo wɛ otapeaka mole ; modi oko mole mua mopeaka wɛ .
45011019	Odi bosɔmbeja bo , Bitape bitongo bitɛndɔmɔ bo mbi nakatane na mole .
45011020	Soti ; bitape ko bitɛndɔmɔ cina epɛndɔ , na wɛ odi a esika ewɛ a mojɔ moejimeli . Pɛ boda na egbo a mojɔ momina ; da oko na bɔ .
45011021	Mojɔ bo , isa Njambe adaka na bopipo na bitape bimole mɛnɛ , âda koko na bopipo a mojɔ mowɛ .
45011022	Toma lɛ bo Njambe adi na monganji , na adi na bopipo pongono . Bopipo bonde bodi ai bakwake ; monganji monde ko modi ai wɛ , okayeyoa a monganji monde . Omiti kɔ boa , wɛ ôtɛndɔmɔ pongono .
45011023	Ibo pongono bakakina pɛndɔ ebu , bâkatana koko ; mojɔ bo Njambe adi na ngulu bo abakatanejae koko .
45011024	Isa wɛ otɛndɔmɔ a mole moolive moesika , na okatana na mole moolive mogbie , esingaiti bitape bimole na soti ! Bidi bokatana koko na mole mobitape bimina .
45011025	Baninga , mbi napalaka bo ocingeeni mojɔ mu mobombamake , osaka dani na egbo . Modi oko bo likma libondo liYisalaele lidi na miso mago , na bâda boa oko a ehole êbwana etango ebapakano .
45011026	Oko boa BaYisalaele basusu bâhela . Mosɔnɔmɔ koko boa bo , Moheleja âhula Siona A boheleja Yakobo a bobe bonde .
45011027	Imu modi mokongo môbakea mbi na bu Yana âdongeja mbi jibe jibu .
45011028	Badi na Njambe soki a njea eMwako Mopele , na mojɔ momina mobɔngejai no . A njea ebohɔ boNjambe ko , yo abapalaka a mojɔ mobatata babu .
45011029	Mojɔ bo Njambe akapa bipeeli , isa akabea bato , aditina dosa a mojɔ momina .
45011030	Bosoboso ino odakani na lipanga ai Njambe ; edɛye ko osɔkɔni monganji moNjambe mojɔ bo ’ bo badi na lipanga .
45011031	Ibo koko boa ; badi na lipanga edɛye , bo basɛ monganji ngɔngɔ o asɔkɔ no monganji .
45011032	Mojɔ bo Njambe akinea bato basusu a lipanga libu , bo anejae basusu monganji monde .
45011033	Ee soti ! Ndinda ebowɛi boNjambe enɔi mwɛngi momoto , na ejebeli ende pongono . Moto atahɔnɔ bokokeleja bisambi binde , na bocingea njea jinde .
45011034	Mojɔ bo , Ocingeaka mokano moNjambe nda ? Molehi onde nda ?
45011035	Omopa ekina epeeli nda , Bo Njambe adae na nongo ai yo ?
45011036	Leka kanga losusu mɛnɛ lodi ai yo , lohelaka a mojɔ monde na losukeaka oko na nde . Ekumu ai yo na bosusu . Amen .
45012001	Baninga , mbi nangɔɔnɔkɔ no oko na monganji moNjambe bo opejaeni mikuku minu ai Njambe , epeeli yena edi mɔ na esɛnɔke a bosepeja Njambe . Bosakoa bua bobwani na nu oko bu .
45012002	T’odaeni oko na ekɔmɛli ebato bangondo ye . Toma dani na milema miyene bo okindoeni elimo etongo ; oko boa odini bojeba bolulea boNjambe na soti , bolulea bonde bopele , bobɔngɔke na bobwanake .
45012003	Mbi nalehaka no basusu na monganji mosɔ mbi , bo moto atasakumeja yo mɛnɛ . Adi bosa’ngɛ na bolɛ , na mwɛngi moejimeli mokabaka Njambe ai moto na moto .
45012004	Mokuku momoto modi na binama binɛnɛ . Ibi bisusu ko bidi na bilomu tongotongo .
45012005	Iso bodi koko boa . Nongo adi so banɛnɛ , bodi mokuku momɔci a tei eMasiya , na bokatani so basusu , moto na moto .
45012006	Bipeeli bisu biditi amɛci ; bicingi oko na monganji moNjambe ai moto na moto . Yona odi na epeeli ebotɔndɔ mwako , abwani botɔndɔ mwako na mwɛngi monde moejimeli .
45012007	Isa edi epeeli ebokɔmeja , moto adi bokɔmeja ; na mokoja adi bokɔ elomu ebokoja .
45012008	Molehi adi na elomu eboleha . Yona opaka bipeeli adi bopa na likabo limonganji . Yona odi na elomu a boso bobato , adi boda na bingi ; na yona okɔmejaka bato na wa adi boda na sepi .
45012009	Yɛ epaeli enu edae epaeli esoti . Dani na maneene a mojɔ mobobe ; dani ko na posa engando jipele .
45012010	Toma palanani na epaeli emoto ai mwangwa’nde ; moto adi boduka ekumu emoto otongo , te ekumu ende mɛnɛ .
45012011	T’okineni oko bo bingi enu embɛ ; kɔmɛni Kumu na peye eMwembo .
45012012	Kinani njingo enu esepejae no . Dani na lingbangba a tei emonɔngɔ . T’ongwaeni oko bo’nga .
45012013	Dani na likabo ai bato baDenga baya badi na taka ; asɔni bakɛndɛli bopele .
45012014	Jongoani bato baya badingojaka no ; bajongoani , pɛ bobasingani .
45012015	Sepani na bato baya badi na sepi ; yeani na bato baya bayeaka .
45012016	Dani na molema momɔci . T’odaeni oko na jala a milema minu ; katanani na bato baya badi na milema mititake . Pɛ bosakumejani na bowɛi bonu .
45012017	Moto akakɔ no bobe , t’osɔmbejaeni oko bobe ai yo . Lɛni oko mijɔ mipele pɛ a boso bobato basusu .
45012018	Isa njea edi , kɔni na milema minu misusu bo otadani na mijɔ na bato batongo .
45012019	Baninga , T’okundeni oko likundu . Kinani mijɔ misusu a kɛnjɔ eNjambe ; mojɔ bo , mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Njamhe abala bo , Likundu lidi oko ai mbi . Mbi nadi bosea ndese .
