45012020	Soki ewɛ akada na nja , mopa dia . Akada na ekangola , monusa madiba . Okakɔ boa , odi bomokeja sɔni enɛnɛ mɛnɛ .
45012021	T’ogbokeni oko na bobe ; Gbokejani bobe ko na bopele .
45013001	Moto na moto abwani bosuma bakumu bakpaci , mojɔ bo edi Njambe yona opaka kpaci esusu . Makumu maya madi , masɔ kpaci ai yo .
45013002	Oko boa , moto akakotoa kpaci emina , adi soki emokano moNjambe , na soki jimina jisamboa .
45013003	Moto akakɔ bopele , atabanga nongo bajuji ; moto ko akakɔ bohe , adi bohanga bajuji . Oko boa isa opalaka boda pɛ nongo bɔ a mojɔ mokumu , toma da na ekɔmɛli epele , na yo adi bosepa na wɛ .
45013004	Mojɔ bo yo adi mokɔmɛli oNjambe a bokɔmeja wɛ . Okakɔ bobe ko , obwani bobanga , mojɔ bo juji aditi na kpaci ebowa boangasa ; adi mokɔmɛli oNjambe , a bodumba moto yona okɔkɔ bobe .
45013005	Oko boa , moto abwani boda na lisuma , te cina ebɔ bomokindo , oko a mojɔ momojimo momolema monde .
45013006	Oputakani koko tako a mojɔ momina . Bakumu badi bakɔmɛli baNjambe , na ehole ehu esusu edi oko a elomu ebu .
45013007	A mojɔ momina , kabani ai bato basusu leka lua lobwani na bu ; tako ai yona osɔkɔ tako , nongo ai yona osɔkɔ nongo ; lisuma ai yona obwani bosɔ lisuma , na ekumu ai yona obwani bosɔ ekumu .
45013008	Pɛ bodani na nongo ai moto , oko nongo eepaeli pɛ , bo opalaneni , moto na mina’nde moto . Mojɔ bo yona opalaka moto otongo asumaka Mibeko .
45013009	T’ongɛ oko bɔɔli . T’owoe oko . T’obe oko . T’omboe oko . Mibeko mk na mibeko mitongo isa midi , midi a tei eekenge ye , Toma pala motuteano mowɛ o asapalaka wɛ mɛnɛ .
45013010	Epaeli t’ekɔke bobe ai motuteano . Oko boa epaeli ebɔngejaka Mibeko .
45013011	Mojɔ motongo ; ojebakani bo ehole emei , ehole ebosisoa ta hiɔ . Mojɔ bo , bokangɛ ehole ebanga so bojima na ehole ye , bohela bosu bobatami edɛye .
45013012	Bulu bobengi bosia , na busa bobengi bohoa . Yɛni so bobulɛe ngando jimodidi bo bolwae molilo mobohu .
45013013	Yɛni bodae na ekɔmɛli epele ebato baya badalaka a bohu , te na ebueli na bolangoa , isa na ndukeli na lisɔngi , isa na miano na likaka .
45013014	Lwani oko Yesu Masiya o elwaeli enu ; t’okineni oko pokiso a mojɔ momunu , a bogoleja posa jimunu .
45014001	Isa moto aditi mombilimake a ejimeli ende , mosɔni bopele ; pɛ bomodumbani a mojɔ mongando jijimaka yo .
45014002	Okina moto ajimaka bo abwani boyaka leka losusu ; moto ko yona odi na bwɛmbu ayakaka oko njua pɛ .
45014003	Moto yona oyakaka eka , abwaniti bosɛtoja moto yona odi na bikia . Na yona odi na bikia abwaniti bodumba moto yona oyakaka , mojɔ bo Njambe amojimaka .
45014004	Wɛ nda ? Wɛ obwani bosambeja mokɔmɛli omoto otongo ? Moswa’nde mɛnɛ ajebaka isa amai mema isa akwi . Adi bo’ma mema ko , mojɔ bo Kumu adi na ngulu bo amombilimejae .
45014005	Moto omɔci alɛkɛ bo busa bomɔci na busa botongo masangiti ; moto otongo ko alɛkɛ bo masu masusumadi amɛci . Moto na moto abwani bojima na sotia molema monde .
45014006	Moto yona olɛkɛ bo bokina busa bodi bonɛnɛ , akɔkɔ boa na lisuma ai Kumu ; yona opeliti bikia , ayakaka koko na lisuma ai Kumu , na asakoaka Njambe ; yona odi na bikia , akiaka koko na lisuma ai Kumu , na asakoaka Njambe pongono .
45014007	Mojɔ bo moto t’ahelake a mojɔ monde mɛnɛ pɛ , na moto t’agwake a mojɔ monde mɛnɛ pɛ .
45014008	Adi so mɔ , hodi oko ai Kumu ; na bokagwa , bodi oko ai Kumu . Oko boa , isa bodi mɔ , isa bokagwa , bodi oko ai Kumu .
45014009	Yesu agwa na ahela koko oko a mojɔ momina , bo adae Kumu obagwake , na Kumu obato baya badi mɔ .
45014010	Wɛ ko , osambejaka mwangwao mojɔ moye ? Osɛtojaka mwangwao mojɔ moye ? Iso basusu bodi bo’ma a boso bomongbɛlɛngɔ moesambi eNjambe .
45014011	Mojɔ bo mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Kumu abalaka bo , Mbi nadi mɔ ; Bato kanga basusu mɛnɛ badi botita na magbunda a boso bombi . Bato kanga basusu mɛnɛ badi bosakoa Njambe na minɔkɔ mibu .
45014012	Oko boa so basusu bodi bosɔmbeja Njambe , moto na moto a mojɔ monde mɛnɛ .
45014013	Oko boa bobwaniti bosambejana koko ; jimani oko bo obwanitini hokɔ mokina mojɔ mua mobwani boda libaku isa elambo anjea emwangwao .
45014014	Mbi najebaka ; najebaka na soti , oko na Kumu Yesu , bo ekia eeka ecingiti na eka mɛnɛ , oko na moto yona okiaka eka emina . Akajima bo eka emina edi na ekia , edi boa oko ai yo .
45014015	Wɛ ko okayaka ekina eka , na mwangwao akada na wa a mojɔ momina , otasusaka koko njea eepaeli . Yesu agwea moto omina , na wɛ obwaniti bomobeja a mojɔ moeyakeli ewɛ .
45014016	Isa mokina mojɔ mua modi mopele a miso mawɛ , modi mobe a miso mabato batongo , pɛ bokɔ mojɔ momina .
45014017	Mojɔ bo , Bokumu BoNjambe bocingiti na boyaka na bomwaka ; bodi mojɔ mobodongo , na bowi , na sepi , a tei eMwembo Mosɛnɔke .
45014018	Moto yona okɔmɛkɛ Masiya a njea jimina , adi na esako epele a tei ebato , na Njambe amojimaka pongono .
45014019	Oko boa , kinani milema misu midae oko na posa a ngando jibowi , ho bokɔmejane moto na moto .
45014020	T’obejae oko elomu eNjambe a mojɔ moeka eboyaka . Leka losusu lobwani na boyaka soti ; endele ko , moto akasakeja bato batongo na leka loyakaka yo , akɔkɔ bobe .
45014021	Okakia tito , isa okalona bomwaka vino , isa okalona mokina mojɔ motongo mua mobwani bosakeja mwangwao , okɔkɔ bopele .
45014022	Odi na ejimeli ; banea ejimeli emina a tei enu na Njambe . Isa moto aditi na mokakwano a mojɔ mongando jijimaka yo , moto omina adi na sepi .
45014023	Isa moto ko adi na mokakwano a mojɔ moekina eka , na akayaka eka emina , asadumbaka yo mɛnɛ ; mojɔ bo atajimaka na soti mua mokɔkɔ yo . Mojɔ bo , isa mokina mojɔ mocingiti na ejimeli , modi oko mobe .
45015001	Iso baya badi na ngulu bobwani bolwa mina mibato bayɛmbu . Bobwaniti bokɔ oko ngando jipalaka so bɛnɛ pɛ .
45015002	Moto na moto adi bokɔ mua mosepejaka motuteano monde , isa modi mopele , bo amombilimejae a ejimeli ende .
45015003	Mojɔ bo Masiya aipala bo mijɔ midae o apalaka yo mɛnɛ ; mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Biloli bibu baya balolea wɛ bihekoi ai mhi .
45015004	Bikenge bi bisusu bisɔnɔmɔ eyou a bokoja so , bo bodae na njingo , mojɔ bo Misɔnɔ mipaka so lingbangba na eci .
45015005	Yɛ Njambe yona opaka lingbangba na eci , akɔe bo odaeni na molema momɔci , o apalaka Masiya Yesu ,
45015006	bo okataneni na molema momɔci , na monɔkɔ momɔci , a bokumeja Njambe Sange ’ Kumu osu Yesu Masiya .
45015007	Asɔnɔni bopele a bokumeja Njambe , mojɔ bo Yesu Masiya asɔ no bopele .
45015008	Mbi natɔndɔkɔ no bo Masiya adaka mokɔmɛli oBaYisalaele bo angamejae sako jikinea Njambe batata bo jidi soti ,
45015009	na bo bapakano bakumejae Njambe a mojɔ momonganji monde . Mosɔnɔmɔ boa bo , A mojɔ momina , mbi nâsakoa wɛ a tei emakota ; Nâkumeja kombe ewɛ na njembo .
45015010	Abala koko bo , Ino makota , sepani na bato bande .
45015011	Na koko bo , Sakoani Kumu , mo bamakota masusu ; Yɛ makota masusu mamosakoe .
45015012	Yisaya abala koko bo , Monjeli moYisai motɔbi ; Iyo adi bongɔ bo adae kumu omakota ; Njingo emakota edabí oko ai yo .
45015013	Yɛ Njambe onjingo alumejae no na sepi na bowi a ejimeli enu , bo njingo enu enɛnge a mojɔ mongulu eMwembo Mosɛnɔke .
45015014	Baninga , mbi najimaka na soti bo olumini na ngando jipele ; odini na ejebeli engando jisusu , na obwanini bopana bilebo .
45015015	Endele ko , mbi nasɔnei no mikina mijɔ na ebaeli epipo a bolɛjɛ no , mojɔ bo Njambe akɔni monganji
45015016	bo nadae mokɔmɛli oMasiya Yesu a tei ebapakano , a elomu eMwako Mopele moNjambe . Oko boa bapakano bâda epeeli ebwanake , epeeli esɛnɔke , a mojɔ moMwembo Mosɛnɔke .
45015017	A mojɔ momina , nabwani bosepa a tei eMasiya Yesu , a mojɔ moelomu embi ai Njambe .
45015018	Ebɔngiti bo nabale a mojɔ mongando jitongo , oko ngando jikɔ Njambe na mbi a bogbokeja bapakano na ebaeli , na elomu ,
45015019	na ngulu ebimbete na mindumba , na ngulu eMwembo Mosɛnɔke . Oko boa , abanga mbi a Yelusalema , nananganejai Mwako Mopele a makota matongo , suka oko Ililiko .
45015020	Mojɔ bo posa embi edaka bo natɔndɔe Mwako Mopele a makota maya maipaka ka kombe eMasiya , bo nasaka yoa a diko dieyoeli-ecina emoto otongo .
45015021	Mosɔnɔmɔ koko boa ; Ibaya basɔkini mwako monde badi bonɛ ; Ibaya bakakmi mojɔ monde badi bocingea .
45015022	Cina edaka mbi pɛ bonɛ njea a bokɛ oho ai no oko yena .
45015023	Edɛ-ye ko napeliti koko pokiso a makota mamina a mojɔ moelomu . Na adi mbi na posa bianga bi binɛnɛ ebomea oho ai no ,
45015024	nadi na njingo bo nanɛnɛe na nu a njea , yana akɛkɛ mbi mɔngɔ oho Sepania . Nâda na sepi eboyeyoa na nu mweka , na nadi na njingo bo osukejaeni mbi a njea ngɔngɔ .
45015025	Edɛye ko , nakɛkɛ oho Yelusalema na bipeeli ai bato baDenga .
45015026	Mojɔ bo bato baMakedonia na baAkaya bajimi bo balɔkɔe likonja a mojɔ mobato babokwali baDenga diYelusalema .
45015027	Bakɔi mojɔ momina na sepi , mojɔ bo badi oko na nongo ai bo ; isa bapakano basangoi iikabo libipeeli biMwembo a mojɔ mobu , babwani bobakɔmeja na bipeeli bileka .
45015028	Oko boa , namaka sieja mojɔ momina , na namaka bapeja bipeeli bi , nasa ko nakɛe mɔngɔ a Sepania , na nânɔ njea enu .
45015029	Najebaka bo nakadoa ai no , nadi bodoa na bojongoa boMasiya bua bonɔi .
45015030	Baninga , mbi nangɔɔnɔkɔ no a kombe eKumu osu Yesu Masiya , na epaeli eMwembo , bo okataneni na mbi a bokɔmeja mbi na ma’nga manu ai Njambe ,
45015031	bo nahele a mɔmɔ mabato oho Yuda baya bapeliti nongo ejimeli , na bo bato baDenga basepe na bipeeli bitombaka mbi oho Yelusalema .
45015032	Na Njambe akajima nadi bodoa oho ai no na sepi , na nâhema mweka a tei enu .
45015033	Yɛ Njambe obowi adae na nu basusu . Amen .
45016001	Napalaka bo osɛni ngɛnɛ esu Poibe bopele . Iyo adi mokɔmɛli oDenga diKɛnkɛlɛ .
45016002	Mo’sɔni yo a kombe eKumu osu , o akɔkɔ bato baDenga . Akapala bo omokɔmejaeni na ngando jinde , mokɔmejani ; mojɔ bo yo mɛnɛ adi mokɔmeja obato banɛnɛ , na mbi mɛnɛ pongono .
45016003	Abɛjɛni Pilisila na Akwila , bma’mbi a elomu eMasiya Yesu .
45016004	Ibo bapa njupi a boheleja mbi . Mbi nasepaka na bu , na te mbi pɛ , oko Menga masusu mamakota matongo .
45016005	Abɛjɛni Denga dia didi a ndako ebu . Abɛjɛni Epainɛtɔ , mina’mbi oepaeli . Iyo adi tɔmi eMasiya oho Asia .
45016006	Abɛjɛni Malia ; yo akɔi elomu enɛnɛ a tei enu .
45016007	Abɛjɛni Anduloniko na Yunia , baninga bambi baya badi a njango o adi mbi mɛnɛ . Badi na gala epele a tei ebabwɛnji , na bajima Masiya oko mbi napetakini jima .
45016008	Abɛjɛni Ampuliato , mina’mbi oepaeli a tei eKumu .
45016009	Abɛjɛni Ulubano yona okɔmejaka so a elomu eMasiya , na Setakusa mina’mbi oepaeli .
45016010	Abɛjɛni Apele yona olonga a elomu eMasiya . Abɛjɛni bato baKumu baya badi a ndako eAlisitɔbulo .
45016011	Abɛjɛni Elodiona , moto ombi mɛnɛ . Abɛjɛni bato baKumu baya badi a denga diNalukiso .
45016012	Abɛjɛni Tulupaina na Tuluposa ; badi bakɔmɛli baKumu . Abɛjɛni Pelesida , mwali oepaeli yona okɔkɔ elomu enɛnɛ a mojɔ moKumu .
45016013	Abɛjɛni Lupu , mokɔmɛli obonɔ oKumu ; abɛjɛni koko ngwa’nde yona odaka o ngwa’mbi mɛnɛ .
45016014	Abɛjɛni Asunkulito , na Pɛlɛgɔnta , na Elume , na Patuloba , na Eluma , na baninga baya badi na bu .
45016015	Abɛjɛni Pilologa na Yulia , na Nele na ngɛnɛ ende , na Olumpa , na bato basusu baDenga baya badi na bu .
45016016	Abɛjɛnɛni njɛbɛ na bohia bosɛnɔke . Menga masusu maMasiya malomaka no njɛbɛ .
45016017	Baninga , mbi nangɔɔnɔkɔ no bo onganjameni a mojɔ mobato baya bapangoaka na basakejaka bato libaku , baya balonaka bokoja bosɔ no ; pɛ bopanganani na bu .
45016018	Bato bamina batakɔmɛkɛ Masiya Kumu osu ; badi oko babuli basɔpɔ jibu bɛnɛ ; bakoseaka milema mibato bayɛmbu na bibaeli bibu bipele , na poloso ebu .
45016019	Bato basusu bajebaka mojɔ molisuma linu , na mbi nasepaka a mojɔ monu . Endele ko , napalaka bo ejebeli enu edae oko a ngando jipele ; a mojɔ mobobe , dani o bana .
45016020	Njambe obowi atayeyoa a bodɛhɛ Satana na bibota binu . Yɛ monganji moKumu osu Yesu Masiya modae na nu .
45016021	Timoteo , yona ocingi na mbi a elomu , abɛjɛkɛ no njɛbɛ . Lukio na Yasona na Sosipatalo yona odi bwela bombi , babɛjɛkɛ no .
45016022	Mbi Tɛlɛti , yona osɔnɔkɔ mokanda mu , nabɛjɛkɛ no na njɛbɛ eKumu .
45016023	Gayo yona osɔ mbi a ndako ende , na asɔ koko Denga disusu a ndako ende , yo abɛjɛkɛ no . Elasuto , mobanei olikonja lingando abɛjɛkɛ no , na Kwaluto mwangwa’su pongono .
45016024	Yɛ monganji moKumu osu Yesu Masiya modae na nu basusu . Amen .
45016025	Okina adi yona obwani bombilimeja no a Mwako Mopele moMasiya motɔndɔkɔ mbi . Mwako momina mobolojaka mojɔ mua modaka mobombamake a bobanga mɛnɛ .
45016026	Moboloi ko edɛye a mojɔ momikanda misɔnɔ batɔndɔi , cina emobeko moNjambe yona odi na bosusu . Na moboloi ai bato bamakota masusu bo badae na lisuma na ejimeli .
45016027	Ekumu ai Njambe — odi na bowɛi oko yo pɛ — na bosusu , a mojɔ moYesu Masiya . Amen .
46001001	Njɛbɛ esu Paulo yona obeama na bolulea boNjambe bo adae obwɛnji oYesu Masiya , na mwangwa’su Sosotene ,
46001002	a Denga diNjambe dia didi oho Kolinto , oko bahɛngɛmɛkɛ baMasiya Yesu , baya babeama bo badae basɛnɔke , na bato basusu baya bangaka a kombe eKumu Yesu Masiya a bisika na bisika . Adi Kumu obu na Kumu osu pongono .
46001003	Yɛ monganji na bowi boNjambe Sangwa ’ su na Kumu Yesu Masiya bodae na nu .
46001004	Mbi nasepaka na Njambe bihole bisusu a mojɔ momonganji mosɔ no a tei eMasiya Yesu .
46001005	Osɔni bojongoa bonɛnɛ mɛnɛ a tei ende , na bɛtɛ ebotɔndɔ , na ejebeli esusu pongono ;
46001006	mojɔ bo Mwako moMasiya modaka mopipo a tei enu .
46001007	A mojɔ momina , pɛpɛ nongo ekina epeeli eMwembo ebwani botaka na nu . Ombakani oko bodoa boKumu osu Yesu Masiya .
46001008	Iyo adi bombihmeja no oko a suka mɛnɛ , bo otadani na mojɔ nongo momɔci , a busa boKumu osu Yesu Masiya .
46001009	Njambe atakputoja nongo sako ende . Edi oko yo , yona obea no a bokatana na Mwana’nde Yesu Masiya Kumu osu .
46001010	Baninga , mbi nangɔɔnɔkɔ no basusu a kombe eKumu osu Yesu Masiya bo odaeni na monɔkɔ momɔci . T’odaeni oko na miano a tei enu . Katanani ko na molema momɔci na mokano momɔci .
46001011	Baninga , bato baKuloe bajebejai mbi bo odini na miano .
46001012	Cina emina edi bo , ebaeli emoto na moto a tei enu edi bo , Mbi moto oPaulo , isa , Mbi moto oApolo , isa , Mbi moto oPɛtɛlo , isa , Mbi moto oMasiya .
46001013	Masiya adi na bobɔtɔ ? Paulo agwea no a mole-mobokea ? Obati-samani a kombe ePaulo ?
46001014	Mbi nadi na sepi mojɔ bo nabatisa oko Kulusipo na Gayo pɛ , te nongo bato batongo a tei enu .
46001015	Oko boa moto abwaniti bobala bo abatisama a kombe embi
46001016	Nabatisa bato bandako eSɛtɛpana pongono ; nitajeba isa nabatisa okina otongo .
46001017	Mojɔ bo Masiya ailoma mbi a bobatisa ; aloma mbi a botɔndɔ Mwako Mopele , te na bɛtɛ ebobala , bo mole-mobokea moMasiya mosaka da eka engasa , pɛpɛ ngulu .
46001018	Mojɔ bo mwako momole-mobokea modi oko ebalabala ai bato baya badi a njea ebogwa ; modi ngulu eNjambe ko ai so baya bahelaka .
46001019	Mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Mbi nâgegeaneja bowɛi bobato babowɛi ; Nâgbogboaneja gatea ebato bagatea .
46001020	Moto obowɛi adi jɔ ? Mosɔni omikanda adi jɔ ? Moto okitɛ ongondo ye adi jɔ ? Njambe aigegeaneja bowɛi bongondo ?
46001021	Mojɔ bo Njambe akolea na bowɛi bonde , bo ngondo etamojeba na bowɛi bongondo ; na ajima bo ahelejae bato baya bajimaka , a mojɔ moyebe eetɔndɔli eMwako Mopele .
46001022	BaYuda bapalaka bo banɛe bimbete , na BaEla badukaka bowɛi .
46001023	Iso ko botɔndɔkɔ Mwako moMasiya yona ogwa a mole-mobokea . Mojɔ momina modi oko libaku ai BaYuda , na yebe ai BaEla .
46001024	Endele ko , Masiya adi ngulu eNjambe , na bowɛi boNjambe , ai bato baya babeama , isa BaYuda isa BaEla .
46001025	Mojɔ bo , na bogegele boNjambe na bowɛi bobato , bogegele boNjambe bonɔi na bowɛi ; na boyɛmbu boNjambe , na ngulu ebato , boyɛmbu boNjambe bonɔi na ngulu .
46001026	Baninga , lɛni mbea enu bɛnɛ ; bato babowɛi bongondo ye baditi banɛnɛ a tei enu , isa bato bakpaci , isa bakumu .
46001027	Njambe ahɔkɔ bato bayebe bangondo , a bosamboja bato babowɛi . Njambe ahɔkɔ bato bayɛmbu bangondo , a bosamboja bato bapipo .
46001028	Njambe ahɔkɔ bato bangasangasa baya bapeliti nongo ekumu a miso mabato , ee oko bato bangasa mɛnɛ , a bodumba ngando jia jidi edɛye .
46001029	Oko boa , pɛpɛ nongo moto obwani bosakumeja a boso boNjambe .
46001030	Bomɔ bonu a tei eMasiya Yesu bohulaka oko ai yo . Njambe akɔ bo Masiya Yesu adae bowɛi , na bodongo , na bosɛnɔ , na lisiko , a mojɔ mosu .
46001031	Mosɔnɔmɔ boa bo , Moto yona osakumejaka , yɛ asakumejae oko a mojɔ moKumu .
46002001	Baninga , yana akɛ mbi ai no a botɔndɔ Mwako Mopele moNjambe , naikɛ nongo na bɛtɛ ekɔpi , isa na bowɛi .
46002002	Mbi najima na molema mombi mosusu bo mtajeba mokina mojɔ motongo a tei enu , oko Yesu Masiya pɛ yona ogwa a mole-mobokea .
46002003	Adaka mbi na nu , nadaka na bwɛmbu , na bɔ , na mongongoma .
46002004	Mwako mombi na etɔndɛli embi , biidaka na bikenge bibowɛi ; bidaka oko na bimbete na ngulu eNjambe ,
46002005	bo ejimeli enu etada a bowɛi bobwato , oko a ngulu eNjambe .
46002006	Iso botɔndɔkɔ ngando jibowɛi oko ai bato bapingamake . Bowɛi bomina ko boditi bowɛi bongondo ye , isa bowɛi bobakumu bangondo ye , baya badi bodimoa .
46002007	Botɔndɔkɔ oko bowɛi boNjambe bobo-mbamake , bowɛi bosɛlingoa yo a mojɔ moekumu esu oko a bobanga mɛnɛ .
46002008	Bakumu bangondo ye batacingeaka bowɛi bomina . Akɔkɔ bo cingea , ka baiwa Kumu oEkumu a mole-mobokea .
46002009	Mojɔ bo mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Miso mainɛ , matoi maika , Na molema momoto moipaka lɛ Ngando jisɛlingoa Njambe a mojɔ mobato baya bamopalaka .
46002010	Njambe ko ajibolojai ai so oko na Mwembo . Mojɔ bo Mwembo modukaka ngando jisusu , ee ngando jiNjambe jindinda pongono .
46002011	Ocigeaka bilɛli bimoto nda ? te mwembo momoto mua modi a tei ende ? Oko boa koko , pɛpɛ nongo moto ocingeaka bilɛli biNjambe ; Mwembo moNjambe pɛ mobicingeaka .
46002012	Iso bositi mwembo mongondo ye . Bosi oko Mwembo moNjambe , bo bocingee bipeeli bipa Njambe so na monganji monde .
46002013	Iso botɔndɔkɔ ngando ji , oko na bibaeli bikojaka Mwembo so , te nongo na bibaeli bibowɛi bobato . Bokojaka ngando jiMwembo oko na kɔpi eMwembo .
46002014	Moto ko , o abotama yo , t’asɔke ngando jiMwembo moNjambe ; jidi oko yebe pɛ a miso mande . Abwaniti bojicingea , mojɔ bo adi bojicingea oko na Mwembo .
46002015	Moto oMwembo ko akokelejaka ngando jisusu ; pɛpɛ nongo moto ko odi bomokokeleja yo .
46002016	Ojebaka bolɛ boKumu nda bo amokojae ? Iso ko bodi na bolɛ boMasiya .
46003001	Baninga , yana atɔndɔ mbi mwako , naihɔnɔ bobala na nu o bato baMwembo . Mojɔ bo odakani bato bamunu ; oipaka botamani a tei eMasiya .
46003002	Mbi nanungeja no mabɛi pɛ . Naibɔkɔ no na dia mɛnɛ , mojɔ bo oibwanani boyaka dia , na obwanakinini nongo edɛye , mojɔ bo odini oko bato bamunu .
46003003	Odini na likaka na misoo a tei enu ; oko boa oditini bato bamunu ? ekɔmɛli enu , te ekɔmɛli ebato bangondo ?
46003004	Okina onu abalaka bo , Mbi moto oPaulo ; na otongo abalaka bo , Mbi moto oApolo ; oko boa oditini bato bangondo ?
46003005	Apolo adi nda ? Paulo adi nda ? Badi oko bakɔmɛli baNjambe a bojimeja no , mojɔ bo Kumu apaka moto na moto elomu ende .
46003006	Mbi na’na ngua ; Apolo amɛsɛ madiba ; edi Njambe ko yona otɔjɔ ngua .
46003007	Oko boa , yona onaka ngua na yona omɛsɛkɛ madiba , badi oko ngasa mɛnɛ ; yona otɔjɔkɔ ngua — oko Njambe pɛ .
46003008	Yona onaka ngua na yona omɛsɛkɛ madiba badi amɛci ; na moto na moto adi bosɔ ndese yena ebwani na elomu ende .
46003009	Iso bodi bakɔmɛli baNjambe , na bokɔkɔ elomu na nde . Ino odini gbie eNjambe ; odini eyoeli endako eNjambe .
46003010	Njambe akɔni monganji bo nadae moyoeli obowɛi . Natanda matai macina , na moto otongo ayoaka diko . Moto na moto yona oyoaka abwani bonganjama na eyoeli ende .
46003011	Eyoeli-ecina edi oko Yesu Masiya ; pɛpɛ nongo moto odi boyoa eyoeli-ecina etongo .
46003012	Moto akayoa a diko dieyoeli emina na likonja , isa wɔlɔ , isa palata , isa na matai mayumu , isa na mele , isa na njienjie , isa na sobe , elomu emoto na moto edi boboloa a bohu ,
46003013	mojɔ bo Busa bomina bobo-lojabí elomu emina a bohu . Eboloabí oko na mosa . Mosa momina modi bomeka elomu emoto na moto .
46003014	Moto akayoa diko dieyoeli ecina , na elomu ende ekayeyoa , moto omina adi bosɔ ndese .
46003015	Elomu emoto ko eka’ngoa , yo adi bodika ngasa ; endele ko , yo mɛnɛ adi bohela , o moto yona ohelaka a mosa .
46003016	Ino otajebakani bo odini tempelo eNjambe , na bo Mwembo moNjambe modi a tei enu ?
46003017	Moto akabeja tempelo eNjambe , Njambe adi bomobeja yo pongono . Mojɔ bo tempelo eNjambe edi esɛnɔke , na mo odini tempelo emina .
46003018	Moto abwaniti bosakosea . Okina onu akalɛ bo adi na bowɛi bongondo ye , yɛ apete da oko egegele , bo adae moto obowɛi soti .
46003019	Mojɔ bo bowɛi bongondo ye bodi oko yebe a miso maNjambe . Mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Iyo ataejaka bato babowɛi a poloso ebu bɛnɛ .
46003020	Na mosɔnɔmɔ koko bo . Kumu ajebaka bo bilɛli bibato babowɛi bidi oko bilɛli bingasa .
46003021	A mojɔ momina , moto abwaniti bosakumeja na bato ; mojɔ bo ngando jisusu jidi ai no ,
46003022	isa Paulo , isa Apolo , isa Kepa , isa ngondo , isa bomɔ , isa bogwa , isa ehole ye , isa ehole yena ekɛkɛ adoe ; jisusu jidi oko ai no ;
46003023	na ’ no bɛnɛ odini ai Masiya , na Masiya ai Njambe .
46004001	Iso bodi oko bakɔmɛli baMasiya , na babanei bangando jibo-mbamake jiNjambe ; na moto akalɛ so , abwani bolɛ so oko boa .
46004002	Mojɔ moboso mua mobwani na babanei , modi oko bo badae bato basoti mɛnɛ .
46004003	Mbi nakasamba na nu , isa na esambi ebato , pɛ mojɔ ; na nitasambejaka mijɔ mimbi mɛnɛ .
46004004	Nongo nakalɛ bo naditi na mojɔ , nitalonga a mojɔ momina , cina bo Kumu yo mɛnɛ asambejaka mbi .
46004005	Oko boa , pɛ bosambejani oko ehole ebwanakini . Kumu akadoa , yo adi bomeja ngando jibombamake jimodidi a bohu , na adi boboloja ndungu jimilema mibato . A ehole emina , moto na moto adi bosɔ ndese ende ai Njambe .
46004006	Baninga , mbi nabali na nu ngando jimina o mondɛ , a mojɔ mosu na Apolo , bo okoeni na ekoaneli esu , na bo odaeni na lisuma a Misɔnɔ . Obwanitini bokumeja okina osu na bolona yona otongo .
46004007	Wɛ mɛnɛ oditi na bato batongo amɛci ? Opeli ekina eka yena edi wɛ pɛ bosɔ ? Oko boa , isa oesɔ oko bosɔ , osakumejaka mojɔ moye o moto yona oisɔ epeeli emina ?
46004008	Ino ko ogolini . Okonjini makonja . Okweini a bokumu bonu no bɛnɛ , te nongo na sn . Posa embi edi oko bo odaeni bakumu soti , bo so bokumee na nu .
46004009	Mbi nalɛkɛ bo Njambe adejai so babwɛnji ngɔngɔ jibato basusu , o bato baya bahɛngɛmɛ a bogwa ; mojɔ bo bodi o makou pɛ a mojɔ mongondo , na babwɛnji badiko , na bato pongono .
46004010	Iso bodi oko bigegele a mojɔ moMasiya . Ino ko odini na bowɛi a tei eMasiya ! Iso bodi bayɛmbu ; mo ko odini bapipo ! Ino odini na ekumu ; iso ko bosamboi .
46004011	Iso bogwaka nja , na bodi na ekangola oko edɛye . Bodi mbundu , bodingoaka , bodi oko bakɛndɛli pɛ , pɛpɛ ngando .
46004012	Bokɔkɔ elomu epipo na mɔmɔ masu bɛnɛ . Bato bakasinga so , iso bobajongoaka . Bakadingoja so , bodi oko bogo . Bakatangola so , iso bodi oko na ebaeli eepaeli .
46004013	Bodi oko bɔnɔ engondo ; bodi edɛye oko leka lobodumba pɛ .
46004014	Nasɔneaka no ngando jiji , te a bokeja no sɔni , oko a boleha no o bana bambi baepaeli .
46004015	Nongo okadani na bakoja koto domi a tei eMasiya , sangwa’nu adi oko omɔci pɛ . Mojɔ bo mbi nabota no na Mwako Mopele a tei eMasiya .
46004016	Oko boa nangɔɔnɔkɔ no bo okoaneni na mbi .
46004017	A mojɔ momina , nalomei no Timoteo , mwana ’ mbi oepaeli na lisuma a tei eKumu . Iyo adi bolɛjɛ no ekɔmɛli embi a tei eMasiya , yena ekojaka mbi a Menga masusu a bisika bisusu .
46004018	Bakina banu ko basakumejaka ; balɛkɛ bo nitadoa ai no .
46004019	Kumu ko akajima , nitayeyoa a bodoa ai no ; nasa ko najebe isa bato bamina baegbo badi na ngulu , isa badi oko na bibaeli pɛ .
46004020	Mojɔ bo Bokumu boNjambe bodi mojɔ mongulu , te bibaeli .
46004021	Opalakani bo ? Opalakani bo nadoe ai no na pimbo , isa na epaeli , na molema moyɛmbu ?
46005001	Bato babalaka bo bɔɔli bodi a tei enu . Nongo bapakano bataje-baka bɔɔli bomina , bo moto adae na mwali osangwa’nde .
46005002	Ino odini na egbo , na obwanini boyea bio a mojɔ momina . Enɔi na bopele bo odongejaeni ai no moto yona okɔkɔ mojɔ momina .
46005003	Mokuku mombi moditi oho adi no ; mwembo mombi ko modi na nu . Na mbi , o moto yona odi a tei enu , nasambejai moto yona okɔ mojɔ momina , a kombe eKumu Yesu .
46005004	Okaboleani likita , mwembo mombi modi boda na nu , na ngulu eKumu osu Yesu ,
46005005	hɛngɛni moto omina ai Satana a mojɔ mohogwa bomunu , bo mwembo monde mohele a Busa boKumu .
46005006	Ino obwanitini bosakumeja . Otajebakani bo eketa ekɛkɛ elipetu edi bohekoja mitɛkɛ misusu oko lipetu ?
46005007	Dumbani lipetu liyou , bo odaeni molɛmbɛ moyene , pɛpɛ nongo lipetu a tei enu . Mojɔ bo , Mwana-Bata osu oKola-eBonɔ agwa , oko Masiya yo mɛnɛ .
46005008	A mojɔ momina , kinani so boyake Kola na molɛmbɛ mua mopeliti lipetu , molɛmbɛ mobosɛnɔ na mosoti , te nongo na lipetu liyou , lipetu lilisoki na libobe .
46005009	Nasɔnea no a mokanda mombi bo otapanganani na bato balisɔngi .
46005010	Cina emina editi bo obambaeni bato balisɔngi bangondo ye , na bato bambengea , na bato baliba , na bato babole . Ekada boa , ka odini bodonga a ngondo oko bodonga .
46005011	Mbi nasɔnea no bo otapanganani na moto oDenga yona odi na lisɔngi , isa mbengea , isa moto obole , isa moto oebaeli ebe , isa moto obolangoa , isa mobi . Obwanitini boyaka dia na moto yona odi na bikɔmɛli bimina .
46005012	A mojɔ mobato batongo baya badi sokolu , moditi mojɔ mombi a bosambeja bato bamina . Endele ko , obwanini bosambeja baya badi a tei eDenga .
46005013	Njambe asambejaka baya badi a sokolu . Dongejani moto mobe yona odi a tei enu .
46006001	Okina onu akada na mwangwa ’ nde mojɔ , abwani boleneja mojɔ oko na bato baDenga , te nongo na bapakano .
46006002	Otajebakani bo bato baDenga badi bosambeja ngondo ? Oko boa , isa ngondo edi bosamba na nu , ino obwanitini bolena mijɔ mikɛkɛlɛkɛ ?
46006003	Otaje-bakani bo so bodi bosambeja babwɛnji-baDiko ? esingaiti mijɔ mingondo ye !
46006004	Oko boa , isa odini na mijɔ mimina , omisambejakani na bato baya badi ngasa mɛnɛ a miso maDenga mojɔ moye ?
46006005	Mbi nabalaka boa a bokeja no sɔni . Moto omɔci obowɛi ataboloa a tei enu yona obwani bolena mijɔ mibato baDenga ?
46006006	Moto na moto ko akɛkɛ na mwangwa’nde a esambi , ee , esambi ebato baya badi pɛ bojima Njambe .
46006007	Moto akakɛ a esambi na mwangwa ’ nde , mojɔ momina modi mobe . Enɔi na bopele bo moto adingoe , na bo abungejae likonja linde .
46006008	Ino bɛnɛ ko okɔkɔni bobe , na okoseakani baninga banu bɛnɛ .
46006009	Otajebakani bo bato babe batasangoa Bokumu boNjambe ? T’opanganeni ; bato balisɔngi bato babole , bato babɔɔli , bimwalimwali , bibamibami ,
46006010	babi , bato bambengea , bato babolangoa , babosambolu , na mibɛngɔ , batasangoa nongo Bokumu boNjambe .
46006011	Bakina banu badaka boa ; osɛnoani ko , ohɛngɛmɛni ai Njambe , na odini na lilonga , a kombe eKumu Yesu Masiya na a Mwembo moNjambe osu .
46006012	Mbi nabwani bokɔ ngando jisusu . Ngando jisusu ko jibɔngiti na mbi . Nabwani bokɔ ngando jisusu ; endele ko , nitajimaka bo nagboke na ekina ngando .
46006013	Dia didi a mojɔ mosɔpɔ , na sɔpɔ edi a mojɔ modia . Njambe ko adi bosieja sɔpɔ na dia pongono . Mokuku moditi a mojɔ molisɔngi . Modi oko a mojɔ moKumu , na Kumu adi Kumu omokuku .
46006014	Njambe angɔjɔ Kumu a bogwa , na adi bongɔjɔ so pongono na ngulu ende .
46006015	Otajebakani bo mikuku minu midi binama biMasiya ? Natombe binama biMasiya bo nabicingee na mwali obɔɔli ? Pɛpɛ nongo mweka !
46006016	Otajebakani bo yona okatani na mwali obɔɔli adi na nde mokuku momɔci ? Mojɔ bo , mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Ibo babae bâda munu momɔci .
46006017	Moto ko akakatana na Kumu , ibo babae badi mwembo momɔci .
46006018	Toma gbeseani bɔɔli . Bobe botongo bokɔkɔ moto bocingiti na mokuku ; moto ko yona ongɛkɛ bɔɔli akɔkɔ bobe a mokuku monde mɛnɛ .
46006019	Otajebakani bo mikuku minu midi tempelo eMwembo Mosɛnɔke ; mojɔ bo Mwembo Mosɛnɔke modi a tei enu ? Omosɔni ai Njambe .
46006020	Oditni baswa banu bɛnɛ , mojɔ bo osikoamani na bobuno bonɛnɛ . A mojɔ momina , toma bakeani Njambe kumu omikuku minu .
46007001	A mojɔ mongando jisɔnea no mbi — bopele bo moto atabɛnjɛe nongo mwali .
46007002	Endele ko , momi abwani boda na mwali onde mɛnɛ , na mwali abwani boda na muma’nde mɛnɛ , a bogbesea bɔɔli .
46007003	Momi abwani bobakea mwali onde mɛnɛ bokonde , na mwali abwani bokɔ boa na muma’nde .
46007004	Mojɔ bo , mwali aditi moswa omokuku monde mɛnɛ ; muma’nde adi moswa omokuku momwali . Muma’nde koko boa ; aditi moswa omokuku monde mɛnɛ ; moswa omokuku monde , oko mwali onde .
46007005	Momi abwaniti bobulɛ mwali onde , na mwali abwaniti bobulɛ muma’nde . Okakɔni boa bo osahɛngɛeni a mojɔ moho’nga ekina ehole , kɔni oko na mojimo mobasusu babae . Mojɔ momina mokasia ko , siejani ekia emina , bo Satana asaka meka no , na otahɔnɔkɔni bogbokeja posa jinu .
46007006	Mojɔ mobali mbi modi oko eleho , te mobeko .
46007007	Posa embi edi bo bato basusu badae o adi mbi mɛnɛ . Moto na moto ko asɔkɔ libondo linde ai Njambe ; okina ekɔmɛli emɔci , otongo ekɔmɛli etongo .
46007008	Eleho embi ai bandengi , na ai bali babogwa , edi bo bayeyoe o adi mbi mɛnɛ .
46007009	Bamiti hɔnɔ bosabekea ko , babwani bolongana . Na bolongana , na posa a tei enu o mosa , enɔi na bopele oko bolo ngana .
46007010	A mojɔ mobato baya balongani , mobeko modumbaka mbi moditi mombi mɛnɛ , modi oko mobeko moKumu ; modi bo mwali atadonga ai muma’nde .
46007011	Isa adongi ko , adi boyeyoa oko mondengi , isa adi bosɔmbɔ ai muma ’ nde . Na momi koko boa ; abwaniti bodonga ai mwali onde .
46007012	Eleho embi ai bato batongo , te eleho eKumu , edi oko ye ; isa moto oDenga adi na mwali yona odi pɛ hojima Njambe , na apalaka bo adae na muma’nde , momi omina abwaniti bomodongeja .
46007013	Isa mwali adi na momi yona odi pɛ bojima Njambe , na momi omina apalaka bo adae muma’nde , mwali omina abwamti bomolona .
46007014	Mojɔ bo momi yona odi pɛ bojima Njambe akatani na bojongoa bomwali onde ; na mwali yona odi pɛ bojima Njambe akatani na bojongoa bomuma’nde . Emiti da boa , o bana banu badae bana basɔni , te nongo bana baya bahɛngɛmɛ ai Njambe .
46007015	Isa momi , isa mwali , yona odi pɛ bojima Njambe apalaka adonge , yɛ adonge . Ekada boa , moto oDenga , isa momi isa mwali , aditi na mbɔci . Mojɔ bo Njambe abea so bo bodae na bowi .
46007016	Wɛ mwali otajebaka bo obwani boheleja muma’we ? Na wɛ momi , otajebaka bo obwani boheleja mwali owɛ ?
46007017	Moto na moto adi bosusa njea emonejaka Kumu . Isa Njambe abea moto a ekina ekɔmɛli , yɛ adae oko na ekɔmɛli emina . Mobeko mombi a Menga masusu modi boa .
46007018	Isa balenea moto ganda oko Njambe aipaka mobea , abwaniti bodongeja bimbete bibolena . Na moto akabeama yana adi yo oko na mwea , abwaniti bolenama ganda .
46007019	Mojɔ bo , bolena boganda bodi eka engasa , na mwea modi koko eka engasa . Mojɔ mosoti modi oko lisuma a mibeko miNjambe .
46007020	Moto na moto adi boyeyoa o adi yo a ehole embea ende .
46007021	Isa odaka mobuli yana abeama wɛ , pɛ mojɔ . Okanɛ njea ebosɔmi ko , t’okputoe oko .
46007022	Kumu akabea moto yona odi mobuli , moto omina adi na bosɔmi boKumu . Na Kumu akabea moto yona odi sɔmi , moto omina adi mobuli oMasiya .
46007023	Ino osikoamani na lisiko linɛnɛ . T’odaeni oko babuli babato .
46007024	Baninga , Njambe akabea moto , yɛ ayeyoe o adaka yo yana abeama yo .
46007025	Naditi na mobeko moKumu a mojɔ mobandengi . Mbi ko nadi na bolɛ bombi mɛnɛ , na obwanini bojima mbi , mojɔ bo Kumu akɔni monganji .
46007026	Mbi nalɛkɛ bo moto abwani boyeyoa o adi yo edɛye , mojɔ bo masu ma madi na minɔngɔ .
46007027	Okatani na mwali ? Pɛ boduka njea ebobɔtɔ . Odi mondengi ? Pɛ boduka mwali .
46007028	Momi ko akalongana , atakɔkɔ nongo bobe . Na moseka akalongana , atakɔkɔ nongo bobe . Bato bamina ko badi bonɛ jɔɔlɔ a ngondo ye , na mbi napalaka bo nahelejae no a jɔɔlɔ emina .
46007029	Baninga , cina emojɔ mobalaka mbi edi bo masu masu maditi manɛnɛ . A mojɔ momina , baya badi na bali babwani boda na ekɔmɛli ebato baya bapeliti bali .
46007030	Bato baya bayeaka bio babwani boda o bato baya baditi na bio . Bato baya badi na sepi babwani boda o bato baya baditi na sepi . Baya basombaka leka babwani boda o bato baya bapeliti eka .
46007031	Baya badi na bilomu bingondo babwani boda o bato baya babɔtɔnɔ na ngondo , mojɔ bo ngando jingondo ye jisiaka oko bosia .
46007032	Mbi nitapalaka bo odaeni na mokakwano . Mondengi adi na bolɛ oko a ngando jiKumu , bo asepejae Kumu .
46007033	Momi ko , yona odi na mwali , adi na bolɛ a ngando jingondo ye , bo asepejae mwali onde .
46007034	Mojɔ momwali obolongana , na mwali yona odi mondengi , modi koko boa ; baditi amɛci . Mwali yona opeliti momi , adi na bolɛ a ngando jiKumu , bo mokuku monde na mwembo monde midae mihɛngɛmɛke ai Kumu . Mwali ko yona odi na momi , adi na bolɛ a ngando jingondo ye , bo asepejae muma’nde .
46007035	Nabalaka boa a bokɔmeja no , te a bobindaneja no , bo ekɔmɛli enu ebɔnge , na bo okataneni na Kumu na milema minu misusu .
46007036	Okina momi ko yona opandi mwali , akalɛ bo ekɔmɛli ende ai mwali omina ebɔngiti , mojɔ bo posa jinde jigbasoi , babwani bolongana . Mojɔ mokada boa , yɛ akɔe o apalaka yo , atakɔkɔ nongo bobe .
46007037	Moto ko akada na ngulu a molema monde , na abwani bosabekea bo atagboka na posa jinde jimokuku , na andi ngapa bo atalongana na mwali omina , akɔkɔ bopele .
46007038	Oko boa , yona olonganaka na mwali opanda yo akɔkɔ bopele , na yona odi pɛ bolongana akɔkɔ bopele mɛnɛ .
46007039	Mwali omoto akatani na muma’nde oko a bogwa bomuma’nde . Muma’nde ko akagwa âcingoama ai yo ; na akapala bo alongane na okina momi otongo , pɛ mojɔ — a tei eKumu ko .
46007040	Bolɛ bombi mɛnɛ bodi bo enɔi na bopele akayeyoa o adi yo . Na nalɛkɛ bo nadi na Mwembo moNjambe .
46008001	A mojɔ momasiko mapejaka bato a bilimo , bojebaka so basusu cina emina . Ejebeli ko ehuulejaka moto na egho ; epaeli ko embilimejaka .
46008002	Moto akalɛ bo adi na ekina ejebeli , ajebakini na soti .
46008003	Moto ko akapala Njambe , Njambe ajebaka moto omina .
46008004	Oko boa , a mojɔ moboyaka tito bamasiko mabilimo , bojebaka bo elimo edi eka engasa mɛnɛ a ngondo ye . Njambe adi oko omɔci pɛ , pɛpɛ okina otongo .
46008005	Nongo bakabakea kombe banjambe ai bakina , isa oho Diko isa ya nase — na banjambe badi banɛnɛ , na bakumu koko banɛnɛ —
46008006	ai so ko , Njambe adi oko omɔci pɛ , oko Njambe Sango . Leka losusu lohulaka ai yo , na so bodi oko ai yo . Na Kumu adi oko omɔci pɛ , oko Yesu Masiya . Leka losusu lodi a mojɔ monde , na so bodi a mojɔ monde .
46008007	Bato basusu ko bapeliti ejebeli emina . Bakina bato baya balandoa na bilimo , bayakaka leka lomina na bolɛ a masiko mabilimo , na milema mibu miyɛmbu mikɔkɔ mabai .
46008008	Lilonga lisu a boso boNjambe liditi mojɔ modia . Botalonga a mojɔ moboyaka , na bota-beha na ekia .
46008009	Ino ko haya bayakaka dia dimina , toma nganja mani bo ekɔmɛli enu etasakeja bayɛmbu libaku .
46008010	Wɛ moto yona odi na ejebeli emijɔ , — moto otongo yona odi moyɛmbu akanɛ wɛ yana adi wɛ a boyaka a tei etempelo ebilimo , otalindaka moto omina yona odi na molema moyɛmbu a boyaka masiko mabilimo pongono ?
46008011	Oko boa , moto yona moyɛmbu , oko mwangwao mɛnɛ , adi bobeha a mojɔ moejebeli ewɛ ; na Masiya agwea moto omina .
46008012	Okabejani baninga boa na okababenejani a milema mibu miyɛmbu , okɔkɔni bobe ai Masiya yo mɛnɛ .
46008013	A mojɔ momina , mbi nakasakeja mwangwa’mbi na boyaka , nadi bokia tito na bosusu , bo nitasakeja mwangwa’mbi libaku .
46009001	Mbi naditi sɔmi ? Mbi naditi obwɛnji ? Nanɛ Yesu Kumu osu ? Elomu embi a tei eKumu , te no bɛnɛ ?
46009002	Isa batongo bataji-maka bo nadi obwɛnji , nadi obwɛnji ai no , mojɔ bo odini embete bo Kumu apani elomu eobwɛnji .
46009003	Bosɔmbeja bombi ai baya basambejaka mbi bodi oko bu .
46009004	Iso bobwaniti boyaka na bomwaka ?
46009005	Iso bokapala , bobwamti bosɔ mwali oejimeli bo bodale na nde o akɔkɔ babwɛnji batongo , na bananango baKumu , na Kepa pongono ?
46009006	Adi so babae pɛ , so na Balanaba , pɛpɛ kpaci a bokɔ boa ?
46009007	Soda adi bokɛ a bila , na pɛ moto bomobɔkɔ ? Moto aka’na mole , atayaka mbuma jimole momina ? Mobanei obata atamwaka mabɛi mabata ?
46009008	Nabalaka mojɔ momina na kpaci emoto pɛ ? Pɛpɛ . Mojɔ momina moditi a Mibeko ?
46009009	Mojɔ bo , mosɔnɔmɔ a Mibeko miMose bo , T’okande oko ebombo engɔmbɔ yona ondaka ndongo . Adi Njambe na bolɛ oko ai ngɔmbɔ pɛ ?
46009010	Atabalaka boa a mojɔ mosu pongono ? Ee , mosɔnɔmɔ a mojɔ mosu ; mojɔ bo moto yona oliaka gbie , adi boha na njingo , na yona ondaka ndongo , adi bonda na njingo ebosɔ libondo .
46009011	Boka’na dona dingando jiMwembo a tei enu , bobwamti bosɔ libondo lileka lonu ?
46009012	Isa ojimakani bo bakina batongo bakɔe na nu boa , esingaiti so ! Iso ko boikɔkɔ boa , pɛpɛ nongo mweka . Bodingoaka oko bodingoa bo botabindaneja Mwako Mopele moMasiya .
46009013	Otajebakani bo bato baya bakɔkɔ elomu etempelo bayakaka leka lotempelo , na baya bakɔkɔ elomu elitumbu limasiko basɔkɔ libondo limasiko .
46009014	Oko boa , Kumu abekea bo baya batɔndɔkɔ Mwako Mopele badi bosɔ libondo libu lileka a mojɔ moMwako Mopele .
46009015	Mbi ko , nongo adaka mbi na kpaci ebokɔ boa , naidaka nongo na ekɔmɛli emina ; na nitasɔnɔkɔ ngando jimina na njingo bo nadae na kpaci emina . Mbi nasakumejaka na ekɔmɛli emina , na najimi bo nadi bopeta gwa , bo moto asaka katoa ekumu emina ai mbi .
46009016	Atɔndɔkɔ mbi Mwako Mopele , nitasaku-mejaka na mojɔ momina , mojɔ bo nalindamaka a botɔndɔ Mwako Mopele . Namiti tɔndɔ Mwako Mopele nadi boda na monɔngɔ monɛnɛ a molema mombi .
46009017	Nakakɔ mojɔ momina na bolulea bombi mɛnɛ , nasɔkɔ ndese . Nakakɔ boa ko a mojɔ mobolulea bua boditi bolulea bombi mɛnɛ , cina edi bo nasi elomu emina bo naekɔe .
46009018	Na ndese embi edi bo ? Edi oko bo , nongo adi mbi na kpaci a bosɔ likonja a mojɔ moetɔndɛli embi , natɔndɔkɔ Mwako Mopele boangasa , pɛ bosɔ nongo likonja .
46009019	Mbi naditi mobuli omoto . Endele ko , nasapika mobuli obato basusu bo nadihe bato banɛnɛ .
46009020	Nadi MoYuda ai Bayuda , bo nalɛnge BaYuda . Nadi moto yona osumaka Mibeko ai bato baya basumaka Mibeko , bo nalɛnge bato baya basumaka Mibeko . ( Mbi mɛnɛ ko naditi cina jiMibeko . )
46009021	A mojɔ mobato baya bapeliti Mibeko , nadi o moto yona opeliti Mibeko , ( te nongo bo naditi cina jiMibeko miNjambe ; nadi cina jiMibeko miMasiya ) bo nalɛnge bato baya bapeliti Mibeko .
46009022	Nadi moyɛmbu ai bayɛmbu , bo nalɛnge bayɛmbu . Nadi tungu jisusu ai bato basusu bo nameke njea jisusu a boheleja bakina bato .
46009023	Nakɔkɔ boa a mojɔ moMwako Mopele , bo nadae na libondo limbi a elomu emina .
46009024	Otajebakani bo bato bakapota mbambano , bapotaka bo basusu ? yona osɔkɔ ndese ko , oko omɔci pɛ . Oko boa toma potani a bosɔ ndese .
46009025	Moto na moto yona osɛlingoaka a mojɔ mombambano asumaka bikia . Ibo bakɔkɔ boa bo basɛ likongo lingasa lia lidi bogwa ; iso ko bokɔkɔ a mojɔ molikongo lia lidi boyeyoa oko an bosusu .
46009026	A mojɔ momina , mbi napotaka bojo , te epotapota . Na’naka boma na soti te na busubusu .
46009027	Nadingojaka na nagbokejaka mokuku mombi , bo nasaka samboe , mbi yona otɔndɔ Mwako Mopele ai bato , batongo .
46010001	Baninga , mbi napalaka bo ojebeni bo batata basu basusu badaka a cina eeyembi , na bo basusu banɔ a njea emadiba-mamukwa .
46010002	Ibo basusu babatisama a tei eeyembi , na a tei emadiba-mamukwa , ai Mose .
46010003	Ibo basusu bayaka dia dimɔci dimwembo ,
46010004	na bamwaka ’ bo basusu emwakeli emɔci emwembo . Mojɔ bo bamwaka a litai limwembo lia libasusaka , na litai limina lidaka oko Masiya .
46010005	Njambe ko aisepa na banɛnɛ babu , na bagwa a lisobe .
46010006	Ngando jimina jidi bileho ai so , bo botada na posa jibe o adaka bo .
46010007	T’odaeni oko basakoi babilimo o adaka bakina babu ; mosɔnɔmɔ boa bo , Bato bada na mbondo a boyaka na bomwaka , Na bangɔ a bobua ngɔmɔ .
46010008	Bobwaniti boda na lisɔngi o adaka bakina babu , na bagwa Busa bomɔci bato koto licinda-na-jisato .
46010009	Bobwaniti bodingea Kumu o akɔ bakina babu , na njɔ babawa .
46010010	Bobwaniti boda na manungunungu o adaka bakma babu , na obwɛnji-obogwa abawa .
46010011	Ngando jimina jidoa ai bato bamina o bileho ; jisɔnɔmɔ ko a bokoja so baya badi a ehole ye esuka .
46010012	A mojɔ momina , moto na moto yona odingaka bo adi mombilimake , abwani bonganjama bo asaka kwa .
46010013	Ino onɛkinini bomeka bua bonɔi ngulu enu . Njambe t’akputojake sako jinde , na yo atajima bo odaeni na bomeka bua bonɔi ngulu enu ; mojɔ bo bomeka bokadoa ai no , yo adi bopa no njea ebohela , bo ohɔneni bomeka bomina .
46010014	A mojɔ momina baninga , toma gbeseani bosakoa bobilimo .
46010015	Nabalaka na bato babowɛi . Lɛni no bɛnɛ mojɔ mobalaka mbi .
46010016	Kɔpɔ ejongoaka so , te bokatana bosu na makia maMasiya ? Molɛmbɛ mobukaka so , te bokatana bosu na mokuku moMasiya ?
46010017	Molɛmbɛ modi momɔci ; oko boa , nongo adi so banɛnɛ , bodi oko mokuku momɔci , mojɔ bo so basusu bosɔkɔ libondo limolɛmbɛ momɔci .
46010018	Lɛni ekɔmɛli eYisalaele ; baya bayakaka masiko malitumbu bakatani na litumbu .
46010019	Nitabalaka bo masiko mabilimo madi na cina , isa bo elimo edi eka .
46010020	Pɛpɛ ; cina ebalaka mbi edi bo bapakano bakapa masiko , bamapaka a miembo mibe , te nongo ai Njambe . Mbi nitapalaka bo okataneni na miembo mibe .
46010021	Obwanitini bomwaka kɔpɔ eKumu , na kɔpɔ emiembo mibe pongono . Obwanitini bosɔ libondo a mesa maKumu , na a mesa mamiembo mibe pongono .
46010022	Iso bodi bokeja Njambe likaka ? Iso bomonɔi na ngulu ?
46010023	Nakapala , nabwani bokɔ ngando jisusu ; ngando jisusu ko jibɔngiti . Nakapala , nabwani bokɔ ngando jisusu ; ngando jisusu ko jitabɔngejaka .
46010024	Moto abwaniti bokɔ ngando jipalaka yo mɛnɛ , oko ngando jia jikɔmejaka moto otongo .
46010025	Yakani leka losusu longɛjɛkɛ bato a esanjo ; pɛ bodani na mokakwano a mojɔ momina .
46010026	Mojɔ bo ngondo esusu mɛnɛ edi ai Kumu , na leka losusu lua lodi a ngondo pongono .
46010027	Moto yona oditi na ejimeli akabea no a boyaka , na okakɛni , yakani leka losusu loneaka yo no ; pɛ bodani na mokakwano a mojɔ momina .
46010028	Okina moto ko akabala na nu bo , Iye edi tito emasiko ; t’oyakeni oko , mojɔ bo moto omina ajebejai wɛ . Mojɔ momina modi mojɔ momolema monde , te monu .
46010029	Molema momoto otongo modi boneja mbi mua mobwani na mbi ?
46010030	Nakajongoa dia , na nakayaka , okina adi bolemoa na mbi mojɔ bo nalijongoaka ?
46010031	Cina edi bo , okayakani isa okamwakani , isa okakɔni mokina mojɔ motongo , kɔni mijɔ misusu a bokumeja Njambe .
46010032	T’osakejaeni oko bato batongo libaku , isa BaYuda , isa BaEla , isa bato baDenga diNjambe .
46010033	Mbi mɛnɛ nakengaka bosepeja bato basusu na ngando jisusu jikɔkɔ mbi , bo bahele ; te nakɔke a mojɔ mombi mɛnɛ , oko a mojɔ mobato batongo banɛnɛ .
46011001	Ikoanani na mbi o akoanaka mbi na Masiya .
46011002	Nasakoaka no mojɔ bo olɛkɛni mbi bihole bisusu , na otabosakani ngando jikoja mbi no .
46011003	Endele ko , napalaka bo ocingeeni bo Masiya adi molo momoto ; molo momwali modi oko muma’nde ; na Njambe adi molo moMasiya .
46011004	Moto aka’nga , isa akatɔndɔ mwako na egbala a molo , asambojaka molo monde .
46011005	Mwali ko aka’nga , isa akatɔndɔ mwako , na apeliti eka a molo , asambojaka molo monde ; ekɔmɛli ende ebwani na yena emwali , bamaka nwɛ swe jinde .
46011006	Mwali amiti lwa eka a molo , abwani bolena swe jinde . Na isa edi sɔni ai mwali a bolena isa a bonwɛ swe jinde , yɛ akunde molo monde .
46011007	Momi ko abwaniti bokunda molo monde cina bo yo adi elimo na ekumu eNjambe ; mwali ko adi ekumu emomi .
46011008	Mojɔ bo momi aimana ai mwali ; mwali ko amana ai momi .
46011009	Na momi aikɔmɔ a mojɔ momwali ; mwali ko akɔmɔ a mojɔ motni .
46011010	A mojɔ momina , mwali abwani bolwa a molo embete ekpaci emomi , a mojɔ moba-bwɛnji .
46011011	A tei eKumu ko , mwali t’adake yo buki ; acingi oko na momi . Na momi pongono t’adake yo buki ; acingi oko na mwali .
46011012	Mwali amana ai momi ; edɛye mwali abotaka momi ; na leka losusu lohulaka ai Njambe .
46011013	Lɛni no bɛnɛ ; Mwali aka’nga Njambe , pɛ bopeta lwa eka a molo , mojɔ momina mobɔngi ?
46011014	Ekɔmɛli ebato basusu etakojaka no bo momi akada na swe jiyai , edi sɔni .
46011015	Mwali ko akada na swe jiyai , jidi oko ekumu ende . Mojɔ bo yo asɔ swe jimina a bosakunda .
46011016	Isa okina moto ko adi na kitɛ , so boditi na ekina ekɔmɛli etongo , isa Menga maNjambe .
46011017	Nadi na eleho a bopa no , na mtasakoa no ; mojɔ bo matitana manu matakɔmejaka no ; mabejaka no oko bobeja .
46011018	Mojɔ moboso oko mu ; mbi na’kaka bo odini na misoo a matitana manu maDenga , na mbi najimaka mweka bo mojɔ momina modi soti .
46011019	Odini mabondo-mabondo soti ; oko boa bato basoti badi boboloa a tei enu .
46011020	Okatitanani , otayakani nongo Kola eKumu .
46011021	Mojɔ bo , yana ayakaka no , moto na moto ayakaka mia mande mɛnɛ ; na okina adi ngasa na otongo alangoi .
46011022	Boni ! opelitini ndako jinu bɛnɛ a mojɔ moboyaka na bomwaka ? Osambojakani Denga diNjambe , na okejakani bato babokwali sɔni . Nâbala na nu bo ? Nâsakoa no ? Pɛpɛ nongo mweka .
46011023	Mojɔ bo mbi nasɔ oko ai Kumu mua mopeja mbi no , bo Kumu Yesu atomba molɛmbɛ na bulu bokabama yo ;
46011024	ajongoa , abuka molɛmbɛ , na abala bo , Imu modi mokuku mombi mua mobukei a mojɔ monu . Kɔni boa bo osalɛjeni ai mbi .
46011025	Ama bo sieja boyaka , yo ami tomba oko kɔpɔ pongono , na abala bo , Kɔpɔ ye edi Mokongo Moyene momakia mambi . Kɔni boa , bihole hisusu himwakaka no , bo osalɛjeni ai mbi .
46011026	Mojɔ bo , bihole bisusu biyakaka no molɛmbɛ mu , na bimwakaka no kɔpɔ ye , otɔndɔkɔni mwako mobogwa boKumu oko a bodoa bonde koko .
46011027	A mojɔ momina , moto akayaka molɛmbɛ mu , isa akamwaka kɔpɔ ye eKumu , na yo pɛ bobɔngɔ , adi na lindo jimokuku na jimakia maKumu .
46011028	Yɛ moto asakokelejae yo mɛnɛ , asa ko ayake molɛmbɛ na amwake kɔpɔ .
46011029	Mojɔ bo , moto akayaka na akamwaka , pɛ ko bombetea mokuku moKumu , ayakaka na amwakaka bodumba bonde mɛnɛ .
46011030	A mojɔ momina , bakina banu banɛnɛ badi na bwɛmbu , na bapekaka , na bakma bahwɛkɛ hiɔ .
46011031	Bokasasambeja na soti , botasamba .
46011032	Endele ko , bokasamba , bodi bosɔ mokindo ai Kumu , bo botasamboa na ngondo .
46011033	Oko boa baninga , okatitanani a mojɔ moboyaka , ambanani .
46011034	Okina onu akada na nja , yɛ ayake a ndako ende mɛnɛ , bo botitana bonu botasamboa . Nadi bokolea ngando jitongo oko namaka doa mbi mɛnɛ .
46012001	Baninga , mbi napalaka bo ocingeeni mojɔ mobipeeli bimwembo .
46012002	Yana adaka no bapakano , ojebakani bo ojimani bo bato balabojae no a bosakoa banjambe-babokosea baya badi oko bimimi .
46012003	A mojɔ momina , napalaka bo ocingeeni bo Mwembo moNjambe mokabaleja moto , moto omina atahɔnɔ bosinga Yesu . Na moto amiti da na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke , atahɔnɔ bobala bo Yesu adi Kumu .
46012004	Bipeeli bidi tungu-tungu , Mwembo ko modi oko momɔci pɛ .
46012005	Bilomu pongono bidi tungu-tungu , Kumu ko adi oko omɔci .
46012006	Na njea jibokɔ na elomu jidi tungu-tungu , Njambe ko yona okɔkɔ ngando jisusu ai bato basusu adi oko omɔci .
46012007	Moto na moto asɔkɔ epeeli ende eMwembo a bokɔmeja bato basusu .
46012008	Okina asɔkɔ ebaeli ebowɛi a Mwembo , na otongo asɔkɔ ebaeli eejebeli a Mwembo momina .
46012009	Okina asɔkɔ ejimeli a Mwembo , na otongo asɔkɔ epeeli ebosengoa a Mwembo momina .
46012010	Okina asɔkɔ epeeli a bokɔ mindumba , na otongo asɔkɔ epeeli a botɔndɔ mwako moNjambe . Okina asɔkɔ epeeli a bombetea miembo , na otongo asɔkɔ epeeli ekɔpi jitongo-tongo , na otongo koko a’kaka kɔpi jitongo-tongo .
46012011	Mwembo ko mua mokɔkɔ ngando jisusu na okabaka ai moto na moto libondo lipalaka yo , modi oko Mwembo momɔci pɛ .
46012012	Mokuku modi eka emɔci , binama ko bidi binɛnɛ . Na binama bisusu , nongo bikada binɛnɛ , bikɔkɔ oko mokuku momɔci . Modi oko boa na Masiya .
46012013	Mojɔ bo bobatisama so basusu a Mwembo momɔci bo bodae mokuku momɔci , isa BaYuda , isa BaEla , isa babuli , isa basɔmi ; na bomwaka so basusu na Mwembo momɔci .
46012014	Mojɔ bo , mokuku moditi elembo emɔci pɛ ; modi na bilembo binɛnɛ .
46012015	Nongo ebota ekabala bo , Mbi nacingiti na mokuku mojɔ bo naditi ebɔ , ebaeli emina etadongeja ebota a mokuku .
46012016	Na litoi likabala bo , Mbi nacingiti na mokuku mojɔ bo mbi naditi diso , ebaeli emina etadongeja litoi a mokuku .
46012017	Mokuku mosusu mokada oko diso pɛ , njoki edi boda jɔ ? Mokuku mosusu mokada oko litoi pɛ , soo edi boda jɔ ?
46012018	Njambe akolea binama bisusu a mokuku , emɔci-emɔci , o apalaka yo .
46012019	Binama bisusu bikada oko emɔci pɛ , mokuku modi boda jɔ ?
46012020	Oko boa binama bidi bmɛnɛ , mokuku ko oko omɔci .
46012021	Diso libwaniti bobala na ebɔ bo , Mbi nitajebaka wɛ . Na molo mobwaniti bobala na mako bo , Mbi nitaje-baka no .
46012022	Pɛpɛ nongo mweka ; binama bimokuku bia bidi oko ngasa a miso mabato bibɔngejaka mokuku .
46012023	Na bokumejaka binama bia bilɛkɛ so oko ngasa ; na bia bidi bibombamake bidi na ekumu enɛnɛ , na bia bidi a bohu bibwani boa .
46012024	Njambe abɔngeja mokuku mosusu , bo yena edi ngasa edae na ekumu .
46012025	A mojɔ momina , mokuku mopeliti bobɔtɔ , na binama bisusu bikɔmejanaka .
46012026	Enama emɔci ekapeka , bisusu bitongo bipekaka pongono .
46012027	Ino odini mokuku moMasiya , odini binama binde , moto na moto oko enama .
46012028	Njambe akolea bato a tei eDenga , boso oko babwɛnji , na ngɔngɔ jibu oko batɔndɔi . Bacingi na bu ngɔngɔ oko bakoja , na bato baya bakɔkɔ mindumba , bato basengo , bakɔmeja , bato babilomu , bato bakɔpi jinɛnɛ .
46012029	Basusu badi babwɛnji ? Basusu badi batɔndɔi ? Basusu badi bakoja ? Basusu bakɔkɔ mindumba ?
46012030	Basusu badi basengoi ? Basusu babalaka na kɔpi jinɛnɛ ? Basusu bakaka kɔpi jinɛnɛ ?
46012031	Dukani oko bipeeli bia binɔi na bopele . Mbi ko nadi boneja no njea yena enɔi na bopele .
46013001	Nongo nakabala na kɔpi jibato , isa jibabwɛnji-badiko , na napeliti epaeli , nadi oko doi dieboli , isa lisanga lia likɔkɔ ngɛ-ngɛ-ngɛ .
46013002	Namiti da na epaeli , nadi eka engasa mɛnɛ ; nongo nakatɔndɔ mwako , nongo nakacingea ngando jibombamake , nongo nakada na ejebeli esusu , nongo nakada na ejimeli enɛnɛ a bodongeja meno minɛnɛnɛ , pɛ mojɔ .
46013003	Namiti da na epaeli , nitabɔngɔ nongo mweka , nongo nakakaba leka lombi a bobɔkɔ bato babokwali , isa nakapa mokuku mombi a botumbama , pɛ mojɔ .
46013004	Epaeli edi na lingbangba ; edi koko na likabo . Epaeli editi na likaka , na editi na egbo .
46013005	Epaeli editi na jala , na editi na ebaeli ebe . Epaeli editi na bolɛ a ngando jinde mɛnɛ pɛ , editi na misuba , na editi na kɛlɛ .
46013006	Epaeli etasepaka a mojɔ mobobe , esepaka oko a mojɔ mobopele pɛ .
46013007	Epaeli ehɔnɔkɔ ngando jisusu ; ejimaka ngando jisusu ; edi na njingo a tei engando jisusu , na edi na lingbangba a tei engando jisusu .
46013008	Epaeli epeliti nongo suka . Bitɔndɛli bidi bosia , na kɔpi jiyɛyɔ bogo ; ejebeli edi bodimoa .
46013009	Mojɔ bo ejebeli esu edi oko ekenge pɛ , na etɔndɛli esu edi oko ekenge pɛ ;
46013010	Mua mobɔngi kanga mosusu ko mokaboloa , mua modi oko ekenge pɛ môsia .
46013011	Amaka mbi da yɛngɛ , nadaka na ebaeli eyɛngɛ , bolɛ bombi bodaka bolɛ boyɛngɛ , molema mombi modaka molema moyɛngɛ ; ama mbi kandoa ko , nami kina oko ngando jibwɛngɛ .
46013012	Bonjaka edɛye oko a talatala na ehindahindi ; bô’nɛnɛ ko ngɔngɔ o bato baya bayɛlɛni . Edɛye , ejebeli embi edi oko ekenge pɛ ; a busa bomina ko , nadi bojeba o ajebamaka mbi .
46013013	Edɛye ngando ji jisato jidikai , oko ejimeli , na njingo , na epaeli ; yena enɔi jisusu ko edi oko epaeli .
46014001	Bakeani milema minu a epaeli . Dani na posa a bipeeli bimwembo , bou oko epeeli ebotɔndɔ .
46014002	Moto yona otɔndɔkɔ na kɔpi etongo atabalaka na bato , abalaka oko na Njambe . Bato bata-mocingeaka mojɔ bo abalaka ngando jibombamake .
46014003	Moto ko yona otɔndɔkɔ mwako , abalaka na bato bo abalehe , abakɔmejae , na agɔmbejae milema mibu .
46014004	Moto akabala na kɔpi etongo asapingejaka oko yo mɛnɛ pɛ ; yona ko otɔndɔkɔ mwako , apingejaka Denga .
46014005	Mbi napalaka bo obaleni no basusu na kɔpi jitongo , bou oko bo otɔndɔeni mwako . Moto akabala na kɔpi jitongo , pɛ ko bojebeja Denga cina emina , atakɔmeja Denga . Oko boa yona otɔndɔkɔ mwako adi boso bonde .
46014006	Baninga , mbi nakadoa ai no a bobala na kɔpi jitongo , pɛ ko botɔndɔ na eleho , na bokoja , na boboloja , nadi bokɔmeja no soti ?
46014007	Leka logo lodi na doi , o adi polongo na ebumba . Bomiti bɔteja ko doi dimina , odi bocingea ebomeli eleka lomina nda ?
46014008	Doi limondule limiti da na bohu , odi bosɛlingoa a mojɔ mobila nda ?
46014009	Mojɔ monu modi koko boa ; okabalani mojɔ na kɔpi etongo yena edi bato pɛ bo’ka , pɛpɛ nongo moto odi bocingea mojɔ mobalaka no , mojɔ bo obalakani oko bibalabala pɛ .
46014010	Kɔpi jidi a ngondo jinɛnɛ mɛnɛ , na jisusu jidi na cina .
46014011	Moto ko akabala na ekina kɔpi , na mbi pɛ bo’ka kɔpi emina , mbi nadi boda MoDɔkɔ a miso mamoto yona obalaka , na yo adi boda MoDɔkɔ a miso mambi .
46014012	Oko boa , ino okamboani bipeeli bimwembo , dani oko na posa ebipeeli bia bidi bokɔmeja Denga na soti .
46014013	A mojɔ momina , moto yona obalaka na kɔpi etongo abwani bo’nga bo asɛ epeeli ebocingea bato cina .
46014014	Mojɔ bo naka’nga na kɔpi etongo , modi mwembo mombi mua mongaka , molema mombi motacingea eka .
46014015	Oko boa nâkɔ bo ? Nadi bonga na mwembo , na nadi bonga na bocingea pongono . Nadi bo’mba njembo na mwembo , na nadi bo’mba njembo na bocingea pongono .
46014016	Okajongoa na mwembo , moto otongo yona oditi na epeeli ewɛ , atajeba nongo bojima Amen yana ajongoaka wɛ , mojɔ bo atacingeaka mojɔ mobalaka wɛ .
46014017	Wɛ mɛnɛ ojongoaka soti , yona otongo ko atapinga nongo a ejimeli ende .
46014018	Mbi nasakoaka Njambe mojɔ bo nanɔi no basusu na bɛtɛ ekɔpi .
46014019	Endele ko , na bobala bikenge koto domi na kɔpi etongo , na bikenge bitano na bocingea bombi mɛnɛ , napalaka gbo oko bo nabale na Denga oko na bikenge bitano na bocingea .
46014020	Baninga , t’odaeni oko na bocingea bobɛngɛ . Dani na ekɔmɛli ebana bakɛkɛ a mojɔ mobobe ; dani basuku ko a mojɔ mobocingea .
46014021	Mosɔnɔmɔ a Mibeko bo , Kumu abali bo , Nongo nakaloma bwɛnji bombi ai bato ba , Na bato bakɔpi jitongo , Isa na minɔkɔ miDɔkɔ , Batahokea mbi nongo mweka .
46014022	Oko boa , kɔpi jidi oko embete ai bato baya bajimakini , te nongo ai bato baejimeli . Etɔndɛli ko emwako moNjambe edi embete ai baya bajimaka , te nongo ai baya bajimakini .
46014023	A mojɔ momina , okadani na botitana boDenga disusu , na bato basusu bakabala na kɔpi jitongo-tongo , bato batongo bakakwea , bato baya badi pɛ boji-ma , batalɛ bo odini na malale ?
46014024	Bato basusu ko bakatɔndɔ mwako , na moto otongo akakwea yona odi pɛ bojima isa pɛ bocingea , adi bosɔ eleho ehu basusu , na adi bosamba na bu basusu .
46014025	Ngando jibombamake jimolema monde jidi boboloa a bohu , adi bokwa a boso bonde a bosakoa Njambe , na adi bojima bo Njambe adi a tei enu soti .
46014026	Cina emina edi bo , baninga ? Edi oko bo , omakatitanani , isa okina onu adi na eyembo , na otongo adi na eleho , isa na bokoja , isa na kɔpi , isa na bocingea , kɔni ngando jisusu a bopingeja ejimeli enu .
46014027	A mojɔ mobobala na kɔpi etongo , bopele bo bato babale omɔciomɔci , bato babae isa basato , suka oko bato basato .
46014028	Endele ko , isa moto yona okaka kɔpi jimina aditi , bopele bo badae oko bogo a botitana , na babale na milema mibu bɛnɛ , na Njambe .
46014029	Batɔndɔi babae isa basato badi bobala , na bato batongo badi bohokea .
46014030	Njambe ko akaboloja mokina mojɔ ai okina moto otongo yona odi ena , motɔndɔi yona obalaka adi boyɛyɔ bogo .
46014031	Obwanini botɔndɔ mwako no basusu , moto omɔci-omɔci ; oko boa bato basusu badi bokoa , na badi bopinga a ejimeli ebu .
46014032	Miembo mibatɔndɔi misumaka batɔndɔi .
46014033	Mojɔ bo Njambe adi Njambe obowi , te nongo Njambe oyikiyiki . Ekɔmɛli eMenga masusu mabato baejimeli
46014034	edi bo bali badae bogo a makita maDenga . Baditi na kpaci ebobala , na Mibeko mibalaka bo badi boda na lisuma .
46014035	Isa bapalaka bojeba mokina mojɔ , badi bohɔjɔ bami babu a ndako jibu bɛnɛ ; mojɔ bo ebɔngiti na mwali bo abale a likita liDenga .
46014036	Boni ! Ebaeli eNjambe eboloi boso ai no ? emei oko ai no pɛ ?
46014037	Isa okina onu alɛkɛ bo adi motɔndɔi , isa bo adi na bipeeli bimwembo , adi bocingea bo mijɔ misɔnei mbi no midi mobeko moKumu .
46014038	Moto yona odi pɛ bojeba , yɛ adae oko a libumi .
46014039	Oko boa baninga , bakeani milema minu a botɔndɔ mwako moNjambe . Pɛ bosiani bato a bobala na kɔpi jitongo .
46014040	Kɔni ngando jisusu oko na bowi na bongɛbɛnɛ .
46015001	Baninga , mbi napalaka bo nabale na nu a mojɔ moMwako Mopele motɔndɔ mbi no . Ojimani mwako momina , na odini bambihmake a mwako momina .
46015002	Ohelani oko na mwako momina , okamobaneani bopele — omiti kɔni boa , ejimeli enu edi eka engasa .
46015003	Mojɔ bo mbi napa no mojɔ monɛnɛ mosɔ mbi , bo Masiya agwa a mojɔ mojibe jisu , o abalaka Misɔnɔ .
46015004	Bamopusea , na angɔ koko a busa bomasato , o abalaka Misɔnɔ .
46015005	Kepa amonɛ , na babwɛnji domi-na-babae pongono .
46015006	Ekina ehole etongo , baninga mikama mitano bamonɛ ; bakina babu banɛnɛ badi oko busa bu , na bakina babu bagwa .
46015007	Yakobo amonɛ ngɔngɔ , na babwɛnji basusu pongono .
46015008	Suka mɛnɛ , asaboloja ai mbi pongono , mbi mwana obongoa .
46015009	Mojɔ bo mbi nadi ngɔngɔ jibabwɛnji basusu . Nabɔngiti bosɔ kombe eobwɛnji , mojɔ bo nadingoja Denga diNjambe .
46015010	Nadi adi mbi , oko a mojɔ momonganji moNjambe , na monganji monde ai mbi moinama . Mbi nakɔ elomu epipo , pɛpɛ nongo okina obu obwana na mbi a njea emina ; mbi mɛnɛ ko naikɔ , oko monganji moNjambe mua modi ai mbi .
46015011	Oko boa , mwako motɔndɔkɔ so basusu , isa mbi mɛnɛ , isa bo batongo , modi oko boa , na ojimani oko na mu .
46015012	Atɔndɔkɔ so bo Masiya angɔ a bogwa , bakina banu babalaka bo bagwake batangɔ mojɔ moye ?
46015013	Isa bagwake batangɔ , Masiya yo mɛnɛ aingɔ a bogwa .
46015014	Na isa Masiya aingɔ a bogwa , mwako motɔndɔkɔ so modi eka engasa , na ejimeli enu enami oko bonama .
46015015	Isa bagwake batangɔ , so bodi batati babokosea , mojɔ bo botataka bo Njambe angɔjɔ Masiya a bogwa .
46015016	Isa bagwake batangɔ , ka Masiya yo mɛnɛ aingɔ .
46015017	Isa Masiya aingɔ , ejimeli enu edi eka engasa , na odini oko a jibe jinu .
46015018	Na pongono , bato baya bagwa a tei eMasiya badimoa .
46015019	Isa njingo esu ai Masiya edi oko a mojɔ moehelo ye pɛ , bonɔi bato basusu na molɔbɔ .
46015020	Masiya ko angɔ a tei ebagwake soti , o mbuma eboso ebaya bagwa .
46015021	Mojɔ bo bogwa bodoa na moto , na bongɔ bobagwake bodoa na moto pongono .
46015022	Basusu bagwaka na Adama ; oko boa basusu bâsɔ bomɔ a tei eMasiya , moto na moto a libondo linde .
46015023	Masiya adi o mbuma eboso , ngɔngɔ jinde oko baya badi bato bande a bodoa bonde .
46015024	Ngɔngɔ jimina , suka emijɔ misusu edoabí . A ehole emina , oko amaka gbokeja makumu masusu , kpaci jisusu , ngulu esusu , asɔmbejabí bokumu ai Njambe Sango .
46015025	Mojɔ bo yo adi boda na kpaci ebokumu , oko adi yo pɛ bopeta cingea bibota binde a diko disoki jinde jisusu .
46015026	Soki yena egbokabí suka mɛnɛ edi oko bogwa .
46015027	Mojɔ bo Njambe adumba ngando jisusu a cina jibibota binde . Abalaka yo bo ngando jisusu jidi a cina jibibota binde , edi bohu mɛnɛ bo yo mɛnɛ yona odumba ngando ji jisusu , acingiti na ngando jimina .
46015028	Ngando jisusu jikada a cina ende , Mwana mɛnɛ adi bosuma yona odumba ngando jisusu a cina ende , bo Njambe adae ngando jisusu ai bato basusu .
46015029	Emiti da boa , cina ebatisimo ebato a mojɔ mobagwake edi bo ? Isa bagwake batangɔ , bato babatisamaka a mojɔ mobu cina eye ?
46015030	Na mbi napaka njupi bihole bisusu mojɔ moye ?
46015031	Mbi nayɛli bogwa tu busa ; nabalaka na nu boa baninga , mojɔ bo odini ekumu embi a tei eMasiya Yesu Kumu osu .
46015032	Isa bagwake batangɔ , mbi nana na tito babila a Ɛpɛsɔ na ngulu embi esusu mojɔ moye ? Êsɔ mbi nde ? Ekada boa , bopele bo boyake na bomwake , mojɔ bo bodi bogwapuma .
46015033	Yɛ bosakoseani ! Mambaci mabe mabejeka ekɔmɛli epele emoto .
46015034	Sisoani , na dani na yongi epele . Yɛni bokɔ bobe . Natɔndɔkɔ no , a bokeja no sɔni , bo bakina banu batajebaka nongo Njambe .
46015035	Okina moto ko adi bohɔjɔ bo , Bagwake badi bongɔ na ye ? Mikuku mibu midi boda bo ?
46015036	Wɛ egegele ! Ngua jinaka wɛ jimiti gwa , jitatɔ nongo .
46015037	Na jia jinaka wɛ jidi oko ngua , isa jindongo , isa jiekina eka etongo , te nongo mokuku mua modi bomana ngɔngɔ .
46015038	Njambe ko aepaka mokuku mopalaka yo , tu mongua oko na mokuku mua mobwani na mu .
46015039	Mikuku misusu miditi amɛci . Mokina modi a mojɔ mobato , motongo a mojɔ motito , mokina motongo a mojɔ mombulu , na motongo koko a mɔjɔ moswi .
46015040	Mikuku midiko midi , na mikuku minase . Ekumu emikuku midiko na ekumu emikuku minase bisangiti .
46015041	Ekumu emodika-busa na yena esonge bisangiti ; na ekumu enjɔtɔ edi tungu etongo , mojɔ bo ekumu emonjɔtɔ omɔci na yena emonjɔtɔ otongo bisangiti .
46015042	Bongɔ bobagwake bodi koko boa ; mokuku mosaka so ta kpɔtɔ modi mokuku mobopɔ ; mua modi bongɔ a bogwa môtapɔ .
46015043	Mo puseamaka , pɛpɛ nongo ekumu ; modi bongɔ na ekumu . Mopuseamaka eka eyɛmbu , modi bongɔ oko na ndangasa .
46015044	Mongua monaka so modi mokuku momoto ; modi bongɔ oko mokuku momwembo .
46015045	A mojɔ momina , mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Adama , moto oboso , adaka moto obomɔ . Adama osuka adi mwembo mua mopaka bomɔ .
46015046	Mua momwembo moidaka boso ; moto mɛnɛ boso , mwembo ko oko ngɔngɔ .
46015047	Moto oboso ahula a kpɔtɔ , moto onase . Moto obabae ahula oho Diko .
46015048	Bato banase badi oko na elimo emoto yona onase . Bato baDiko badi na elimo emoto oDiko .
46015049	Adi so na elimo emoto onase , bodi boda koko na elimo emoto oDiko .
46015050	Baninga , mbi natɔndɔkɔ no bo mini na makia mabwaniti bosangoa Bokumu boNjambe ; na eka ebopɔ ebwaniti bosangoa yena edi na bosusu .
46015051	Hokeani ! Nadi boboloja mojɔ mobombamake ai no . Iso basusu botahwɛ ; iso basusu ko bokindoabí .
46015052	Bokindoabi so basusu bundumo , o bogbatimeja bomiso a mondule mosuka . Mojɔ bo mondule mohwiamabí , bagwake badi bongɔ na mikuku mia mibwaniti bopɔ , na so basusu bokindoabí .
46015053	Mojɔ bo mokuku mu mobopɔ modi bolwa mokuku mua mobwamti bopɔ ; na mokuku mu mobogwa , modi bolwa mokuku mua mobwaniti bogwa .
46015054	Mokuku mobopɔ mokalwa mokuku mua mobwaniti bopɔ , na mokuku mobogwa mokalwa mokuku mua mobwaniti bogwa , ekenge yena esɔnɔmɔ edi bongama bo , Bogwa bogboki na lilonga .
46015055	Wɛ bogwa , lilonga liwɛ lidi jɔ ? Wɛ bogwa , ngɛngɛ ewɛ edi jɔ ?
46015056	Ngɛngɛ ebogwa edi bobe . Ngulu ebobe edi Mibeko .
46015057	Yɛni bosakoe Njambe yona okɔkɔ bo so bogbokejae a mojɔ moKumu osu Yesu Masiya .
46015058	A mojɔ momina , baninga bambi baepaeli , dani bambilimake , pɛ bombɛni nongo mweka ; kɔmɛni Kumu na elomu enɛnɛ masu masusu , mojɔ bo ojebakani bo elomu enu ai Kumu êtanama nongo .
46016001	A mojɔ mobipeeli ai bato baDenga , kɔni o akoja mbi Menga maGalatia .
46016002	Moto na moto adi bohɛngɛ libondo lilikonja lia libwani na nde a busa boNjambe ; pɛ bo’mbani bodoa bombi a bolɔkɔ bipeeli .
46016003	Mbi nakamea , odini bohɔ bato , na mbi nâbapa mokanda , bo nabalome na bipeeli binu a Yelusalema .
46016004	Mokabwana bo nakɛe mbi mɛnɛ , bato bamina badi bopaka mbi a njea .
46016005	Namaka sieja likota liMakedonia nasa ko nadoe ai no , mojɔ bo mokano mombi modi bo nanɔe a njea eMakedonia .
46016006	Isa nadi boyeyoa na nu ; kako nadi bosieja edidi epio a tei enu , bo osukejaeni mbi a njea ekɛkɛ mbi .
46016007	Ehole ye , nitapalaka ho nanɛnɛe na nu oko a njea pɛ . Kumu akajima , nadi na njingo bo nayeyoe na nu .
46016008	Nadi bopeta yeyoa ko a Ɛpɛsɔ oko a busa boDomitano ,
46016009	mojɔ bo njea enɛnɛ na epele ehoi a boso bombi bo nakɔe elomu ; soki ko jidi jinɛnɛ .
46016010	Timoteo akamea , kɔni bo adae a tei enu o bina’nde , mojɔ bo akɔkɔ elomu eNjambe o akɔkɔ mbi mɛnɛ .
46016011	Moto abwaniti bomokpɛkoja . Mosukejani a njea na bowi , bo ahule ai mbi , mojɔ bo namo-njaka yo na baninga batongo pongono .
46016012	A mojɔ momwangwa’su Apolo , mbi namolehi bou mɛnɛ bo akɛe na baninga oho adi no . Iyo ko apalakiti bo akɛe edɛye . Adi bokɛ , akanɛ ehole epele .
46016013	Ino , toma sɛnjɛlɛni bopele ; dani bambilimake a ejimeli enu ; dani bami mɛnɛ ; dani bato bapipo .
46016014	Kɔni bilomu binu bisusu oko na epaeli .
46016015	Ojebakani bato baSɛtɛpana ; baya bahekoa ai Kumu boso a likota liAkaya , oko ’ bo ; na badi na bingi enɛnɛ a bokɔmeja bato ba-Denga .
46016016	Mbi nalehaka no baninga bo odaeni na lisuma ai bato baya badi na ekɔmɛli emina , na bato basusu baya babakɔmejaka , na baya bakɔkɔ elomu eNjambe .
46016017	Nadi na sepi mojɔ bo Sɛtɛpana , na Polotunato , na Akaiko bamei jɔno ; adi no bohali , bo basepejai mbi .
46016018	Bagɔmbejai molema mombi na milema minu pongono . Obwamni bosuma bato baya badi na ekɔmɛli emina .
46016019	Menga maMasiya oho Asia mabɛjɛkɛ no njɛbɛ . Akwila na Pilisila , na Denga disusu dia dititanaka a ndako ebu , babɛjɛkɛ no bou a kombe eKumu .
46016020	Baninga basusu mɛnɛ babɛjɛkɛ no njɛbɛ . Sabɛjɛnɛni no bɛnɛ na njɛbɛ esɛnɔke .
46016021	Mbi Paulo nabɛjɛkɛ no njɛbɛ ye na ebɔ embi mɛnɛ .
46016022	Isa okina moto aditi na epaeli ai Kumu , yɛ alakejame . Yɛ Kumu adoe !
46016023	Yɛ monganji moKumu osu Yesu Masiya modae na nu .
46016024	Epaeli embi ai no basusu a tei eMasiya Yesu . Amen .
47001001	Njɛbɛ esu Paulo obwɛnji oMasiya Yesu a mojɔ mobolulea boNjambe , na mwangwa’mbi Timoteo , a Denga diNjambe dia didi a Kolinto , na ai bato basusu baMasiya baya badi a likota lisusu liAkaya .
47001002	Yɛ monganji na bowi boNjambe Sangwa’su na Kumu Yesu Masiya bodae ai no .
47001003	Mbi nasakoaka Njambe Sange ’ Kumu osu Yesu Masiya , Sango yona odi na monganji mosusu , na Njambe obogɔmbeja bosusu .
47001004	Iyo agɔmbejaka so a tei eminɔngɔ misu misusu , bo so bogɔmbejae bato batongo baya badi na minɔngɔ , o agɔmbejaka Njambe so bɛnɛ .
47001005	Mojɔ bo , bokakatana na Masiya a madingoa mande manɛnɛ , bodi bosɔ libondo linɛnɛ libogɔmbeja a mojɔ moMasiya .
47001006	Isa so bodi na minɔngɔ , cina eminɔngɔ mimina edi bo ino osɛni bogɔmbeja na mohelo . Na so bokasɔ bogɔmbeja , bodi a bogɔmbeja no , na odini bosɔ bogɔmbeja bomina , okadani na lingbangba a tei emadingoa , o adingoaka so .
47001007	Iso bodi na njingo enɛnɛ ai no . Bojebaka bo okaka-tanani na su a madingoa masu , odini bokatana na su koko a bogɔmbeja bosu .
47001008	Baninga , iso bopalaka bo ojebeni mojɔ momonɔngɔ monɛ so a Asia . Iso bobukana oko bobukana na muna momonɔngɔ . Mojɔ momina monɔ ngulu esu , na boidaka na njingo ebohela .
47001009	Bolɛ bo ehole esu ebogwa emea , na mojɔ momina mohekoja ejimeli esu ai Njambe yona ongɔjɔkɔ bagwake , te nongo ai so bɛnɛ .
47001010	Iyo aheleja so a bogwa bua bobe ; ahelejaka so koko edɛye , na njingo esu edi oko ai yo bo ahelejae so a masu mangɔngɔ .
47001011	Kɔmejani so na bingeeli binu , bo bato banɛnɛ basakoe Njambe a mojɔ momonganji mosɔ so , cina ebingeeli bibu .
47001012	Iso bosepaka na mojɔ mumu ; molema mosu motataka bo ekɔmɛli esu a miso mabato , na a miso manu bɛnɛ , edaka na bosɛnɔ na lisuma ai Njambe ; te nongo na bowɛi bongondo , oko na mo-nganji moNjambe .
47001013	Mikanda misɔneaka so no miditi na cina etongo ; midi oko na mijɔ milangaka no na micingeaka no . Nadi na njingo bo odini bocingea soti ,
47001014	o acingeaka no mweka edɛye , bo obwanini bosepa a mojɔ mosu , na bo so bodi bosepa a mojɔ monu a busa boKumu Yesu .
47001015	A mojɔ momina , mbi nadaki na njingo bo napete kɛ oho ai no a bohɛjɛ sepi enu oko bohɛjɛ .
47001016	Mokano mombi modaka bo nanɔe njea enu a bokɛ oho Makedonia , na bohula Makedonia koko ai no , bo osukejaeni mbi a njea eYuda .
47001017	Adaka mbi na mokano momina , nadaka na milema mibae ? Mijɔ mikanaka mbi midi mijɔ mimoto ongondo ? Adi mbi na minɔkɔ mibae , Ee ! ee ! na Pɛpɛ ! pɛpɛ !
47001018	Oko Njambe ! monɔkɔ mosu ai no moditi na mojimo na bongana , Ee na Pɛpɛ .
47001019	Iso na Silwano na Timoteo botɔndɔ no oko mwako moMwana ’ Njambe , Yesu Masiya . Iyo aditi Ee na Pɛpɛ ; a tei ende edi oko Eɛ .
47001020	Mojɔ bo sako jisusu jiNjambe jingami oko na nde ; a mojɔ momina , so bokumejaka Njambe na Amen , a kombe ende .
47001021	Njambe yo mɛnɛ apingejaka so na no a tei eMasiya , na ahɛngɛ so a elomu .
47001022	Abakea embete ende ai so , na abopa Mwembo a tei emilema misu o ndanga .
47001023	Mbi nabeaka Njambe o motati omolema mombi — mbi naidoa obo Kolinto , mojɔ bo naipalaka bohɛjɛ monɔngɔ monu .
47001024	Iso ko boditi nongo bakumu baejimeli enu ; bokɔkɔ elomu na nu bo odaeni na sepi , mojɔ bo odini bambilimake a ejimeli enu .
47002001	Mbi najima a molema mombi bo nitadoa koko ai no a bokeja no wa .
47002002	Nakakeja no wa , odi bosepeja mbi nda ? oko yona odi na wa a mojɔ mombi ?
47002003	Cina emokanda mosɔnɔ mbi edaka bo bato baya babwani bosepeja mbi a bodoa bombi , batakeja mbi wa . Nalɛ a molema mombi bo odini bosepa no basusu a mojɔ mosepi embi .
47002004	Nasɔnea no boso , na monɔngɔ , na jɔɔlɔ a molema mombi , na mbisoli jinɛnɛ , te bo nakejae no wa , oko bo ojebeni epaeli embi enɛnɛ ai no .
47002005	Isa okina moto anɔngeja batongo , ainɔngeja mbi ; anɔngeja oko no bosusu , isa bakina banu banɛnɛ . ( Nitapalaka bohɛjɛ mojɔ momina . )
47002006	A mojɔ momoto omina , mokindo mosɔ yo ai banɛnɛ banu mobwani .
47002007	Edɛye , obwanini bohekoa a bokina mojɔ monde , na a bogɔmbeja moto omina , bo asaka dinda a monɔngɔ monde monɛnɛ .
47002008	Oko boa , mbi nangɔɔnɔkɔ no bo omonejaeni koko epaeli enu .
47002009	Nasɔnea no boso a mojɔ momina , bo nameke no , a bojeba isa odini na lisuma a ngando jisusu .
47002010	Okakineani moto , mbi namo-kineaka pongono . Mojɔ mokini mbi ( isa nakini mokina mojɔ ) modi a mojɔ monu , a boso boMasiya ,
47002011	bo bosaka samboa na Satana ; mojɔ bo bojebaka poloso ende .
47002012	Iyana amea mbi a Toloa a botɔndɔ Mwako Mopele moMasiya , Kumu ahoja njea ai mbi bohu mɛnɛ .
47002013	Molema mombi ko modaka na manji , cina bo nainɛ mwangwa’mbi Tito oho . A mojɔ momina , naseana na bu , na nakɛ a Makedonia .
47002014	Mbi nasakoaka Njambe mojɔ bo adalejaka so mondinda na Yesu , na ekumu ende , masu masusu . Na ejebeli ende enanganaka na su a bisika bisusu o soo epele .
47002015	Mojɔ bo , so bodi ai Njambe oko soo epele eMasiya , a mojɔ mobato baya bahelaka , na baya bagwaka pongono ;
47002016	soo ebogwa ai baya bagwaka , na soo ebomɔ ai baya bahelaka . Obwani na ngando jimina nda ?
47002017	Iso botakɔkɔ bwasa na Ebaeli eNjambe , o akɔkɔ bakina . Bodi bato basoti , baya basɔ elomu emina ai Njambe . Bobalaka a boso boNjambe na a tei eMasiya .
47003001	Iso bobengi bosakumeja koko so bɛnɛ ? Iso bobwani bosɔ mikanda o asɔkɔ bakina bato , a bojebeja no ekɔmɛli esu , isa mikanda minu a bojebeja bato ekɔmɛli esu ?
47003002	Ino bɛnɛ odini mokanda mosu mua mosɔnɔmɔ a milema misu ; bato basusu bamolangaka na bamojebaka .
47003003	Na onejakani bo odini mokanda molomi Masiya na su , mua mosɔnɔmɔ na Mwembo moNjambe obomɔ , te nongo na madiba mamokanda ; mosɔnɔmɔ a Inilema mibato , te a matai .
47003004	Ejimeli esu edi boa ai Njambe a mojɔ moMasiya .
47003005	Bobwaniti bobala bo bodi bohɔnɔ mokina mojɔ na ngulu esu bɛnɛ . Ngulu esu ecingi oko na Njambe pɛ ,
47003006	yona obɔngeja so bo bodae bakɔmɛli baMokongo Moyene , bakɔmɛli baMwembo , te nongo bakɔmɛli babi-kenge bia bisɔnɔmɔ ; mojɔ bo , mibeko mia misɔnɔmɔ miwaka oko bowa ; Mwembo ko mopaka bomɔ .
47003007	Isa mojɔ mobogwa mua mosɔnɔmɔ a matai modoa na ekumu , esingaiti mua moMwembo !
47003008	Mojɔ bo BaYisalaele baihɔnɔ bonja boso boMose cina ebolailai a boso bonde , bolailai bua bodimoaka .
47003009	Oko boa isa elomu ebodumba edaka na ekumu , esingaiti elomu ebolongeja !
47003010	Soti mɛnɛ , mua modaka boso na ekumu , mopeliti koko ekumu edɛye , mojɔ bo ekumu etongo yena enɔi emodimoja .
47003011	Mojɔ bo , isa mojɔ mua moidaka na boyeyoa modoa na ekumu , esingaiti mojɔ mua moyeyoaka !
47003012	Oko boa , adi so na njingo emina , bobalaka na nu a bohu mɛnɛ .
47003013	Botakɔkɔ o akɔ Mose yona ohua hoso bonde , bo BaYisalaele bata’nɛ ekumu yena edimoaka .
47003014	Milema mibu ko miidaka nongo na njɛnɛ ; nongo bakalanga Mokongo Moyou busa bu , ehuako emina edi oko , mojɔ bo ehuako emina edi bodonga oko na Masiya .
47003015	Ee , oko busa bu , bakalanga mokanda moMose , ehuako ehuaka milema mibu .
47003016	Moto ko akahekoa ai Kumu , ehuako emina edi hodonga .
47003017	Kumu adi oko Mwembo , na bosɔnii bodi oko a esika edi Mwembo moKumu .
47003018	Iso basusu , maso masu a bohu , bonjaka ekumu eKumu , o anjaka so a talatala , na bokindoaka a elimo ende . Bokinaka ekumu emɔci a bosɔ ekumu etongo ; mojɔ momina mocingi oko na Kumu yona odi Mwembo .
47004001	Oko boa , adi so na elomu ye a mojɔ momonganji moNjambe , botangwa .
47004002	Iso boloni bikɔmɛli bibosambolu na bipoloso ; ekɔmɛli esu editi nongo na epulu ; botahekojaka Ebaeli eNjambe a ekina cina etongo . Botɔndɔkɔ mijɔ misoti a bohu , bo bodae na lilonga a boso bobato basusu , na a boso boNjambe .
47004003	Isa Mwako Mopele mosu modi mobombamake , mobombami oko ai bato baya bagwaka .
47004004	Mojɔ bo njambe ongondo ye ahua milema mibato bamina baya badi pɛ bojima , bo bata’nɛ bohu boMwako Mopele moekumu eMasiya yona odi elimo eNjambe .
47004005	Iso botɔndɔkɔ Mwako Mopele moYesu Masiya , bo yo adi Kumu , te nongo mijɔ misu bɛnɛ . Iso bɛnɛ bodi oko bakɔmɛli banu a kombe eYesu .
47004006	Mojɔ bo , Njambeyona obala bo , Kma bohu bohoe a tei emodidi , ahojai milema misu bohu mɛnɛ , bo apɛ bohu boejebeli eekumu eNjambe a boso boMasiya .
47004007	Ngulu yena enɔi edi ngulu eNjambe , te ngulu esu ; na edi a tei esu o likonja liyumu linɛnɛ a tei eteni ehbali .
47004008	Bohangami a bisika bisusu ; endele ko , bobindaniti . Adi so na monɔngɔ , bodi oko na njingo .
47004009	Bakanɔngeja so , botadikaka so buki pɛ . Bakadumba so nase , botagwaka .
47004010	Iso bolwaka bogwa boYesu oko bolwa , a tei emikuku misu bihole bisusu , bo bomɔ boYesu boboloe a tei emikuku misu pongono .
47004011	Mojɔ bo , adi so mɔ , bolindoamaka a bogwa bihole bisusu a mojɔ moYesu , bo bomɔ boYesu boboloe a tei emikuku misu mibogwa .
47004012	Oko boa , bogwa bokɔkɔ elomu a tei esu , bomɔ ko a tei enu .
47004013	Adi so na mwembo momɔci moejimeli mua modaka na nde yona osɔnɔ bo , Mbi najimi ; a mojɔ momina nabali ; iso koko bojimaka na bobalaka ;
47004014	mojɔ bo bojebaka bo yona ongɔjɔ Yesu a bogwa , adi bongɔjɔ so na Yesu , na adi bokweja so na nu a boso bonde .
47004015	Mojɔ mu mosusu modi ai no , bo monganji moNjambe mokanɛngɛ , bosakoa bodi bonɛngɛ pongono a bokumeja Njambe .
47004016	A mojɔ momina , bota’ngwa nongo . Isa moto osu osokolu agwaka , moto yona odi a tei asɔkɔ ngulu eyene busa na busa .
47004017	Monɔngɔ mosu mokɛkɛlɛkɛ mua moditi boyeyoa , mosɛlingoaka ekumu enɛnɛ mɛnɛ a mojɔ mosu , ekumu yena edi boyeyoa oko na bosusu .
47004018	Mojɔ bo , iso botanjaka ngando jinɛkɛ bato na miso ; bonjaka oko ngando jia jibwaniti bo’nɛmɛ . Ngando jinɛkɛ bato na miso jitayeyoa nongo . Ngando ko jidi so pɛ bonɛ na miso , jiyeyoaka na bosusu .
47005001	Iso bojebaka bo diako disu diboda ya nase dikagwa , bodi bosɔ ndako mɛnɛ ai Njambe . Etayoama na mɔmɔ mabato , na êyeyoa oko na bosusu oho Diko .
47005002	Bobemaka a diako di , oko na posa bo bobolame atei endako esu oho Diko .
47005003	Bokada na elwaeli emina , botada nongo mbundu .
47005004	Adi so a diako di , boyeaka , na bodi na milema manji . Editi bo bopalaka bohwa mokuku mu o ahwaka so bisenja . Edi bo bopalaka bo bolwae elwaeli etongo , bo mokuku mobo gwa mokindoe bomɔ .
47005005	Njambe yo mɛnɛ asɛlingoa so a mojɔ momina , na abopa Mwembo o ndanga .
47005006	Oko boa bodi na eci masu masusu . Bojebaka bo boditi na Kumu esika emɔci yana adi so a mokuku mu .
47005007	Mojɔ bo , bodalaka oko na ejimeli , te na njɛnɛ emiso .
47005008	Bodi na eci , na posa esu edi bo bodo-nge a mokuku mu , bo bodae a esika edi Kumu .
47005009	A mojɔ momina , bodukaka njea bo bomosepejae , isa a mokuku mu , isa oho .
47005010	Mojɔ bo , iso basusu bodi bo’ma a bohu a boso bomongbɛlɛngɔ moesambi eMasiya , bo moto na moto asɛ ndese ende a mojɔ mobopele , isa a mojɔ mobobe bokɔ yo a mokuku mu .
47005011	Iso bokengaka bojimeja bato , mojɔ bo bonjaka Kumu oko na bɔ . Iso bɛnɛ bodi a bohu a miso maNjambe . Nadi koko na njingo bo ekɔmɛli esu edi bohu a Inilema minu .
47005012	Botasalongejaka koko ai no . Bopaka no oko njea ebosepa a mojɔ mosu . Oko boa odini bosɔnibeja ai bato baya basakumejaka a mojɔ mongando jingasa , te ngando jisoti
47005013	Isa bodi na lilale , lidi a mojɔ moNjambe . Isa bodi na yongi epele , edi a mojɔ monu .
47005014	Bosusaka njea engɛnjɔ eMasiya ; mojɔ bo bojebaka na soti bo omɔci agwea bato basusu ; oko boa bato basusu bagwa .
47005015	Na yo agwea bato basusu bo mihelo mibato baya badi mɔ , mitaya da ai bo bɛnɛ , oko ai yona obagwea , yona ongɔ koko a bogwa a mojɔ mobu .
47005016	A mojɔ momina , iso botajeba koko moto a mokuku pɛ . Bojeba Masiya a mokuku boso ; edɛye ko botamojebaka koko boa .
47005017	Mojɔ bo , isa moto adi a tei eMasiya , adi moto moyene . Ngando jiyou jisia . Ngando jisusu jidi oko jiyene .
47005018	Mojɔ mu mosusu mocingi na Njambe yona ohuleja so ai yo mɛnɛ a tei eMasiya , na abopa elomu ebosiili .
47005019	Cina emina edi bo , Njambe yo mɛnɛ adaka a tei eMasiya mosiili ongondo ye ai yo mɛnɛ , pɛ bolanga jibe jibu o nongo , na abopa bwɛnji bobosiili .
47005020	Oko boa so bodi babwɛnji baMasiya . Njambe alehaka no na ebaeli esu , na so bongɔɔnɔkɔ no a kombe eMasiya bo ojimeni mokongo moNjambe .
47005021	Masiya aijeba nongo bobe ; Njambe ko amokɔ bo adae bobe a mojɔ mosu , bo so bodae bodongo boNjambe a tei ende .
47006001	Akɔkɔ so elomu na Njambe yo mɛnɛ , bongɔɔnɔkɔ no bo otasɔni monganji moNjambe esɔ’sɔ .
47006002	Mojɔ bo yo abalaka bo , Mbi nahokea wɛ a ehole yena ebwana ; Nakɔmeja wɛ a busa bobohela . Hokeani ! ehole yena ebwani edi oko edɛye . Busa bobohela bodi oko edɛye .
47006003	Iso bokɔkɔ bo botasakeja nongo moto libaku , bo elomu esu esaka samboa .
47006004	Adi so bakɔmɛli baNjambe , bokɔkɔ ngando jisusu bo bodae na esako epele . Bodi na lingbangba linɛnɛ a tei eminɔngɔ , na taka , na jɔɔlɔ ,
47006005	na nji , na blɔkɔ , na bigbomegbome , na bilomu , na taka ehiɔ , na nja ,
47006006	na ekɔmɛli epele , na ejebeli esoti , na eci , na monganji , na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke , na epaeli mɛnɛ ,
47006007	na ebaeli esoti , na ngulu eNjambe , na molilo mobila mobodongo a ebɔ ebami na a ebɔ ebali ,
47006008	na ekumu , na bosamboa , na bosakoa , na biloli . Adi so na mwako mosoti , babalaka bo bodi bato babokosea .
47006009	Bodi na esako epele , bato ko pɛ bojeba so . Bodi o bagwake , endele ko bodi oko mɔ ; asɔkɔ so nji , pɛ ko bogwa .
47006010	Adi so na molɔbɔ , bosepaka bihole bisusu . Adi so bɛnɛ bato babokwali , bohɛjɛkɛ likonja libato batongo . Bodi boangasa ; endele ko , leka losusu lodi oko ai so .
47006011	Bobalaka na nu BaKolinto na bohu mɛnɛ . Milema misu midi bwase ai no .
47006012	Odini na esika enɛnɛ a tei emilema misu ; milema minu bɛnɛ ko midi na sii .
47006013	Oko boa , bopele bo bosɔnibɔtɔne o ekɔmɛli ebɛngɛ ; hojani milema minu pongono .
47006014	T’okataneni oko na bato baya badi pɛ bojima Njambe , mojɔ bo bopele na bobe te bapandake nongo limbaci . Na bohu na modidi te bapandake limbaci .
47006015	Masiya na Beliala baditi na monɔkɔ momɔci ; na moto oejimeli , na moto yona opeliti ejimeli , baditi a libondo limɔci .
47006016	Tempelo eNjambe ebɔngiti nongo na bilimo . Iso bodi tempelo eNjambe obomɔ ; mojɔ bo Njambe abala bo , Mbi nâda a tei ebu , na nadala a tei ebu ; Nada Njambe obu , na bo bâda bato bambi .
47006017	A mojɔ momina , Kumu abalaka bo , Imanani a tei ebu ; sahɛngɛni ; Pɛ bobɛnjɛni nongo eka ebosɔtɔ , Na mbi nâsɔ no bopele .
47006018	Mbi nâda sangwa’nu ; Ino ôdani bana-bami bambi na bana-bali bambi . Kumu ongulu ebonɔ abalaka boa .
47007001	Baninga , adi so na sako jiji , bopele bo bosasɛnojae a mbindo jisusu jimokuku na jimwembo , na bo bosahɛnge ai Njambe na soti , oko na lisuma ai yo .
47007002	Pani so pokiso a tei emilema minu . Iso boikɔ nongo bobe ai moto . Boilaboja nongo moto . Boikɔ nongo moto poloso .
47007003	Nita-balaka boa a bodumba no . Odini a tei emilema misu , isa bokahela , Isa bokagwa , o ami mbi bala na nu boso .
