47007004	Mbi najimaka no na soti mɛnɛ . Nasakumejaka bou a mojɔ monu . Molema mombi mogɔmbi soti , na sepi embi epetoaka a tei eminɔngɔ misu .
47007005	Mojɔ bo , yana amea so a Makedonia , boinɛ nongo bowi ; bopukaka a bisika bisusu , mane a sokolu , na bɔ a tei .
47007006	Njambe ko , yona ogɔmbejaka baya badi na milema mititake , agɔmbeja so na bodoa boTito ,
47007007	te na bodoa bonde pɛ , oko a mojɔ mobogɔmbeja bosɔ yo ai no , yana atɔndɔ yo so mojɔ moposa enu enɛnɛ ai so , na wa enu , na bingi enu a mojɔ mombi . Sepi embi edaka enɛnɛ a mojɔ momina .
47007008	Isa nakeja no wa na mokanda mombi , naditi na dosa a mojɔ momina . Yana anɛ mbi bo odini na wa a mojɔ momokanda mombi — eiyeyoa ko — mbi nadaka na wa pongono .
47007009	Edɛye ko nasepaka , te a mojɔ mowa enu , oko cina bo wa emina ehekoja milema minu . Njambe ajima bo odaeni na wa , bo otadingoani na mojɔ mokɔ so .
47007010	Mojɔ bo , Njambe akakeja moto wa , wa emina esukeaka oko na bohekoja bomolema a mojɔ mobohela , te nongo na bio . Suka ko ewa engondo edi oko bogwa .
47007011	Anjani bingi yena edi na nu edɛye a mojɔ mowa ekeja Njambe no , na posa enu bo osalongejaeni , na kɛlɛ enu , na posa enu , na bingi enu , na bodingoa bonu . Onejaini bo oditini nongo na lindo .
47007012	Oko boa , isa mbi nasɔnea no mokanda , naisɔnɔ a mojɔ momoto yona okɔ bobe , isa a mojɔ momoto yona osɔ monɔngɔ momina ; nasɔnɔ bo epaeli enu enɛnɛ ai mbi eboloe ai no bɛnɛ a boso boNjambe .
47007013	Milema misu midi mihahanake a mojɔ momina . Te nongo bo milema misu pɛ midi mihahanake ; sepi esu ehɛ bou mɛnɛ a mojɔ mosepi eTito , mojɔ bo ohahanejani molema monde .
47007014	Isa mbi nasakoa no ai yo , naisamboa na nu ; o ami mbi bala na nu mijɔ misoti , mua mobala mbi na Tito a bosakoa no modaka soti pongono .
47007015	Epaeli emolema monde ai no edi enɛnɛ mɛnɛ , mojɔ bo atabosaka bo omosɔni na lisuma na mongongoma .
47007016	Mbi nadi na sepi , mojɔ bo naditi nongo na mokakwano a mojɔ monu .
47008001	Baninga , bodi bojebeja no edɛye mojɔ momonganji mokɔ Njambe O a Menga maMakedonia .
47008002	Bamekama na monɔngɔ monɛnɛ , na badaka na bokwali bonɛnɛ ; sepi ebu ko ehɛ oko hohɛ , na badaka na likabo linɛnɛ mɛnɛ .
47008003	Mbi natɔndɔkɔ na soti bo mwɛngi mobipeeli bibu mobwana na mwɛngi molikonja libu ; ee , likonja libu liibwana na mwɛngi mobipeeli bipa bo na milema mibu misusu .
47008004	Bangɔɔnɔ so na bopipo mɛnɛ bo bobapɛ njea ebokɔmeja bato baNjambe na bipeeli .
47008005	Na bakɔ boa , te nongo a njea edaka so na njingo ; basapa bo bɛnɛ boso ai Kumu o epeeli , na ngɔngɔ ai so , oko na bolulea boNjambe .
47008006	A mojɔ momina , so bobei Tito bo asiejae elomu ye emonganji a tei enu , o ama yo banga bokɔ .
47008007	Odini na bingi a ngando jisusu , na ejimeli , na bɛtɛ ebobala , na ejebeli , na lingbangba , na epaeli enu ai so ; oko boa toma dani na bingi a elomu ye emonganji pongono .
47008008	Nitadumbaka nongo mobeko . Nangɛkɛ oko epaeli enu na bingi ebato batongo , isa edi epaeli esoti .
47008009	Ojebakani monganji moKumu osu Yesu Masiya ; nongo adaka yo konji , akindoa moto obokwali a mojɔ monu , bo bokwali bonde bopɛ no makonja manɛnɛ .
47008010	Mbi nalehaka no oko boleha ; bopele bo osejaeni mojɔ mokana no yanga yena enɔ , mojɔ mobanga no bokɔ .
47008011	Kinani bingi enu ebokɔ mojɔ momina ebwane na posa yena edaka na nu ebokɔ , oko na mwɛngi molikonja linu .
47008012	Isa moto adi na posa ebopa epeeli , abwani bopa libondo lilikonja lipeli yo ; isa apeliti likonja abwaniti bopa .
47008013	Nitabalaka boa a bohɛjɛ muna monu , na bokamoa muna mobato batongo , oko a bobwaneja mojɔ mosusu .
47008014	Adi no na likonja linɛnɛ edɛye , obwanini bosieja taka ebu . Oko boa , likonja libu likahɛ , na ino okadani na taka , badi bokɔmeja no . Oko boa ôdani amɛci .
47008015	Mosɔnɔmɔ boa bo , Iyona ondoa leka lonɛnɛ aidika na eka ; Iyona ondoa oko mweka pɛ , aitaka .
47008016	Mbi nasakoaka Njambe mojɔ bo yo alumeja molema moTito na bolɛ ai no , o adi mbi mɛnɛ .
47008017	Ajimi mojɔ mongɔɔni mbi yo ; yo mɛnɛ ko adaka na posa bo akɛe oho ai no , na adi bodoa na bingi enɛnɛ .
47008018	Bolomaka na nde , mwangwa’su yona odi na esakoli epele a Menga masusu a mojɔ moetɔndɛli ende eMwako Mopele .
47008019	Mojɔ motongo koko — Menga mamohɔ bo adale na mbi a elomu ye emonganji , yena ekɔkɔ so na bingi enɛnɛ a bokumeja Kumu .
47008020	Bokɔkɔ boa , bo moto asaka da na mokakwano a mojɔ molikonja linɛnɛ lia lidi na su a bokaba .
47008021	Bomekaka bo ngando jikɔkɔ so jibɔnge , te a miso maKumu pɛ , oko a miso mabato pongono .
47008022	Bomeka bingi emwangwa’su bou mɛnɛ bihole binɛnɛ ; na bingi ende ehɛi oko bohɛ cina eepaeli ende ai no . A mojɔ momina bomo-lomaka na bu batongo .
47008023	A mojɔ moTito — yo adi mopakali ombi , na acingami na mbi a elomu enu ; a mojɔ mobaninga basu , badi babwɛnji baMenga , badi ekumu eMasiya .
47008024	Oko boa nejani bato bamina epaeli enu , bo Menga manɛe epaeli emina pongono ; nejani bo so botasakoaka no ngasa .
47009001	Ebɔngiti bo nasɔnee no mokanda a mojɔ mobipeeli ai bato baMasiya ,
47009002	mojɔ bo najebaka bingi enu . Nasakoaka no ai bato baMakedonia a mojɔ momina . Nabatɔndɔkɔ bo mosɛlingo moAkaya mobwana yanga yena enɔ ; na bingi enu esisoja bato babu banɛnɛ .
47009003	Nalomaka baninga ko bo onejaeni bo mbi naisakoa no ngasa , na bo odaeni na mosɛlingo o ami mbi bala .
47009004	Bato baMakedonia bakadoa na mbi , na bakatana no pɛpɛ nongo mosɛlingo , so bodi bosamboa cina eejimeli esu ai no , na no bɛnɛ pongono .
47009005	A mojɔ momina , mbi nalɛi bo nabwani bosueja baninga boso ai no . Oko boa badi bokolea bipeeli bidikeja no , Obwanini bopa bipeeli bimina na likabo mɛnɛ , te nongo na ekɔmɛli etako .
47009006	Pɛ bobosani mojɔ mumu ; moto aka’na dona na lima , atabuka ndongo jinɛnɛ , na moto yona onaka dona na likabo , adi bobuka ndongo jinɛnɛ .
47009007	Moto abwani bopa epeeli ekani yo a molema monde , te nongo na misuba , isa na lima , mojɔ bo Njambe apalaka bo moto apɛ epeeli ende na sepi .
47009008	Na Njambe abwani bojongoa no na majongoa manɛnɛ mɛnɛ , bo otatakani nongo eka , na bo odaeni na libondo linɛnɛ a mojɔ mobilomu bisusu bipele .
47009009	Mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Akabi na monganji ; api bipeeli ai babokwali . Bodongo bonde bodi boyeyoa oko na bosusu .
47009010	Iyo , yona opaka moswa ’ gbie ngua a bona , na molɛmbɛ a boyaka , adi bopa no ngua na likabo linɛnɛ mɛnɛ ; na adi bohɛjɛ mbuma jinu jibodongo .
47009011	Oko boa , ôjongoamani na majongoa masusu bo odaeni na likabo linɛnɛ ai bato batongo , na so bokapa bipeeli bimina ai bato batongo , badi bosakoa Njambe a mojɔ momina .
47009012	Mojɔ bo , suka eelomu ye ebokɔmeja editi a bokɔmeja baMasiya a taka ebu pɛ ; ekɔkɔ bo bato banɛnɛ basakoaka Njambe bou mɛnɛ .
47009013	Baku-mejaka Njambe a mojɔ mohsuma linu , na ejimeli enu , a Mwako Mopele moMasiya , na monganji mobipeeli binu ai bo bɛnɛ na ai bato basusu , yana anɛkɛ bo elomu ye ebokɔmeja .
47009014	Bangaka Njambe a mojɔ monu , na badi na bolɛ ai no bou mɛnɛ , a mojɔ momonganji monɛnɛ mokɔ Njambe no .
47009015	Yɛni bosakoe Njambe a mojɔ moepeeli ende yena enɔi kɔpi emoto .
47010001	Mbi Paulo , nakada a tei enu , nadi o moto-ngasa , bohali ko ko nadi na bogale ; mbi nangɔɔnɔkɔ no na bowi na boyɛmbu boMasiya .
47010002	Nangaka no bo nakadoa oho ai no , otalindani mbi a bobala na bopipo , o akanaka mbi bobala na bakina bato baya balɛkɛ bo ekɔmɛli esu edi oko ekɔmɛli ebato bangondo .
47010003	Bodi a ngondo soti ; bila enaka so ko editi bila engondo .
47010004	Mojɔ bo molilo mosu mobila moditi molilo mongondo ; molilo momina ko modi na ngulu eNjambe a bogbokeja bisika bipipo bisoki .
47010005	Bobejaka ndungu jibato , na egbo yena esakumejaka a bolona ejebeli eNjambe , na bopeaka malɛ masusu masungu , bo madae na lisuma ai Masiya .
47010006	Na lisuma linu likabwana , bodi na mosɛlingo bo bodingojae lipanga lisusu .
47010007	Ino onjakani oko boso bomoto pɛ ? Isa okina moto ajimaka bo adi moto oMasiya , abwamti bobosa bo so bodi koko bato baMasiya , o adi yo mɛnɛ .
47010008	Nongo nakasakumeja bou mɛnɛ a mojɔ mokpaci esɔ mbi ai Kumu , nadi bolonga , mojɔ bo apani kpaci emina a bopingeja no , te a bodumba no .
47010009	Nitapalaka bo bato balɛe bo nangbengbejaka no na mikanda mimbi .
47010010	Bakina babalaka bo , Mikanda minde midi mipipo , na midi na kpaci ; yo mɛnɛ ko akada a tei esu , adi oko na boyɛmbu , na etɔndɛli ende edi ngasa mɛnɛ .
47010011	Bato baya babalaka boa babwani bocingea bo bikenge bisu a mikanda yana adi so bohali , na bikɔmɛli bisu a tei enu bidi oko amɛci .
47010012	Iso botapalaka bo bosa’ngɛe na bo bosabwanejae na bato baya basakumejaka bo bɛnɛ . Ibo basa’ngɛkɛ na mwɛngi mobu bɛnɛ ; moto na moto anjaka okina otongo bo asa’ngɛe na nde ; bapeliti bocingea .
47010013	Iso ko botasakumeja bou ; bodi bosakumeja oko na mwɛngi mopa Njambe so , na mwɛngi momina momeaka ai no .
47010014	Iso botanɔkɔ mwei mosu ; elomu esu editi ai no ? Omea boso ai no na Mwako Mopele moMasiya nda ? te so ?
47010015	Botasakumejaka ngasa ; bota-sakumejaka a mojɔ mobilomu bibato batongo ; na ejimeli enu ekahɛ , njingo esu edi bo mwei moelomu esu a tei enu modi bokɛ bohali mɛnɛ ,
47010016	bo botɔndɔe Mwako Mopele a makota maya manɔi no , pɛ bosakumeja nongo na elomu ekɔ moto otongo a esika etongo .
47010017	Moto akapala bo asakumejae , yɛ akumejae oko Kumu .
47010018	Mojɔ bo , Kumu akalongeja moto , moto omina adi molongi , te moto yona osalongejaka yo mɛnɛ .
47011001	Nitapalaka bo ongwaeni bogegele bombi bokba ; dani na lingbangba a mojɔ mombi .
47011002	Nadi na likaka a mojɔ monu , na likaka limina lihuli ai Njambe , mojɔ bo mbi nahanga no moki o moseka mosɛnɔke ai muma’nde omɔci , bo napɛ no ai Masiya .
47011003	Njɔ ko akosea Ewa na poloso ende ; na mbi nadi na mokakwano bo milema minu misaka beha boa pongono , na osaka kinani lisuma linu lisɛnɔke ai Masiya .
47011004	Mojɔ bo okina moto akadoa a botɔndɔ mojɔ moYesu otongo , — te yona otɔndɔkɔ so — osɔkɔni moto omina ; na osɔkɔni mwembo motongo — te nongo mwembo mosɔ no ; na ojimakani mokina mwako motongo — te nongo Mwako Mopele mosɔ no .
47011005	Mbi nalɛkɛ bo naditi nongo ngɔngɔ jibabwɛnji bamina bagala .
47011006	Isa napeliti bɛtɛ ebobala , nadi na ejebeli ; naneja no mojɔ momina bohu mɛnɛ a ngando jisusu .
47011007	Mbi natɔndɔ no Mwako Mopele moNjambe , pɛ ko bosɔ nongo likonja a mojɔ momina ; yana asatiteja mbi boa a bokumeja no , nakɔ mojɔ mobe ?
47011008	Menga matongo madika ngasa mojɔ bo nasɔ likonja ai bo , bo nabwane bokɔmɛ no ngasa .
47011009	Adaka mbi na taka a tei enu nainɔngeja moto bo akɔmejae mbi , mojɔ bo baninga baya badonga oho Makedonia bakɔmejani na leka lotakaka na mbi . Mbi nakɔ bo nitada nongo muna ai no , na nadi bokɔ boa .
47011010	Natɔndɔkɔ no na soti eMasiya mɛnɛ yena edi a tei embi , bo mtakma bosakumeja na mojɔ momina a makota masusu maAkaya .
47011011	Mojɔ moye ? Naditi na epaeli ai no ? Njambe ajebaka bo nadi na epaeli ai no .
47011012	Mbi ko nadi bokɔ o akɔkɔ mbi edɛye , bo nagegeanejae bato baya basakumejaka bo babwani na su .
47011013	Bato bamina badi babwɛnji babokosea , bakɔmɛli baepulu ; badi oko na elwaeli pɛ ebabwɛnji baMasiya .
47011014	Iso boditi na bokamoa a mojɔ momina , cina bo Satana yo mɛnɛ adi na elwaeli eobwɛnji obohu .
47011015	Oko boa , bakɔmɛli bande bakakosea bo badi bakɔmɛli babodongo , bobwaniti bokamoa . Suka ebu êbwana na bikɔmɛli bibu .
47011016	Natɔndɔkɔ no koko bo pɛpɛ nongo moto onu obwani bolɛ bo mbi nadi egegele . Okalɛni ko bo nadi egegele , asɔni mbi o egegele , bo mbi nasakumejae pongono .
47011017	Abalaka mbi boa , nitabalaka na ebaeli eKumu ; nabalaka oko na bogegele , cina eejimeli embi bo nabwani bosakumeja .
47011018	Bato banɛnɛ basakumejaka na ngando jingondo ; oko boa mbi koko nadi bosakumeja .
47011019	Adi no bato babowɛi no bɛnɛ , otangwani bigegele .
47011020	Moto akapika no babuli , akayaka leka lonu losusu , akasamboja no , akada na egbo , akaboma maso manu , otalonani moto omina .
47011021	Nadi na sɔni a bobala na nu bo mbi naihɔnɔ bokɔ boa . Pɛ mojɔ ; isa bato bamina basakumejaka , mbi nadi bosakumeja pongono . ( Nabalaka o egegele ! )
47011022	Isa bo badi BeEbele , mbi nadi MoEbele pongono , isa bo badi BaYisalaele , mbi nadi MoYisalaele pongono ; isa bo badi bana baAbalayama , mbi nadi mwana oAbalayama pongono .
47011023	Isa bo badi bakɔmɛli baMasiya , esingaiti mbi . ( Nabalaka o moto olilale . ) Mbi nakɔ bilomu bmɛnɛ ; nakwea a blɔkɔ bihole binɛnɛ ; batuani nji pɛ njɛngi ; napa njupi bihole binɛnɛ ;
47011024	BaYuda batua mbi nji bihole bitano , nji domi-isato na libwa , nji domi-isato na libwa .
47011025	Batuani na miba-kake bihole bisato . Ba’la mbi matai ehole emɔci . Nasopea na masua bihole bisato . Nadaka dusu limɔci a madiba-mamukwa oko a boliko .
47011026	Nakɛ mɛngɔ minɛnɛ . Napa njupi a dua , napa koko njupi a mojɔ momibengo ; napa njupi a mojɔ mobato bahkota limbi mɛnɛ , na a mojɔ mobapakano pongono ; napa njupi a ngando , na njupi a lisobe ; napa njupi a madiba-mamukwa , na njupi a mojɔ mobaninga babokosea .
47011027	Nadaka na bilomu na minɔngɔ bou mɛnɛ , pɛ bohwɛ na bulu , oko na nja , na ekangola bou mɛnɛ , na bikia bihole binɛnɛ , na pio na mbundu pongono .
47011028	Te nongo ngando jimina pɛ ; nadi na muna a molema mombi tu busa a mojɔ moMenga masusu .
47011029	Okina akapeka , mbi napekaka pongono . Okina akakwa , molema mombi mongoaka oko bongoa .
47011030	Isa nadi bosakumeja , nasakumeja oko a mojɔ mongando jia jinejaka boyɛmbu bombi .
47011031	Njambe , Sange ’ Kumu Yesu yona odi na bojongoa oko na bosusu , ajebaka bo nitakosaka .
47011032	Adaka mbi oho Damaseke , gouverneur ongando , mokɔmɛli oAleta yona odaka kumu , adukeja mbi a ngando esusu eDamaseke bo apee mbi .
47011033	Mbi ko nahela a mɔmɔ mande ; banɔjɔ mbi a linanisa na basoloja mbi a mongba mongando a tei eekɔlɔ .
47012001	Moto abwaniti bosakumeja ; mbi ko nadi bosakumeja ; nadi bobala a mojɔ monjɔti na maboloja maKumu .
47012002	Mbi naje-baka moto a tei eMasiya yona otombama oho a Diko yena enɔi , bianga bisii edɛye domi-na-binɛi . ( Isa a mokuku , isa amana a mokuku , nitajeba ; Njambe pɛ ajebaka . )
47012003	Najebaka bo moto omina atombama a Paladiso . ( Isa a mokuku , isa amana a mokuku mtajeba ; Njambe pɛ ajebaka . )
47012004	Na aka mijɔ mibombamake Inia mibɔngiti na moto bobala .
47012005	Mbi nadi bosakumeja a mojɔ momoto omina ; a mojɔ mombi mɛnɛ ko , nadi bosakumeja oko a mojɔ moboyɛmbu bombi pɛ .
47012006	Akɔki mbi pala bo nasakumejae , ka nitada nongo egegele , mojɔ bo nabwani bobala oko ngando jisoti . Nadi bokina mojɔ momina ko ; mojɔ bo mtapalaka bo bato balɛe bo nadi ekina elimo etongo , oko moto onɛkɛ bo na miso , na gala ekaka bo na matoi .
47012007	Mbi mɛnɛ nasɔ njubɛ a mokuku , bo nasaka huula na egbo a mojɔ momaboloja maNjambe manɛnɛ , oko obwɛnji oSatana a bopukeja mbi , bo nasaka da na egbo .
47012008	Nangɔɔnɔ Kumu bihole bisato bo aedongejae .
47012009	Iyo ko abala na mbi bo , Monganji mombi mobwani na wɛ , mojɔ bo ngulu embi edi boboloa na soti oko a tei eboyɛmbu . A mojɔ momina , nadi bosakumeja na sepi mɛnɛ a mojɔ moboyɛmbu bombi , bo ngulu eMasiya edae ai mbi .
47012010	Oko boa , nasepaka na boyɛmbu , na biloli , na minɔngɔ , na madingoa , na jɔɔlɔ , a mojɔ moMasiya . Mojɔ bo , ehole edi mbi na bwɛmbu , ehole edi mbi na ngulu oko yena .
47012011	Adi mbi na ebalabala ? Ino bɛnɛ olindini mbi , no baya babwani bojima mbi . Mojɔ bo , nongo adi mbi moto-ngasa , naditi nongo ngɔngɔ jibabwɛnji bagala , pɛpɛ nongo mweka .
47012012	Bimbete , na mindumba , na bilomu bipipo , bingameja elomu embi eobwɛnji a tei enu na lingbangba linɛnɛ .
47012013	Ngando jikɔ mbi a Menga matongo , naikɔ a tei enu pongono ? Mojɔ mu momɔci ko modi ; naidaka muna ai no . Yɛni mbi mojɔ mu mobe !
47012014	Hokeani ; nadi na mosɛlingo mobodoa ai no — ehole ebisato ye ; na nitada nongo muna ai no . Mbi mtapalaka leka lonu , napalaka oko no bɛnɛ . Bana te babɔkɔke baboti ; baboti ko babɔkɔkɔ bana babu .
47012015	Mbi nadi bopa leka lombi losusu na sepi , na nadi bosapa mbi mɛnɛ pongono a mojɔ momiembo minu . Epaeli enu ai mbi ekatita , pɛ mojɔ ; epaeli embi ai no ehɛkɛ oko bohɛ .
47012016	Nongo okajimani bo naidaka muna ai no , obalakani bo nadi na epulu , na nakɔ mokina mojɔ mopoloso ai no .
47012017	Yana aloma mbi bato ai no , nasɔ ekina eka enu ai bato bamina ?
47012018	Na’nga Tito bo akɛe , na naloma moninga otongo bo amopakae . Tito akonja likonja linu ? Iso boidaka na ekɔmɛli emina pongono ? Ekɔmɛli esu na nde te emɔci ?
47012019	Olɛkɛni ekoka ye bo so bosalongejaka ai no ? Ngando jisusu jibalaka so baninga jidi a bopingeja no ; na bojibalaka a boso boNjambe na a tei eMasiya .
47012020	Mokakwano mombi modi bo , nakamea oho ai no , nitatana no o adi mbi na njingo ; na bo mbi mɛnɛ nitada o alɛkɛ no . Isa nadi botana no na miano , na kɛnjɔ , na likaka , na misoo , na biloli , na egbo na wokowoko ?
47012021	Nadi na mokakwano isa Njambe adi bokeja mbi sɔni a boso bonu a bodoa bombi ; isa nadi boyea bio a mojɔ mobato banɛnɛ baya bakɔ bobe boso , na bajasakini dosa a mojɔ mobikɔmɛli bibu bibosɔtɔ , na bɔɔli , na bosambolu .
47013001	Ehole ye edi ehole ebisato ebodoa bombi ai no . Bolena bomojɔ bobwani na batati babae isa basato .
47013002	Mbi naleha bato baya bakɔ bobe boso , na basusu batongo pongono ; na nabale-haka koko edɛye , o akɔ mbi yana adaka mbi na nu ehole ebibae , bo mbi nakadoa , nitadoa nongo na bwɛmbu .
47013003	Odukakani embete bo Masiya abalaka a tei embi . Iyo aditi na boyɛmbu ai no ; adi na ngulu a tei enu .
47013004	Iyo agwa a mole-mobokea oko na boyɛmbu ; adi mɔ ko a mojɔ mongulu eNjambe . Iso pongono bodi bayɛmbu a tei ende ; endele ko , bodi na bomɔ bonde a mojɔ mongulu eNjambe bo bokɔe elomu a tei enu .
47013005	Sakokelejani no bɛnɛ , a bojeba isa odini na ejimeli soti . Samekani no bɛnɛ . Otajebakani bo Yesu Masiya adi a tei enu ? Emiti da boa , odini oko badaloi .
47013006	Nadi na njingo bo odini bojeba bo iso boditi badaloi .
47013007	Bongaka Njambe bo otakɔni nongo bobe , te a bolongeja so , oko bo okɔeni bopele pɛ , nongo adi so badaloi .
47013008	Mojɔ bo bobwaniti boda na Soti soki ; bodi oko a dɔngɔ diSoti .
47013009	Iso bosepaka yana adi so na bwɛmbu , isa ino odini na bopipo . Bongaka bo obɔngeni na soti .
47013010	Nasɔnɔkɔ mijɔ mi yana adi mbi bohali , bo nitabala na nu na bopipo a bodoa bombi na kpaci esɔ mbi ai Kumu a bopingeja bato , te a bodumba bato .
47013011	Mojɔ mosuka baninga , — asɔni njɛbɛ embi . Bɔngejani midi minu . Hokeani eleho embi . Dani na molema momɔci . Dani na bowi , na Njambe obowi lida na nu .
47013012	Abɛjɛnɛni na njɛbɛ esɛnɔke .
47013013	Bato basusu baDenga babɛjɛkɛ no .
47013014	Yɛ monganji moKumu Yesu Masiya , na epaeli eNjambe , na bokatana boMwembo Mosɛnɔke bodae na nu basusu .
48001001	Njɛbɛ esu Paulo obwɛnji na baninga basusu baya badi na mbi , a Menga maGalatia .
48001002	( Mbi naditi obwɛnji obato ; naditi na kpaci emoto , oko kpaci eYesu Masiya , na eNjambe Sango yona omongɔjɔ a bogwa . )
48001003	Yɛ monganji na bowi boNjambe Sango , na boKumu osu Yesu Masiya bodae ai no .
48001004	Iyo asapa a mojɔ mojibe jisu bo asikoe so a ngondo ye ebe , o akana Njambe Sangwa’su .
48001005	Yɛ ekumu edae ai yo oko na bosusu . Amen .
48001006	Mbi nakamoaka bo oiyeyoani nongo a bobulɛ yona obea no a monganji moMasiya , na ohekoani a mokina mwako motongo
48001007	Mokina Mwako Mopele motongo moditi ; bakina bato ko banɔngejaka no , na bapalaka botatana Mwako Mopele moMasiya .
48001008	Moto akatɔndɔ no mokina mwako motongo mua moditi Mwako Mopele motɔndɔ so no , isa mbi mɛnɛ , isa okina obwɛnji oDiko , yɛ moto omina asingame .
48001009	Mbi natɔndɔ no eyou , na natɔndɔkɔ no koko e dɛye , bo moto akatɔndɔ no mokina mwako motongo mua moditi Mwako Mopele mosɔ no , yɛ asingame .
48001010	Edukaka mbi e dɛye nde ? — gala epele a miso mabato , isa a miso maNjambe ? Mbi napalaka bo nasepejae bato soti ? Akɔki mbi pala bosepeja bato pɛ , ka naditi nongo mokɔmɛli oMasiya .
48001011	Baninga , mbi natɔndɔkɔ no bo Mwako Mopele motɔndɔkɔ mbi moditi mojɔ momoto .
48001012	Naimosɔ ai moto , na moto aikojani Mwako Mopele ; edi oko Yesu Masiya yona omoboloja ai mbi .
48001013	Ino ojebakani moda mombi moyou yana adaka mbi na ejimeli eBaYuda ; ojebakani bo nadingoja na nabeja Denga diNjambe .
48001014	Nanɔ kola jilikota limbi jinɛnɛ na ejebeli engando jiBaYuda , na nadaka na bingi enɛnɛ mɛnɛ a mojɔ mongando jibatata .
48001015	Njambe ko , yona ohɛngɛ mhi oko a bobotama bombi , abea mbi na monganji monde ,
48001016	na ajima bo abolojae Mwana’nde ai mbi , bo natɔndɔe Mwako monde ai bapakano . A ehole emina , naibala nongo na moto a mojɔ momina .
48001017	Naikɛ nongo a Yelusalema a bo’nɛnɛ na bato baya badaka babwɛnji boso bombi . Nakɛ oko a Alabia , na nahula ngɔngɔ a Damaseke .
48001018	Yana anɔ bianga bisato , nakɛ a Yelusalema a bo’nɛnɛ na Pɛtɛlo , na nayeyoa na nde masu domi-na-matano .
48001019	Nainɛ babwɛnji batongo ; nanɛ oko Yakobo pɛ , mwanange ’ Kumu .
48001020	Mijɔ misɔneaka mbi no midi soti mɛnɛ — oko Njambe !
48001021	Nakɛ ngɔngɔ a makota maSilia na Kilikia .
48001022	A ehole emina , baipaka nɛ boso bombi a Menga maMasiya oho Yuda .
48001023	Bama ka oko boka pɛ bo , Yona onɔngeja so boso , atɔndɔkɔ e dɛye mwako moejimeli emeka yo bobeja .
48001024	Na basakoa Njambe a mojɔ mombi .
48002001	Yana anɔ koko bianga domi-na-binɛi , nasɔmbɔ koko na Balanaba a Yelusalema . Nabea Tito pongono bo apakae mbi .
48002002	Mbi nakɛ mojɔ bo Njambe aboloja mokina mojɔ ai mbi , na nabalakea Mwako Mopele motɔndɔkɔ mbi a tei ebapakano . Nakɔ boa oko na basuku bakpaci pɛ , te na bato batongo , bo najebe isa njea ema mbi susa na yena esusaka mbi e dɛye ebɔngi .
48002003	Tito , yona odaka na mbi , adaka MoEla ; ibo ko baibekea bo bamolene ganda .
48002004	Bakina baninga babokosea ko bakwea kɛngi a tei esu na poloso , bo bakoke-lejae bosɔmi bosu bua bodi na su a tei eMasiya Yesu , a bohuleja so a libuli .
48002005	Iso ko boibabokea , pɛpɛ nongo mweka , bo Mwako Mopele moSoti moyeyoe na nu .
48002006	Na baya badaka na kpaci ( Gala ebu editi eka a miso mambi ; Njambe anjaka bato basusu amɛci , ) baibakea nongo mokina mojɔ a mwako mombi .
48002007	Endele ko , yana acinea ’ bo bo mbi nasɔ Mwako Mopele a mojɔ mobapakano , o ama sɔ Pɛtɛlo a mojɔ mobato baejimeli eBaYuda ,
48002008	( Mojɔ bo , yona ohɔ Pɛtɛlo bo adae obwɛnji ai bato baejimeli eBaYuda , ahɔ koko mbi bo nadae obwɛnji ai bapakano , )
48002009	na yana anɛ bo monganji moNjambe mosɔ mbi , Yakobo na Pɛtɛlo na Yoane , baya badaka makwe maDenga , bapa so na Balanaba ebɔ ebami ebocinama , bo so bokɛe oko ai bapakano , na bo bɛnɛ ai BaYuda .
48002010	Balɛjɛ so oko mojɔ momɔci , bo botabosa bato babokwali , na mbi nadaka na bingi a mojɔ momina .
48002011	Yana ko adoa Pɛtɛlo a Antiokia , mbi nalemoa na nde na bopipo mɛnɛ ; mojɔ bo adaka na lindo .
48002012	Yakobo aloma bakina bato oho , na yana adaka bo pɛ bopeta mea , Pɛtɛlo ayakaka na bapakano . Yana ko amea bato bamina , asahɛngɛ , na abɔtɔnɔ na bapakano , mojɔ bo abangaka BaYuda .
48002013	Bakina BaYuda batongo bakɔ na poloso boa , na Balanaba yo mɛnɛ ajima ekɔmɛli ebu .
48002014	Mbi ko , yana anɛ mbi bo batasusaka njea esoti eMwako Mopele , nabala na Pɛtɛlo yana adaka bo basusu baboli ; nabala bo , Isa wɛ MoYuda okɔkɔ o akɔkɔ bapakano , te nongo ekɔmɛli eBaYuda , omekaka na bopipo a bohekoja bapakano a ekɔmɛli eBaYuda mojɔ moye ?
48002015	Nongo adi so BaYuda a mojɔ mobobotama bosu , te bapakano babe ,
48002016	bojebaka bo moto adi bolonga oko a mojɔ moejimeli ai Yesu Masiya pɛ , te nongo a mojɔ mobilomu biMibeko ; mojɔ bo so bɛnɛ bojimea Masiya Yesu bo bolonge a mojɔ moejimeli ai Masiya , te nongo a bilomu biMibeko ; cina bo pɛpɛ nongo moto odi bolonga a mojɔ mobilomu biMibeko .
48002017	Endele ko , isa bonɛ bo so pongono bodi bato babe yana adukaka so lilonga atei eMasiya , bobe bomina bocingi na Masiya ? pɛpɛ nongo mweka !
48002018	Naka-ngɔjɔ ngando jidumba mbi , najimaka bo nadi moto mobe .
48002019	Mojɔ bo mbi nagwa a Mibeko oko cina eMibeko , bo nahele ai Njambe .
48002020	Mbi nagwa na Masiya a mole-mo-bokea ; endele ko nadi mɔ , te mbi mɛnɛ ko , oko Masiya yona odi mɔ a tei embi . Bomɔ bua bodi na mbi a mokuku e dɛye bodi bomɔ boejimeli , ejimeli ai Mwana oNjambe yona opala mbi na osapa a mojɔ mombi .
48002021	Mbi nitalona monganji moNjambe , cina bo , isa lilonga licingi na Mibeko , bogwa boMasiya boditi nongo na cina .
48003001	Ino BaGalatia , ino bindanga . Oseli no nda ? ino baya banɛ na miso manu Yesu Masiya a mole-mobokea , bohu mɛnɛ .
48003002	Mbi napalaka bohɔjɔ no mojɔ momɔci pɛ . Osɔni Mwembo cina ebilomu biMibeko , isa cina eejimeli a Mwako Mopele ?
48003003	Adi no bindanga soti ? Abanga no na Mwembo , opalakani bosukeja oko na ngando jimini ?
48003004	Minɔngɔ minɛ no midaka oko ngasa ? Isa midaka ngasa soti ?
48003005	Iyona opaka no Mwembo na okɔkɔ mindumba a tei enu , akɔkɔ boa cina ebilomu biMibeko , isa a mojɔ moejimeli eMwako Mopele ?
48003006	Abalayama ajima Njambe , na ejimeli emina elangama ai yo o bodongo .
48003007	Oko boa toma jebani bo baya badi na ejimeli , badi bana baAbalayama .
48003008	Mosɔnɔ moneja eyou bo Njambe adi bolongeja bapakano a mojɔ moejimeli , na mojebeja Abalayama Mwako Mopele na ebaeli ye , Makota masusu mangondo mâjongoama oko na wɛ .
48003009	Oko boa , baya badi bato baejimeli bajongoamaka na Abalayama , moto oejimeli .
48003010	Bato basusu baya bajimaka oko bilomu biMibeko badi cina jinakeja . Mojɔ bo mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Moto amiti suma ngando jisusu jia jisɔnɔmɔ a mokanda moMibeko adi cina jinakeja .
48003011	Pɛpɛ nongo moto odi bolonga a boso boNjambe cina eMibeko ; mojɔ momina modi bohu mɛnɛ . Mojɔ bo yona odi na bodongo a cina eejimeli , yo âhela .
48003012	Mibeko ko micingiti na ejimeli , mojɔ bo yona okɔkɔ ngando jimina adi boda a tei engando jimina .
48003013	Masiya asikoa so a esinga eMibeko , mojɔ bo yo mɛnɛ adaka esinga a mojɔ mosu . Mojɔ bo mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Moto na moto yona ogwaka a mole alakejami .
48003014	Modaka boa bo bojongoa boAbalayama bodae ai bapakano oko na Masiya Yesu , na bo so bosɛ Mwembo mua modikejama oko a cina eejimeli .
48003015	Baninga , yɛ nabale na mondɛ mobato . Moto akadikaneja leka na mokanda , nongo mokada mokanda momoto pɛ , na bato bakajima mokanda momina , okina otongo atahakoa mokanda momina , ata-bakea mokina mojɔ motongo a mokanda momina .
48003016	Oko boa , njikano jidaka ai Abalayama na ai mbota ende . Aibala bo , Ai mbota jiwɛ , o mbota jinɛnɛ ; oko , Ai Mbota ewɛ , mbota ewɛ emɔci , oko Masiya .
48003017	Cina emojɔ mobalaka mbi edi oko ye ; Njambe abakea mokongo . Mibeko ko mia midoa ngɔngɔ , yana anɔ bianga mikama minɛi na domi-isato , miikputoja mokongo momina , miidongeja nongo njikano .
48003018	Mojɔ bo , isa lisango lidi a njea eMibeko , liditi a njea enjikano . Njambe ko alidikaneja ai Abalayama oko na njikano .
48003019	Oko boa , mojɔ moMibeko modi bo ? Mibeko Mibakeama a mojɔ mojibe , oko a ehole ebodoa bomwana omina , mwana onjikano ; na babwɛnji-aDiko bapeja Mibeko a mɔmɔ mamosiili .
48003020	Mosiili aditi a mojɔ momoto omɔci pɛ ; Njambe ko adi omɔci .
48003021	Ekada boa , Mibeko mikɛsɛni na njikano jiNjambe ? pɛpɛ nongo mweka ! Mojɔ bo , Njambe , akɔkɔ yo pa Mibeko mia Mibwani bopa bomɔ , ka bodongo bocingi oko na Mibeko .
48003022	Misɔnɔ ko minejaka bo bato basusu badi cina ebobe , bo baya bajimaka basɛ njikano , oko na ejimeli ai Yesu Masiya .
48003023	Boso-boso , yana adaka ejimeli emina pɛ bopeta doa , Mibeko mihika so a bobanea so , oko a ehole ehoboloa boejimeli ngɔngɔ .
48003024	Oko boa , Mibeko midaka o moto yona opea so ebɔ a boneja so njea ai Masiya , bo bolonge a mojɔ moejimeli .
48003025	Adi so ko na ejimɛli e dɛye , boditi koko a mɔmɔ mamolɔndi .
48003026	Mojɔ bo odini no basusu bana baNjambe a mojɔ moejimeli ai Yesu Masiya .
48003027	Ino basusu baya babatisama ai Masiya , balwa Masiya oko bolwa .
48003028	A tei ende , moto aditi MoYuda isa MoEla , isa mobuli isa sɔmi , isa momi isa mwali , mojɔ bo odini no basusu moto omɔci a tei eMasiya Yesu .
48003029	Isa odini bato baMasiya , odini bana baAbalayama , na basangoli banjikano .
48004001	Mojɔ mobalaka mbi modi bo , Isa sangoli adi yɛngɛ , nongo akada moswa ’ ngando , adi o mobuli .
48004002	Adi a mɔmɔ mabakoja na babanei oko a ehole ejimaka sangwa’nde .
48004003	Iso bodi koko boa . Amaka so da bɛngɛ , bomi daka oko a iibuli lingando jingondo ye .
48004004	Yana ko abwana ehole , Njambe aloma Mwana’nde yona obotama na mwali , yona obotama cina jiMibeko ,
48004005	a bosikoa baya badaka cina jiMibeko , bo bosɛ bosɔmi bosu bobana .
48004006	Na adi no bana bande , Njambe aloma Mwembo moMwana’nde a tei emilema misu , na Mwembo mosembaka bo , Aba ! Sesa !
48004007	Oko boa oditi koko mobuli , odi mwana mɛnɛ . Na adi wɛ mwana , odi sangoli , cina emonganji moNjambe .
48004008	Boso-boso , oijebakani nongo Njambe ; odakani babuli baba-njambe baya baditi banjambe na soti .
48004009	E dɛye ko ojebakani Njambe , — gbo oko Njambe yona ojebaka no ; oko boa osɔmbɔkɔni koko a ngando jingasangasa jia jipehti nongo ngulu , na opalakani bo odaeni koko a libuli lingando jimina mojɔ moye ?
48004010	Bolɛ bonu bodi oko a masu , na songe , na bididi , na bianga .
48004011	Mbi nadi na mokakwano isa elomu embi a tei enu enami oko bonama .
48004012	Baninga , mbi nangaka no bo odaeni na mbi o adaka mbi na nu . Mbi naditi na nu nongo mojɔ .
48004013	Ojebakani bo natɔndɔ no Mwako Mopele ehole eboso oko na yogo a mokuku .
48004014	Na osɔni mbi o obwɛnji oNjambe , o Yesu Masiya yo mɛnɛ . Oilonani mbi ; oisɛtojani mbi nongo adaka no na jeti a mojɔ momokuku mombi .
48004015	Monganji mua modaka na nu a ehole emina modi jɔ ? Mojɔ bo , mbi natɔndɔkɔ no bo , Akɔkɔ no hɔnɔ , ka ohwani miso manu a hopa mbi .
48004016	E dɛye ko odini nambi soki , mojɔ bo natɔndɔkɔ no mua modi soti ?
48004017	Ibo batongo badi na bingi enɛnɛ a mojɔ monu ; editi ko bingi esoti . Bapalaka bo babɔtejae no na su , bo odaeni na bingi a mojɔ mobu .
48004018	Isa odini na bingi a mojɔ mongando jipele , obwanini boda na bingi emina bihole bisusu , te yana adi mbi na nu pɛ .
48004019	Bana bambi , mbi napekaka koko na bipeko bilibota a mojɔ monu , bo elimo eMasiya eboloe a tei enu .
48004020	Posa embi edi bo nadae na nu e dɛye , bo nabale na nu na monɔkɔ motongo , cina bo nadi na mokakwano a mojɔ monu .
48004021	Tɔndɔni mbi mojɔ mu ; ino baya bapalaka boda cina jiMibeko , otahokeani Mibeko ?
48004022	Mojɔ bo mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Abalayama adaka na bana-bami babae . Abota okina na mobuli , na yona otongo na mwali osɔmi .
48004023	Yona obotama na mobuli , abotama o abota-maka bana basusu ; yona ko obotama na mwali osɔmi , abota cina esako eNjambe .
48004024	Mojɔ momina modi oko mondɛ . Bali bamina badi o mikongo Mibae . Okina obu , Agala , yona obota bana a mojɔ molibuli , adi o Mono moSinai .
48004025	Iyo Agala adi o Mono moSinai a Alabia . Cina emina edi oko Yelusalema ; mojɔ bo ngando eYelusalema yena edi e dɛye , edi a libuli , na bana bande pongono .
48004026	Yelusalema oho diko ko edi na bosɔmi , na yo adi ngwa’su .
48004027	Mojɔ bo , mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Da na sepi , wɛ motete yona opeliti libota ; Imba na sepi , wɛ yona oditi na bipeko bilibota ; Mojɔ bo , bana bamwali yona odikai elengeli , Banɔi bana bamwali yona odi na momi .
48004028	Baninga , iso bodi bana banjikano , o adaka Isaka .
48004029	Yona obotama a ehole emina o moto omini , anɔngeja yona obotama o moto oMwembo , na edi koko boa e dɛye .
48004030	Mosɔnɔ ko mobalaka bo ? Mobalaka bo , Bengana mobuli-mwali na mwana’nde , mojɔ bo mwana omobuli atasangoa na mwana omwali yona odi sɔmi .
48004031	Oko boa baninga , so boditi bana bamobuli ; bodi oko bana bamwali yona odi sɔmi .
48005001	Masiya asikoa so bo bodae na bosɔmi . A mojɔ momina , dani bambihmake a bosɔmi bonu ; T’ojimeni oko bo opikameni koko a libuli .
48005002	Eleho embi Paulo ai no edi oko ye ; isa ojimakani mojɔ mobolena ganda , Masiya adi oko ngasa ai no .
48005003	Mbi najebejaka no bo moto na moto yona ojimaka mojɔ mobolena ganda , abwani bosuma Mibeko kanga misusu mɛnɛ .
48005004	Isa odukakani lilonga a njea eMibeko , obɔtɔni na Masiya oko bobɔtɔnɔ ; okwani , na okwani monganji moNjambe .
48005005	Mojɔ bo njingo elilonga lisu edi oko na Mwembo , na licingi oko na ejimeli .
48005006	Bolena boganda , isa bodi isa boditi , boditi nongo na cina a tei eMasiya ; mojɔ mosusu modi oko ejimeli yena esanejaka na epaeli .
48005007	Ino opotakani mbango bopele boso ; ombɛjɛi no nda bo otasumani mwako mosoti ?
48005008	Bopangoa bomina bocingiti nongo na yona obea no .
48005009	Mitɛkɛ misusu Mibongoaka oko na ekenge ekɛkɛ elipetu .
48005010	Mbi nadi na njingo ai Kumu bo so na no bodae na molema momɔci . Moto ko yona onɔngejaka no âsɔ mokindo monde mɛnɛ .
48005011	Baninga , isa mbi nakojaka mojɔ mobolena ganda , banɔngejaka mbi mojɔ moye ? Akɔki mbi kɔ boa , ka mole-mobokea moditi koko libaku .
48005012	Yɛni baya banɔngejaka no babejae mikuku Mibu bɛnɛ .
48005013	Baninga , obeamani bo odaeni na bosɔmi ; endele ko , pɛ boji-mani bo bosɔmi bonu bopɛ no mokalo a bosuma posa jimokuku . Moto na moto adi bokɔmɛ mina’nde oko na epaeli .
48005014	Mojɔ bo cina eMibeko misusu edi a ekenge ye emɔci , Toma pala motuteano mowɛ o asapalaka wɛ mɛnɛ .
48005015	Okaswianani na okakokalanani , nganjamani bo otawanani .
48005016	Mbi nabalaka bo , Sumakani Mwembo bo otagbokani na posa jimokuku .
48005017	Mojɔ bo posa jimokuku jinaka na Mwembo , na posa jiMwembo jinaka na mokuku ; jilonanaka oko bolonana , bo otakɔni ngando jipalaka no .
48005018	Okasumakani Mwembo , oditini cina jiMibeko .
48005019	Bikɔmɛli bimokuku bidi bohu mɛnɛ , oko bibi , — bɔɔli , ndukeli , lisɔngi ,
48005020	bole , demba , lisoki , miano , likaka , kɛnjɔ , bolonana , misoo , ejimeli ebokosea ,
48005021	soki , bolangoa , matanga , na ngando jisusu jia jidi boa . Mbi nalehaka no e dɛye o aleha mbi no boso , bo baya badi na bikɔmɛli bimina batasangoa bokumu boNjambe .
48005022	Mbuma jiMwembo ko jidi oko jiji , — ngɛnjɔ , sepi , bowi , lingbangba , monganji , bodongo , likabo , bosangbindea .
48005023	Pɛpɛ nongo mokina mobeko modi bodumba ngando jimina .
48005024	Ibaya badi bato baMasiya bakaaleja mokuku a mole-mobokea , na posa na masɔngi mamokuku pongono .
48005025	Isa bohelaka a mojɔ moMwembo , bobwani bosuma Mwembo pongono .
48005026	Bobwamti bosakumeja ; pɛ bodingeanani ; pɛ bokejanani likaka .
48006001	Baninga , okahuoajani moto na mojɔ mobe , mo baya badi na Mwembo odini bohuleja moto omina na milema mi yɛmbu . Nganjama ko bo otamekama wɛ mɛnɛ .
48006002	Kamoanani mina , moto na moto akamoe muna momina’nde ; oko boa odini bosuma Mibeko miMasiya .
48006003	Moto yona odi oko moto-ngasa pɛ , akalɛ bo adi moto monɛnɛ , usakoseaka yo mɛnɛ .
48006004	Moto na moto adi bokokeleja ekɔmɛli ende mɛnɛ . Oko boa âda na njea bo asakumejae na ngando jinde mɛnɛ , pɛ bosa’ngɛ na moto otongo .
48006005	Mojɔ bo moto na moto adi botomba muna monde mɛnɛ .
48006006	Moto akakoja moto otongo Ebaeli , moto omina abwani bomokɔ monganji na leka londe losusu .
48006007	T’osakoseeni oko ; moto atasɛkɛ Njambe , mojɔ bo moto adi bojua oko jia jinaka yo .
48006008	Moto aka’na dona oko a mojɔ momokuku , adi boyaka mbuma jibopɔ a mokuku monde mɛnɛ . Moto ko aka’na dona a Mwembo , adi bojua ejueli a Mwembo , oko bomɔ bua bodi na bosusu .
48006009	Ebɔngiti bo bongwae bilomu bipele ; mojɔ bo , bomiti ’ ngwa , ehole ekahwana , iso bodi bojua .
48006010	Oko boa , boka’nɛ njea a bokɔ bopele , yɛni bokɔe bopele ai bato basusu , gbo oko ai baya badi a denga diejimeli .
48006011	Anjani mboa ji jinɛnɛnɛ jisɔnɔkɔ na mbi mokanda ai no na ebɔ embi mɛnɛ .
48006012	Bato baya badi na bingi ai no a mojɔ mobolena ganda , badi oko na posa eembete emokuku , bo batadingoa a mojɔ momole-mobokea moMasiya .
48006013	Mojɔ bo , ibo bɛnɛ , bato baya bajimaka bolena , batasumaka Mibeko , na bapalaka bo balenejae no , bo basakumejae na mikuku minu .
48006014	Mbi ko naditi nongo na ekina ekumu etongo , oko yena emole-mobokea moKumu osu Yesu Masiya , mojɔ bo ngondo ebakeama a mole-mobokea ai mbi , na mbi nabakeama a mole-mobokea a ngondo , a mojɔ monde .
48006015	Bolena boganda , isa bodi isa boditi , bodi mojɔ mongasa ; mojɔ momɔci mua mobwani modi oko moto moyene .
48006016	Bowi na wa , ai bato basusu baya badalaka a njea ye , na ai Yisalaele oNjambe .
48006017	E dɛye , yɛ bonɔngeja mbi koko , pɛpɛ nongo moto , mojɔ bo nadi na bihuli biYesu a mokuku mombi .
48006018	Baninga , yɛ monganji moKumu osu Yesu Masiya modae na miembo minu . Amen .
49001001	Njɛbɛ embi Paulo , obwɛnji oMasiya Yesu a mojɔ mobolulea boNjambe , ai baMasiya baya badi oho Ɛpɛsɔ , na baya badi na lisuma ai Masiya Yesu .
49001002	Yɛ monganji na bowi boSangwa’su Njambe na Kumu osu Yesu Masiya hodae na nu .
49001003	Yɛni bosakoe Njambe Sange eKumu osu Yesu Masiya , yona ojongoa so a tei eMasiya na majongoa masusu mamwembo na ma-Diko .
49001004	Iyo ahɔ so a tei ende oko ngondo ye epetakini yoama , ho bodae basɛnɔke , pɛpɛ nongo litɔnɔ a boso bonde .
49001005	Ahɛngɛ so na ngɛnjɔ ende bo bodae bana bande mɛnɛ balisango cina eYesu Masiya . Mokano monde modaka boa na sepi ,
49001006	bo angamejae ekumu emonganji monde , na akɔ so monganji momina a tei eMwana’nde ongɛnjɔ .
49001007	Lisiko lisu lidi oko a tei ende a mojɔ momakia mande , na bo yɛ bojibe jisu a mojɔ momonganji monde mua monɔi .
49001008	Iyo anɛngeja monganji monde ai so boa cina ebowɛi na bocingea bonde .
49001009	Ajima bo ajebejae so cina ebolulea bonde , na aneja so bo cina emokano monde edi bo
49001010	atitanejae ngando jisusu a tei eMasiya , ngando jiDiko , na ngando jinase , oko etango emasu emaka bwana .
49001011	Lisango lisu lidi a tei ende , lia lihɛngɛmɛ na mokano monde yona okɔkɔ ngando jisusu na bowɛi na bolulea bonde mɛnɛ .
49001012	Cina emina edi bo gala eekumu ende ehɛe a mojɔ mosu baya bajima Masiya boso .
49001013	Ino pongono , ama no ka Ebaeli eSoti , oko Mwako Mopele moboheleja bonu , omi jimani oko yo , na o’sɔni embete eMwembo Mosɛnɔkɛ monjikano ,
49001014	mua modi ndanga elisango lisu , oko a ehole ebosɔ lisango limina , a mojɔ mobosakoa ekumu ende .
49001015	Mbi naka mwako moejimeli enu ai Kumu Yesu , na ngɛnjɔ enu ai bato bande basusu .
49001016	A mojɔ momina , nasakoaka Njambe bihole bisusu a mojɔ monu , yana alangaka mbi kombe jinu a ma’nga mambi .
49001017	Nangaka koko bo Njambe oKumu osu Yesu Masiya , Sango yona odi na ekumu esusu , apɛ no mwembo mobowɛi na bocingea , a bojebeana na nde soti ,
49001018	na bo ahojae miso mamilema minu , bo ocingeeni njingo ebobea bonde , na ekumu enɛnɛ mɛnɛ elisango linde a tei ebasɛnɔke ,
49001019	na ndangasa ende pɛ njɛngi ai so baya bajimaka ; mwɛngi momina modi oko elomu ekɔ yo na bopipo bongulu ende
49001020	a tei eMasiya yana amongɔjɔ a bogwa , na amo-bakea oho Diko a ebɔ ende ebami
49001021	bo anɔe bakumu basusu bou mɛnɛ , na kpaci jisusu , na ngulu jisusu , na makumu masusu , na kombe jisusu boya jia jidi a ehole ye , na a ehole ebodoa .
49001022	Na adeja ngando jisusu cina jibibota binde , na amobakea bo adae Kumu oDenga a mojɔ mongando jisusu ,
49001023	mojɔ bo Denga didi mokuku monde , na yo alumejaka mokuku momina o alumejaka yo leka losusu mɛnɛ .
49002001	Ino odakani kanga bagwake mɛnɛ a mojɔ momalaboa manu na jibe jinu .
49002002	Mida minu midaka oko moda mongondo ye , na odakani na lisuma ai kumu yona odi na bokumu bonde a pwea , oko mwembo mua modi na ngulu a tei ebana balipanga e dɛye .
49002003	Iso pongono , so basusu , bopangana na bu , na lisuma lisu lidaka oko a posa jimokuku . Bodaka babuli baposa jimokuku na jimolema . Bodaka bana bakɛlɛ oko a bobotama bosu , iso na ’ bo tungu emɔci .
49002004	Njambe ko anɔi na wa , na apalaka so na ngɛnjɔ enɛnɛ ;
49002005	a mojɔ momina , nongo adaka so bagwake a mojɔ mojibe jisu , iyo apa so bomɔ yana apa yo Masiya bomɔ ( ohelni oko a mojɔ momonganji moNjambe ) , na angɔjɔ so na Masiya , na adeja so na nde a bisika biDiko , a tei eMasiya Yesu ,
49002006	
49002007	bo anejae monganji monde pɛ njɛngi , na likabo linde ai so , a tei eMasiya Yesu , a bilulu bia bidoakini .
49002008	Mojɔ bo ohelini a mojɔ moejimeli , cina emonganji moNjamhe ; mojɔ momina mocingiti na nu bɛnɛ ; modi oko epeeli eNjambe .
49002009	Mocingiti nongo na bilomu , bo moto asaka sakumeja .
49002010	Mojɔ bo ’ so bodi elomu ekɔkɔ Njambe ; boyoama a tei eMasiya a mojɔ mobilomu bipele , na Njambe abisɛlingoa eyou bo bokɔe bilomu bimina . Bokatana a tei eMasiya
49002011	BaYuda baya basɔkɔ embete ubolena-ganda a mokuku oko a mɔmɔ mabato , babeaka no bamwea . A mojɔ momina obwanitini bobosa bo obotamani oko bapakano .
49002012	A ehole emina odakani habɔtɔnɔke na Masiya , pɛpɛ nongo lisango a bokumu boYisalaele , pɛpɛ nongo libondo a mikongo minjikano , pɛpɛ nongo njingo , pɛpɛ nongo Njambe a ngondo .
49002013	E dɛye ko , a tei eMasiya , mo baya badaka boso bohali , obatamani hulelu a mojɔ momakia maMasiya .
49002014	Mojɔ bo yo adi mokongo mosu mobosiili . Iyo akataneja so baya badaka babae bo bodae oko omɔci pɛ , na abuka ngbungbu ebobɔteja a tei esu .
49002015	Abakea mokongo mobosiili na mokuku monde mɛnɛ , bo asiejae mokongo moMibeko na mongila , na bo apɛ bowi oko na boyoa bomoto omɔci moyene a tei ende mɛnɛ , oko na bu babae .
49002016	Akɔ boa bo akatanejae so babae na Njambe , o mokuku momɔci a mojɔ momole-mobokea . Oko boa asieja lisoki limina .
49002017	Iyo adoa , na atɔndɔ mwako mobowi ai no baya badaka bohali , na ai baya badaka hulelu .
49002018	Mojɔ bo so basusu babae bodi na njea ebokwea ai Sango na mwembo momɔci a mojɔ monde .
49002019	Oko boa oditini koko midoa na bakɛndɛli ; mo na basɛnɔke odini ngando emɔci , na odini bana badenga diNjambe .
49002020	Babwɛnji na batɔndɔi badi eyoeli-ecina enu , na Masiya Yesu yo mɛnɛ adi litai limogbukusu .
49002021	Eyoeli esusu ekatani a tei ende , na eyoamaka bo edae tempelo esɛnɔke a tei eKumu .
49002022	Na okatanani no bɛnɛ a tei ende o ndako , bo odaeni tempelo eMwembo a mojɔ moNjambe .
49003001	A mojɔ momina , mbi Paulo , nadi lisungu liYesu Masiya a mojɔ monu bapakano .
49003002	Nadingaka bo o’kani mwako momonganji mokɔ Njambe ai mbi , bo nakɔe elomu ai no .
49003003	Njambe aboloja ai mbi cina emokano monde mua modaka mobombamake , o ami mbi sɔnɔ mweka .
49003004	Okalangani bikenge bimina odini bocingea ejebeli embi emojɔ mobombamake moMasiya .
49003005	Mojɔ momina moipaka boloa ai bato babilulu bitongo ; moboloi ko e dɛye ai babwɛnji basɛnɔke , na ai batɔndɔi bande , oko na Mwembo .
49003006	Cina emina edi bo bapakano badi basangoli pongono ; badi binama bimokuku momɔci , na basangoaka njikano yena edi a tei eYesu Masiya a mojɔ moMwako Mopele .
49003007	Mbi nahɔmɔ bo nadae mokɔmɛli oMwako Mopele , cina eepeeli emonganji moNjambe mua mosɔ mbi ai yo na ndangasa engulu ende .
49003008	Mbi nasɔ monganji mu , bo nabolojae ai bapakano mijɔ miyumu miMasiya mia midi na bonɛtɔ , oko mbi yona odi ngɔngɔ jibasɛnɔke basusu ,
49003009	na bo nanejae bato basusu cina emojɔ mua modaka mobombamake oko a libangake mɛnɛ a tei eNjambe yona okɔ leka losusu .
49003010	Cina emina edi bo bakumu na bato basusu bakpaci oho Diko hacingee mojɔ mobowɛi bonɛnɛ boNjambe a mojɔ moDenga .
49003011	Mokano mokana yo a libangake a tei eMasiya Yesu Kumu osu modaka boa .
49003012	Na so bodi na njea bohu mɛnɛ a bodoa ai Njambe , pɛpɛ nongo mokakwano , cina eejimeli esu ai yo .
49003013	A mojɔ momina , mbi nangaka no bo otangwaeni cina eminɔngɔ misɔkɔ mbi a mojɔ monu ; midi oko ekumu enu .
49003014	A mojɔ momina , mbi natitaka na magbunda a boso boSango (
49003015	menga masusu , isa oho Diko , isa ya nase , masɔkɔ kombe oko ai yo ) ,
49003016	bo apɛ no bopingeja bongulu eMwembo monde a tei enu , moto namoto , oko nalikabo liekumu ende yena enɔi .
49003017	Nangɔɔnɔkɔ bo Masiya adihe esika eboda a milema minu cina eejimeli enu , na bo odaeni bambilimake na ngbi a epaeli ;
49003018	bo odini bohɔnɔ a bocingea na basɛnɔke basusu , cina esasa , na boyai , na ndinda , na boka , bongɛnjɔ eMasiya ,
49003019	na bo ojebeni ngɛnjɔ eMasiya yena enɔi ejebeli esusu , na bo olumeni botɔ na boluma boNjambe kanga boya mɛnɛ .
49003020	E dɛye , ekumu ai yo yona obwani bokɔ ngando jisusu jia jinɔi mijɔ misusu mingaka so , na milɛkɛ so bou mɛnɛ , cina engulu yena ekɔkɔ a tei esu ,
49003021	ekumu ai yo a tei eDenga , na a tei eMasiya Yesu a bilulu bisusu pɛ suka . Amen .
49004001	Oko boa , mbi lisungu liMasiya , nangɔɔnɔkɔ no bo odaeni na mida mia Mibwani na bobea bobeama na nu ,
49004002	oko na bosatiteja bonɛnɛ , na bombɔki , na lingbangba . Moto adi boda na moto otongo oko bowi a mojɔ moepaeli .
49004003	Dani na bingi a bobanea bokatana boMwembo ; sakandanani na licinga libowi .
49004004	Mokuku modi momɔci pɛ , na Mwembo modi momɔci pɛ , mojɔ bo obeamani a njingo emɔci yana abeama no .
49004005	Kumu adi oko omɔci pɛ , ejimeli emɔci , batisimo emɔci ,
49004006	na Njambe omɔci , yona odi Sange ’ bato basusu ; iyo anɔi basusu ; adi a ndanda ebasusu na adi a tei ebasusu .
49004007	Iso ko bosɔ monganji , moto na moto oko na mwɛngi moepeeli eMasiya .
49004008	A mojɔ momina abala bo , Iyana akɛ yo oho diko , akɛ na lindundu limasungu , Na akaba bipeeli ai bato .
49004009	Cina emina edi bo , lyo akɛ diko ? Edi oko bo ama soloa oko a bisika binase bingondo .
49004010	Yona osoloa , adi oko yo yona okɛ diko , na anɔ busa mɛnɛ , bo alumejae ngando jisusu .
49004011	Na bipeeli bipa yo bidaka bo bakina bato badae babwɛnji , bakina batɔndɔi , bakina balehi , na bakina bo badae banjeli na bakoja ,
49004012	a bobɔngeja basɛnɔke , a mojɔ moelomu ebokɔmɛ Denga , na a mojɔ moeyoeli emokuku moMasiya ,
49004013	oko a ehole ehomea bosu basusu a boka-tana boejimeli , na a ejebeli eMwana ’ Njambe , bo bokandoe bato bapingake , na bo mwɛngi mosu mobwane na mwɛngi mobobɔngɔ boMasiya .
49004014	Bobwaniti boda koko bana bakɛkɛ , baya bahombahombaka na bapɛpɛnɛkɛ na pwea jisusu jibokoja bobato baepulu baya badi na poloso a bokoja ngando jibokosea .
49004015	Bobwani bopea boku mijɔ misoti , oko na epaeli , bo bokandoe a njea jisusu a tei eMasiya yona odi molo .
49004016	Edi oko a mojɔ monde na bokatana bongulu ende , bo mokuku mosusu mocingami o eyoeli emɔci , na mopingi na macinga masusu ; elomu ebinama bisusu epingejaka mokuku bo mokandoe na mosapingejae na epaeli .
49004017	Ebaeli embi , na eleho embi ai no a kombe eKumu , edi bo otadani koko na mida Mibapakano baya basumaka mabunga mamilema Mibu .
49004018	Bocingea bobu bodi bokutubanake , na babɔtɔnɔ na bomɔ boNjambe cina elibumi libu lia licini na milema Mibu mipipo .
49004019	Baditi koko na sɔni ; basa’pa a ngando jibosɔtɔ , na badi oko na posa ebokɔ mijɔ misusu Mibosambolu .
49004020	Ino ko oikoani na Masiya boa ,
49004021	isa omohokeani na soti , na isa osɔni bokoja ai yo , oko mijɔ misoti mia midi a tei eYesu .
49004022	Toma hwani moto moyou yona odaka na ekɔmɛli eyou , yona odi mopɔke mɛnɛ a mojɔ moposa jibokosea .
49004023	Dani bato bayene a tei emiembo na milema minu .
49004024	Toma lwani moto moyene yona oyoama a elimo eNjambe , na bodongo , na bosɛnɔ bosoti .
49004025	A mojɔ momina , toma lonani bokosea ; balani moto na mina’nde moto oko mua modi soti , mojɔ bo bodi binama bia bicingani .
49004026	Okadani na kɛlɛ t’okɔeni oko bobe . T’ojimeni oko bo kɛlɛ enu edipe na busa .
49004027	T’okineni oko pokiso a mojɔ moSatana .
49004028	Isa moto adaka mobi , abwaniti boba na ikina . Abwani bokɔ elomu epele na mɔmɔ mande , bo adihe likonja a bopa baya badi na taka .
49004029	T’okineni oko ekenge ebe emane a Ininɔkɔ minu ; dani ko na ebaeli epele , a boleha na bokɔmeja baya bakaka .
49004030	T’okejaeni oko Mwembo Mosɛnɔke moNjambe sɔni , mojɔ bo o’sɔni embete ende a mojɔ mobusa bobosikoa .
49004031	Toma dongejani lisoki lisusu , na kɛlɛ , na kɛnjɔ , na misoo , na malɔngi , na bikɔmɛli bisusu bibe .
49004032	Na dani na monganji , moto ai mina’nde moto , na molema mo yɛmbu ; kinanani jibe , moto na mina’nde moto , o akwa Njambe jibe jinu a tei eMasiya .
49005001	Ikoanani na Njambe o bana baepaeli .
49005002	Dani na ngɛnjɔ o O adaka Masiya na ngɛnjɔ ai so , na asapa ai Njambe a mojɔ mosu , epeeli eso epele elitindi na lisiko .
49005003	A mojɔ mobɔɔli , na ngando jibosambolu , na mbengea , t’okineni oko bo mijɔ mi midae a minɔkɔ minu ; Mibɔngiti nongo na bato baMasiya .
49005004	Pɛ bobala nongo mijɔ misɔni , isa ebalabala , isa ngɛkɛ ; Sakoani ko Njambe .
49005005	Toma iebani mojɔ mu na soti ; pɛpɛ nongo moto obɔɔli , pɛpɛ nongo moto obosambolu , pɛpɛ nongo moto ombengea ( cina emina edi moto yona osakoaka njambe obokosea ) odi bosangoa lisango a Bokumu boMasiya na boNjambe .
49005006	T’ojimeni oko bo moto akosee no na ebalabala , mojɔ bo kɛlɛ eNjambe edi ai bana balipanga a mojɔ mongando jimina .
49005007	A mojɔ momina , t’opanganeni oko na bato bamina .
49005008	Odakani bosoboso modidi ; e dɛye ko odini bohu atei eKumu ; oko boa , toma dani na bikɔmɛli bibana babohu .
49005009	Mojɔ bo bohu bobotaka oko ngando jisusu jipele , jibɔngɔke na jisoti .
49005010	Jimani oko ngando jia jisepejaka Kumu .
49005011	Toma bulɛni ngando jingasangasa jimodidi ; anejani na bikɔmɛli binu bo ngando jimina jidi jibe .
49005012	Mojɔ bo edi sɔni mɛnɛ a bobala a mojɔ mongando jikɔkɔ bato bamina a libombi .
49005013	Bohu bokahoja mojɔ , modi boholoa a bohu ; cina bo , mokaboloa modi a bohu .
49005014	A mojɔ momina , abala bo , Wɛ yona ohwɛi hiɔ , sisoa ! Angɔ a bogwa , Na Masiya âpa wɛ bohu .
49005015	Toma nganjamani a mojɔ momida minu ; dani na bopasa , pɛpɛ bogegele .
49005016	Pɛ bonamejani masu manu , mojo bo masu ma madi mabe .
49005017	T’odaeni oko na yebe ; cingeani ko bolulea boNjambe .
49005018	T’olangoeni oko na vino ; mojɔ momina modi bosambolu ; endele ko dani balumake na Mwembo .
49005019	Masolo manu mabwani boda na njembo jipele , njembo jibosakoa na njembo jiMwembo . Imbani na sakoani Kumu na milema minu misusu .
49005020	Sakoani Njambe Sango bihole hisusu , a mojɔ mongando jisusu , a kombe eKumu osu Yesu Masiya .
49005021	Sumanani moto na moto oko na lisuma ai Masiya .
49005022	Ino bali , dani na lisuma ai bami banu , o asumaka no Kumu .
49005023	Mojɔ bo momi adi molo momwali , o adi Masiya molo moDenga , dia didi mokuku monde , na yo adi Moheleja omokuku momina .
49005024	Denga disumaka Masiya ; oko boa bali badi bosuma bami babu a ngando jisusu .
49005025	Ino bami , dani na ngɛnjɔ ai bali banu , o adaka Yesu na ngɛnjɔ a Denga , na asapa a mojɔ moDenga
49005026	bo ahsɛnojae cina ebosɛnɔ bobososa bomadiba maEbaeli .
49005027	Akɔ boa bo Denga dimae a boso bonde na ekumu enɛnɛ , lihɛngɛmɛke na lisɛnɔke , pɛpɛ nongo litɔnɔ , isa maninginingi , isa mojɔ motongo .
49005028	Oko boa , bami babwani boda na ngɛnjɔ ai bali babu o apalaka bo mikuku Mibu bɛnɛ . Moto yona odi na ngɛnjɔ ai mwali onde adi na ngɛnjɔ ai yo mɛnɛ .
49005029	Mojɔ bo moto t’alonake mini minde mɛnɛ ; amibɔkɔkɔ na amibaneaka , o akɔkɔ Masiya na Denga .
49005030	Mojɔ bo so bodi binama bimokuku monde .
49005031	A mojɔ momina , motoadi bokina sango na nango a bokatana na mwali onde bo ibo babae badae munu momɔci .
49005032	Mojɔ momina modi na cina enɛnɛ ebombamake . Mbi nabalaka a mojɔ moMasiya na Denga .
49005033	Oko boa , yɛ moto na moto adae na mwali onde ngɛnjɔ o asapalaka yo mɛnɛ , na mwali adae na lisuma ai muma’nde .
49006001	Ino bana , toma sumani baboti banu a tei eKumu ; mojɔ mu mobɔngi .
49006002	Toma suma sangwao na ngwao , ( imu modi mobeko moboso na njikano )
49006003	bo mijɔ miwɛ Mibɔnge , na oyeyoe ekoka a ngondo ye .
49006004	Ino basango , t’okejaeni oko bana banu kɛlɛ ; babɔkɔni , na balehani na bokoja boKumu .
49006005	Ino bakɔmɛli , toma sumani baya badi baswa banu ya nase , oko na bɔ na mongongoma , na molema mosoti , o asumaka no Kumu .
49006006	Kɔni ngando jipalaka Njambe na milema minu , o bakɔmɛli baMasiya , te nongo a bosepeja bato baya banjaka no na miso pɛ .
49006007	Kɔni elomu enu na bingi , te nongo ai bato , oko ai Kumu yo mɛnɛ .
49006008	Jebani bo moto na moto adi bosɔ ndese ai Kumu a mojɔ mongando jisusu jipele jikɔkɔ yo , nongo akada mobuli isa mwana’sɔmi .
49006009	Ino baswa , toma kɔni koko boa na bakɔmɛli banu . Yɛni bogbilimwana kɛnjɔ . T’obosaeni oko bo Moswa’bu na onu adi oho Diko , na yo anjaka bato basusu amɛci .
49006010	Mojɔ mosuka , — sapingejani a tei eKumu na bopipo bondangasa ende .
49006011	Lwani molilo mosusu mobila moNjambe bo ohɔneni ndungu jiSatana .
49006012	Mojɔ bo , bila enaka so editi na mini na makia ; edi oko na makumu , na kpaci , na bakumu bangondo ye emodidi , na mandundu mamiembo Mibe a bisika bidiko .
49006013	A mojɔ momina , toma tombani molilo mosusu mobila moNjambe , bo ohɔneni bila a busa bua bobe ; na omaka gbokejani , osa ko odikaeni oko bambilimake .
49006014	Imani ngbi . Kandani njingo eSoti a moongo manu . Lwani bosɛnɔ o ebende a bupa .
49006015	Kinani mosɛlingo moMwako Mopele mobowi modae sapata a bibota binu .
49006016	Toma tombani nguba eejimeli a bokumba ndɛ jimosa jiyona Mobe ; mojɔ mu modi monɛnɛ mɛnɛ .
49006017	Lwani egbala epipo eboheleja , na tombani abɛnɛ oMwembo yona odi Ebaeli eNjambe .
49006018	Ingakani bihole bisusu na Mwembo , tungu jisusu jibingeeli na mangɔɔnɔ ; toma nganjamani na bopipo a mojɔ momina , na ingakani a mojɔ mobaMasiya basusu ,
49006019	na a mojɔ mombi pongono , bo nadae na bɛtɛ ebobala a botɔndɔ na eci cina eMwako Mopele .
49006020	Nadi ohwɛnji a minyɔlɔ oko a mojɔ momina . Ingakani bo nadae na eci yena ebwani na mbi a bobala .
49006021	Odini boka miako mimbi na Lukiko mwangwa’su , yona odi mokɔmɛli olingbangba oKumu ; yo adi bojebeja no mijɔ misusu .
49006022	Mbi namolomi oho ai no oko a mojɔ momina , bo ojebeni mijɔ mimbi , na bo agɔmbejae milema minu .
49006023	Yɛ bowi na ngɛnjɔ na ejimeli eNjambe Sango , na Kumu Yesu Masiya , edae ai baninga .
49006024	Yɛ monganji moNjambe modae na bato basusu baya bapalaka Kumu osu Yesu Masiya na ngɛnjɔ yena etasia .
50001001	Paulo na Timoteo , bakɔmɛli baMasiya Yesu , ai basɛnɔke basusu baMasiya Yesu baya badi a Pilipoi , na ai banjeli na basuku baDenga pongono .
50001002	Yɛ monganji na bowi boNjambe Sangwa’su , na boKumu osu Yesu Masiya , bodae na nu .
50001003	Mbi nasakoaka Njambe bihole bisusu bilɛkɛ mbi no .
50001004	Te nakinake bosepa a bingeeli bimbi bisusu a mojɔ monu basusu ,
50001005	cina ebokɔmeja bonu a elomu eMwako Mopele , banga na busa boboso mɛnɛ oko a ehole ye .
50001006	Mbi najebaka na soti bo yona obanga elomu epele a tei enu âesukeja bopele a mojɔ mobusa boYesu Masiya .
50001007	Ebɔngi bo mbi nadae na bolɛ bomina a mojɔ monu basusu , cina bo nabaneaka no a tei emolema mombi , isa a mbɔci ji , isa a elomu ebobanea na bopingeja elomu eMwako Mopele , oko no baya bakatani na mbi a bosɔ monganji moNjambe .
50001008	Njambe yo mɛnɛ ajebaka na soti bo nadi na nu posa oko na ngɛnjɔ eMasiya Yesu .
50001009	Na mojɔ mongaka mbi modi bo epaeli enu ehɛe bou mɛnɛ , na bo elume na ejebeli na bocingea ,
50001010	a bombetea ngando jia jinɔi na bopele , bo odaeni pɛpɛ nongo mojɔ , pɛpɛ nongo pita , a mojɔ mobusa boMasiya .
50001011	Yɛ lituna linu lidae lituna limbuma jipele jibodongo jia jidi a tei eYesu Masiya , a bokumeja na bosepeja Njambe .
50001012	Baninga , napalaka bo ojebeni bo mijɔ minɛkɛ mbi mikɔmejaka elomu eMwako Mopele oko bokɔmeja .
50001013	Bajebaka ya a ngando ebasoda , na a bisika bisusu bitongo , bo nadi a blɔkɔ a mojɔ moMasiya .
50001014	Na baninga banɛnɛ bahɛi na ejimeli ai Kumu a mojɔ mombɔci jimbi , na badi na eci a botɔndɔ mwako moNjambe , pɛpɛ nongo bɔ .
50001015	Bakina batɔndɔkɔ mwako moMasiya oko na likaka na misoo , batongo ko batɔndɔkɔ na milema mipele .
50001016	Ibaba bakɔkɔ boa cina eepaeli . Bajebaka bo mbi nadi ya a bokakela Mwako Mopele .
50001017	Iba batongo ko batɔndɔkɔ mwako moMasiya na miano , te nongo na soti , oko na njingo bo bapukejae mbi ya a blɔkɔ .
50001018	Pɛ mojɔ ! batɔndɔkɔ mwako moMasiya a njea ji jisusu , isa a mojɔ moegbo , isa a mojɔ mosoti ; mbi nasepaka a mojɔ momina , na nitakina bosepa .
50001019	Najebaka bo suka emojɔ mu êda oko bohela bombi cina ebingeeli binu , na bokɔmeja boMwembo moYesu Masiya .
50001020	Posa embi enɛnɛ na njingo embi jidi bo nitasamboa nongo ; bou oko bo nakumejae Masiya na eci enɛnɛ a mokuku mombi , isa na mohelo mombi , isa na bogwa bombi .
50001021	Mojɔ bo , ai mbi , bomɔ bodi oko Masiya , na bogwa bodi ndese .
50001022	Endele ko , isa ebɔngi bo nayeyoe a mokuku mu a mojɔ moelomu embi , nadi na mokakwano a mojɔ mobohɔ bombi .
50001023	Nadi a mɛlɛ manjea . Posa embi edi bo nayane bo nadae na Masiya ; mojɔ mua monɔi na bopele oko mu .
50001024	Endele ko , ebɔngi bo nayeyoe a mokuku mu a mojɔ monu .
50001025	Adi mbi na ejimeli emina , najebaka bo nadi boda na nu , na nâyeyoa na nu basusu , a bodaleja no , na a bosepeja no a ejimeli .
50001026	A mojɔ momina , sepi enu a tei eMasiya Yesu edi bohɛ a mojɔ mobodoa bombi koko ai no .
50001027	Ino ko , toma dani na ekɔmɛli yena ebwani na Mwako Mopele moMasiya . Oko boa , nongo nakadoa a bo’nɛnɛ na nu , isa nakadika ya , nadi boka mwako monu , bo odini bambilimake na molema momɔci , a bo’na o moto omɔci a mojɔ moejimeli eMwako Mopele .
50001028	T’obangeni oko soki jinu nongo mweka . Mojɔ mu modi embete ai bo a mojɔ mobokwa bobu , na a mojɔ moboheleja bonu bua bohulaka ai Njambe .
50001029	Mojɔ bo libondo linu liditi ejimeli ai Masiya pɛ ; lidi oko bo odingoeni a mojɔ monde .
50001030	O’kakani e dɛye bo mbi nanaka bila ; oko boa , bila enaka mbi , yena enɛ no na mbi boso , edi bila enu pongono .
50002001	Isa bogɔmbeja bodi a tei eMasiya , na peye eepaeli , na bokatana boMwembo , na wa , na monganji
50002002	sepejani mbi na soti a mojɔ mobokatana bonu na molema momɔci . Dani na epaeli emɔci , mokano momɔci , na mwembo momɔci .
50002003	Pɛ bokɔni mokina mojɔ na likaka , isa a mojɔ moegbo . Satitejani a milema minu , oko na bolɛ bo bato batongo banɔi no na bopele .
50002004	Moto na moto a tei enu abwani boda na bolɛ ai bato batongo , te a mijɔ minde mɛnɛ .
50002005	Kinani bo molema mua modaka a tei eMasiya modae a tei enu .
50002006	Mojɔ bo , yo , nongo adaka yo na elimo eNjambe , ailɛ nongo bo bobwana bonde na Njambe bodi eka eyumu a bobanea .
50002007	Asahangoja , na alwa elimo emobuli , na abotama na mokuku momoto .
50002008	Adaka yo na elimo emoto , asatiteja , na adaka na lisuma oko a bogwa , ee oko a bogwa bomole-mobokea .
50002009	A mojɔ momina , Njambe amokumeja bou mɛnɛ , na amopa ekina kombe yena enɔi kombe jisusu boya ,
50002010	bo muuli masusu boya madi bo’mbama a kombe eYesu , isa oho Diko isa ya nase , isa cina enase ye ,
50002011	na bo minɔkɔ nususu mijime bo Yesu Masiya adi Kumu , a mojɔ moekumu eNjambe Sango .
50002012	Baninga , ino odakani na lisuma bihole bisusu yana adaka mbi na nu . A mojɔ momina , toma dani na bingi e dɛye adi mbi bohali , a hongameja bohela honu , na bɔ na mongongoma .
50002013	Mojɔ bo Njambe yo mɛnɛ akɔkɔ elomu ende a tei enu , bo opaleni na okɔeni bolulea bonde bopele .
50002014	Kɔni bilomu bisusu , pɛpɛ nongo manungunungu na miano ,
50002015	bo odaeni bana baNjambe baya baditi nongo na mojɔ , baya badi na milema mi yɛmbu , pɛpɛ nongo litɔnɔ a tei eelulu ye engulumake elipanga . Ino odini a tei ebu o paka jia jihojaka ngondo .
50002016	Peani Ebaeli ebomɔ oko boku . Oko boa mbi nadi bosepa a busa boMasiya bo naipota epotapota , na bo naikɔ elomu ekɔkɔ .
50002017	Ee , nongo makia mambi makasopea a diko di epeeli enu elitumbu , oko ejimeli enu , nadi na sepi , na nasepaka na nu basusu .
50002018	Oko boa toma sepani pongono , na sepani na mbi .
50002019	Njingo embi edi ai Kumu Yesu bo nalomee no Timoteo ngɔngɔ bosme ; oko boa nadi boka miako minu , na molema mombi modi bogɔmbɔ .
50002020	Naditi na moto otongo yona obwani na nde , mojɔ bo yo alɛkɛ no na soti mɛnɛ .
50002021	Ibo batongo balɛkɛ oko ngando jibu bɛnɛ pɛ , te nongo jia jiMasiya .
50002022	Ino ko ojebakani bo yo apasami a elomu eMwako Mopele yena ekɔkɔ yo na mbi , o akɔmejaka mwana sangwa’nde .
50002023	Oko boa nadi na njingo bo namaka nɛ suka emojɔ mombi , namolome oho ai no .
50002024	Na nadi na ejimeli ai Kumu bo nitayeyoa a bodoa ai no mbi mɛnɛ .
50002025	Mbi ko najimi bo nalomee no e dɛye mwangwa’mbi Epapu-lodito yona ocingami na mbi a elomu na a bila , obwɛnji onu ai mbi na toma jinu a bokɔmeja mbi a taka embi .
50002026	Mojɔ bo yo adi na posa bo anɛnɛe na nu , na adi na monɔngɔ cina bo mwako moyogo ende momea oho ai no .
50002027	Yo adaka na yogo soti , na apaka gwa ; Njambe ko amokea wa , te nongo yo pɛ , oko mbi pongono , bo monɔngɔ mombi mosaka gbasoe .
50002028	Oko boa nadi na posa enɛnɛ bo namolome ai no , bo odaeni na sepi a bo’nɛnɛ na nde , na bo molema mombi mogɔmbe pongono .
50002029	Mo’sɔni bopele a kombe eKumu na sepi enɛnɛ , na dani na liSuma ai bato baya badi o adi yo .
50002030	Mojɔ bo yo apaka gwa a elomu eMasiya ; na apa njupi bo akɔmɛe mbi a kombe enu .
50003001	Mojɔ motongo baninga , sepakani a tei eKumu . Mbi nitangwa nongo bosɔnea no ekenge emina , na obwanini boejima .
50003002	Toma dingani a mojɔ mombwa ; toma dingani a mojɔ mobato baya badi na bikɔmɛli bibe ; toma dingani a mojɔ mobato babolena-ganda babokosea .
50003003	Babolena-ganda basoti badi oko so baya basakoaka Njambe a mwembo , baya bakumejaka Masiya Yesu , na bapeliti nongo ejimeli a ngando jimokuku .
50003004	Akɔki mbi pala , ka nabwani bojima ngando jimokuku . Isa okina moto alɛkɛ bo abwani boda na ejimeli a ngando jimokuku , esingaiti mbi !
50003005	Balena mbi ganda yana adaka mbi na masu bomwambe . Nadi moto ombota eYisalaele , moto olikota liBenyamina . Nadi moEbele , mwana oBaEbele . A njea eMibeko , nadaka MoPalusi .
50003006	Nadaka na bingi a bonɔngeja Denga . Nadaka na lisuma mɛnɛ a Mibeko , pɛpɛ nongo mojɔ .
50003007	Mbi ko nadumba ngando ji jisusu a mojɔ moMasiya , oko ngando jia jidaka na yumu a miso mambi .
50003008	Ee soti , mbi nalangaka ngando jisusu o ngando jingasa pɛ , a mojɔ moejebeli eMasiya Yesu Kumu ombi yena enɔi na yumu . Najima bo nabungejae ngando jisusu a mojɔ monde ; najilangaka o pita pɛ , bo Leka lombi loyumu lodae oko Masiya pɛ , na bo nadae a tei ende ,
50003009	te nongo a mojɔ mobodongo bombi mɛnɛ bua bocingi na Mibeko , oko a mojɔ mobodongo bua bocini na ejimeli ai Masiya , bua bohulaka ai Njambe a mojɔ moejimeli .
50003010	Nakɔ boa bo najebe Masiya , na ndangasa yena engɔ na nde a bogwa , bo nakatane na nde a madingoa mande , na bo nakatane na nde a bogwa bonde
50003011	oko na njingo ebomea a bongɔ bobagwake .
50003012	Editi bo mbi namei a suka emina , isa bo mbi nabɔngi na soti . Endele ko , nakɔkɔ na bopipo bo namee a mwɛngi mua mobwani , cina bo Masiya apee mbi oko a mojɔ momina .
50003013	Baninga , mbi nitalɛkɛ bo nabɔngi ; endele ko , nakɔkɔ mojɔ mu momɔci ; nabosaka ngando jia jidi ngɔngɔ , na nasalindaka na bopipo a ngando jia jidi boso .
50003014	Napotaka oko na miso mambi a suka enjea , na ndese edi oko bobea boNjambe bua bonɔi , a tei eMasiya Yesu .
50003015	A mojɔ momina , so baya badi bato bapingake bobwani boda na mokano momina . Isa odini na mokina mokano motongo , Njambe yo mɛnɛ adi bocingea no mojɔ momina .
50003016	Mojɔ momɔci ko , bobwani bodala a njea yena edi boso , oko na lisuma a ngando jijebaka so .
50003017	Baninga , ikoanani na mbi . Anjani baya banejaka no ekoaneli o anejaka so .
50003018	Cina bo , ekɔmɛli ebato banɛnɛ edi oko ekɔmɛli ebato baya badi soki jimole-mobokea moMasiya . Natomba bobala na nu a mojɔ mobu bihole binɛnɛ , na natɔndɔkɔ no koko e dɛye na bio .
50003019	Suka ebato bamina edi oko bogwa . Njambe obu adi oko sɔpɔ jibu bɛnɛ , na basakumejaka na sɔni ebu . Badi na bolɛ oko a ngando jingondo ye .
50003020	Iso ko bodi na bosɔmi bosu oho Diko , na bonjaka na tɛndɛ bo Moheleja , Kumu osu Yesu Masiya ahule ena .
50003021	Iyo adi bokindoja mokuku mosu monase , bo modae na elimo emokuku monde mɛnɛ moekumu , oko na ngulu yena edi ai yo a bogbokeja ngando jisusu .
50004001	A mojɔ momina , baninga bambi baepaeli , toma dani bambilimake boa a tei eKumu . Mbi nadi na posa ai no ; sepi embi edi ai no , na odini ekumu embi .
50004002	Mbi nalehaka Ewodia , na nalehaka Suntuke , ho badae na molema momɔci a tei eKumu .
50004003	Na nangaka wɛ pongono , wɛ limbaci limbi a elomu , bo okɔmejae bali bamina , mojɔ bo bakɔ elomu eMwako Mopele a dɔngɔ dimbi , ibo na Kelemento na bina’mbi batongo baya badi na kombe jibu a mokanda mobomɔ .
50004004	Sepakani ai Kumu bihole bisusu ; najɔkɔ na nu koko bo , Sepakani .
50004005	Kɔni bo bato basusu banɛe bombɔki bonu . Kumu adi mbuci mɛnɛ .
50004006	T’odaeni oko na mokakwano nongo mweka ; jebejani Njambe ko ngando jisusu jia jitakaka na nu , oko na bo’nga , na bongɔɔnɔ , na bosakoa .
50004007	Na bowi boNjambe bua bonɔi bocingea bomoto , bodi bobanea milema minu na miembo minu a tei eMasiya Yesu .
50004008	Mojɔ mosuka baninga , baneani a milema minu oko ngando jia jidi soti , jia jibɔngi , jia jidi bojo , jia jidi jisɛnɔke , jia jidi na epaeli , jia jidi na gala epele , — isa jinɔi na bopele , isa jibwani na bosakoa .
50004009	Kɔni ngando jikoa no na jisɔ no ai mbi , ngando ji’ka no na jinɛ no na mbi ; na Njambe obowi âda na nu .
50004010	Mbi nadi na sepi enɛnɛ ai Kumu , mojɔ bo bolɛ bonu ai mbi bosisoi koko e dɛye . Odakani na bolɛ ai mbi soti , na etaka na nu oko njea a boneja bolɛ bonu .
50004011	Nitabalaka boa a mojɔ motaka embi , cina bo mbi najebi e dɛye njea ebosepa na ngando jimbi tungu jisusu .
50004012	Nalandoi na taka , nalandoi koko na lituna . Najebi boda na ligola , isa na nja , na leka lonɛnɛ , isa na bokwali .
50004013	Nahɔnɔkɔ ngando jisusu a tei ende yona opaka mbi ngulu .
50004014	Endele ko , okɔini bopele a bokatana na mbi a minɔngɔ mimbi .
50004015	Ino BaPilipoi , ojebakani bo pɛpɛ nongo dikwa Denga ditongo dijima na mbi a mojɔ mobopa na bosɔ bipeeli , oko no pɛ , yana adonga mbi a Makedonia a libangake lielomu eMwako Mopele .
50004016	Nongo adaka mbi a Tɛsalɔnike , olomeani mbi bipeeli bihole bibae a bokɔmeja mbi a taka embi .
50004017	Yena edukaka mbi ko editi epeeli mɛnɛ ; nadukaka oko bo odaeni na mbuma jinɛnɛ a mojɔ moesako enu .
50004018	Mbi ko nasi leka losusu . Nadi na lituna lileka , mojɔ bo nasi toma eloma no na Epapulodito . Naditi koko na taka , na toma enu edi o epeeli esoo epele ejimaka Njambe , na emosepejaka .
50004019	Njambe ombi adi bopa no ngando jisusu jia jitakaka na nu , oko na mwɛngi momakonja maekumu ende a tei eMasiya Yesu .
50004020	Ekumu ai Njambe Sangwa’su oko na bosusu . Amen .
50004021	Abɛjɛni bato basusu baDenga a tei eMasiya Yesu . Baninga baya badi na mbi ya babɛjɛkɛ no .
50004022	Bato baMasiya basusu babɛjɛkɛ no , gbo oko baya badi bakɔmɛli bandako eKaisala .
50004023	Yɛ monganji moKumu osu Yesu Masiya modae na miembo minu .
51001001	Paulo , obwɛnji oMasiya Yesu oko na bolulea boNjambe , na Timoteo mwangwa’su ,
51001002	ai bato baDenga , na ai baninga basusu balisuma ai Masiya a Kɔlɔsai . Yɛ monganji na bowi boNjambe Sangwa’su bodae na nu .
51001003	Iso bosakoaka Njambe , Sange ’ Kumu osu Yesu Masiya a mojɔ monu , na bongaka a mojɔ monu bihole bisusu ,
51001004	cina bo boka mwako moejimeli enu ai Masiya Yesu , na epaeli enu ai bato basusu baejimeli ,
51001005	a mojɔ monjingo yena ehɛngɛmɛ oho Diko a mojɔ monu . O’kani mojɔ monjingo emina boso oko na bikenge bisoti , bikenge biMwako Mopele .
51001006	Mwako momina momea ai no , mojɔ bo monanganaka a ngondo esusu . Mobotaka mbuma na mokɛkɛ bohɛ ; modi oko boa a tei enu pongono , banga na busa boka no , na bojeba no , cina emonganji moNjambe na soti .
51001007	Okoani mojɔ momina na Epapala , moninga osu oepaeli a elomu . Iyo adi mokɔmɛli osoti oMasiya a mojɔ monu ,
51001008	na ajebeja so mojɔ moepaeli enu a tei eMwembo .
51001009	Iso bobanga bonga Njambe a mojɔ monu a busa boka so mojɔ momina , na botakinaka bonga . Bongaka bo olumeni na ejebeli ebolulea boNjambe , oko na bowɛi na bocingea bosusu boMwembo ,
51001010	bo odaeni na mida mia midi bokumeja kombe eKumu , mia midi bomosepeja na soti , na bo oboteni mbuma a tei ebilomu bisusu bipele , na bo ohɛeni na ejebeli eNjambe .
51001011	Yɛ ngulu ende yena enɔi , epingejae no na ngulu esusu , bo ohɔneni mijɔ misusu na lingbangba , na eci , na sepi pongono .
51001012	Sakoani Sango yona obɔngejai so bo bosangoe libondo lihsango libasɛnɔke a bohu .
51001013	Iyo ahelejai so a ngulu emodidi , na akwejai so a Bokumu boMwana’nde ongɛnjɔ .
51001014	A tei ende , iso bodi na lisiko , bo yɛ bojibe .
51001015	Iyo adi elimo eNjambe yona odi so pɛ bonɛ na miso ; adi Sɔmi obato basusu baya bayoama .
51001016	Leka losusu loyoama na nde , oho Diko na ya nase ; leka lonɛkɛ so na miso , na leka lodi so pɛ bonɛ na miso , na bakumu na makumu , kpaci na ngulu — ngando jisusu jiyoama na nde , na a mojɔ monde .
51001017	Iyo adi boso bongando jisusu , na ngando jisusu jicingi na nde .
51001018	Denga didi mokuku monde , na yo adi molo . Iyo adi libangake . Iyo abotama boso a tei ebagwake bo adae boso bongando jisusu .
51001019	Mojɔ bo Njambe ajima na bolulea bonde bopele bo bonjambe bonde bosusu bodae a tei ende ,
51001020	bo yo adae mosili , na abakea mokongo mobosiili na makia mande a mole-mobokea , a bohuleja ngando jisusu ai yo mɛnɛ , isa oho Diko isa ya nase .
51001021	Ino odakani na lipɔlɛ ai yo ; odakani na nde soki a milema minu , bato babikɔmɛli bibe .
51001022	Iyo ko akwea bosiili , na akataneja no koko a njea ebogwa bomokuku monde , bo amejae no a boso bonde na bosɛnɔ , pɛpɛ nongo litɔnɔ , pɛpɛ nongo mojɔ ,
51001023	okayeyoani bambilimake na ngbi a ejimeli , pɛ nongo bodonga a njingo eMwako Mopele moka no . Mwako momina motɔndɔmɔ ai bato basusu ya nase , na mbi Paulo nahɛngɛmɛ ho nadae mokɔmɛli omwako momina .
51001024	Mhi nasepaka e dɛye a mojɔ mominɔngɔ minɛkɛ mbi a kombe enu . Masiya adingoaka a mini mimbi a mojɔ momokuku monde , oko Denga dinde ; na mbi napalaka bo nabwanejae libondo limadingoa mamina .
51001025	Mojɔ bo nadi mokɔmɛli oDenga cina ekpaci esɔ mbi ai Njambe a mojɔ monu , bo natɔndɔe Mwako moNjambe kanga mosusu mɛnɛ ,
51001026	oko mojɔ mua modaka mobombamake ekoka enɛnɛ mɛnɛ ai bilulu binɛnɛ ; moboloi ko e dɛye ai baejimeli baNjambe .
51001027	Mojɔ bo Njambe ajima bo abanejae bo mojɔ mu mobo-mbamake modi mojɔ moekumu enɛnɛ mɛnɛ a tei ebapakano , — cina emina edi Masiya a tei enu , njingo eekumu .
51001028	Iso botɔndɔkɔ mwako monde ; bolehaka bato basusu , na bokojaka bato basusu na bowɛi bosusu , bo bokwejae a boso boNjambe moto na moto mobɔngɔke a tei eMasiya .
51001029	Elomu ekɔkɔ mbi edi oko a mo jɔ momina ; naekɔkɔ na molema mombi mosusu , oko na ngulu ende yena elindaka mbi na bopipo .
51002001	Napalaka bo ojebeni bo nanaka bila enɛnɛ a mojɔ monu , a mojɔ moBaLaodikea , na bato basusu baya banɛkini boso bombi na miso .
51002002	Nakɔkɔ boa bo Inilema Mibu mihɛe na eci o akatanaka ho na epaeli , na bo babɔnge a mojɔ mobowɛi bosoti a bocingea mojɔ mobombamake moNjambe , oko Masiya .
51002003	Mijɔ misusu miyumu Mibowɛi na miejebeli midi a tei ende .
51002004	Nabali boa , bo moto asaka kosea no na bikenge biepulu .
51002005	Nadi na nu bohali ; endele ko nadi na nu a mwembo , na nanɛkɛ na sepi mɛnɛ mida minu mingɛbɛnɛkɛ , na ejimeli enu embilimake a tei eMasiya .
51002006	Oko boa , ami no sɔ Kumu Yesu Masiya , toma dalani a tei ende oko boa .
51002007	Kinani njeli jinu jidae a tei ende ; dani bambilimake a diko dieyoeli ecina yena edi a tei ende , o asɔ no bokoja ; dani koko na bosakoa bonɛnɛ ai Njambe .
51002008	Toma nganjamani bo moto atakosea no na bikenge bibowɛi , na mijɔ mingasangasa mia mihulaka ai bato pɛ , na micingi na ejimeli a miembo mingondo , te nongo na Masiya .
51002009	Mojɔ bo bonjambe bosusu mɛnɛ bodi a tei eMasiya o mokuku ,
51002010	na bomɔ bodi bolumeja no , oko a tei ende yona odi Kumu omakumu masusu na bakumu basusu .
51002011	Ino o’sɔni embete ebolena-ganda te nongo a mɔmɔ mabato a bodongeja mini mimokuku , oko ai Masiya na bolena bonde ;
51002012	na opuseamani na nde a batisimo , na ongɔni koko a bogwa oko na nde , a mojɔ moejimeli a ngulu eNjambe yona omongɔjɔ a bogwa .
51002013	Njambe amopa bomɔ , na apa no bomɔ a tei ende , oko no baya badaka bagwake a tei ejibe , pɛpɛ nongo embete ebolena-ganda a mokuku , na akina jibe jinu jisusu .
51002014	Ahakoa mokanda momijɔ mia midaka o nongo jisu , na aseja mojɔ momina ; aebakea a mole-mobokea monde na kala .
51002015	Abeja makumu na bakumu ; abasambo-ja a boso bobato na abagbokeja a mole-mobokea .
51002016	T’ojimeni oko bo moto asambejae no a mojɔ moboyaka na bomwaka , isa a mojɔ momabonje , na Sabata , na ekɔmɛli enu yana atɛkɛ songe .
51002017	Ngando ji jisusu jidi oko esie pɛ engando jia jidi boda ngɔngɔ ; mokuku mɛnɛ modi oko Masiya .
51002018	T’ojimeni oko bo obungejaeni ndese enu a mojɔ momoto yona obekeaka no bo osatitejaeni a bosakoa babwɛnji badiko . Moto omina alɛkɛ oko mijɔ minjɔti pɛ , na egbo emolema monde mobe .
51002019	Aciniti nongo na Molo ; mojɔ bo bmama bisusu bimokuku bikatani a mojɔ momongi na sisa , na mokuku mosusu mokandoaka na ngulu eNjambe .
51002020	Isa ogwani na Masiya a mijɔ mingondo , odini na ekɔmɛli ebato bangondo mojɔ moye ?
51002021	Osumakani Mibeko mi mojɔ moye ? — Yɛ bobakea ebɔ a eka emina ; yɛ boyaka eka emina ; yɛ bopea eka emina ,
51002022	( oko leka lua logwaka a elomu ) Ngando jimina jidi oko Mibeko na bokoja bobato pɛ .
51002023	Jidi na bokina bowɛi a miso mabato , a mojɔ mobosakoa bonɛnɛ , na bosatiteja , na bodingoja bomokuku ; endele ko , jidi oko ngasa mɛnɛ , na jitakɔmejaka nongo a bogbokeja posa jimokuku .
51003001	Ino , isa ongɔini na Masiya a bogwa , dukani ngando jidiko , a esika edi Masiya a ebɔ ebami eNjambe .
51003002	Bakeani milema minu a ngando jidiko , te a ngando jinase .
51003003	Mojɔ bo ino odini bagwake , na bomɔ bonu bobombami na Masiya a tei eNjambe .
51003004	Masiya adi bomɔ bosu ; iyo akamana a bohu ino ômanani na nde Pongono a ekumu .
51003005	A mojɔ momina toma wejani ngando jingondo ye a tei enu , bɔɔli , mijɔ Mibosambolu , lisɔngi , posa jibe , mbengea . ( Mojɔ momina modi bosakoa bobokosea . )
51003006	Kɛnjɔ eNjambe edi ai bana balipanga a mojɔ mongando jimina .
51003007	Ino odakani na bikɔmɛli bimina yana adaka no a tei engando jimina .
51003008	E dɛye ko , toma dumbani ngando ji jisusu ; kɛlɛ , kɛnjɔ , ekɔmɛli ebe , bolɔngɔ , bikenge bibosambolu a minɔkɔ minu .
51003009	T’okoseanani oko , mojɔ bo ohwani moto moyou na bikɔmɛli binde ,
51003010	na olwani moto moyene yona odi na elimo eyene , oko elimo ende yona omoyoa a mojɔ moejebeli ende .
51003011	A eyoeli emina , bato baditi BaEla isa BaYuda , bato babolena-ganda isa pɛ bolena-ganda , isa bato babohali , isa BaSukutea , isa babuli , isa basɔmi ; mojɔ mosusu modi Masiya a tei ebato basusu .
51003012	Njambe ahɔ no , basɛnɔke na bato baepaeli . A mojɔ momina kwani elwali enu edae milema miwa , na peye , na bosatiteja , na bo yɛmbu , na bowi .
51003013	Isa moto adi na moto otongo mojɔ , aditi bokɛnjɔ na nde , adi bomoyɛ . Masiya a yɛ no ; oko boa toma yɛnu Pongono .
51003014	Ngɛnjɔ ko enɔi ngando ji jisusu ; ekatanejaka na boka-tana bosoti .
51003015	Kinani bowi boMasiya bodae na bokumu a milema minu ; obeamani bo odaeni mokuku momɔci oko a mojɔ momina . Dani koko na bosakoa .
51003016	Kinani Ebaeli eMasiya edae a tei enu , na enɛnge a tei enu na bowɛi bosusu . Ikojanani na lehanani na njembo jiNjambe , njembo jibosakoa , njembo jiMwembo . Imbani njembo ai Njambe na sepi a milema minu .
51003017	Okakɔni mokina mojɔ , isa bobala , isa elomu , kɔni ngando jisusu a kombe eKumu Yesu , na sakoani Njambe Sango a kombe ende .
51003018	Ino bali , toma dani na lisuma ai bami banu ; obwanini boda boa a tei eKumu .
51003019	Ino bami , toma dani na ngɛnjɔ ai bali banu ; pɛ bodani na bu bɛlɛbɛlɛ .
51003020	Ino bɛngɛ , toma sumani baboti banu a ngando jisusu ; mojɔ momina mosepejaka Kumu .
51003021	Ino basango , pɛ botukoani bana banu , bo milema Mibu misaka ngwa .
51003022	Ino bakɔmɛli , sumakani baswa banu ya nase a mijɔ misusu ; pɛ bokɔni elomu enu a miso mabu pɛ , a bosepeja bato ; kɔni na milema minu misusu na lisuma ai Kumu .
51003023	Kɔni bilomu binu bisusu na bingi , o bakɔmɛli baKumu , te bakɔmɛli babato .
51003024	Jebani bo ôsɔni lisango ai Kumu o ndese enu . Kɔmɛni Masiya Kumu .
51003025	Mojɔ bo moto yona okɔkɔ bobe âsɔ ndese ebobe . Njambe adi oko na mwɛngi momɔci pɛ a mojɔ mobato basusu .
51004001	Ino baswa , anejani ekɔmɛli epele ebɔngɔke ai bakɔmɛli banu ; pɛ bobosani bo ino bɛnɛ odini koko na Moswa’nu a Diko .
51004002	Dani na lingbangba a bonga ; sɛnjɛlɛni a bonga na sepi .
51004003	Ingani a mojɔ mosu pongono , bo Njambe ahojae njea ai so a botɔndɔ mojɔ mobombamake moMasiya ; mbi nadi a minyɔlɔ oko a mojɔ momina .
51004004	Ingani bo nabolojae mojɔ momina a bohu na ebaeli yena ebwani .
51004005	Kinani bikɔmɛli bmu bidae na bowɛi a mojɔ mobato basokolu ; pɛ bonamejani masu manu .
51004006	Kinani epaeli ehenge ebaeli enu o ahengaka moto mia na mukwa , bo ojebeni bosɔnibeja ebaeli yena ebwani ai moto na moto .
51004007	Tukiko adi botɔndɔ no mijɔ mimbi misusu . Iyo adi mwangwa ’ mbi oepaeli , na mokɔmɛli osoti , na akɔmɛkɛ Kumu o akɔkɔ mbi .
51004008	Mbi namolomi ai no oko a mojɔ momina , bo ake mwako monu , na apingejae milema minu .
51004009	Nalomi koko Onesimo , mwangwa’mbi osoti na oepaeli , yona odi moto onu bɛnɛ . Ibo badi bopa no mwako mosusu mosu jɔnɔ .
51004010	Alisitaluko , yona odi na mbi a blɔkɔ , alomeaka no njɛhɛ , na Malako pongono , pako eBalanaba ( o’sɔni monɔkɔ a mojɔ monde ; akadoa ai no , mo’sɔni bopele ) ,
51004011	na Yesu yona odi na kombe Yuse-to ; BaYuda baya bakɔmejaka mbi a elomu eBokumu boNjambe , oko bo basato pɛ , na bagɔmbejai molema mombi .
51004012	Epapulo , moto onu bɛnɛ , alomeaka no njɛbɛ pongono . Iyo adi mokɔmɛli oMasiya , na angaka a mojɔ monu na bingi bihole bisusu , bo odaeni bato bapingake na bambilimake a bosuma bolulea boNjambe bosusu .
51004013	Mbi nadi monjɛnɛki obingi ende a mojɔ monu , na a mojɔ mobato baLaodikia , na bato baYelapoli .
51004014	Luka , monganga oepaeli , na Dema , babɛjɛkɛ no njɛbɛ .
51004015	Abɛjɛni baninga baLaodikia ; abɛjɛni Numpa , na Denga lia lidi a ndako ende .
51004016	Okasiejani bolanga mokanda mu a tei enu , pɛ bobosani bo bamolange a Denga diLaodikia ; ino ko toma langani mokanda moLaodikia pongono .
51004017	Pani Alukipo monɔkɔ mu ; Banea elomu esɔ wɛ ai Kumu , bo okɔe elomu emina na soti .
51004018	Asɔni njɛbɛ embi Paulo na ebɔ embi embi mɛnɛ . Pɛ bobosani minyɔlɔ mimbi . Yɛ monganji moNjambe modae na nu .
52001001	Paulo na Sakwano na Timoteo a Denga diBaTɛsalɔnike dia didi a a tei eNjambe Sango na Kumu Yesu Masiya . Yɛ monganji moNjambe na bowi bodae na nu .
52001002	Iso bosakoaka Njambe bihole bisusu a mojɔ monu , na bota-bosaka no nongo mweka a ma’nga masu .
52001003	Mojɔ bo bolɛkɛ elomu eejimeli enu , elomu enu eepaeli , na njingo enu yena etambɛkɛ , ai Kumu osu Yesu Masiya , a boso boNjambe Sangwa’su .
52001004	Baninga , Njambe adi na nu ngɛnjɔ , na so bojebaka bo yo ahɔ no .
52001005	Mwako Mopele mosu moidoa ai no na kɔpi pɛ ; modoa na ngulu , na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke , na ejimeli enɛnɛ . Ojebakani ekɔmɛli yena edaka na su a tei enu a mojɔ monu .
52001006	Okoanani na su , na Masiya pongono , yana asɔ no Ebaeli a minɔngɔ minɛnɛ , na osepani na sepi eMwembo Mosɛnɔke .
52001007	Oko boa onejani ekoaneli ai bato basusu baejimeli a Makedonia na a Akaya .
52001008	Mojɔ bo onanganejani Mwako Mopele moKumu , te a Makedoma na a Akaya pɛ ; bato bajebaka mojɔ moejimeli enu a bisika bisusu , so bɛnɛ pɛ bobatɔndɔ .
52001009	Bato bamina babalaka a mojɔ mobodoa bosu ai no , bo o’sɔni so bopele , na bo okwani bosakoa bobilimo , na ohekoani ai Njambe , a bokɔmɛ Njambe osoti na obomɔ ,
52001010	na a bo’mba bohula boMwana’nde oho Diko yona ongɔjɔ yo a bogwa , oko Yesu yona ohelejaka so a likundu lia likɛkɛ adoe .
52002001	Baninga , ojebakani no bɛnɛ bo mɔngɔ mokɛ so ai no moidaloa nongo .
52002002	Nongo ama so dingoa na ama so samboa a Pilipoi , bomi hɛ oko na eci eNjambe , o ajebaka no , a botɔndɔ no Mwako Mopele moNjambe o bila mɛnɛ .
52002003	Eleho esu editi na bokosea , isa bosɔtɔ , isa epulu .
52002004	Iso botɔndɔkɔ mwako a bokumeja Njambe yona onjaka milema misu , te a bosepeja bato ; mojɔ bo Njambe yo mɛnɛ ajima bo akine Mwako Mopele a mɔmɔ masu .
52002005	Ojebakani no bɛnɛ bo boitombea no na bibaeli bisu . Na boimeka bodiha likonja na poloso ; Njambe yo mɛnɛ adi monjɛnɛki osu .
52002006	Boipala bo bato bakumejae so , isa no bɛnɛ , isa bato batongo . Nongo adaka so babwɛnji baMasiya , boipala bo bodae muna ai no .
52002007	Bodaka na bo yɛmbu mɛnɛ a tei enu , o ekɔmɛli emwali yona obimbaka bana bande lipaapoko .
