52002008	Oko boa , adaka so na epaeli enɛnɛ ai no , bodaka na posa a bopa no milema misu bɛnɛ , te Mwako Mopele moNjambe pɛ , mojɔ bo bodaka na nu ngɛnjɔ .
52002009	Baninga , otabosakani elomu na monɔngɔ mosu . Yana atɔndɔkɔ so Mwako Mopele moNjambe a tei enu , bokɔkɔ elomu mabulu na mei bo botada nongo muna ai no .
52002010	Ekɔmɛli esu a tei enu baejimeli edaka esɛnɔke na bojo , pɛpɛ nongo mojɔ ; ino bɛnɛ odini banjɛnɛki bamojɔ momina , na Njambe pongono .
52002011	Ojebakani bo bodaka na nu basusu o adi sange ebana na bana bande . Boleha no moto na moto , bopingeja milema minu , na bongɔɔnɔ no
52002012	bo okumejaeni Njambe na mida minu , oko Njambe yona obea no a Bokumu bonde na ekumu ende .

52002014	Baninga , odakani bakoaneli baMenga maNjambe a tei eMasiya oho a Yuda ; mojɔ bo ino o’sɔni minɔngɔ ai bato balikota linu bɛnɛ , o asɔ bo ai BaYuda .

52002016	Batandanejaka so bo bosaka tɔndɔ bapakano Mwako Mopele bo bahele . Oko boa balume — jaka mwɛngi mojibe jibu bihole bisusu . Likundu ko liNjambe limei oko ai bo .

52003001	Mojɔ momina mogbasoa na su oko bogbasoa . A mojɔ momina , bojima bo mbi nadikae a Atena mbi buki .
52003002	Na boloma mwangwa’su Timoteo , mokɔmɛli oNjambe , a elomu eMwako Mopele moMasiya . Bomoloma bo ambilimejae no a ejimeli enu , na a boleha no ,
52003003	bo pɛpɛ nongo okina onu ombɛ a mojɔ mominɔngɔ mi . Ojebakani no bɛnɛ bo minɔngɔ midi oko libondo lisu .
52003004	Iso botomba botɔndɔ no eyou , yana adaka so a tei enu , bo bodi bonɛ minɔngɔ ; na ojebakani e dɛye bo modi oko boa .
52003005	A mojɔ momina , naihɔnɔ bo’mba koko , na naloma bo najebe mojɔ moejimeli enu . Nadaka na mokakwano bo Momeki asaka meka no , na elomu esu esaka nama .
52003006	Timoteo ko adongi oho ai no na amei ya . Na yo atɔndɔi so mwako mopele moejimeli enu , na epaeli enu . Ajebejai so koko bo odini na bolɛ bopele ai so masu masusu , na bo odini na posa a bonɛnɛ na su , o adi so na posa a bonɛnɛ na nu .
52003007	A mojɔ momina baninga , nongo adi so na minɔngɔ na jɔɔlɔ so bɛnɛ , ejimeli enu esejai mokakwano mosu a mojɔ monu .

52003011	Yɛ Njambe Sangwa’su yo mɛnɛ , na Kumu osu Yesu , bapɛ so njea ai no .

52004001	Mojɔ motongo baninga ; okoanani na su ekɔmɛli yena ebwani na nu a bosepeja Njambe . Oko boa bongɔɔnɔkɔ no , na bolehaka no e dɛye a kombe eKumu Yesu , bo odaeni na ekɔmɛli emina . Okɔkɔni boa ; endele ko , toma nɔjɔni mwɛngi momina .
52004002	Ojebakani bokoja bosɔ so ai Kumu Yesu a bopa no .

52004006	Moto abwaniti bokosea , isa bokɔ bobe ai mwangwa’nde na mojɔ momina . Mojɔ bo Njambe akundaka likundu a mojɔ mojibe jia jisusu , o aleha so no na bopipo ehele .
52004007	Njambe aibea so bo bodae na bosɔtɔ ; abea so bo bodae na bosɛnɔ .
52004008	Oko boa , moto akasɛtoja ebaeli ye , atasɛtojaka moto ; asɛtojaka oko Njambe yona opaka no Mwembo Mosɛnɔke monde .
52004009	Ebɔngiti bo nasɔnee no a mojɔ moepaeli ai baninga , mojɔ bo Njambe yo mɛnɛ akoja no bo opalaneni .
52004010	Na ekɔmɛli enu edi boa soti ai baninga basusu baya badi a Makedonia . Pɛ mojɔ ; bole-haka no koko bo ohɛeni koko na epaeli bou mɛnɛ .
52004011	Kinani mida minu midae na bombɔki . Lɛni mijɔ minu bɛnɛ . Kɔni bilomu na mɔmɔ manu , o aleha so no boso .
52004012	Oko boa , bato bangondo badi bonɛ ekɔmɛli enu epele , na otadani nongo na taka .
52004013	Baninga , botapalaka bo odaeni a libumi a mojɔ mobato baya bagwa . Obwanitini bobayea o akɔkɔ bato batongo baya bapeliti nongo njingo .

53001004	A mojɔ momina , so bosakoaka no a Menga maNjambe , a mojɔ molingbangba na ejimeli enu , a tei eminɔngɔ na madingoa masɔkɔ no .

53001010	yana âdoa yo , bo basɛnɔke bande bamokumejae , na bato basusu baya bajimaka bakamoe a busa bomina ( cina bo ojimani tati esu a tei enu ) .
53001011	A mojɔ momina , so bongaka bihole bisusu a mojɔ monu , bo Njambe abɔngejae no a mojɔ mobobea bonu ; yɛ abɔngejae na ngulu ende mikano minu misusu mipele , na bilomu bisusu biejimeli enu ,

53002005	Obosaini bo mbi natɔndɔ no mijɔ mimina yana adaka mbi oho ai no ?

54002008	Napalaka bo bami ba’nge a bisika bisusu , na bangɔjɔe mɔmɔ masɛnɔke , pɛpɛ kɛlɛ , pɛpɛ kitɛ .
54002009	Napalaka koko bo bali baiwae bisenja bia bibɔngi , te nongo na jala , na posa bo basanejae . Babwaniti bobaka swe jimosɛsɛ , isa na manaka na leka loyumu , isa mokina molilo moyumu .
54002010	Elwali yena ebwani na bali baejimeli edi oko bikɔmɛli bipele .
54002011	Mwali adi bohokea bokoja na bowi , na lisuma linɛnɛ .
54002012	Mbi nitajimaka bo mwali akojae bami isa bo adae na kpaci ai bo ; adi boda oko bogo .
54002013	Mojɔ bo Adama ayoama boso , Ewa ko ngɔngɔ .
54002014	Na Adama ailɛngɛmɛ ; yona olɛngɛmɛ na yona okwa , oko mwali .
54002015	Endele ko , mwali adi bohela na bohota , akayeyoa na ejimeli , na epaeli , na bosɛnɔ , na yongi .
54003001	Isa moto apalaka asɛ elomu emonjeli oDenga , apalaka elomu epele ; mojɔ momina modi soti .
54003002	Monjeli oDenga ko adi boda na esako epele mɛnɛ , momi omwali omɔci pɛ , moto obowi na molema motitake , moto oyongi epele yona odi na monganji ai bato , na bowɛi a bokoja ;
54003003	te nongo moto obolangoa , isa moto okɛlɛ , oko moto obowi ; te nongo moto omiano , isa moto yona odi na posa eli-konja .
54003004	Abwani boda na kpaci a ndako ende mɛnɛ , na bobanea bana bande mɛnɛ , bo badae na lisuma , na ekɔmɛli epele .
54003005	Mojɔ bo , moto amiti hɔnɔ elomu endako ende mɛnɛ , adi bobanea Denga diNjambe na ye ?
54003006	Monjeli abwaniti boda mocingami moyene , asaka sɛ bodumba boSatana a mojɔ moegbo ende .
54003007	Abwani boda na gala epele a boso bobato basokolu , bo atasamboa , na bo ata’ta elambo eSatana .
54003008	Basuku baDenga pongono badi boda bato bayongi epele , m nongo bato baminɔkɔ Mibae , isa bato babolangoa , isa bato baya badi na posa elikonja .
54003009	Badi bobanea mijɔ miejimeli a milema misɛnɔke .
54003010	Bopele bo bapete meka ; na bakapasama na soti , pɛpɛ nongo mojɔ , babwani bokɔ elomu ebasuku baDenga .
54003011	Bali babu pongono badi boda na yongi epele , te nongo bato babiloli , oko bato babowi na lisuma a ngando jisusu .
54003012	Mosuku oDenga abwani boda na mwali omɔci pɛ ; badi boda na kpaci ai bana babu , na a ndako jibu bɛnɛ .
54003013	Ibaya bakɔkɔ elomu epele emosuku oDenga badi na esako epele , na bahɛkɛ na eci a ejimeli ai Yesu Masiya .
54003014	Nadi na njingo bo nadoe oho ai wɛ ngɔngɔ mweka ; endele ko nasɔnei wɛ mijɔ mimi
54003015	bo nakayeyoa a bodoa , odi bojeba moda mua mobwani na bato bandako eNjambe , yena edi Denga diNjambe obomɔ , likwe na eyoeli-ecina esoti .
54003016	Cina eejimeli esu ai Njambe enɔi bocingea bomoto . Mojɔ momina modi soti mɛnɛ . Iyo asaboloja a mokuku momoto ; Mwembo mongameja mojɔ monde ; Babwɛnji baDiko bamonɛ ; Makota mangondo maka mwako monde ; Bato bangondo bamojimea ; Asɔmɔ a ekumu eDiko .
54004001	Mwembo mobalaka na bohu mɛnɛ bo bakina bato badi bolaboa a ejimeli a masu masuka . Bâhokea miembo Mibokosea , na bokoja bomiembo Mibe ,
54004002	cina epoloso ebakoja babokosea . Milema Mibato bamina midi o migo .
54004003	Balembaka bato bo batalongana , na bakojaka bo bato badi bokia leka . Njambe yo mɛnɛ akɔ leka lomina , bo baya bajimaka na bajebaka mijɔ misoti , baloyaka na sepi na bo’nga .
54004004	Mojɔ bo leka losusu lokɔ Njambe lodi lopele . Pɛpɛ nongo eka emɔci edi na ekia ; bobwani bosɔ leka losusu na bosakoa ;
54004005	edi eka esɛnɔke a mojɔ moEbaeli eNjambe na bo’nga .
54004006	Okalɛjɛ baninga ngando jimina , ôda mokɔmɛli mopele oMasiya Yesu yona obeki na bikenge biejimeli , na bokoja bopele boma wɛ sɔ .
54004007	Toma lona ko masɔ mangasa maya mapeliti cina . Kɔ bo odae mopingake a ngando jiNjambe .
54004008	Bopingeja bomokuku bodi mojɔ mopele mweka ; ngando jiNjambe ko jibɔngejaka a njea jisusu , na jidi na sako a mojɔ momohelo mu , na mua modi ngɔngɔ .
54004009	Mojɔ momina modi soti mɛnɛ , na mobwani na ejimeli esusu .
54004010	A mojɔ momina so bokɔkɔ elomu na bosamboaka , cina bo njingo esu edi ai Njambe obomɔ , yona odi Moheleja obato boya , gbo oko baya bajimaka .
54004011	Leha na koja ngando jimina .
54004012	T’okine oko bo moto asɛtojae wɛ mojɔ bo odi oko mwɛnga pɛ . Aneja bato baejimeli ekoaneli epele na ebaeli ewɛ na moda mowɛ , a mojɔ moepaeli , na ejimeli , na bosɛnɔ .
54004013	Adi mbi pɛ bopeta doa , toma da na bingi a bolanga mokanda moNjambe , a botɔndɔ mwako moNjambe , na a bokoja .
54004014	T’onamejae oko epeeli yena edi a tei ewɛ ; oesɔ na bileho yana abakea basuku baDenga mɔmɔ mabu ai wɛ .
54004015	Kɔ ngando jimina na bingi ; kɔ na molema mowɛ mosusu , bo bato basusu badi bonɛ bo ohɛkɛ na ngulu .
54004016	Toma sɛnjɛlɛ bopele a mojɔ mowɛ mɛnɛ , na a mojɔ mobokoja bowɛ . Okakɔ boa , odi bohela wɛ mɛnɛ , na odi boheleja bato baya bakaka wɛ .
54005001	T’olemoe oko na mosuku na bopipo ; moleha ko o sangwao . Leha bami batongo o baninga .
54005002	Kina basuku bali badae o bangwao , na bali batongo o ngɛnɛ , oko na lisuma linɛnɛ .
54005003	Da na lisuma ai bali-babogwa basoti .
54005004	Isa mwali-obogwa adi na bana , isa pape , ibaba badi bopeta cingea bo babwani boda na likabo ai bato babu bɛnɛ , na monganji ai baboti babu . Njambe yo mɛnɛ ajimaka mojɔ momina .
54005005	Mwali-obogwa ko osoti yona opeliti bato , adi na njingo ai Njambe , na angaka Njambe na bulu na mei , na bingeeli na mangɔɔnɔ .
54005006	Mwali-obogwa ko yona odi na posa engando jingondo , nongo adi yo mɔ , adi oko mogwake .
54005007	Toma baleha na bopipo a mojɔ mongando ji , bo batakwa na mijɔ .
54005008	Isa moto atabaneaka bato bande mɛnɛ , na bato badenga dinde mɛnɛ , moto omina angani ejimeli , na anɔi mopakano na bobe .
54005009	Mwali-obogwa amiti nɔ bianga domi-isamano , mwali omomi omɔci pɛ , kombe ende ebwaniti bosɔnɔmɔ a mokanda mobali-babogwa .
54005010	Adi boda na esako epele a mojɔ mobikɔmɛli binde bipele , mwali yona obɔkɔ bana , yona odaka na monganji ai bakɛndɛli , yona ososa bibota bibato baDenga , yona okɔmeja bato baya badaka na monɔngɔ , na odaka na bingi a ngando jisusu jipele .
54005011	Pɛ bojima bali-babogwa baya badi oko baseka pɛ , mojɔ bo posa jibu jikagbasoa , badi bolona Masiya , na bâpala bo balongane koko .
54005012	Oko boa bakwaka na mojɔ , cina bo bakinaka ejimeli ebu eboso .
54005013	Mojɔ motongo — adi bo pɛ elomu , balandoaka na ekɔmɛli ebongɛ a ndako ndako . Na baditi oko edada pɛ ; badi na bibalabala , na ekpai , na babalaka mijɔ mia Mibɔngiti na bu .
54005014	A mojɔ momina , mbi napalaka bo bali-babogwa baya baditi basuku balongane koko , babote bana na babanee ndako jibu . Oko boa , baya badi na su soki batadiha njea a bololea so .
54005015	Mojɔ bo bakina balaboa soti a bosusa Satana .
54005016	Isa moto oejimeli , kako momi , kako mwali , adi na bali-babogwa baya bacingi na nde , abwani bobakɔmeja . Oko boa Denga ditada na muna mobu , na lidi bokɔmeja bali-babogwa baya badi na taka .
54005017	Bato babwani boda na lisuma linɛnɛ ai basuku baDenga baya bakɔkɔ elomu epele , gbo oko ai baya badi na elomu ebotɔndɔ Mwako Mopele , na ebokoja .
54005018	Mojɔ bo mokanda moNjambe mobalaka bo , T’okande oko ebombo engɔmbɔ yona ondaka ndongo . Na Mokɔmɛli abwani bosɔ likonja linde .
54005019	Bakalanga kombe emosuku oDenga na mokina mojɔ , obwaniti boka mojɔ momina isa batati babae kako basato baditi .
54005020	Isa bakina bakɔkɔ bobe , toma lemoa na bu a boso bobato basusu , bo batongo babange .
54005021	Mbi nalehaka wɛ a hoso boNjambe , na Masiya Yesu , na babwɛnji baDiko baya bahɔmɔ , bo okɔe ngando jimina na bojo mɛnɛ ; da na ekɔmɛli emɔci ai bato basusu amɛci .
54005022	A mojɔ mobobakea mɔmɔ ai moto , pɛ bokɔ mojɔ momina na pɛlɛpɛlɛ . Pɛ bopanda na moto a bobe bonde . Anganjama bo otada nongo na mojɔ .
54005023	T’omwake oko madiba pɛ ; odi bomwaka ekenge ekɛkɛlɛkɛ evino a mojɔ mosɔpɔ na bipeko bipekaka na wɛ mandɛli-mandɛli .
54005024	Jibe jibakina bato jidi a bohu , oko basa-mbakini ; jia jibakwa batongo ko jiboloaka oko ngɔngɔ .
54005025	Bikɔmɛli bipele bidi koko a bohu boa , na bia biditi a bohu biboloa ngɔngɔ .
54006001	Bato basusu baya badi a libuli babwani boda na lisuma ai baswa’bu , bo kombe eNjambe etasamboa , na bokoja bosu pongono .
54006002	Isa baswa’bu badi na ejimeli , babwaniti bobanyamola na mokalo bo badi baninga . Badi bonɔ na bingi a bobakɔmɛ , mojɔ bo bakɔmɛkɛ bato baejimeli baya babwani bosɔ epaeli . Ikoja na leha ngando jimina .
54006003	Isa moto akojaka mijɔ Mibokosea , pɛ bojima bikenge bibɔngɔke biKumu osu Yesu Masiya , na bokoja bua bocingi na ekɔmɛli emoto oNjambe ,
54006004	moto omina adi oko na egbo ; t’ajebake nongo mojɔ . Adi oko na posa emisoo na kitɛ ; na ekɔmɛli emina engɔjɔkɔ likaka , na miano , na biloli , na nduki emijɔ ,
54006005	na bibalabala a tei ebato baya badi balaboake a milema Mibu ; bapeliti nongo mojɔ mosoti , na badingaka bo ejimeli al Njambe edi njea a bokonja likonja .
54006006	Ejimeli ai Njambe ko yena editi na bomboa boleka , ebwani na bokonja bolikonja lmɛnɛ .
54006007	Mojɔ bo bodoaka a ngondo ye boa ngasa , na bokayana , botahɔnɔ botomba eka ernɔci .
54006008	Isa bodi na mia na bisenja , leka lomina lobwani na su .
54006009	Ibaya badi na posa elikonja bakwaka a ndingea , na bataka elambo , na balaboaka na posa jibe jingasa jia jidindejaka bato a bogwa na bodimoa .
54006010	Mojɔ bo posa elikonja edi cina ejibe jisusu . Bakina bato balaboi a njea eejimeli oko a mojɔ moposa emina , na basandeaka na ndɛ jiminɔngɔ minɛnɛ .
54006011	Wɛ ko , moto oNjambe , toma bulɛ ngando jimina . Dala a njea ebodongo , na yongi epele , na epaeli , na lingbangba , na bombɔki .
54006012	Ina bila epele eejimeli . Pea bomɔ boku , bomɔ bua botasia . Obeama a mojɔ momina , na otata tati epele a boso bobatati banɛnɛ .
54006013	Nalehaka wɛ a boso boNjambe yona opaka bato basusu bomɔ , na a boso boMasiya Yesu yona otata tati epele a boso boPontio Pilato ,
54006014	bo osume mobeko , bo moda mowɛ motada na litɔnɔ , pɛpɛ nongo mojɔ , oko a bodoa boKumu osu Yesu Masiya .
54006015	Iyona obojongoa , yona odi na ngulu esusu , Koi o baroi , na Kumu obakumu , adi boneja mojɔ momina oko ehole ekabwana .
54006016	Iyo pɛ aditi nongo na bogwa ; adi a bohu bua bonɔi , bo moto atahɔnɔ bobatama ; moto amonɛkini na atahɔnɔ bomonɛ . Ekumu ai yo , na bokumu , oko na bosusu . Amen .
54006017	Leha bato baya badi na likonja a ngondo ye bo batasakumeja , na bo batada na ejimeli a makonja maya madi na mokakwano , oko ai Njambe yona opaka so leka na likabo linɛnɛ a bosepeja so .
54006018	Baleha bo bakɔe bopele , bo bahɛe na bikɔmɛli bipele , na bo badae na monganji na likabo .
54006019	Oko boa badi bobomba likonja liyumua mojɔ moehole ebodoa , a edejai esoti , bo badae na bomɔ bua bodi bomɔ bosoti .
54006020	Ee Timoteo , banea elomu esɔ wɛ a bobanea . Bulɛ ko bibaeli bibokosea , na bibalabala biejebeli yena editi ejebeli esoti ,
54006021	mojɔ bo bakina bato basɔ mijɔ mimina , na balaboa a njea eejimeli . Yɛ monganji moNjambe modae na wɛ .
55001001	Mbi Paulo , obwɛnji oMasiya Yesu cina ebolulea boNjambe , a mojɔ mosako ebomɔ bua bodi a tei eMasiya Yesu , ai Timoteo , mwana’mbi oepaeli
55001002	yɛ monganji , na wa , na bowi boNjambe Sango , na Masiya Yesu Kumu osu bodae na wɛ .
55001003	Mbi nasakoaka Njambe yana alɛkɛ mbi wɛ a ma’nga mambi bihole bisusu na bulu na moi , mbi yona omokɔmɛkɛ na molema mosɛnɔke o amokɔmɛ basangwa’mbi .
55001004	Alɛkɛ mbi mbisoli jiwɛ , nadi na posa a bo’nɛnɛ na wɛ , bo molema mombi molume na sepi .
55001005	Mbi te nabosake bo odi na ejimeli esoti , oko ejimeliyena edaka na Loi tata owɛ , na ngwao Eunike . Najebaka koko na soti bo ejimeli emina edi a tei ewɛ pongono .
55001006	A mojɔ momina , nalehaka wɛ a bohɛjɛ epeeli eNjamhe a tei ewɛ , o abwanejaka moto mosa , oko epeeli esɔ wɛ na bobakea bomɔmɔ mambi .
55001007	Mojɔ bo Njambe aipa so mwembo mobomɛli , oko mwembo mongulu , na epaeli , na bowɛi .
55001008	A mojɔ momina , obwaniti boda na sɔni a botata tati ai Kumu osu , isa a mojɔ mombi lisungu linde . Asɔ ko libondo limonɔngɔ mosɔkɔ mbi a mojɔ moMwako Mopele , o apaka Njambe wɛ ngulu .
55001009	Iyo abohelejai na abobei a elomu esɛnɔke , te a mojɔ mobilomu bisu bɛnɛ , oko a mojɔ momokano monde mɛnɛ , na monganji monde mopa yo so a tei eMasiya Yesu oko a libangake mɛnɛ .
55001010	Monganji momina moboloi e dɛye na bodoa boMoheleja osu Masiya Yesu , yona ogbokeja bogwa , na ameja bomɔ a bohu , na bomɔ bua botagwa , a mojɔ moMwako Mopele .
55001011	Mbi nahɛngɛmɛ bo nadae motɔndɔi , na obwɛnji , na mokoja oMwako momina ,
55001012	na nadingoaka a mojɔ momina ; pɛ mojɔ , naditi nongo na sɔni , cina bo mbi najebaka yona ojimaka mbi , na najebaka na soti bo yo abwani bobanea mua mopeja mbi yo , oko a Busa bomina .
55001013	Kina bokoja bosoti bosɔ wɛ ai mbi bodae ekoaneli ai wɛ ; bobanea na ejimeli , na epaeli , ai Masiya Yesu .
55001014	Banea mojɔ moyumu mosɔ wɛ , oko na ngulu eMwembo Mosɛnɔke , mua modi a tei ewɛ .
55001015	Ojebaka bo bato basusu baAsia baloni mbi , na Pugelo na Elumogene pongono .
55001016	Nangaka Kumu bo adae na monganji a denga diOnesipolo , mojɔ bo yo asepeja molema mombi bihole binɛnɛ , na aika sɔni a mojɔ mominyɔlɔ mimbi .
55001017	Yana amea yo a Loma , aduka mbi na bingi enɛnɛ na aboloja mbi .
55001018	Yɛ Kumu ajime bo Kumu amokɔe monganji a Busa bomina . Ojebaka koko na bopele mɛnɛ bo akɔmeja mbi a Ɛpɛsɔ bou mɛnɛ .
55002001	Wɛ ko mwana’mbi , da moto ongulu a mojɔ momonganji mua modi a tei eMasiya Yesu .
55002002	Jebeja bato baejimeli ngando jika wɛ ai mbi a boso bobatati banɛnɛ , bo babwane bokoja bato batongo .
55002003	Adi wɛ soda mopele oMasiya Yesu , asɔ libondo liwɛ limonɔngɔ .
55002004	Isa moto adi soda , abɔtɔni na bilomu bitongo bingondo , bo ase-pejae kapitɛni onde .
55002005	Na moto yona opotaka mbambano amiti suma Mibeko mimakou , atalonga nongo .
55002006	Moswa ’ gbie , yona okɔkɔ elomu , abwani bosɔ libondo liboso limbuma jigbie .
55002007	Toma lɛ mijɔ Mibalaka mbi ; Kumu adi bopa wɛ bocinea a mojɔ mongando jisusu .
55002008	Kina bolɛ bowɛ bodae ai Yesu Masiya ombota eDawidi yona ongɔ a bogwa ; Mwako Mopele mombi oko mu .
55002009	Mbi nadingoaka o moto mobe , na nadi a minyɔlɔ a mojɔ momina . Ebaeli eNjambe ko editi a minyɔlɔ .
55002010	Na mbi nahɔnɔkɔ ngando ji jisusu a mojɔ moBahɔmɔke , ho ’ bo pongono basɛ mohelo mua modi ai Masiya Yesu , na ekumu yena edi na hosusu .
55002011	Ebaeli ye edi soti ; isa bogwi na nde , bôhela na nde pongono .
55002012	Bokayeyoa na lingbangba , bôkumejama koko na nde . Bokamongana ko , yo adi bongana so .
55002013	Nongo ejimeli ekataka na su , yo t’akputojake nongo sako , mojɔ bo aditi bosa’ngana yo mɛnɛ .
55002014	Toma lɛjɛ bato ngando jimina , na baleha a boso boNjambe bo batanoana moano a mojɔ mobikenge bikɔpi . Mojɔ momina mobɔngiti , na mobejaka milema Mibato baya bakaka .
55002015	Kɔ na ngulu ewɛ esusu bo opasame a boso boNjambe , o moto yona oditi na sɔni a mojɔ moelomu ende , yona odi na bɛtɛ a elomu eEbaeli eSoti .
55002016	Toma bɔtɔnɔ ko na bibalabala na kitɛ jingasangasa . Mojɔ bo ngando jimina jidi bolaboja bato a njea jibe ,
55002017	na bokoja bobu bodi o pola emonio yena ehɛkɛ a boyaka mokuku .
55002018	Umenaio na Pileto badi a libondo limina . Ibo bapengoi a njea esoti ; babalaka bo bo’ngɔ a bogwa bosia ehele , na babejaka ejimeli ebakina bato .
55002019	Pɛ mojɔ ; eyoeli-ecina embilimake eNjambe eyeyoaka , yena edi na mosɔnɔ mu , Kumu ajebaka bato bande mɛnɛ . na Yɛ moto na moto yona ongaka a kombe eKumu acie bobe .
55002020	Ndako enɛnɛ editi na bisɛi biwɔlɔ na palata pɛ . Bikina biyoama na mole na libali pongono . Bikina bidi a mojɔ moelomu epele , na bikina bitongo bidi a mojɔ moelomu engasa .
55002021	Moto akasabanea na bosɛnɔ , na akabɔtɔnɔ na ngando jimina , yo ada esɛi eekumu yena esɛnoi a mojɔ moelomu emoswa’nde , na ebwani na bilomu bisusu bipele .
55002022	Cia posa jibe jimwenga . Susa na bingi njea ebodongo , ejimeli , epaeli , bowi , na bato baya basakoaka Kumu na milema misɛnɔke .
55002023	Toma lona ko bibalabala bingasa na bikitɛ . Ojebaka bo bingɔjɔkɔ oko miano pɛ .
55002024	Mokɔmɛli ko oKumu abwaniti bonoana moano ; adi boda na molema mo yɛmbu ai bato basusu , na bɛtɛ ebokoja , moto olingbangba .
55002025	Adi boleha baya badi na nde soki oko na bo yɛmbu , na njingo bo Njambe abasɛ dosa bo bajɛbɛ Soti .
55002026	Oko boa , bakasisoa , badi bohela a elambo eSatana yona obapea masungu bo bakɔe bolulea bonde .
55003001	Toma jeba bo ehole eminɔngɔ edabi a masu masuka .
55003002	Mojɔ bo epaeli ebato edabi oko ai bo bɛnɛ ; badabi na posa elikonja , bato baegbo na jala , bato babosambolu , bato balipanga ai baboti , pɛ lisuma , bato bapɔmbɔli ,
55003003	bato baya bapeliti nongo epaeli , bato baya bakputojaka sako , bato babiloli , bato baya basumaka oko posa jibu bɛnɛ , bato basanga , soki jibato bapele ,
55003004	bato bangabi , bato baelabe baya basakumejaka bo bɛnɛ ; na Njambe na bo bɛnɛ , bapa-laka gbo oko bo bɛnɛ .
55003005	Badabi na ekina elimo eejimeli ai Njambe a sokolu , banganabi ko ngulu eejimeli emina .
55003006	Pɛ bopangana nongo na bato baya badi na bikɔmɛli bimina . Mojɔ bo bakina babu bakweaka a tei ebato na poloso , na bapangoaka bali ba yɛmbu baya bangwai muna mojibe jibu , bali baya badingoaka na posa jibe jinɛnɛ ,
55003007	baya bakoaka bihole bisusu , pɛ ko bomea a ejebeli eSoti .
55003008	Yane na Yambele baswiana na Mose eyou ; bato bamina ko baswianaka na Soti ; milema Mibu mipɔi , na ejimeli ebu edi oko ejimeli ebokosea .
55003009	Elomu ebu etabɔngɔ ko , mojɔ bo bato basusu badi bonɛ libunga libu a bohu , o anɛ bo libunga libato ba babae .
55003010	Wɛ ko ojebaka na bopele mɛnɛ bokoja bombi , ekɔmɛli embi , mokano mombi , ejimeli embi , lingbangba limbi , epaeli embi , bombɔki bombi ,
55003011	bodingoa na minɔngɔ mimbi , na mijɔ minɛ mbi a Antiokia , a Ikonia na a Lusetulia . Nasɔ bodingoa bonɛnɛ na eci ; Njambe ko ahelejani a minɔngɔ mi misusu .
55003012	Ee , bato basusu baya bapalaka bosusa Yesu Masiya na soti badi bodingoa .
55003013	Bato babe ko , na bato babokosea badi bohɛ na bobe ; badi balaboake bo bɛnɛ , na balabojaka bato batongo pongono .
55003014	Wɛ ko yeyoa a ngando jikoa wɛ . Ojijimaka na soti , na ojebaka baya bakoja wɛ .
55003015	Olandoa na Mokanda moNjambe oko a bwɛngɛ bowɛ , mua mobwani bopa wɛ bowɛi a mojɔ momohelo cina eejimeli ai Masiya Yesu .
55003016	Njambe asɔneja Misɔnɔ misusu na Mwembo monde ; Mibwani a mojɔ mobokoja , a mojɔ moboleha , a honeja mabunga , na a bojebeja ngando jisoti ,
55003017	bo moto yona odi moto oNjambe adae mobɔngɔke , na adae na molilo mosusu a bokɔ bilomu bisusu bipele .
55004001	Mbi nalehaka wɛ a boso boNjambe , na a boso boMasiya Yesu yona odi bosambeja bahelake na bagwake ; nalehaka wɛ a mojɔ mobodoa bonde na bokumu bonde .
55004002	Tɔndɔ Mwako Mopele na bingi , isa na pela , isa na ngange . Lemoa na bato ; basia , baleha , na pɛ bongwa nongo bokoja .
55004003	Mojɔ bo ehole ekɛkɛ adoe bo bato batahɔnɔ bohokea bokoja bosoti . Badi boduka bakoja banɛnɛ o apa-laka milema Mibu bɛnɛ , mojɔ bo matoi mabu môda na kalakala a boka mijɔ miyene .
55004004	Batahokea koko mijɔ misoti , na bâhekoa oko a masɔ .
55004005	Wɛ ko , sabekea bihole bisusu . Da na eci a tei ebodingoa . Kɔ elomu emotɔndɔi oMwako Mopele . Kɔ ngando jisusu jia jicingi na elomu ewɛ .
55004006	A mojɔ mombi mɛnɛ , edikai mweka pɛ bo makia mambi masopee o lisiko . Ehole embi eboyana edi hulelu .
55004007	Mbi nani etumba epele . Namei a suka enjea embambano . Nabanei ejimeli .
55004008	E dɛye , likongo libodongo lisɛlingoami a mojɔ mombi ; Kumu yona osambejaka na soti , âebakea ai mbi a busa bomina ; te nongo ai mbi pɛ , oko ai bato basusu baya badi na posa ebodoa bonde .
55004009	Kenga bodoa ai mbi ngɔngɔ mweka , mojɔ bo Dema akini mbi .
55004010	Iyo adi oko na posa engando jingondo ye , na akɛi a Tɛsalɔnike . Kulusene akɛi a Galatia . Tito akɛi a Dalamatia .
55004011	Odikai na mbi oko Luka pɛ . Bea Malako ; doa na nde pongono , mojɔ bo yo abwani bokɔmeja mbi a elomu .
55004012	Nalomi Tukiko a Ɛpɛsɔ .
55004013	Okadoa , doa na kasaka eyai ekina mbi a ndako eKalupo a Toloa , na mikanda pongono ; na pɛ bobosa nongo mikanda Mibosɔnɔ .
55004014	Alesandele , molui oliboma , anɔngeja mbi bou mɛnɛ . Kumu ko adi bomopa ndese yena ebwani na bikɔmɛli binde .
55004015	Toma nganjama wɛ mɛnɛ na moto omina , mojɔ bo adaka na lisoki linɛnɛ a mwako mosu .
55004016	A ehole eesambi embi eboso , pɛpɛ nongo moto oyeyoa a dɔngɔ dimbi . Ibo basusu bakina mbi oko bokina . Nangaka bo Njambe aba yɛe mojɔ momina .
55004017	Kumu ko adaka ami a dɔngɔ dimbi , na apani ngulu a botɔndɔ Mwako Mopele mosusu , bo bapakano basusu ba’ke . Oko boa nahela a mino magbɔngɔ .
55004018	Kumu adi boheleja mbi a ndungu jisusu jibe , na âbanea mbi a mojɔ moBokumu bonde boDiko . Ekumu ai yo oko na bosusu ! Amen .
55004019	Abɛjɛ Puliseka na Akwila , na denga dionesipolo .
55004020	Elaseto adikai a Kolinto ; nakwa Tulopimo na yogo a Melita .
55004021	Kenga na bopipo a bodoa oko adi edidi epio pɛ bopeta mea . Yubulu abɛjɛkɛ wɛ njɛbɛ , na Pude , na Kulaudia , na baninga basusu babɛjɛkɛ wɛ pongono .
55004022	Yɛ Kumu adae na mwembo mowɛ . Yɛ monganji moNjambe modae ai no .
56001001	Mbi Paulo , mobuli oNjambe , na obwɛnji oYesu Masiya a mojɔ moejimeli ebahɔmɔke baNjambe , na ejebeli engando jisoti yena ebwani na ekɔmɛli ebato baNjambe ,
56001002	bo badae na njingo ebomɔ bua bodi na bosusu , bomɔ bodikeja Njambe a libangake mɛnɛ ; na yo Pakputojake nongo sako .
56001003	Na angameja ebaeli ende a ehole ebwanake , oko na bwɛnji bosɔ mbi na mobeko moNjambe Mobeleja osu :
56001004	Ai Tito , mwana’mbi osoti a tei eejimeli esu na wɛ . Yɛ monganji na bowi boNjambe Sango na Yesu Masiya Moheleja osu bodae na wɛ .
56001005	Mbi nakina wɛ a Kulete bo okolee mijɔ mia midika a bokolea , na a bohɔ basuku baDenga a ngando na ngando , o ama mbi tɔndɔ wɛ .
56001006	Mosuku oDenga abwani boda na ekɔmɛli esɛnɔke mɛnɛ , oko momi yona odi na mwali omɔci pɛ , na bana bande bato baejimeli baya baditi na lipanga , na baya baditi na gala ebe .
56001007	Mojɔ bo monjeli oDenga abwani boda na ekɔmɛli esɛnɔke yena ebwani na mokɔmɛli oNjambe , te nongo moto oegbo na kɛlɛ , isa moto obolangoa , isa moto odane , isa moto yona odi na posa elikonja .
56001008	Abwani boda na monganji ai bakɛndɛli , moto yona opalaka ngando jipele , moto obowi , moto oyongi , mosɛnɔke , moto obodongo ;
56001009	moto yona oPeaka Ebaeli esoti oko boku , oko Ebaeli esɔ yo na bokoja , bo abwane bokoja ngando jisoti na bogbokeja bato bakitɛ .
56001010	Mojɔ bo bato balipanga badi banɛnɛ , bato babibalabala na babokosea , gbo oko bato baejimeli eBaYuda .
56001011	Bato bamina babwani bogboka mojɔ bo babejaka milema mimenga manɛnɛ , na bakojaka ngando jia jibɔngiti nongo mweka , oko na njingo elikonja pɛ .
56001012	Okina obu , mowɛi obu bɛnɛ , abala bo , BaKulete badi bakosei bihole bisusu , tito babe , bato bayenga na baekusu .
56001013	Ekenge emina edi soti mɛnɛ . A mojɔ momina toma baleha na bopipo bo badae bato banjilake a Ejimeli ,
56001014	na bo batahokea masɔ maBaYuda , na Mibeko Mibato baya baloni njea esoti .
56001015	Ngando jisusu jidi jisɛnɔke ai bato basɛnɔke . Pɛ nongo mojɔ momɔci ko modi mosɛnɔke ai bapɔke na ai bato baya badi pɛ bojima , mojɔ bo milema Mibu , na bilɛli bibu , bidi bipɔke .
56001016	Batɔndɔkɔ na monɔkɔ bo bajebaka Njambe ; bamonganaka ko na bikɔmɛli bibu . Badi bato babosambolu , bato balipanga ; babɔngiti nongo na ekwa ekɔmɛli epele .
56002001	A mojɔ mowɛ mɛnɛ , koja mijɔ mia Mibwani na bokoja bosoti .
56002002	Leba basuku-bami bo badae na bodongo , bato bayongi na bombɔki , bato banjilake a Ejimeli , na epaeli , na lingbangba .
56002003	Leha basuku-bali bo badae na ekɔmɛli elisuma , te nongo na biloli , na bo batada nongo babuli babolangoa .
56002004	Badi bopa bileho bipele ; oko boa badi bokoja bali baya badi oko baseka pɛ , bo badae na epaeli ai bami babu na ai bana babu ,
56002005	bo badae na yongi epele , te nongo na ndukeli , bato babingi a elomu endako jibu , bato baepaeli na lisuma ai bami babu , bo Ebaeli eNjambe etasamboa .
56002006	Leha koko menga bo basabekee .
56002007	Aneja wɛ mɛnɛ ekoaneli epele na bikɔmɛli biwɛ bisusu . Kina bokoja bowɛ bodae bokoja bosoti , bobwanake ; kina ebaeli ewɛ edae ebaeli esoti .
56002008	Oko boa batahɔnɔ bodumba wɛ , na yona odi na wɛ soki adi bosamboa , mojɔ bo ata’nɛ mojɔ mobe bo alolee so .
56002009	Leha babuli bo badae na lisuma ai baswa’bu , na bo babasepejae na bilomu bibu bisusu ; baditi boboma na bu kitɛ ;
56002010	baditi boda na liba ; babwani boda na lisuma linɛnɛ lisoti , bo bokoja boNjambe Moheleja osu bodae na gala epele a mojɔ mobikɔmɛli bibu bisusu .
56002011	Mojɔ bo monganji moNjambe moboloa a bohu a boheleja bato basusu .
56002012	Mokojaka so bo bolone ngando jisusu jia jikɛsɛni na njea eNjambe , bo bolone posa jingondo , bo bosangbindee , bo bodae na ekɔmɛli yena edi bojo , na lisuma ai Njambe a ngondo ye .
56002013	Bodibo’mba njingoesuyena enɔi , okoboboloa boekumu eNjambe osu monɛnɛ na Moheleja osu Yesu Masiya ,
56002014	yona osapa a mojɔ mosu , bo abosikoe a bobe bosusu , na bo abosɛnojae bo bodae oko ai yo mɛnɛ , bato babingi a bikɔmɛli bipele .
56002015	Koja ngando jimina . Leha , na lemoa na bato na kpaci enɛnɛ . T’ojime oko bo moto asɛtojae wɛ .
56003001	Lɛjɛ bato bo badi bosuma bakumu na basuku . Babwani boda na lisuma ; badi boda na mosɛlingo a bokɔ bilomu bisusu bipele .
56003002	Babwaniti bolɔngɔ nongo moto , isa boda na nduki emijɔ ; badi boda na milema mi yɛmbu , na bombɔki mɛnɛ , ai bato basusu .
56003003	Mojɔ bo so bɛnɛ bodaka boso na bogegele , na lipanga , bato balaboake , na babuli baposa jibe , na balisɔngi . Mida misu midaka masu masusu oko na bobe na likaka . Bato balona so , na so bolonana so bɛnɛ .
56003004	Yana ko aboloa monganji moNjambe Moheleja osu , na epaeli ende ai bato ,
56003005	yo aheleja so , te cina ebikɔmɛli bisu bipele , oko a mojɔ mowa ende mɛnɛ , na bosɛnoja bobobotama boyene , na eyoeli eyene eMwembo Mosɛnɔke
56003006	mosopa yo na likabo linɛnɛ ai so a tei eYesu Masiya Moheleja osu ,
56003007	bo bolonge cina emo-nganji monde , na bo bodae basangoli babomɔ bua bodi na bosusu o adi so na njingo .
56003008	Ekenge emina edi soti , na mbi napalaka bo okojae ngando jimina na bingi , bo bato baya bajimaka Njambe badae na bingi a bikɔmɛli bipele . Mijɔ mi midi mipele mɛnɛ na Mibɔngejaka bato .
56003009	Toma lona ko mabɔjɔ maya mapeliti cina , na mijɔ mimbota jibato , na miano , na mosoo a mojɔ moMibeko . Ngando jimina jidi oko ngasa mɛnɛ , na jibɔngiti nongo mweka .
56003010	Moto akabɔtɔ na nu , moleha ehole emɔci , isa bihole bibae , na mokina yo .
56003011	Ojebaka bo moto omina adi molaboake , moto mobe , na asadumbaka yo mɛnɛ .
56003012	Namaka loma Alutema isa Tukiko ai wɛ , kenga bodoa ai mbi bokpa a Nikɔpɔli , mojɔ bo najimi bo nayeyoe oho edidi esusu epio .
56003013	Sɛlingoa na bopele mɛnɛ a mojɔ momɔngɔ moSena yona odi juji , na Apolo , ho batataka nongo eka .
56003014	Bato basu badi bokoa bo bakɔe bilomu bipele .
56003015	Bato basusu baya badi na mbi ya babɛjɛkɛ wɛ njɛbɛ . Abɛjɛ bato baya bapalaka so a Ejimeli . Yɛ monganji moNjambe modae na nu basusu .
57001001	Mbi Paulo , lisungu liMasiya Yesu , na Timoteo mwangwa’su ai Pilemona moninga osu a elomu ,
57001002	ai ngɛnɛ esu Apia , a Alukipo moninga osu a bila , na a Denga lia lidi a ndako ewɛ .
57001003	Yɛ monganji na bowi boNjambe Sangwa’su , na Kumu osu Yesu Masiya , bodae na wɛ .
57001004	Mbi nasakoaka Njambe bihole bisusu yana alangaka mbi kombe ewɛ a ma’nga mambi .
57001005	Mojɔ bo nakaka mwako moepaeli ewɛ , na ejimeli ewɛ , ai Kumu Yesu , na ai bato basusu baDenga .
57001006	Mbi nangaka Njambe bo bakakatana na wɛ a ejimeli , badi bohɛ na ejebeli ebopele bosusu bua bodi ai so a tei eMasiya .
57001007	Moninga , yana aka mbi mwako moepaeli ewɛ , mbi nasepa bou mɛnɛ , cina bo milema mibato baDenga misɔ ngulu a mojɔ mowɛ .
57001008	A mojɔ momina , nongo adi mbi na kpaci a tei eMasiya a botɔndɔ wɛ ngando jia jibwani na wɛ a bokɔ ,
57001009	napalaka bongɔɔnɔ wɛ a mojɔ moepaeli , oko mbi Paulo yona odi mosuku mɛnɛ , na lisungu liMasiya Yesu e dɛye .
57001010	Nangɔɔnɔkɔ wɛ a mojɔ momwana’mbi Onesimo . Mbi namobota adi mbi ya a minyɔlɔ .
57001011	Iyo adaka na wɛ boso oko moto-ngasa . Edɛye ko abwani bokɔmeja so na wɛ .
57001012	Mbi namosɔmbejaka ai wɛ , o molema mombi mɛnɛ .
57001013	Nadaki na posa bo adikae na mbi ya a bokɔmɛ mbi a kombe ewɛ , yana adi mbi ya a minyɔlɔ a mojɔ moMwako Mopele .
57001014	Napaliti ko bokɔ boa , adi wɛ pɛ bopeta jima mojɔ momina . Okakɔ mbi monganji , mobwani boda na bolulea bowɛ mɛnɛ , te a mojɔ mokpaci embi .
57001015	Isa abɔtɔi na wɛ ehole ye ekue bo omosɛ koko na bosusu ,
57001016	te nongo o mobuli , oko moto yona onɔi mobuli , oko moninga oepaeli . Isa adi moninga ombi oepaeli , esingaiti ai wɛ , o moto mɛnɛ , na a tei eKumu pongono .
57001017	Oko boa , isa onjaka mbi o minao , mosɔ yo o mbi mɛnɛ .
57001018	Isa akɔ mokina mojɔ mobe ai wɛ , isa adi na nongo ai wɛ , langa mojɔ momina o nongo embi .
57001019	Mbi Paulo nasɔnɔkɔ mojɔ mu na ebɔ embi mɛnɛ — Nadi bosɔmbeja nongo emina . Nabwaniti bolɛjɛ wɛ bo odi na nongo ai mbi ; nongo emina edi oko we mɛnɛ .
57001020	Ee moninga , kɔ mbi monganji mu a kombe eKumu . Gɔmbeja molema mombi a tei eMasiya .
57001021	Nasɔnei wɛ mokanda mu mojɔ bo najimaka bo odi na lisuma . Najebaka bo otakputoa bokɔ mojɔ mopalaka mbi ; ee , odi bonɔ mojɔ momina na monganji .
57001022	Mokina mojɔ motongo , — sɛlingoa ekina ekenge endako a mojɔ mombi ; nadi na njingo bo osɛni mbi koko o epeeli , cina ebingeeli binu .
57001023	Epapulo lisungu liMasiya Yesu yona odi na mbi ya , abɛjɛkɛ wɛ njɛbɛ .
57001024	Malako , na Alisitaluko , na Dema , na Luka , bina’mbi a elomu , babɛjɛkɛ wɛ pongono .
57001025	Yɛ monganji moKumu Yesu Masiya modae na mwembo mowɛ .
58001001	Njambe abala na batata basu eyou bihole binɛnɛ na njea jitongotongo na minɔkɔ Mibatɔndɔi .
58001002	Edɛye ko abali na su a masu ma masuka , oko na Mwana’nde . Amohɔ bo adae sangoli ongando jisusu , na ayoa koko ngondo ye na ngulu ende .
58001003	Iyo adi bolailai boekumu eNjambe ; adi elimo esoti eNjambe , na abeaka ngondo jisusu na ebaeli engulu ende . Ama yo pa lisiko a mojɔ mojibe , ami ko da oko a dɔngɔ diebɔ ebami eKumu oDiko .
58001004	Na kombe esangoi yo , na kombe jibabwɛnji , kombe esangoi yo enɔi bou mɛnɛ ; oko boa yo mɛnɛ anɔi babwɛnji bou mɛnɛ .
58001005	Njambe abala na okina obwɛnji-odiko ekina ehole bo ? Wɛ odi Mwana’mbi , Mbi naboti wɛ busa bu isa Mbi nâda Sangwa’nde , Na yo âda Mwana’mbi .
58001006	Na Pongono , yana akwejaka yo Mwana’nde sɔmi a ngondo , abalaka bo , Yɛ babwɛnji basusu baNjambe bamosakoe .
58001007	A mojɔ mobabwɛnji-baDiko , abalaka bo , Akɔkɔ bo babwɛnji bande badae o mahweya , Na bakɔmɛli bande o biemi bimosa .
58001008	A mojɔ moMwana ko , abalaka bo , Ee Njambe , ngɛndɛ ewɛ edi na bosusu mɛnɛ . Tondo eBokumu bowɛ edi tondo ebosambeja bojo .
58001009	Wɛ opalaka bodongo na olonaka bobe . A mojɔ momina , Njambe , Njambe owɛ asuoa wɛ Sali esepi bo odae boso bobabinao .
58001010	Na Wɛ Kumu , oyoa ngondo a libangake mɛnɛ . Busa bodi koko elomu emɔmɔ mawɛ .
58001011	Ngando jimina jidi bodimoa ; wɛ ko oyeyoaka na bosusu . Ngando jimina jidi bogwa o agwaka bisenja .
58001012	Ojibulabí o abulaka moto kasaka , Na jikindoabí elimo etongo . Wɛ oko odi na bosusu oko elimo emɔci , Na bianga biwɛ bipeliti nongo suka .
58001013	Iyo ko abala na okina obwɛnji-oDiko bo ? Da ya a ebɔ embi ebami Bo mbi nadumbe soki jiwɛ o ebakei ebibota biwɛ .
58001014	Babwɛnji-baDiko basusu baditi miembo Mibokɔmeja ? Abalomaka bo bakɔmɛe basangoli bamobelo .
58002001	A mojɔ momina , so bobwani bopea boku ngando jika so , na bopipo mɛnɛ , bo bosaka laboa bohali .
58002002	Mojɔ bo , isa bwɛnji bua bodoa na babwɛnji-baDiko bodaka na kpaci , na baya balona na basopa mobeko basɔ mokindo mua mobwana ,
58002003	esingaiti so ; bokabulɛ boheleja bu bonɛnɛ , bodi bohela na ye ? Kumu yo mɛnɛ abanga botɔndɔ mojɔ moboheleja bomina , na baya bamoka banga-meja mojɔ momina ai so .
58002004	Na Njambe aneja bo tati ebu edi soti , oko na bimbete , na mindumba , na mijɔ Mibokamoa , na bipeeli biMwembo , o ajima yo na bolulea bonde .
58002005	Iso bobalaka a mojɔ mongondo ebodoa ; na Njambe aideja ngondo emina a kpaci ebabwɛnji-badiko .
58002006	Tati emoto a ekina esika edaka bo , Moto adi nda ? Wɛ odi na bolɛ ai yo mojɔ moye ? Mwana’moto adi nda ? Omobaneaka mojɔ moye ?
58002007	Omodeja a ngɔngɔ jibabwɛnji-baDiko ehole ekue . Omokumeja na ekumu na lisuma o likongo a molo monde . Omopa kpaci a ngando jikɔ wɛ na mɔmɔ mawɛ .
58002008	Odeja ngando jisusu a cina jibibota binde . Yana amopa yo kpaci a ngando jisusu , Njambe aikina nongo eka emɔci yena editi a kpaci ende . Endele ko , so bonɛkini ngando jisusu a cina ekpaci ende .
58002009	Bonɛkɛ Yesu ko , yona odejama ekina ehole a ngɔngɔ jihabwɛnji-baDiko ; bomonɛkɛ yo yona okumejama na ekumu , na lisuma , o likongo a molo monde a mojɔ mobogwa bonɛ yo , bo adingoe na bogwa a mojɔ mobato basusu , oko na monganji moNjambe .
58002010	Mojɔ bo , yona oyoa leka losusu , na leka losusu lodi a mojɔ monde , adi oko yona opala bo akwejae bana banɛnɛ a ekumu , mobwana na nde soti bo abɔngejae yona ohoja njea ebu ebohela , oko na bodingoa .
58002011	Mojɔ bo , yona osɛnojaka , na baya basɛnɔi badi na sango omɔci . A mojɔ momina yo aditi na Sɔni a bobabakea kombe bananango .
58002012	Abala bo , Mbi nadi bojebeja banangwa’mbi kombe ewɛ ; Nadi bosakoa wɛ a tei eDenga .
58002013	Abala koko bo , Mbi nadi bobakea molema mombi ai yo . Na Mbi yona , na bana bapani Njambe .
58002014	Oko boa , isa bana basangoaka mokuku na makia , yo mɛnɛ alwa elimo ebu , bo agbokejae yona odi na kpaci ebogwa , oko Satana mɛnɛ , a mojɔ mobogwa bonde ,
58002015	na bo acingoe basusu baya badaka a libuli masu mabu masusu , a cina ebɔ bobogwa .
58002016	Mojɔ bo elomu ende editi a mojɔ mobabwɛnji-baDiko , oko a mojɔ mobana baAbalayama .
58002017	Oko boa ebɔngɔ na nde bo adae na bananango elimo emɔci , amɛci mɛnɛ , bo adae nganga monɛnɛ owa na ejimeli a elomu eNjambe , a bopa lisiko a mojɔ mojibe jibato .
58002018	Iyo adi na ngulu a bokɔmeja baya badi a tei ebomeka , mojɔ bo adingoa yo mɛnɛ yana amekama yo .
58003001	Baninga basɛnɔke , baya babeama a bokatana a elomu eDiko , toma lɛni Yesu , Obwɛnji na Nganga Monɛnɛ oejimeli esu .
58003002	Iyo adaka na lisuma ai yona omohɔ , o amaka da Mose na lisuma a ndako ende esusu .
58003003	Na Yesu na Mose ko , Yesu anɔi na ekumu ; mojɔ bo moyoeli ondako adi na ekumu , te ndako eyoaka yo .
58003004	Tu ndako edi na moyoeli ; edi Njambe ko yona oyoa leka losusu .
58003005	Mose adaka na lisuma o mokɔmɛli ondako eNjambe bo atate tati engando jia jibalama oko ngɔngɔ .
58003006	Masiya ko adaka na lisuma limwana a ndako eNjambe . Ndako emina edi oko so , bokapea boku oko a suka ejimeli esu , na njingo esu yena edi ekumu esu .
58003007	A mojɔ momina Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mobalaka bo , Oka’kani monɔkɔ monde busa bu ,
58003008	T’opingejaeni oko milema minu o akɔ bo a ehole ebokeja kɛlɛ , A busa bobomeka a lisobe .
58003009	Batata banu bameka mbi a esika emina , Na banɛ bilomu bimbi bianga macinda mabae .
58003010	A mojɔ momina , mbi naka kɛlɛ na elulu emina , na nabala bo , Milema Mibu midi na bosusu oko milaboake , Baijeba nongo njea jimbi .
58003011	Na mbi nabɛlɛ bɛli a kɛlɛ embi bo , Batakwea nongo a liheme limbi .
58003012	Anganjamani baninga , bo okina onu asaka da na molema mobe mokitɛ , mua modi bolaboja no a njea eNjambe obomɔ .
58003013	Salehanani tu busa yana adi so na ekenge ye “ busa bu ” a kɔpi esu , okina onu asaka da na ebaso a molema , cina eepulu ebobe .
58003014	Mojɔ bo libondo lisu lidi a tei eMasiya , bokapea boku oko a suka , ejimeli yena edaka na su a libangake ,
58003015	yana adi so na ehole eekenge ye , Oka’kani monɔkɔ monde busa bu , T’opingejaeni oko milema minu o akɔ bo a ehole ebokeja kɛlɛ .
58003016	Na badaka na lipanga ndani ? oko baya baka , ee , oko bo basusu baya bamana na Mose a Ejipeto .
58003017	Na bakeja Njambe kɛlɛ bianga macinda mabae ndani ? Oko baya bakɔ bobe , na njemba jibu jidika a lisobe .
58003018	Na abɛlɛ bɛli ai nda bo batakwea a liheme linde ? — oko baya badaka na lipanga .
58003019	Oko boa bocineaka bo baibɔngɔ bo bakwee a mojɔ mokitɛ .
58004001	Oko boa , adi so na sako ebokwea a liheme linde , yɛni so bodae na bɔ bo okina onu asaka kputoa .
58004002	Mojɔ bo iso boki koko Mwako Mopele , o ama bo ka . Bwɛnji ko boka bo bonama oko bonama , ema bo baya baka bwɛnji baibosɔ na ejimeli .
58004003	Iso ko baya bajimi bokweaka a liheme , o ahala yo bo , Nabɛlɛ bɛli a kɛlɛ embi bo , Ibo batakwea nongo e liheme limbi . Bilomu binde ko bisia oko a bobanga bongondo .
58004004	Mojɔ bo abala a ekina esika a mojɔ mobusa bosambo bo , Njambe ahema a bilomu binde bisusu a busa bosambo .
58004005	Abala koko a esika ye bo , Ibo batakwea nongo a liheme limbi .
58004006	Oko boa , isa baya baka Mwako Mopele baibɔngɔ bo bakwee cina elipanga , sako ebokwea edikai a mojɔ mobakina batongo , bo bakwee .
58004007	Njambe ajima koko bokina busa a mojɔ momina , oko busa bu , o abala yo na Dawidi ngɔngɔ mɛnɛ ekenge emi so bala bo , Oka’kani monɔkɔ monde busa bu , T’opingejaeni oko milema minu .
58004008	Mojɔ bo , Yoswa , akɔkɔ yo pa bato liheme , ka Njambe aibala ngɔngɔ a mojɔ mobusa botongo .
58004009	Oko boa , liheme liSabata lidikai a mojɔ mobato baNjambe .
58004010	Mojɔ bo , moto akakwea a liheme liNjambe , ahemaka a hilomu hinde , o ahema Njambe a bilomu binde .
58004011	A mojɔ momina , bobwani boda na bingi a bokwea a liheme limina , bo pɛpɛ nongo moto odi bokwa na ekɔmɛli emina elipanga .
58004012	Mojɔ bo , Ebaeli eNjambe edi mɔ , edi na ndangasa , na enɔi ambombo na bopɔlu . Ekwɛlɛkɛ moto a bobɔteja molema na mwembo , na mongi na libɔngɔ ; na esambejaka malɛ na mikano mimolema .
58004013	Pɛpɛ nongo moto odi bosabomba ai yo , na mijɔ misusu midi bohu na mbundu mɛnɛ a miso mande yona osambejaka so .
58004014	Adi so ko na Nganga Monɛnɛ yona onɔi oho Diko , oko Yesu Mwana ’ Njambe , kwani bopee boku ejimeli esu .
58004015	Mojɔ bo , iso boditi na Nganga Monɛnɛ yona opeliti wa ai so yana adi so na bwɛmbu , oko Nganga Monɛnɛ yona onɔ njea jisusu jibomeka o akɔkɔ so , pɛ ko bokɔ nongo bobe .
58004016	A mojɔ momina , so bobwani bobatama na mongbɛlɛngɔ momonganji , pɛpɛ nongo mokakwano , bo bosɛ wa , na bo bobolojae monganji a bokɔmeja so a ehole etaka .
58005001	Bahɔkɔ Nganga Monɛnɛ bihole bisusu a tei ebato bo akwee bosiili a sibano ebato na Njambe , na bo apɛ bipeeli na masiko a mojɔ mojibe .
58005002	Ajebi boda na molema mo yɛmbu ai bato baya badi na libumi , na baya badi balaboake , mojɔ bo yo abindani na bwɛmbu yo mɛnɛ .
58005003	A mojɔ momina , abwani bopa masiko , te a mojɔ mojibe jibato pɛ , oko a mojɔ mojibe jinde mɛnɛ pongono .
58005004	Moto atasabakea a ekumu emina yo mɛnɛ ; Njambe amobeaka o akɔ yo na Alona .
58005005	Oko boa , Masiya aisabakea Nganga Monɛnɛ yo mɛnɛ . Okina amohɔ , oko yona obala na nde bo , Wɛ odi Mwana’mbi ; Mbi naboti wɛ busa bu .
58005006	Na abalaka koko a esika etongo bo , Wɛ odi Nganga na bosusu mɛnɛ , Oko na bonganga boMalekisedeke .
58005007	Yesu , yana adaka yo ya nase , angaka , na angɔɔnɔkɔ na bopipo , na mbisoli pongono , ai yona obwana bomoheleja a bogwa . Na yo amoka cina elisuma linde ai Njambe .
58005008	Nongo adaka yo Mwana , akoa lisuma oko na minɔngɔ misɔ yo .
58005009	Na ama yo bɔngɔ a njea jisusu , ami da oko moboloja omohelo na bosusu ai bato basusu baya bamosumaka .
58005010	Na Njambe amobakea Nganga Monɛnɛ obo-nganga boMalekisedeke .
58005011	Iso bobwani bobala na nu ngando jinɛnɛ a mojɔ momina ; jidi ko na kpɔkɔsɔ a bocingea , mojɔ bo odini na bohoka mweka e dɛye .
58005012	Ino obwanini boda bakoja ehole eyai ; e dɛye ko otakakani moto no bɛnɛ a bokoja no koko mijɔ Miboso mɛnɛ miEbaeli eNjambe . Okindoini bato baya babwani na mabɛi , te nongo dia dimosuku .
58005013	Mojɔ bo , yona onungaka mabɛi alandoakini na mijɔ Mibodongo ; adi oko mwana mokɛkɛlɛkɛ .
58005014	Dia lidi a mojɔ mobato bapingake , baya balandoi na ekɔmɛli ebokokeleja mijɔ , baya babwani bobɔteja bopele na bobe .
58006001	A mojɔ momina , bobwani bokina mijɔ miMasiya mia midi o mijɔ Mibana , bo bonɔe a mijɔ Mibosuku . Bobwaniti bosɔnibɔ koko a botanda eyoeli-ecina , oko bohekoja bomolema a bokina bilomu bingasangasa , na ejimeli ai Njambe ,
58006002	na bileho a mojɔ batisimo , bobakea bomɔmɔ , bongɔ bobagwake , na bosambeja bua bodi na bosusu .
58006003	Njambe akajima , so bodi bokɔ boa .
58006004	Mojɔ bo , isa bato basi bohu , na balɛli epeeli eDiko , na basi epeeli eMwembo Mosɛnɔke ,
58006005	na balɛli ebaeli epele eNjambe , na ngulu engondo ebodoa ,
58006006	bato bamina bakalaboa , njea editi bo bahekojae koko milema , mojɔ bo babakeaka koko Mwana ’ Njambe a mole-mobokea na bolulea bobu bɛnɛ , na bamopɔmbejaka a boso bobato .
58006007	Mojɔ bo , mokpɔtɔ mokasɔ mbua baya bakwaka a esika emina bihole hisusu , na mokabota leka a mojɔ mobato baya balia gbie , bojongoa boNjambe bodi a mokpɔtɔ momina .
58006008	Isa ko mobotaka oko njubɛ na njani pɛ , motabɔngɔ nongo , moditi na bojongoa ; mobwani oko na mosa .
58006009	Baninga , nongo abalaka so boa , njingo esu a mojɔ monu editi boa ; edi a mojɔ mongando jipele jia jicingi na boheleja .
58006010	Mojɔ bo Njambe t’abungake mojɔ ; atabosa elomu enu , na epaeli enejaka no a kombe ende yana akɔmɛkɛ no bato baNjambe , na obakɔmɛkɛni oko e dɛye .
58006011	Posa esu edi bo moto na moto a tei enu adae na bingi a bobanea tɛndɛ ende esusu oko a suka mɛnɛ .
58006012	PƐ bodani na bomɛli . Ikoanani ko na bato baya basangoaka njikano cina eejimeli na lingbangba .
58006013	Mojɔ bo , yana akina Njambe Abalayama sako , abɛlɛ bɛli a kombe ende mɛnɛ . Aihɔnɔ bobɛlɛ bɛli a kombe eokina otongo , mojɔ bo pɛpɛ nongo okina otongo odi boso bonde .
58006014	Abala bo , Soti mɛnɛ , mbi nâjongoa wɛ oko na bojongoa ; Nâhɛjɛ mbota ewɛ oko bohɛjɛ .
58006015	Oko boa , Abalayama , ama yo da na lingbangba , ami ko sɔ oko bodikeja .
58006016	Bato babɛlɛkɛ bɛli a kombe emoto yona odi boso bobu , na isa badi na kitɛ , kitɛ emina edi bosia a mojɔ mobɛli .
58006017	Oko boa Njambe abɛlɛ bɛli pongono , mojɔ bo apala bo basangoli bandi-keja bacingee na soti bo bodikeja bonde botakputoa nongo .
58006018	A mojɔ momina , so baya bacii bo bobolame , bobwani bosapingeja na bopea boku njingo yena edi a boso bosu , cina emijɔ mi Mibae mia mitakputoa nongo , mojɔ bo Njambe atahɔnɔ bokosea na mijɔ mimina .
58006019	Iso bopeli njingo emina o longo emwembo , njingo esoti na embilimake yena ekweaka a dɔngɔ ditongo diehuako .
58006020	Na Yesu yo mɛnɛ asui hoso bosu , na akwei a tei eesika emina a mojɔ mosu , mojɔ bo adi Nganga Monɛnɛ na bosusu , oko na bonganga boMalekisedeke .
58007001	Iyo Malekisedeke , kumu oSalema , adaka nganga oNjambe obonɔ . Asongana na Abalayama yana ahulaka yo a bowa bakumu a bila , na amojongoa .
58007002	Abalayama amokaba libondo lidomi lileka losusu . Cina ekombe ende edi boso Kumu oBodongo ; na adi koko Kumu oSalema ; cina emina edi Kumu oBowi .
58007003	Apeliti sango isa nango , pɛpɛ koko mbota ; masu mande pɛpɛ libangake , ehelo ende pɛpɛ suka ; adi nganga na bosusu na elimo eMwana ’ Njambe .
58007004	Lɛni moto omina monɛnɛ , mojɔ bo Abalayama amopa libondo lidomi lileka lopea yo a bila .
58007005	Bana baLewi baya badi a elomu enganga , badi na kpaci eMobeko bo basɛ libondo lidomi ai bato , oko ai bato babu bɛnɛ , nongo adi bo bana baAbalayama .
58007006	Iyo ko yona oditi na bu mbota , asɔ libondo lidomi ai Abalayama yona odaka na ndikeja , na amojongoa .
58007007	Mojɔ modi bohu mɛnɛ bo moto yona ojongoaka anɔi yona osɔkɔ bojongoa , pɛ kitɛ .
58007008	Ibaya basɔkɔ libondolidomi ya , badi oko bato babogwa ; iyo ko adi mɔ , na tati edi a mojɔ momina .
58007009	Oko boa bobwani bobala bo Lewi yo mɛnɛ , yona osɔkɔ libondo lidomi , akaba libondo lidomi yana akɔ Abalayama boa ,
58007010	mojɔ bo adaka oko a sɔpɔ jitata onde yana asongana yo na Malekisedeke .
58007011	Isa bonganga boLewi bodi bobɔngeja bato soti , ( mojɔ bo bato basɔ Mibeko cina ebonganga bomina ) ebɔngi bo okina nganga otongo adoe mojɔ moye , te nongo na bonganga boAlona , oko na bonganga boMalekisedeke ?
58007012	Mojɔ bo bonganga boyene bodi na Mobeko moyene pongono .
58007013	Mijɔ mi Mibalama a mojɔ momoto olikota litongo , na pɛpɛ nongo moto olikota limina okɔ elomu ehtumbu .
58007014	Na mojɔ modi bohu mɛnɛ ho Kumu osu adaka olikota liYuda , na Mose ailanga nongo kombe elikota limina a mojɔ mobonganga .
58007015	Mojɔ momina monɔi na bohu a mojɔ monganga otongo yona odoa na elimo eMalekisedeke ,
58007016	yona odi nganga na ngulu ebomɔ bua bodi na bosusu , te nongo na kpaci emokina mobeko a mojɔ mombota ende .
58007017	Mojɔ bo tati edi a mojɔ monde bo , Wɛ odi nganga na bosusu obonganga boMalekisedeke .
58007018	Ekina ekɔmɛli eyou ehɛngɛmɛ cina bo edaka e yɛmbu , na eibɔngɔ .
58007019	( Mojɔ bo Mobeko moibɔngeja eka ) . Na njingo etongo eboloi yena enɔi na bopele , na so bodi bobatama na Njambe oko na njingo emina .
58007020	Mojɔ momina moitaka bɛli .
58007021	BaLewi bakwea a elomu enganga , pɛ bobɛlɛ nongo bɛli . Yesu ko adi nganga cina ebɛli ende yona obala na nde bo , Kumu abɛli bɛli , na aditi na ebaeli etongo . Wɛ odi nganga oko na bosusu .
58007022	A mojɔ momina , Yesu adi mokando moMokongo mua monɔi na bopele .
58007023	Mojɔ motongo , nganga badaka banɛnɛ ; baihɔnɔ boyeyoa , a mojɔ mobogwa .
58007024	Iyo ko adi nganga oko na bosusu , cina bo yo mɛnɛ adi oko na bosusu .
58007025	A mojɔ momina , yo abwani boheleja na bosusu mɛnɛ , baya badoaka al Njambe na njea ende , mojɔ bo yo adi mɔ oko na bosusu bo adae mosili a mojɔ mosu .
58007026	Nganga monɛnɛ yona odi boa abwana na su soti , mosɛnɔke , pɛpɛ nongo lindo , pɛpɛ nongo litɔnɔ , mobɔtɔnɔke na babe , yona ongɔjɔmɔ a Diko yena enɔi .
58007027	Iyo abwaniti bopa masiko tu busa , o akɔkɔ nganga batongo a mojɔ mojibe jibu bɛnɛ na jibato batongo pongono . Iyo akɔ boa ehole emɔci yena ebwani na bosusu , yana asapa yo mɛnɛ lisiko .
58007028	Mobeko mohɛngɛkɛ bato a elomu enga-nga baya badi oko ba yɛmbu ; ebaeli ebɛli ko , yena edoa ngɔngɔ jiMobeko , ehɛngɛkɛ Mwana yona odi mobɔngɔke oko na bosusu mɛnɛ .
58008001	Cina engando jimi so bala edi bo , Iso bodi na Nganga Monɛnɛ o boa , yona odi a ebɔ ebami emongbelɛngɔ moKumu oDiko .
58008002	Adi mokɔmɛli a tei eesika esɛnɔke , a tei eEtondo esoti yena epika Kumu , te moto .
58008003	Nganga basusu bahɛngɛmɛkɛ a bopa bipeeli na masiko . Oko boa yo koko abwani boda na eka a bopa .
58008004	Akɔki yo da ya nase , ka aditi nongo nganga , cina bo nganga badi ya baya bapaka bipeeli o adi ekɔmɛli eMobeko .
58008005	Elomu ekɔkɔ bo edi embete na elimo eesika esɛnɔke oho Diko ; mojɔ bo yana akana Mose bopika Etondo , Njambe amoleha bo , Toma nganjama bo okɔe leka losusu oko na elimo yena eboloi ai wɛ a mono .
58008006	E dɛye ko , elomu esɔ Masiya enɔi yena ebu bou mɛnɛ , mojɔ bo adi mosili oMokongo mua monɔi mua moyou , cina bo modi na madikeja maya manɔi na bopele .
58008007	Isa mokongo moboso mobɔngɔ na soti , ka pokiso eiboloa a mojɔ momokongo moMibae .
58008008	Njambe anɛ mijɔ Mibu yana abala yo bo , Kumu abalaka bo , A masu mangɔngɔ , Mbi nadi bobakea mokongo moyene Na likota liYisalaele , na likota liYuda .
58008009	Te nongo o mokongo mobakea mbi na basangwa’bu , A busa bopea mbi bo na ebɔ Bo nabamanejae a Ejipito ; Mojɔ bo , ibo baiyeyoa a mokongo mombi , Na mbi nababulɛ oko bobulɛ . Ebaeli eKumu edi boa .
58008010	Kumu abalaka bo , Mokongo mobakeabí mbi a masu mangɔngɔ Na likota liYisalaele modi oko mu ; Mbi nasabí Mibeko mimbi a tei emiembo mibu ; Namisɔnɔbí a milema mibu . Mbi nadabí Njambe obu , Na bo badabí bato bambi .
58008011	Moto atabalabí koko na mina’nde Isa moto na mwangwa’nde bo , Jeba Kumu . Mojɔ bo bajebabí mbi kanga basusu mɛnɛ , Na bakɛkɛlɛkɛ na banɛnɛnɛ pongono .
58008012	Mojɔ bo nadabí na wa a mojɔ momabunga mabu , Na nitalɛ koko jibe jibu .
58008013	Abalaka yo a mojɔ moMokongo moyene , anjaka mua moboso o eka yena editi koko na cina . Na isa eka editi koko na cina , na isa ebengi bogwa , edikai mweka pɛ bo edimoe na bosusu .
58009001	Mokongo moboso modaka na Mibeko a mojɔ mobosakoa , na modaka na esika ebosakoa ya nase .
58009002	Mojɔ bo bapika Etondo , na epei-epaka , na mesa , na milɛmbɛ mia mitandama a boso boNjambe ; leka lomina lodaka a ekenge eboso ; kombe eesika emina edi Esika-eBosɛnɔ .
58009003	Etondo etongo edaka a tei , a ngɔngɔ jingbungbu ejibae ; kombe eesikaemina edi Esika-enɔi-Bosɛnɔ .
58009004	Litumbu lia liluama na wɔlɔ lidaka ena , na edejai emokongo yena ehuama na wɔlɔ ; esei yena eluama na wɔlɔ edaka a tei a mojɔ momanna , na pango aAlona yena etɔ , na matai maMokongo .
58009005	Bilimo biekumu bidaka a diko diedejai , na esie emina ehua mongbelɛngɔ mowa . Botabala a mojɔ mocina jileka lu losusu e dɛye .
58009006	Bakolea leka losusu boa , bo nganga bakwee a etondo eboso masu masusu a mojɔ moelomu ebu .
58009007	A tei eetondo ebibae ko , nganga monɛnɛ akweaka oko yo buki tu yanga ehole emɔci , na t’akputoake botomba makia bo amapejae a mojɔ monde mɛnɛ , na a mojɔ mojibe jibato .
58009008	Mwembo Mosɛnɔke monejaka na mojɔ momina bo njea ebokwea a tei eEsika-enɔi-Bosɛnɔ eipaka boloa a ehole edaka Etondo eboso .
58009009	Mojɔ momina modi oko mondɛ a mojɔ moehole ye , yana apaka bo bipeeli na masiko maya mabwaniti bobɔngeja molema momoto yona osakoaka ;
58009010	ngando jimina jicingi na boyaka , na bomwaka , na bososa na madiba ; Mibeko a mojɔ momokuku mia midi na kpaci oko a ehole ehobɔngeja .
58009011	Yana ko adoa Masiya , Nganga Monɛnɛ a mojɔ mongando jipele jibodoa , yo anɔ njea eetondo yena enɔi na bukɛ na bopele ( eipikama na mɔmɔ , eiyoama na ekɔmɛli engondo ye ) ,
58009012	na akwea a Esika-eBosɛnɔ ehole emɔci pɛ yena ebwani na bosusu ; aikwea na makia makambɛli na bana-bangɔmbɔ , oko na makia mande mɛnɛ , na aboloja lisiko lia lidi oko na bosusu .
58009013	Mojɔ bo , isa makia mangɔmbɔ na kambɛli na mihulu mimwana-ngɔmbɔ mia mimɛsɛkɛ bo ai bato baekia Mibabɔngejaka a njea emokuku ,
58009014	esingaiti makia maMasiya yona osapa lisiko , pɛpɛ nongo litɔnɔ , ai Njambe a njea eMwembo mua modi na bosusu ; madi bosɛnoja milema minu a bilomu bigwake , bo okɔmɛeni Njambe obomɔ .
58009015	A mojɔ momina , yo adi mosili oMokongo Moyene , bo baya babeama basɛ lisango lia lidikejama , lia lidi na bosusu , cina ebogwa bua bobasikoaka a jibe jia jidi a cina eMokongo moboso .
58009016	Mojɔ bo isa lisango lidi , yona okinaka lisango limina adi bopeta gwa .
58009017	Moto amiti gwa , otongo atasangoa ; lisango libwaniti isa moto yona okinaka lisango adi oko mɔ .
58009018	A mojɔ momina Mokongo moboso mobakeama na makia .
58009019	Mojɔ bo , Mose , ama yo langa mijɔ misusu miMiheko ai bato basusu , ami tomba oko makia mabana-bangɔmbɔ na makambɛli , na madiba na makambule makpetu na kasa jilitindi , na amɛsɛ mokanda mɛnɛ na bato basusu pongono .
58009020	Na abala bo , Ima madi makia maMokongo mobakei Njambe na nu .
58009021	Amɛsɛ koko boa Etondo na leka losusu lobo-sakoa , oko na makia .
58009022	Edi Soti bo Mibeko mikojaka bo leka losusu losɛnoaka na makia ; makia mamiti sopea , bo yɛ bojibe boditi .
58009023	Isa leka lua lodaka oko bimbete bingando jiDiko losɛnoa a mojɔ momasiko mamina , ngando jiDiko mɛnɛ jibwana na masiko maya manɔi masiko mamina na bopele .
58009024	Mojɔ bo Masiya aikwea a Esika-eBosɛnɔ yena eyoama na mɔmɔ , yena edi oko embete pɛ eEsika-eBosɛnɔ esoti ; akwea a Diko mɛnɛ bo amae a boso boNjambe e dɛye a mojɔ mosu .
58009025	Aikwea bo asapɛ bihole binɛnɛ , o akweaka Nganga Monɛnɛ a Esika-eBosɛnɔ yanga na yanga na makia maya maditi makia mande mɛnɛ .
58009026	Akɔki yo kɔ boa , ka adingoe bihole binɛnɛ , banga na libangake lingondo . Iyo ko adoa ehole emɔci pɛ a suka ebianga , bo asapɛ yo mɛnɛ lisiko a bodongeja bobe .
58009027	Bato te babambake bogwa , bua bodi ehole emɔci , na ngɔngɔ jimina oko esambi .
58009028	Oko boa Masiya pongono asapa lisiko ehole emɔci , bo atombe muna mojibe jibato banɛnɛ ; na adoabi koko , te a mojɔ mobobe , oko a boheleja haya bamonjaka yo na tɛndɛ .
58010001	Mibeko midi oko embete pɛ engando jipele jibodoa , te elimo mɛnɛ engando jimina . A mojɔ momina , Mibwaniti bolongeja na soti baya badoaka na masiko yanga na yanga .
58010002	Isa mabwani , ka bato bakina bopa masiko . Akɔki bo sɛnoa , ka baya basakoaka batada koko na ejebeli ebobe .
58010003	Masiko mamina ko malɛjɛkɛ bato a mojɔ mobobe yanga na yanga .
58010004	Cina bo makia mangɔmbɔ na maka-mbɛli mabwaniti bodongeja jibe nongo mweka .
58010005	A mojɔ momina , Masiya , yana adoa yo a ngondo , abala bo , Wɛ t’opalake masiko na bipeeli ; Osɛlingoi ko mokuku a mojɔ mombi ;
58010006	Wɛ Posepake nongo na masiko malitumbu , na bipeeli a mojɔ mobobe .
58010007	Oko boa , mbi nabali bo , Mbi yona ; Mbi nadoi bo nakɔe bolulea bowɛ Njambe ; Mojɔ momina mosɔnɔmɔ a mokanda moMisɔnɔ a mojɔ mombi .
58010008	Abala boso bo , Wɛ t’opalake na t’osepake na masiko , na bipeeli , na bipeeli bilitumbu , na masiko a mojɔ mobobe ( bapaka leka lomina cina eMibeko ) .
58010009	Na ngɔngɔ , abala bo , Mbi yona ; mbi nadoi bo nakɔe bolulea bowɛ . Oko boa adongejaka mua moboso , bo abakee mua moMibae .
58010010	Na so bohɛngɛmɛ ai Njambe cina ebolulea bomina , a mojɔ moepeeli emokuku moYesu Masiya o lisiko ehole emɔci , yena ebwani na bosusu .
58010011	Nganga basusu bakɔkɔ elomu ebu busa na busa ; bapaka masiko bihole bisusu amɛci , maya mabwaniti bodongeja jibe nongo mweka .
58010012	Masiya ko , ama yo pa lisiko limɔci lia libwani na bosusu mɛnɛ , ami da oko a ebɔ ebami eNjambe ,
58010013	na ambaka oko bo soki jinde jidae ebakei a cina jibibota binde .
58010014	Cina bo , yo abɔngeja na bosusu , baya bahɛngɛmɛ ai Njambe , oko na lisiko limɔci .
58010015	Mwembo Mosɛnɔke mongamejaka koko mojɔ momina ai so . Mojɔ bo , abala boso bo ,
58010016	Kumu abalaka bo , Imu modi Mokongo mobakeabí mbi na bu A suka emasu mamina ; Nasabí Mibeko mimbi a tei emilema Mibu ; Namisɔnɔbí oko a bolɛ bobu .
58010017	Na abala ngɔngɔ bo , Nitalɛ koko jibe jibu , na mapanga mabu , na ikina .
58010018	Oko boa isa jibe jikinami , jibwaniti koko na lisiko a mojɔ mojibe .
58010019	A mojɔ momina baninga , so bodi na njea bohu a bokwea a Esika eBosɛnɔ , cina emakia maYesu ,
58010020	oko na njea eyene , njea ebomɔ ehoja yo a ngbungbu , oko mokuku monde mɛnɛ .
58010021	Na adi so na Nganga Monɛnɛ a ndako eNjambe ,
58010022	bobwani bobatama na molema mosoti na ejimeli enɛnɛ , pɛpɛ kitɛ , na milema misu mibɔtɔnɔke na ejebeli ebobe , na mikuku misu misosamake na madiba mapele .
58010023	Yɛni so bopee boku njingo ejimaka so , pɛ nongo bokamakama , mojɔ bo yo atakputoja nongo sako ekina yo .
58010024	Kinani bodae na mbambano a mojɔ moepaeli na bilomu bipele .
58010025	Bobwaniti bokputoa a matitana o akɔkɔ bakwa ; hɛjɛni bingi a bolehana moto na mina’nde moto , o anɛkɛ no bo Busa bomina bokɛkɛ adoe .
58010026	Bokakɔ bobe na bolulea bosu bɛnɛ , yana adi so na ejebeli enjea esoti , likina lisiko litongo a mojɔ mojibe liditi .
58010027	Edikai oko njingo eesambi yena ekɔkɔ maneene , na mosa monɛnɛ mua modi botumba soki .
58010028	Isa moto yona osɛtoja Mibeko miMose agwa na sanga , cina etati ebatati babae isa basato ,
58010029	esingaiti moto yona opɔmbejaka Mwana ’ Njambe , yona osɛtojaka makia maMokongo maya mamohɛngɛ ai Njamhe , o eka engasa , na asambojaka Mwembo momonganji moNjambe .
58010030	Mojɔ bo so bojebaka yona obala bo , Likundu lidi mojɔ mombi ; mbi nakundabí . Na abala koko bo , Kumu asambejabí bato bande .
58010031	Modi mojɔ mobɔ bonɛnɛ a bokwa a mɔmɔ maNjambe obomɔ .
58010032	Toma lɛni masu maboso . Yana asɔ no bohu a masu mamina , odakani na lingbangba a tei eminɔngɔ o bila mɛnɛ .
58010033	Bikina bihole basɛkɛ no , batangola no , na bapukeja no ; bihole bitongo ocinamani na bato batongo baya badaka na minɔngɔ mimina .
58010034	Odakani na wa ai bato baya badaka a minyɔlɔ . Yana atomba bato leka lonu , odakani oko na sepi , cina bo ojebakani bo lisango linu linɔi na bopele , lia lidi boyeyoa .
58010035	A mojɔ momina , t’obungejaeni oko eci enu mojɔ bo edi na ndese enɛnɛ .
58010036	Etakaka na nu oko lingbangba bo okɔeni bolulea boNjambe , na bo osɛni mua modikeja yo .
58010037	Mojɔ bo edikai oko mweka pɛ , Na yona odi na sako ebodoa adi bodoa ; atayeyoa a bodoa .
58010038	Moto ombi obodongo adi bohela oko na ejimeli . Akasɔmbɔ mandulendule ko , molema mombi motasepa na nde .
58010039	Iso ko boditi bato baya basɔmbɔkɔ mandulendule bo bobunge , oko bato baya badi na ejimeli a boheleja miembo Mibu .
58011001	Ejimeli edi ndanga engando jilɛndɛkɛ so ; enejaka so bo ngando jidi so pɛ bonɛ na miso jidi soti .
58011002	Bato baehele basɔ tati epele oko a mojɔ moejimeli .
58011003	Edi oko a mojɔ moejimeli bo bocingeaka bo Njambe ayoa ngondo na ebaeli ende , na bo atomba leka lodi so pɛ bonɛ na miso a bokɔ leka lonɛkɛ so .
58011004	Na lisiko lipa Abela , na lisiko lipa Kama , lia liAbela lmɔ na bopele , oko a mojɔ moejimeli . Alonga na du o moto obodongo , mojɔ bo Njambe ajima masiko mande . Iyo agwa ; abalaka ko na su e dɛye a njea eejimeli emina .
58011005	Anoka akindoa a mojɔ moejimeli , bo atanɛe nongo bogwa , na aiboloa koko , mojo bo Njambe amotomba . Adaka yo pɛ bopeta kindoa , adaka na esako bo asepejaka Njambe .
58011006	Isa ejimeli editi , moto t’ahɔnɔke bosepeja Njambe . Mojɔ bo moto yona odoaka a Njambe abwani bopeta jima bo Njambe adi , na bo asepejaka baya bamodukaka .
58011007	Noa asɔ eleho ai Njambe a mojɔ mo ngando jidaka yo pɛ bopeta nɛ na miso ; ahokea , na ayoa masua oko a mojɔ moejimeli , bo ahelejae denga dinde . Oko boa adumba ngondo , na asangoa bodongo bua bocingi na ejimeli .
58011008	Abalayama asuma Njambe cina eejimeli , yana abeama yo bo akɛe a ekina esika , yana adaka yo pɛ bopeta Sangoa esika emina ; na angɔ , pɛ ko bojeba esika ekɛkɛ yo .
58011009	Adaka mokɛndɛli a esika ebodikeja , oko a mojɔ moejimeli ; edaka o esika ebato batongo , na yo apika bitondo a esika emina , bo adae ena na Isaka na Yakobo , basangoli na nde babodikeja bomɔci .
58011010	Mojɔ bo njingo ende edaka oko a ngando mɛnɛ yena edi na eyoeli-ecina eboyeyoa ; yona okana ngando emina , na moyoeli ongando emina adi oko Njambe .
58011011	Sala yo mɛnɛ , nongo adaka yo mobange , asɔ ngulu bo alwae demi cina eejimeli , mojɔ bo ajima bo yona omokinea sako atakpu toja sako .
58011012	Oko boa momi omɔci , mokuku monde oko mogwake , abota bato banɛnɛ pɛ njɛngi , baya badi o njɔtɔ badiko , na mbumee jimbongu emadiba-mamukwa .
58011013	Ibo basusu bagwa na ejimeli , pɛ ko bosɔ ngando jibodikeja . Bajinɛ ko bohali , na basepa a mojɔ momina , cina bo bajima bo badi oko bakɛndɛli na midoa a ngondo .
58011014	Bato baya babalaka boa , banejaka na soti bo badukaka ngando oko boduka , ngando ebu bɛnɛ .
58011015	Akɔkɔ bo lɛ ngando ema bo kina , ka badaka na njea ebosɔnibɔ oho .
58011016	Posa ebu ko edi a ngando yena enɔi na bopele , oko oho Diko . A mojɔ momina , Njambe aditi na sɔni a boda Njambe obu , mojɔ bo yo asɛlingoa ngando a mojɔ mobu .
58011017	Abalayama , yana amekama yo , apa Isaka o lisiko cina eejimeli . Iyo , yona osɔ madikeja , ajima bo apɛ mwana’nde omɔci o lisiko .
58011018	Na sako edaka a mojɔ momwana omina bo , Bato bambota ewɛ badi bomana oko ai Isaka .
58011019	Iyo ajima bo Njambe adi na ngulu a bongɔjɔ bato a bogwa mɛnɛ . Na amosɔ koko boa , mojɔ bo adaka o mogo .
58011020	Isaka ajongoa Yakobo na Esau a mojɔ mongando jibodoa , oko cina eejimeli .
58011021	Yakobo , yana adaka yo oko a bogwa , ajongoa bana-bami baYosepa , omɔci omɔci , cina eejimeli , na asambimeja na pango ende bo ange Njambe .
58011022	Yosepa , yana abenga yo bogwa , abala a mojɔ moboyana boBa-Yisalaele oko cina eejimeli , na akina monɔkɔ a mojɔ monjemba ende .
58011023	Baboti baMose bamobomba songe basato yana abotama yo , cina eejimeli , mojɔ bo banɛ bo adi mwana mopele , na baibanga mobeko mokumu .
58011024	Mose , yana akandoa yo , alona bo bamobee mwana omwa’mwali oPalo .
58011025	Na bocingama na bato baNjambe a bodingoa bobu , na bosepa na sepi yena etayeyoaka a mojɔ mongando jibe , yo apala gbo oko bocingama na bato baNjambe a bodingoa bobu .
58011026	Na biloli a mojɔ moMasiya , na leka loyumu loEjipeto , yo ajima bo biloli a mojɔ moMasiya binɔi na yumu , mojɔ bo abakea miso mande a ndese .
58011027	Adonga a Ejipeto cina eejimeli , pɛ bobanga nongo kɛlɛ ekumu , mojɔ bo adaka na molema mombilimake , o moto yona onjaka okina yona otaboloaka na miso .
58011028	Asɛlingoa Kola eBonɔ , na amɛsɛ makia cina eejimeli , bo obwɛnji-obogwa anɔe basɔmi baYisalaele .
58011029	Baleka Madiba Makpetu o ngondo mɛnɛ ekokake , cina eejimeli . BaEjipeto ko , ameka bo bokɔ boa , bagwa a madiba .
58011030	Ama bo hombâ Yeliko masu sambo , mongba-momatai mongando momi sopea oko bosopea cina eejimeli .
58011031	Laba , mwali ondukeli , aigwa na bato balipanga , cina eejimeli , mojɔ bo asɔ kɛngi na bowi .
58011032	Mojɔ motongo môbala mbi nda ? Ehole etakaka na mbi a botɔndɔ mijɔ miGidona , na Balaka , na Samasona , na Yepeta , na Dawidi , na Samwele , na batɔndɔi .
58011033	Edaka oko a mojɔ moejimeli bo bagbokeja makumu , basambeja mijɔ na soti , basɔ madikeja , badipa minɔkɔ migbɔngɔ ,
58011034	badima ngulu emosa , bahela a mwɛngɔ moabɛnɛ , basɔ ngulu a tei eyogo , badaka bato bapipo a bila , na bacieja mandundu masoki jibu .
58011035	Bali basɔ koko bato babu baya bahula a bogwa . Batongo batuama nji oko a bogwa , pɛ bojima bo bacinoame , bo bangɔe a bomɔ bua bonɔi na bopele .
58011036	Eatongo koko badingoana matangola , na nji , ee na minyɔlɔ , na blɔkɔ pongono .
58011037	Baba’la matai , baba’la na misumani , bagwa na abɛnɛ , balwa biobo bibata na kambɛli ; badaka na bokwali , na esɔpi , na jɔɔlɔ enɛnɛ .
58011038	Ngondo eibɔngɔ a mojɔ mobu ; njea jibu jidaka oko a lisobe , na a meno , a mimbɔndɔ , na a bibubondo bingondo .
58011039	Ibo basusu bangameja ejimeli ebu , pɛ ko bosɔ mua modikejama .
58011040	Mojɔ bo Njambe asɛlingoa mokina mojɔ mua monɔi na bopele a mojɔ mosu , bo bobɔngɔ bobu bodae na su pongono .
58012001	Lindundu linɛnɛ libatati lihikaka so . A mojɔ momina , bopele bo bodumbe mina misusu mitombaka so , na bobe bua bobindanejaka so , bo bopote na lingbangba a njea yena edi a boso bosu .
58012002	Kwani miso masu madae oko ai Yesu , yona obanga na yona odi bobɔngeja ejimeli esu . Iyo ahɔnɔ mole-mobokea , na alɛ bo sɔni emina edi eka engasa , oko a mojɔ mosepi yena edaka a boso bonde , na adi a edie a ebɔ ebami emongbɛlɛngɔ moNjambe .
58012003	Kinani bolɛ bonu bodae ai yo yona ohɔnɔ lisoki libato babe , bo osaka ngwaeni , na oSaka mbɛni a milema minu .
58012004	Anaka no bila na bobe , makia manu masopeakini a bila emina .
58012005	Na obosaini eleho yena elehaka no o bana ; Mwana’mbi , t’olɛe oko bo bosisa boKumu bodi mojɔ mokɛkɛ . Akalemoa na wɛ , t’omɛmɛlɛe oko .
58012006	Mojɔ bo , Kumu akapala moto , amosisaka , Na atuaka bana basusu basɔkɔ yo .
58012007	Dani na lingbangba a tei ebosisa . Njambe akojaka no o bana . Okwa mwana adi , na sangwa’nde pɛ bomotna ?
58012008	Nji jidi a mojɔ monu basusu . Omiti sɔni nji , oditini bana basoti , oko bana babɔɔli .
58012009	Isa bodaka na lisuma ai basangwa’su ya nase baya batua so , bota-suma Sango omiembo na lisuma linɛnɛ bo bohele ?
58012010	Basangwa’su hatua so ehole ekue , yana adaka bo na bolɛ bomina . Njambe ko atuaka so a bobɔngeja so , bo bosɛ libondo libosɛnɔ bonde .
58012011	Bosisa bosusu bodi na mwano a ehole emina , te nongo sepi . Bato ko hakakoa na mojɔ momina , bosisa bomina bobotaka mbuma jibowi na bodongo ai bo .
58012012	A mojɔ momina , pingejani mɔmɔ manu maya mangwai , na muli manu maya madi ma yɛmbu .
58012013	Liani njea jitangboake a mojɔ mobibota binu , bo yona otɛngɔkɔ atabukea ekɔ , oko bo ahɛe na ngulu .
58012014	Kɔni na ngulu enu esusu bo odaeni na bato basusu oko bowi , na bo odaeni na bosɛnɔ , mojɔ bo moto amiti da na bosɛnɔ atanɛ nongo Kumu .
58012015	Nganjamani bo okina moto atakputoa bosɔ monganji moNjambe , bo mokina monginga moboyo mosaka tɔ , a bonɔngeja no , na a bobeja bato banɛnɛ .
58012016	Nganjamani bo okwa onu atada moto obɔɔli , pɛpɛ ejimeli , o adaka Esau yona osɔmbɔtɔnɔ lisango linde lisɔmi a mojɔ moteni emɔci edia .
58012017	Ojebakani bo yana adaka yo na posa ngɔngɔ a bosangoa bopamboa , alonama oko bolonama ; nongo aduka yo na mbisoli , aiboloja nongo pokiso a bohekoja molema .
58012018	Ino oibatamani na mono momɔmɔkɔ bato na mɔmɔ , mua mongoa na mosa , na modidi , na eyembi , na mopomba ,
58012019	na doi limondule , na doi likɔpi ; baya baka kɔpi emina bangɔɔnɔ bo ekinaekenge etongo etabalama na bu .
58012020	Mojɔ bo baihɔnɔ mobeko bo , Nongo tito akabatama na mono , badi bomo’la matai .
58012021	Mojɔ momina modaka maneene mɛnɛ . Mose yo mɛnɛ abala bo , Mbi nadi na bɔ na mongongoma .
58012022	Ino ko odoini a Mono moSiona , a ngando eNjambe obomɔ , Yelusalema yena eDiko , ai mandundu mababwɛnji-baDiko pɛ njɛngi .
58012023	Odoini a likita na denga dibana basɔmi baya badi na kombe jibu oho Diko , ai Njambe yona odi Juji obato basusu , a miembo Mibato baejimeli baya babɔngɔ .
58012024	Na odoini ai Yesu yona okwea bosiili na Mokongo Moyene , na a makia maya mamɛsɛmi ; na makia mande , na makia maAbela , makia mande manɔi na bwɛnji bopele .
58012025	Nganjamani , osaka lonani boka yona obalaka . Mojɔ bo , isa bato baihela baya balona boka yona obaleha ya nase , esingaiti so , boka-sɛtoja yona obalaka oho Diko ; iso bohela na ye ?
58012026	Ngondo ejonga a mojɔ mokɔpi ende a ehole emina . Na sako ende edi e dɛye bo , Mbi nadi bojongeja koko ehole etongo , te ngondo pɛ , oko Diko pongono .
58012027	Koko ehole etongo ; ekenge emina edi na cina bo leka lua lojongabí lodi bokindoa elimo etongo , bo leka lua lobwaniti bokumana lodi boyeyoa .
58012028	Bokumu bosɔkɔ so bobwamti bokumana ; a mojɔ momina , kinani bosakoe Njambe na bosakoa bosoti , oko na lisuma na bɔ .
58012029	Mojɔ bo Njambe osu adi mosa mɛnɛ mua mosiejaka oko bosieja .
58013001	Pɛ bokinani bopalana o baninga .
58013002	T’obosaeni oko bokɔ monganji ai midoa , mojɔ bo bakina baya bakɔ boa basɔ babwɛnji , pɛ ko bojeba .
58013003	Pɛ bobosani bato baya badi a blɔkɔ ; lɛni bo odini na bu a blɔkɔ no bɛnɛ . Pɛ bobosani bato baya badingoaka , mojɔ bo odini na mikuku no bɛnɛ .
58013004	Bolongana bobwani boda mojɔ molisuma ai bato basusu , na esambe emomi na mwali ebwani boda na bosɛnɔ . Mojɔ bo Njambe adi bosambeja bato balisɔngi na bato babɔɔli .
58013005	T’odaeni oko na posa elikonja . Dani na sepi a mojɔ moleka lopeli no , mojɔ bo Njambe abala bo , Mbi nitakwa wɛ , nitabulɛ wɛ nongo mweka .
58013006	A mojɔ momina bobwani bobala na ejimeli esu esusu bo , Kumu adi Mokɔmeja ombi ; nitabanga nongo eka . Moto adi bokɔ ai mbi ndeni ?
58013007	Pɛ bobosani basuku banu baya batɔndɔ no mwako moNjambe . Lɛni suka emihelo Mibu ; ikoanani na ejimeli ebu .
58013008	Yesu Masiya adi busa bu , o adaka yo busa bi , na adi boda boa oko na bosusu mɛnɛ .
58013009	T’ojimeni oko bo makoja mayene matongotongo mala-bojae no . Njea esoti edi bo molema momoto mosɔkɔ ngulu oko na monganji moNjambe , te nongo na leka loboyaka . Baya bajimaka leka lomina baibɔngɔ nongo a mojɔ momina .
58013010	Iso bodi na litumbu limasiko , na baya bakɔkɔ elomu ebu a Etondo baditi na kpaci a boyaka a litumbu limina .
58013011	Mojɔ bo Nganga Monɛnɛ akweaka a Esika-eBosɛnɔ na makia matito , o lisiko a mojɔ mobobe , na batumbaka njemba jitito bamina a sokolu engando .
58013012	Oko boa , Yesu pongono adingoa a sokolu emongba mongando , bo asɛnojae bato na makia mande mɛnɛ .
58013013	A mojɔ momina , atombaka so muna mobiloli a mojɔ monde , kinani bomane ai yo a sokolu engando .
58013014	Mojɔ bo boditi na ngando eboyeyoa ya nase . Ngando edukaka so edi ngando ebodoa .
58013015	Yɛni so bopɛ lisiko libosakoa ai Njambe bihole bisusu , oko na nde ; cina emina edi mbuma jimaposo maminɔkɔ maya majimaka kombe ende .
58013016	Pɛ bobosani bilomu bipele bokɔ , na boda na likabo ; masiko Inaya mase-pejaka Njambe oko ma .
58013017	Sumakani basuku banu , na kɔni o apalaka bo , mojɔ bo badi o banjeli bamilema minu , o bato baya badi boneja elomu ebu . Kɔni bo elomu ebu edae na sepi , te nongo na manji , osaka samboani no bɛnɛ .
58013018	Ingakani a mojɔ mosu . Bojimaka bo boditi na mojɔ a molema . Posa esu edi bo bodae na ekɔmɛli epele a njea jisusu .
58013019	Mbi nalebaka no na bopipo bo Okɔeni boa , bo nasɔmbe ai no bokpa .
58013020	Njambe obowi angɔjɔ koko Kumu osu Yesu a bogwa , Monjeli Monɛnɛ obata , na makia maMokongo mua modi na bosusu .
58013021	Yɛ abɔngejae no na ngando jisusu jipele a bokɔ bolulea bonde , na akɔe a tei enu o apalaka yo , a mojɔ moYesu Masiya . Ekumu ai yo oko na bosusu . Amen .
58013022	Mbi nangɔɔnɔkɔ no baninga bo osɛni bopele ekenge ye eeleho embi , mojɔ bo nasɔnei no oko mokanda mokue .
58013023	Obwanmi bojeba bo bacingoi mwangwa’su Timoteo . Akamea bokpa , iso na nde bodi bo’nɛnɛ na nu .
58013024	Abɛjɛni basuku banu basusu , na bato baDenga basusu . Bato baltalia babɛjɛkɛ no njɛbɛ .
58013025	Yɛ monganji moNjambe modae na nu basusu . Amen .
59001001	Njɛbɛ embi Yakobo , mokɔmɛli oNjambe na oKumu Yesu Masiya , ai makota domi-na-mabae maya manangana .
59001002	Baninga , okanɛni bomeka tungu na tungu , dani na sepi a mojɔ momina .
59001003	Ojebakani bo ejimeli enu ekamekama , lingbangba linu lidi bohɛ .
59001004	Lingbangba ko libwani bokɔ elomu ebɔngɔke mɛnɛ bo odaeni bato babɔngɔke , pɛ botaka nongo mokina mojɔ .
59001005	Okina onu akataka bowɛi , yɛ ange Njambe , nongo asɛ ; mojɔ bo yo adi na likabo linɛnɛ ai bato basusu , atajuma nongo mweka .
59001006	Adi bongako na ejimeli , pɛpɛ nongo kitɛ ; mojɔ bo yona odi na kitɛ adi o mula momadiba mua molindoamaka na mopimboaka na pwea .
59001007	Moto omina abwaniti bolɛ bo adi bosɔ eka ai Kumu ,
59001008	mojɔ bo adi moto omilema Mibae , na ekɔmɛli ende esusu edi na mokakwano .
59001009	Moto obokwali akasɔ ekina ekumu , yɛ adae na sepi a mojɔ momina ;
59001010	na moto olikonja akasamboa , yɛ asepe pongono , mojɔ bo yo adi bogwa o agwaka malɛkɛ manjienjie .
59001011	Busa bokahoa , na moi mokagbasoa , njienjie jiwɔsɔsɔkɔ oko bowɔsɔsɔ , malɛkɛ makwaka na esɛngɔ emina esusu esiaka . Moto olikonja adi bowɔsɔsɔ koko boa a tei ebilomu binde .
59001012	Moto akahɔnɔ bomeka , moto omina adi na bojongoa ; mojɔ bo , akapasama adi bosɔ likongo libomɔ lidikeja Njambe ai baya bamo-palaka .
59001013	Moto akamekama , abwaniti bobala bo , Njambe amekaka mbi ; mojɔ bo Njambe atamekamaka na bobe , na atamekaka moto .
59001014	Moto ko amekamaka yana alaboaka yo na posa jinde mɛnɛ jia jimolɛngɛkɛ .
59001015	Posa ekalwa , ebotaka oko bobe , na bobe bokagbasoa bobotaka oko bogwa .
59001016	Pɛ bobungani , baninga baepaeli .
59001017	Bipeeli bisusu bipele , na toma jisusu jibɔngɔke , jihulaka oho diko ai Sango obohu bosusu . Iyo adi na bosusu oko tungu emɔci ; esie ebohekoa bonde editi .
59001018	Iyo abota so na ebaeli esoti , oko a mojɔ mobolulea bonde mɛnɛ , bo bodae o mbuma jiboso jibato bande .
59001019	Baninga bambi baepaeli , jebani mojɔ mu . Yɛ moto na moto adae na njoki a bohokea , pɛ ko bobala bokpa-bokpa , na pɛ boka kɛlɛ bokpa .
59001020	Mojɔ bo kɛlɛ emoto etasukeaka na bodongo boNjambe .
59001021	Oko boa , toma dumbani bosɔtɔ bosusu , na njani jinɛnɛ jibobe . Kinani Ebaeli ekwee o ngua a tei emilema minu mi yɛmbu , Ebaeli yena ebwani boheleja miembo minu .
59001022	Kɔni o akojaka Ebaeli . T’odaeni oko bato baya ba’kaka pɛ , baya basakoseaka bo bɛnɛ .
59001023	Mojɔ bo yona o’kaka Ebaeli , pɛ ko bokɔ , adi o moto yona onjaka elimo eboso bonde a talatala .
59001024	Anjaka elimo ende , na akadonga , abosaka bokpa elimo ende .
59001025	Yona ko onjaka a tei eMobeko mosoti , Mobeko mobosɔmi , na akada na lingbangba , na akakɔ oko bokɔ , te nongo moto yona o’kaka na abo-saka , moto omina adi bosɔ bojongoa na bokɔ .
59001026	Isa moto alɛkɛ bo adi na ejimeli ai Njambe , pɛ ko bogbokeja yemi ende , akoseaka molema monde mɛnɛ ; ejimeli emoto omina edi eka engasa .
59001027	Ejimeli esoti yena edi na bosɛnɔ a miso maNjambe Sangwa’su edi oko ye , — a bonja bana-bamalike na bali-babogwa a minɔngɔ Mibu , na a bosabanea , pɛpɛ nongo litɔnɔ lipita jingondo .
59002001	Baninga , adi no na ejimeli ai Kumu osu Yesu Masiya , Kumu oEkumu , Podaeni oko na ekɔmɛli ebokumeja bakina bato , na bolona batongo .
59002002	Okina moto akadoa a botitana bonu na elwali ebobuno bonɛnɛ , na pɛtɛ jiwɔlɔ a sapi ; na moto obokwali akakwea oko na bipupu pɛ ;
59002003	na okanjani oko moto yona odi na elwali epele a bobala na nde bo , Da ya a edie ye epele ; na okabalani na moto obokwali bo , Ima oho , isa , Da ya nase a dɔngɔ diegboto embi ;
59002004	okakɔni boa , otakabakani bato a Milema minu ? Otasambe-jakani bato na bilɛli bibe ?
59002005	Baninga baepaeli , hokeani . Njambe ahɔ bato babokwali bangondo mojɔ bo likonja libu lidi oko ejimeli , bo badae basangoli baBokumu bodikeja yo ai baya bamopalaka .
59002006	Ino ko osambojakani moto obokwali . Banɔngejaka no banda , te bato balikonja ? Bagbulaka no a bisambi banda , te bo ?
59002007	Kombe yena ebeama na nu edi na ekumu ; baloleaka ko kombe emina banda , te bato bamina ?
59002008	Okɔkɔni bopele isa osumakani Mobeko moKumu mua mosɔnɔmɔ a Misɔnɔ bo , Toma pala motuteano mowɛ o asapalaka wɛ mɛnɛ .
59002009	Okakumejani ko bakina bato , na okalonani batongo , okɔkɔni bobe ; na Mobeko modumbaka no o bato babe .
59002010	Mojɔ bo , moto aka-kputoa na mojɔ momɔci pɛ , adi na lindo jiMibeko misusu , nongo akasuma misusu mitongo .
59002011	Yona obala bo , T’ongɛe oko bɔɔli , abala koko bo , T’owoe oko moto . Oko boa , okawa moto , osopaka Mobeko , nongo adi wɛ pɛ bongɛ nongo bɔɔli .
59002012	Kinani bibaeli binu na bikɔmɛli binu bibwane na bato baya badi bosamba na Mibeko Mibosɔmi .
59002013	Mojɔ bo , moto yona opeliti wa atasamba na wa . Wa edi bolonga a esambi .
59002014	Baninga , moto akabala bo adi na ejimeli na apeliti bikɔmɛli , adi bobɔngɔ na ye ? Ejimeli emina ebwani bomoheleja ?
59002015	Isa mwananange’moto , isa ngɛnɛ emoto adi mbundu , na adi na nja busa na busa ,
59002016	na okwa onu akabala na bu bo , Kɛ bopele , sahumeja na mosa , na gola na dia , pɛ ko bobapa leka a mojɔ momikuku Mibu , mojɔ momina mobɔngi ?
59002017	Oko boa , ejimeli ngasa , pɛ bikɔmɛli , edi oko eka ego .
59002018	Okina moto ko adi bobala bo , Wɛ odi na ejimeli ; mbi nadi na bikɔmɛli . Anejani ejimeli ewɛ yena edi ngasa , pɛpɛ bikɔmɛli , na mbi nadi boneja wɛ ejimeli embi oko na bikɔmɛli bimbi .
59002019	Ojimaka bo Njambe adi omɔci ; mojɔ momina modi mopele . Endele ko , miembo Mibe mijimaka pongono , na midi na bongongoma .
59002020	Wɛ egegele , otajebaka bo ejimeli ngasa , pɛpɛ bikɔmɛli edi eka engasa ?
59002021	Tata osu Abalayama ailonga a cina ebikɔmɛli yana abakea yo mwana’nde Isaka a litumbu o lisiko ?
59002022	Onɛkɛ bo ejimeli edaka ecingi na bikɔmɛli binde ; ejimeli ende ebɔngɔ oko na bikɔmɛli binde .
59002023	Oko boa mosɔnɔ mongama mua mobalaka bo , Abalayama ajimea Njambe , na mojɔ momina molangama ai yo o bodongo , na bamobea Limbaci liNjambe .
59002024	Onɛkɛ bo moto alongaka na bikɔmɛli , te na ejimeli ngasa .
59002025	Laba , mwali ondukeli , alonga koko boa na bikɔmɛli yana asɔ yo kɛngi na abayaneja a njea etongo .
59002026	Mokuku mokada ngasa , pɛpɛ mwembo , modi oko mogwake ; ejimeli edi koko boa ; isa eciniti na bikɔmɛli edi eka ego .
59003001	Baninga bambi , T’ojimeni oko bo banɛnɛ banu badae bakoja . Mojɔ bo ojebakani bo so baya bakojaka bodi bosamba na esambi epipo .
59003002	Iso basusu bodi na mabunga manɛnɛ . Isa moto aditi nongo na libunga a ebaeli ende , adi moto mobɔngɔke mɛnɛ yona odi na ngulu bo asangbindee mokuku mosusu .
59003003	Bokasa bibende a minɔkɔ mipunda bo basume so , bodi bohekoja mikuku Mibu misusu .
59003004	Lɛni masua pongono ; nongo makada manɛnɛnɛ na mahudamaka na pwea jipipo , madi bohekoa a mojɔ moyenda ekɛkɛlɛkɛ , o apalaka moto oyenda .
59003005	Yemi edi koko boa ; edi licinga likɛkɛ limokuku , esakumejaka ko na ngando jinɛnɛnɛ . Mokonda mosusu mobwani bongoa na mosa mokɛkɛlɛkɛ mɛnɛ .
59003006	Na yemi edi mosa ; yemi edi bokumu bobobe a tei emacinga masu ; ebejaka mokuku mosusu , na etumbaka mohelo momoto na mosa moGehena .
59003007	Bato hahɔnɔkɔ bogbokeja tito , na mbulu , na njɔ , na tito bamadiba ; na babagbokejaka , tungu jisusu .
59003008	Pɛpɛ nongo moto ko ojebaka bogbokeja yemi . Bobe boyemi bopehti mbɔci ; elumi na mbondo mɛnɛ .
59003009	Bosakoaka Kumu na Sangwa’su na yemi , na bosingaka bato baya bayoama a blimo eNjambe oko na yemi .
59003010	Bosakoa na masingi mamanaka a monɔkɔ momɔci ! Baninga , mojɔ momina mobɔngiti .
