59003011	Mokɛlɛ momɔci modi bomeja madiba mapele na madiba mabe pongono ?
59003012	Baninga , bomwe bodi bobota makpa ? Lingolo lidi bobota mamwe ? Oko boa pongono , madiba mamukwa matameja nongo madiba mapele .
59003013	Okina onu adi na bowɛi na ejebeli emijɔ ? Mohelo monde mopele modi boneja bikɔmɛli bipele , oko na molema motitake mobowɛi
59003014	Isa odini na likaka na mosoo a milema minu , pɛ bosa-kumejani , pɛ bonganani mojɔ moSoti .
59003015	Bowɛi bomina boditi bowɛi boDiko ; bodi oko bowɛi bongondo ye , bowɛi bua bocingi na Posa jimokuku , na miembo Mibe .
59003016	Mojɔ bo , isa likaka na misoo midi a ekwa esika , miano na bikɔmɛli bisusu bibe bidi koko ena .
59003017	Bowɛi bodiko bodi boso bosɛnɔke ; bodi koko na bowi na bo yɛmbu ; bohokeaka mijɔ na molema bwase ; bolumi na wa na mbuma jipele ; boditi na minɔkɔ Inibae , isa na bokosea .
59003018	Baya badukaka bowi banaka ngua jibowi , na badi bobuka mbuma jibowi .
59004001	Mane na miano a tei enu mahulaka jɔ ? Mitahulaka a posa jinu jia jinaka a tei ebinama binu ?
59004002	Omboakani pɛ ko bodiha , na owakani . Odini na mbengia , pɛ ko bohɔnɔ bosɔ . Oko boa onakani , na odini na miano . Opelitini eka , mojɔ bo ota’ngakani .
59004003	Onga-kani pɛ ko bosɔ , mojɔ bo ongakani na libunga , na njingo bo onamejaeni mua mongaka no na posa jinu jibe .
59004004	Ino Bali bandukeli ! Otajebakani bo limbaci lingondo lidi lisoki ai Njambe ? Oko boa , moto yona opalaka bo apande limbaci na ngondo adi na Njambe oko soki .
59004005	Ino odingakani bo ebaeli eMisɔnɔ edi ngasa yena ebalaka bo , Epaeli ende edi na likaka a mojɔ momwembo mokɔ yo a boda a tei esu ?
59004006	Iyo ko ahɛjɛkɛ monganji oko bohɛjɛ . A mojɔ momina Misɔnɔ Mibalaka bo , Njambe anaka na bato baegbo , Adi ko na monganji ai bato bamilema mititake .
59004007	Oko boa toma sumani Njambe . Imani a bona na Satana na adi bocia no .
59004008	Sabateani na Njambe , na yo adi bosabatea na nu . Ino bato babe , sɛnojani mɔmɔ manu . Ino bato babokosea , sɛnojani milema minu bopɛɛ .
59004009	Dani na esɔpi ; yeani kɔndɔ na mbisoli . Yɔ enu ebwani bohekoa bio , na sepi enu ebwani bohekoa wa .
59004010	Satitejani a boso boNjambe , na yo adi bongɔjɔ no .
59004011	Baninga , t’olɔngɔneni oko . Moto akalɔngɔ mwangwa’nde , isa akasambeja mwangwa’nde , alɔngɔkɔ Mibeko , na asambejaka Mibeko . Isa osambejaka Mibeko , otasumaka Mibeko , na osabakeaka juji .
59004012	Obakeaka Mibeko oko omɔci pɛ ; juji omɔci oko yo , yona obwani boheleja isa bodumba . Wɛ ko yona osambejaka minao moto , wɛ odi nda ?
59004013	Hokeani e dɛye , no bato baya babalaka bo , Bodi bokɛ a ekina ngando busa bu isa puma ; bodi boyeyoa oho yanga emɔci a bokɔ bwasa na bohɛjɛ likonja lisu .
59004014	Otajehakani nongo mojɔ mua mobwani bokwa puma . Mohelo monu modi bo ? Odini oko lidudu , pɛ , lia liyeyoaka mweka , na lidimoaka oko bodimoa .
59004015	Obwanini bobala bo , Njambe akajima , bôda na bomɔ , bôkɔ mojɔ mu , isa mojɔ mua .
59004016	E dɛye ko , osakumejakani na egbo enu . Bosakumeja bomina bodi mojɔ mobe .
59004017	Moto yona ojebaka bokɔ bopele , pɛ ko bokɔ bopele , akɔkɔ oko bobe .
59005001	Ino bato balikonja , yeani mbisoli e dɛye ; ngbɛngbɛmɛni a mojɔ mominɔngɔ mia mikɛkɛ adoe ai no .
59005002	Makonja manu mapɔi ; bisenja binu bibehi na sɛ .
59005003	Wɔlɔ enu , na likonja linu lipalata , libehi na bikpa ; bikpa bimina bidi botata tati a bodumba no , na bidi boyaka mini minu o ekɔmɛli emosa . Ino obombini likonja linɛnɛ a masu masuka .
59005004	Hokeani ; likonja lisonge libasali banu baya baliaka gbie jinu , likonja litombi no na bokosea , libekoaka oko bobekoa . Bio bibasali baya babisaka a gbie bimei a matoi maKumu oma-ndundu madiko .
59005005	Ogolakani ya nase na leka lopele , pɛ bosajumani nongo eka . Ogolejakani milema minu a busa bomogweli monɛnɛ .
59005006	Odumbini na owoini moto obodongo , na yo pɛ boswiana na nu .
59005007	Baninga , toma dani na lingbangba oko a bodoa boKumu . Anjani moto yona odi na gbie ; yo ambaka mbuma jipele jigbie , na adi na lingbangba oko a ehole ekwaka mbua baboso na mbua basuka a gbie .
59005008	Toma dani na lingbangba koko boa . Pingejani milema minu , mojɔ bo bodoa boKumu bodi hulelu .
59005009	T’ohimaneni oko baninga , osaka sambani . Hokeani ; juji adi a modipe .
59005010	Baninga , ikoanani na batɔndɔi baya babala a kombe eKumu , ikoanani na lingbangba libu a bodingoa .
59005011	Iso bosakoaka bato baya badaka na lingbangba . Ojebakani mojɔ molingbangba liJobo , na onɛni mokano moKumu ai yo , mojɔ bo Kumu adi na wa na monganji botɔ .
59005012	Baninga , mojɔ monɛnɛ mɛnɛ oko mu ; — t’obɛlɛni oko bɛli , isa bɛli a mojɔ moDiko , isa bɛli a mojɔ mongondo , isa ekina bɛli etongo . Kwani mojimo monu modae oko Ee , na bongana bonu oko pɛpɛ , bo otakwani na mojɔ .
59005013	Isa okina onu adi na monɔngɔ , adi bonga Njambe . Isa okina onu adi na sepi adi bo’mba njembo .
59005014	Isa okina onu adi na yogo , adi bobea basuku baDenga . Ibo badi bonga Njambe a mojɔ monde na badi bomosuoa munɛ a kombe eKumu .
59005015	Na bonga bua bodi na ejimeli bodi boheleja moto yona opekaka , na Kumu adi bomo-ngɔjɔ . Isa akɔi mikina mijɔ Mibe , adi bosɔ bo yɛ bojibe .
59005016	A mojɔ momina , toma bolojani jibe jinu , moto ai mina’nde moto , na ingani Njambe , moto a mojɔ momina’nde moto , bo oheleni .
59005017	Elia adaka moto na ekɔmɛli emoto o adi so bɛnɛ . Iyo anga Njambe na bingi bo mbua atakwa , na mbua aikwa a ngondo bianga bisato na songe basamano .
59005018	Anga koko Njambe , na mbua ahula Diko , na kpɔtɔ jibota koko .
59005019	Baninga bambi , okwa onu akalaboa a njea esoti , na okwa otongo akamohuleja ,
59005020	moto omina abwani bojeba bo yona ohulejaka moto mobe a njea elibunga linde , adi boheleja mwembo momoto omina a bogwa , na adi bokunda jibe jinɛnɛ .
60001001	Mbi Pɛtɛlo , obwɛnji oYesu Masiya , ai bato bangabi baya banangana a Ponto , Galatia , Kapodokia , Asia , na Bitunia ,
60001002	ai bato bahɔ Njambe na mbuno ende mɛnɛ , bato bahɛngɛ yo na Mwembo bo badae na lisuma ai Yesu Masiya , na bo bamɛsɛme na makia mande . Yɛ monganji moNjambe na bowi bohɛe ai no bou mɛnɛ .
60001003	Ekumu ai Njambe Sange ’ Kumu osu Yesu Masiya . Edi oko a mojɔ momonganji monde monɛnɛ bo so bobotama koko a boda na njingo ebomɔ , ema ebongɔ boYesu Masiya a bogwa ,
60001004	na bo bosangoe lisango lia litabeha nongo , lisango lisɛnɔke lia litagwa , lia lihɛngɛmɛ ai no oho Diko .
60001005	Njambe abaneaka no na ngulu ende cina eejimeli , a mojɔ momohelo mosɛlingoa yo , mua modi boboloa a bohu a ehole esuka .
60001006	Sepani a mojɔ momina , nongo adingoaka no ehole ekue na minɔngɔ tungu na tungu .
60001007	Oko boa , bomeka boejimeli enu bôda na bosakoa , na ekumu , na lisuma , a bodoa boYesu Masiya . Mojɔ bo , isa bamekaka wɔlɔ na mosa , wɔlɔ eka ebobeha , esingaiti ejimeli enu yena enɔi wɔlɔ na yumu .
60001008	Ino omonɛkinini , omopalakani ko . Nongo adi no pɛ bomonɛ e dɛye , omojimakani , na osepakani a mojɔ monde na sepi pɛ njɛngi yena enɔi kɔpi emoto .
60001009	Suka eejimeli enu edi bo osɛni mohelo momiembo minu .
60001010	Batɔndɔi baya bapa biseko a mojɔ momonganji mua mohɛngɛmɛ ai no , baduka na batunda a mojɔ mobohela bomina .
60001011	Yana apaka bo biseko a mojɔ momadingoa maMasiya , na ekumu yena edaka ecini ngɔngɔ , badaka na posa ebojeba moto omina na ehole elɛjɛkɛ Mwembo moMasiya a tei ebu .
60001012	Mojɔ moboloa ko ai bo , bo ngando jisɔkɔ bo jidaka a mojɔ monu , te nongo a mojɔ mobu bɛnɛ . Na bato baya batɔndɔki no Mwako Mopele na ngulu eMwembo Mosɛnɔke mua mohula Diko , babolojai ngando jimina ai no . Babwɛnji-baDiko badi koko na posa bo bacingee ngando jimina .
60001013	A mojɔ momina , toma ngbimejani bocingea bonu ; sangbi-ndeani ; kinani njingo enu esusu edae a monganji moNjambe mua modoabi ai no yana aboloabi Masiya .
60001014	Dani bana balisuma ; pɛ bogbokani na posa jibe , jia jidaka na nu a ehole elibumi linu .
60001015	Iyona obea no adi mosɛnɔke ; oko boa toma dani basɛnɔke pongono a mida minu misusu .
60001016	Mosɔnɔmɔ bo , Ino ôdani basɛnɔke , mojɔ bo mbi nadi mosɛnɔke .
60001017	Iyo asambejaka moto na moto bongbebongbe cina ebikɔmɛli binde , na okamo’ngani o Sango , kinani mida minu misusu midae oko na bɔ a ehole emɔngɔ monu ya nase .
60001018	Ojebakani bo osikoamani a ngando jingasangasa jibasangwa’nu , te nongo na makonja mabo-beha o adi wɔlɔ na palata ;
60001019	osikoamani oko na makia mayumu maMasiya , o makia mamwana-bata yona opeliti nongo litɔnɔ , pɛpɛ nongo ehuli .
60001020	Iyo ahɛngɛmɛ a mojɔ momina oko ngondo epe-takini yoama , na adoa a masu masuka a mojɔ monu .
60001021	Ejimeli enu ai Njambe edi a njea ende . Na Njambe amongɔjɔ a bogwa , na amokumeja , bo ejimeli enu , na njingo enu , jidae oko ai yo .
60001022	Lisuma linu a mijɔ miSoti lisɛnojai milema minu , bo odaeni na epaeli esoti ai baninga ; oko boa toma palanani na ngulu emilema minu .
60001023	Obotamani koko na bobotama bobomɔ , te nongo na bobotama bobogwa , oko na ebaeli eNjambe yena edi mɔ , yena eyeyoaka oko na bosusu .
60001024	Mojɔ bo , Bato basusu badi o njienjie ; Ekumu emoto edi o ihlɛlɛ jinjienjie ; Njienjie jiwɔsɔsɔkɔ , na fulɛlɛ jikwaka nase ;
60001025	Ebaeli eNjambe ko eyeyoaka oko na bosusu . Ebaeli emina edi oko Mwako Mopele mua motɔndɔmɔ ai no .
60002001	Dumbani bobe bosusu , na epulu esusu , na bokosea , na likaka , na malɔngi masusu .
60002002	Adi no bana baya bapakiti botama , kwani posa enu edae a mabɛ masɛnɔke mamwembo , bo okandoeni a mojɔ mobohela ,
60002003	isa onɛni na soti bo Kumu adi na monganji .
60002004	Doani ai yo , oko a Litai lia lidi mɔ ; bato balilona ; Njambe ko alihɔ , na lidi na yumu a miso mande .
60002005	Ino pongono toma dani matai maya madi mɔ , maya mayoama a ndako emwembo , na nganga basɛnɔke a bopa masiko mamwembo maya masepejaka Njambe a njea eYesu Masiya .
60002006	Modi a Misɔnɔ bo , Anjani ; mbi nasambeaka litai a Siona , Litai lihɔ mbi a mojɔ molikulu , na lidi na yumu . Na yona omojimeaka atasamboa .
60002007	Oko boa yo adi na yumu ai no baya bajimaka . A mojɔ mobato ko baya batajimaka , Litai lilona bayoi Lidi litai limogbukusu lilikulu .
60002008	na Litai limina lidi bosakeja bato , Lidi litai linɛnɛnɛ a bokweja bato . Mojɔ bo basakaka libaku cina bo batasumaka Ebaeli ; suka ebu edi boa .
60002009	Ino ko odini mbota ehɔmɔke , nganga babokumu , likota lihɛngɛmɛke , bato baNjambe , bo onejaeni bilomu bipele binde yona obea no bo omaneni a modidi , a boda a bohu bonde bua bodi mojɔ mobokamoa .
60002010	Odakani boso bato bangasa ; e dɛye ko odini bato baNjambe . A ehole emina , oipaka , sɔni monganji moNjambe ; e dɛye ko osini monganji moNjambe .
60002011	Baninga , mbi nangɔɔnɔkɔ no o midoa na bakɛndɛli , bo okieni posa jibe jimokuku jia jinaka bila na mwembo .
60002012	Dani na mida mipele a tei ebapakano . Oko boa , nongo bakalɔngɔ no o bato babe , badi bonɛ bikɔmɛli binu bipele , na bakumeja Njambe a busa bobo-doa bonde ai bo .
60002013	Dani na lisuma ai bato basusu baya badi na kpaci ai no , a mojɔ mokombe eKumu ,
60002014	isa ai “ roi ” yona odi boso , isa ai bakɔmɛli bande baya basɔ kpaci ai yo , a bosambeja bato babe na bokumeja bato baya bakɔkɔ bopele .
60002015	Mojɔ bo bolulea boNjambe bodi bo ogbokejaeni bibalabala bibato babogegele , oko na bikɔmɛli binu bipele .
60002016	Odini na bosɔmi ; pɛ ko bojimani bo bosɔmi bonu bodae mokalo a mojɔ mobokɔ bobe ; dani o babuli baNjambe .
60002017	Dani na lisuma ai bato basusu . Dani na epaeli ai baninga . Bangani Njambe . Sumani “ roi ” .
60002018	Ino bakɔmɛli , sumani baswa banu na lisuma lmɛnɛ , te baya badi bapele na ba yɛmbu pɛ , oko baya badi na swɛ pongono .
60002019	Isa moto adi na lingbangba a tei eboditigoa boangasa cina elisuma linde ai Njambe , mojɔ momina modi mopele .
60002020	Okakɔni bobe , na bakatua no a mojɔ momina , na okahɔnɔni mokindo monu , obwanini bosakumeja ? Okasɔni ko minɔngɔ a mojɔ mobopele bokɔkɔ no , t’omɛmɛleni oko ; Njambe asepaka na mojɔ momina .
60002021	Mojɔ bo obeamani a njea emina , cina bo Masiya yo mɛnɛ adingoa a mojɔ menu , na akinea no ekoaneli bo osuseni mɔɔlɛ mande .
60002022	Iyo aikɔ nongo bobe . Bokosea boiboloa nongo a monɔkɔ monde .
60002023	Bamo-lolea , yo ko pɛ bosɔnibeja . Yana adingoa yo , aikɛnjɔ nongo ; asakinea a mɔmɔ mande yona osambejaka na soti .
60002024	Iyo alwa yo mɛnɛ muna mobobe bosu a mokuku monde mɛnɛ a mole-mobokea , bo so bogwɛ a bobe , na bo bohele a mojɔ mobodongo . Ino ohelani oko a mojɔ mopola jinde .
60002025	Odakani o bata balaboake ; e dɛye ko ohulini ai Monjeli na Mobanei omiembo minu .
60003001	Ino bali pongono , toma sumani bami banu ; oko boa isa bakina babu batajimaka Ebaeli , badi bohekoa cina emoda mobali babu , nongo adi bo pɛ boka Ebaeli ,
60003002	yana anɛkɛ bo moda monu mosɛnɔke molisuma .
60003003	Molilo monu mobwaniti boda molilo mosokolu , ebakeli eswe na bolwa boleka lowɔlɔ na bisenja .
60003004	Molilo monu mobwani boda a tei , mua mobombami a molema , oko mwembo mo yɛmbu mobowi ; molilo momina motabeha , na modi na yumu enɛnɛ a miso maNjambe .
60003005	Bali basɛnɔke baehele baya bajima Njambe basalila boa , na basuma bami babu .
60003006	Sala asuma Abala-yama boa , na amobea kumu onde . Ino odini bana bande , okakɔni bopɛlɛ , pɛpɛ nongo mokakwano , pɛpa nongo bɔ .
60003007	Ino bami pongono , toma dani na bolɛ ai Bali banu . Dani na lisuma ai bo , mojɔ bo badi ba yɛmbu . Ino na bo pongono odini basangoli bamonganji mobomɔ . Kɔni boa bo mokina mojɔ mosaka bindaneja bingeeli binu .
60003008	Mojɔ motongo ; dani no basusu na molema momɔci , na peye na epaeli ai baninga , na wa , na bombɔki .
60003009	Bakakɔ no bobe , t’osɔnibejaeni oko bobe ; bakalolea no , Tosɔnibejaeni oko na biloli . Sɔmbejani oko na bojongoa . Obeamani bo okɔeni boa , bo osangoeni bojongoa .
60003010	Mojɔ bo , Isa moto apalaka mohelo , Isa apalaka bonɛ masu mapele , Yɛ akine bobala bobe na yemi ende , Na bokosea na biposo bimonɔkɔ monde .
60003011	Yɛ abulɛe bobe oko bobulɛ , bo akɔe bopele ; Yɛ aduke na akimane bowi .
60003012	Mojɔ bo miso maNjambe manjaka bato babodongo , Na matoi mande mahokeaka bo’nga bobu . Boso boKumu ko bolonaka baya bakɔkɔ bobe .
60003013	Isa odini na bingi a mojɔ mobopele , odi bonɔngeja no nda ?
60003014	Nongo okadingoani a mojɔ mobodongo , sepani a mojɔ momina . T’odaeni oko na bɔ a mojɔ mobu , pɛpɛ nongo mokakwano .
60003015	Bakeani Masiya o Kumu a tei emilema minu . Isa moto adi bokokeleja no a mojɔ monjingo yena edi a tei enu , dani na mosɛlingo bihole bisusu a bosalongeja ; mosɔnibejani na ebaeli e yɛmbu elisuma .
60003016	Yɛni boda na lindo a milema minu ; oko boa , nongo bakatɔkɔlɔ no , baya bakɔkɔ boa badi bosamboa , cina eekɔmɛli enu epele a tei eMasiya .
60003017	Na bodingoa a mojɔ mobopele , na bodingoa a mojɔ mobobe , boditigoa a mojɔ mobopele bonɔi na bopele , isa bolulea boNjambe bodi boa .
60003018	Mojɔ bo Masiya yo mɛnɛ agwa ehole emɔci a mojɔ mojibe , yona obodongo a mojɔ mobato babe , bo abatee so na Njambe . Agwa a mokuku , ahela ko a mwembo .
60003019	Na akɛ a mwembo bo alehe miembo a blɔkɔ ,
60003020	oko miembo mia midaka na lipanga ehelehele , yana adaka Njambe na lingbangba a ehole eyoaka Noa masua ; na bato bomwambe a tei emasua bahela a madiba , oko bato baleka pɛ .
60003021	Madiba mamina madi embete ebatisimo ; batisimo emina editi a bodongeja mbindo a mokuku ; edi oko mojimo momolema mopele ai Njambe , na ehelejaka no e dɛye cina ebongɔ boYesu Masiya a bogwa .
60003022	Iyo akɛ oho Diko , na adi a ebɔ ebami eNjambe ; na babwɛnji baDiko na bakumu na bato bakpaci bamosumaka .
60004001	Masiya adingoa a mokuku ; oko boa sapingejani koko na bolɛ bomina . Mojɔ bo moto yona odingoi a mokuku akini bokɔ bobe ,
60004002	bo atasuma koko posa jimokuku a masu maya madikai , oko bolulea boNjambe .
60004003	Ehole yena edaka no na bikɔmɛli bibapakano esii edɛye ; mojɔ bo odakani na lisɔngi , posa jibe , bolangoa , makita mamana , matanga , na bosakoa bobilimo .
60004004	Ibo bakamoaka bo otacingamakani koko na bu a ngando ji jibe , na baloleaka no .
60004005	Bato bamina ko badi bosɔnibeja ai yona odi bosambeja baya badi mɔ na bagwake pongono .
60004006	Mojɔ bo bagwake pongono baka Mwako Mopele oko a mojɔ momina , bo bahele a njea emwembo o adi Njambe , nongo asambama bo o bato a njea emokuku .
60004007	Suka engando jisusu edi hulelu ; a mojɔ momina , sangbindeani , na dani na mongangele a mojɔ mobo’nga .
60004008	Mojɔ monɛnɛ modi bo opalaneni na ngɛnjɔ enɛnɛ , mojɔ bo ngɛnjɔ ekundaka jibe kanga jinɛnɛ mɛnɛ .
60004009	Dani na monganji , moto ai mina’nde moto ; pɛ bodani na lima .
60004010	Sakɔmejani na epeeli esi moto na moto , o bakɔmɛli baya basi monganji moNjambe tungu na tungu .
60004011	Isa moto atɔndɔkɔ mwako , abwani botɔndɔ oko mijɔ miNjambe . Moto akakɔ ekina elomu , abwani boekɔ na ngulu epaka Njambe , bo Njambe asɛ ekumu na ngando jisusu , cina eYesu Masiya . Ekumu na bokumu ai yo oko na bosusu ! Amen .
60004012	Baninga , t’okamoeni oko a mojɔ mobodingoa bua bodoi ai no o mosa a bomeka no ; moditi mojɔ mobokamoa .
60004013	Sepani ko a mojɔ momina , mojɔ bo osɔkɔni libondo limadingoa maMasiya , bo odaeni koko na sepi na enanga a boboloa boekumu ende .
60004014	Bakapɔmbeja no a mojɔ mokombe eMasiya , odini na bojongoa , mojɔ bo Mwembo moekumu , Mwembo moNjambe modi ai no .
60004015	Pɛpɛ nongo moto onu ko obwani bosɔ mokindo momowoi , isa mobi , isa moto obikɔmɛli bibe , isa moto onduki emijɔ .
60004016	Moto ko akadingoa mojɔ bo adi moto oMasiya , abwaniti boda na sɔni ; abwani bokumeja Njambe a mojɔ mokombe emina .
60004017	Mojɔ bo ehole ebosambeja Denga diNjambe emei ; na esambi ekabanga na su , suka ebato baya batasumaka Mwako Mopele moNjambe êda bo ?
60004018	Isa moto obodongo adi bohela oko na pasa , mojɔ momoto mobe , na moto yona odi pɛ bojima Njambe , môda bo ?
60004019	Oko boa , isa bolulea boNjambe bodi bo bato badingoe , badi bokɔ bopele , na badi bopeja miembo mibu a mɔmɔ maMoyoi yona obwani bojimama .
60005001	Mbi nalehaka basuku banu , mojɔ bo nadi mosuku mbi mɛnɛ , na monjɛnɛki omadingoa maMasiya , na sangoli olibondo liekumu yena eboloabí ngɔngɔ .
60005002	Baneani bwela boNjambe bua bodi a tei enu . Dani babanei babu te nongo mojɔ bo edi elomu enu , oko a mojɔ moepaeli , te nongo a mojɔ monjingo elikonja , oko a mojɔ mobingi enu bɛnɛ .
60005003	Adi no na libondo libato a bobanea , pɛ bosakumejani a boso bobu . Anejani ekoaneli epele ai bwela bosusui
60005004	Na Mobanei Monɛnɛ akadoa , ôsɔni corona eekumu yena etagwa .
60005005	Ino menga pongono , dani na lisuma ai basuku . Kinani elwali enu basusu edae oko molema motitake , moto ai mina’nde moto . Mojɔ bo Njambe alonaka bato baegbo , na akɔkɔ monganji ai baya basatitejaka .
60005006	A mojɔ momina , satitejani cina eebɔ epipo eNjambe , bo angɔjɔe no a ehole ebwanake .
60005007	Kinani Njambe akamoe muna momikakwano minu misusu , mojɔ bo bolɛ bonde bodi oko ai no .
60005008	Sangbindeani ; sɛnjɛlɛni . Satana , soki enu , adukaka bato bo aba yake , na ababɛmbɛkɛ na wio o ekɔmɛli egbɔngɔ yona ogbemaka .
60005009	Dani bambilimake a ejimeli enu , na inani na nde . Ojebakani bo baninga banu a ngondo esusu badingoaka boa .
60005010	Omaka dingoani ekina ehole , Njambe yona odi na monganji mosusu , yona obea no a tei eMasiya a ekumu ende yena etasia , adi bobɔngeja no yo mɛnɛ , adi bopingeja na bombilimeja no .
60005011	Bokumu ai yo oko na bosusu . Amen .
60005012	Mbi nanjaka Silwano o mwangwa’mbi oejimeli ; nasɔnei no mokanda mu mokue oko na ebɔ ende , a boleha no , na a bolɛjɛ no a mojɔ momonganji mosoti moNjambe . Dani bambilimake a monganji momina .
60005013	Denga diBabilo , lia lidi koko lihɔmɔke , libɛjɛkɛ no njɛbɛ , na mwana’mbi Malako koko .
60005014	Abɛjɛnɛni na njɛbɛ eepaeli . Yɛ bowi bodae na nu basusu baya badi a tei eMasiya .
61001001	Simona Pɛtɛlo , mobuli na obwɛnji oYesu Masiya , aibaya bakatani na su a ejimeli emɔci a tei ebodongo boNjambe na boMoheleja osu Yesu Masiya .
61001002	Yɛ monganji moNjambe monɛngɛe ai no , na bowi pongono , cina eejebeli enu eNjambe na eYesu Kumu osu .
61001003	Njambe , na ngulu ende , abopi bipeeli bisusu bia bibwani na mohelo na ejimeli , cina eejebeli ende yona obea so a ekumu ende na bosɛnɔ bonde .
61001004	Api so madikeja maya manɔi na yumu na bopele a tei ende , bo oheleni a bopɔ bua bodi a ngondo , bua bocini na posa jibe , cina emadikeja mamina , na bo odaeni na elimo eNjambe a tei enu .
61001005	A mojɔ momina , kɔni na bingi enu esusu a bobakea ekɔmɛli esɛnɔke a ejimeli enu , ejebeli a ekɔmɛli esɛnɔke ,
61001006	bosa-ngbindea a ejebeli , lingbangba a bosangbindea , lisuma a lingbangba ,
61001007	epaeli ai baninga a lisuma , na ngɛnjɔ ai epaeli .
61001008	Isa odini na ngando jimina , na jikanɛngɛ ai no , jikɔkɔ bo otadani bingbendele na batete a mojɔ moejebeli eKumu osu Yesu Masiya .
61001009	Ngando jimina ko jikataka na moto , moto omina adi na miso mago , t’anɛkɛ nongo bohali , na abosai bosɛnoja bonde a jibe jiyou .
61001010	Oko boa baninga , dani na bingi a bongameja bobea bonu na bohɔ bonu . Okakɔni boa otasakani nongo libaku .
61001011	Oko boa , njea ebokwea a Bokumu boKumu osu Yesu Masiya , bua bodi na bosusu , êda kanga bohu mɛnɛ ai no .
61001012	Nongo ajebaka no ngando jimina , nongo adi no bambilimake a mijɔ miSoti mipeli no , mbi nitakputoa a bolɛjɛ no ngando jimina .
61001013	Adi mbi a mokuku mu , nalɛkɛ bo nabwani bosisoja no na bilelo .
61001014	Mojɔ bo najebaka bo edikai mweka pɛ bo nakine mokuku mu , o anejani Kumu osu Yesu Masiya .
61001015	Nadi bokolea koko bo odaeni na njea a bosalɛjɛ ngando jiji , ngɔngɔ jibogwa bombi .
61001016	Mojɔ bo , yana ajebeja so no mojɔ mobodoa boKumu osu Yesu Masiya , na mojɔ mongulu ende , boitɔndɔ no masɔ maya macingi na bowɛi bobato . Iso bonɛ ekumu ende na miso masu bɛnɛ .
61001017	Iyo asɔ bosakoa na ekumu ai Njambe Sango yana ahula kɔpi a ekumu eDiko ai yo bo , Iyoyo adi Mwana’mbi ongɛnjɔ ; nasepaka na nde bou .
61001018	Iso boka kɔpi emina ekahule Diko , mojɔ bo bodaka na nde a mono mosɛnɔke .
61001019	Na bojebaka bo ebaeli ebatɔndɔi edi ebaeli esoti . Ino obwanini bohokea ebaeli emina . Edi o paka yena ehojaka esika emodidi , oko a ehole ehoaka busa na emanaka monjɔtɔ mokembe a milema minu .
61001020	Toma cingeani mojɔ mu monɛnɛ ; — pɛpɛ nongo eseko eMisɔnɔ edi na cina etongotongo a mojɔ mobato .
61001021	Mojɔ bo ebaeli ebatɔndɔi eidoa na bolulea bomoto ; bato ko baya balindama na Mwembo Mosɛnɔke babala mua mohula ai Njambe .
61002001	Batɔndɔi babokosea badaka a tei ebato ehele , na bakoja babokosea badi bongɔ a tei enu pongono . Badi bodoa na mijɔ Mibokosea a bolaboja bato na poloso . Badi bongana Kumu yona obasikoa , na likundu libu litayeyoa a bodoa .
61002002	Bato banɛnɛ ko badi boci-ngama na bu na bosambolu bobu ; na njea esoti êsamboa a mojɔ mobato bamina .
61002003	Bwasa bobu a tei enu bôda oko bikenge bibo-kosea , cina eposa elikonja . Mokindo ko mobato bamina mokoleama eyou , na likundu libu libwɛhti .
61002004	Njambe aikmea nongo babwɛnji-baDiko baya bakɔ bobe ; abadumba a Lifelo , na abadeja a mimbɔndɔ mimodidi a bo’mba esambi .
61002005	Na aikina ngondo eyou ; aheleja oko Noa , motɔndɔi oejimeli , na bato batongo sambo , yana adindeja yo ngondo ebato babe na pela .
61002006	Ajima bo asiejae ngando ji , Sɔdɔmɔ na Gomola ; na ajitumba , bo jidikae oko mihulu mimosa pɛ , bo jidae embete ai bato babe .
61002007	Aheleja Loto , moto oejimeli , yona odaka na monɔngɔ a mojɔ mobikɔmɛli bibosambolu bibato babe .
61002008	( Mojɔ bo , yana adaka moto yona oejimeli a tei ebu , adaka na esɔpi a molema monde masu masusu a mojɔ mobikɔmɛli bibu bibosambolu binɛkɛ yo na miso , na bikaka yo na matoi . )
61002009	Kumu ajebaka boheleja a bomeka baya bamojimaka , na bohɛngɛ bato babe a mojɔ momokindo mobusa boEsambi ,
61002010	ju oko baya badi babuli baposa jibu jibe jibosambolu , na basɛtojaka bato bakpaci . Bato bamina badi na jala na libwano botɔ . Te babangake bololea ngando jiekumu .
61002011	Nongo babwɛnji-baDiko baya banɔi na ngulu na kpaci , batamejaka mijɔ Mibato bamina a boso boKumu .
61002012	Bato bamina ko badi o tito baya basumaka posa jibu , baya babotama a mojɔ mobobengi na bowa ; baloleaka ngando jidi bo pɛ bocingea ; badi bogwa a mojɔ mobopɔ bobu bɛnɛ , na bâsɔ mokindo mua mobwani na bobe bobu .
61002013	Sepi ebu edi oko a bolangoa na mose . Badi bato bapita na bosɔtɔ ; agolaka bo magola a tei enu , basasepejaka oko na ngando jibu jibosambolu .
61002014	Miso mabu malumi na bɔɔli na posa ebobe . Milema Mibu milandoi na mbengia , na balɛngɛkɛ bato baya baditi bambilimake . Badi bana bamasingi .
61002015	Amabo kina njea esoti , bami ko laboa oko bolaboa , na basusaka njea eBalama , mwana ’ Bosɔlɔ yona opala bokɔ bobe a mojɔ molikonja .
61002016	Punda ko , yona opeliti kɔpi , abala na kɔpi emoto , ambɛjɛ lilale limotɔndɔi , na alemoa na nde a mojɔ mobobe bonde .
61002017	Bato bamina badi Miboka ngasa , pɛpɛ nongo madiba , na biyembi bia bilindama na lihweya . Modidi tuu monase mohɛngɛmɛ a mojɔ mobu .
61002018	Mojɔ bo balɛngɛkɛ bato baya bapakiti bɔtɔnɔ na bato balaboake ; babalɛngɛkɛ na ngando jibosambolu na jilisɔngi , oko na bibalabala bingasa biegbo .
61002019	Babadikejaka bosɔmi , ena kobo bɛnɛ badi oko babuli babosambolu . Cina bo , moto akagboka na mokina mojɔ , adi mobuli omojɔ momina .
61002020	Mojɔ bo , isa babɔtɔnɔ na bosɔtɔ bongondo cina eejebeli eKumu na Moheleja osu Yesu Masiya , na basɔmbi koko , na bagboki na ngando jimina , moda mobu mongɔngɔ monɔi moda mobu moboso na bobe .
61002021	Ama bo jeba njea yena edi bojo , ba’mi ko lona oko mobeko mosɛnɔke mosɔ bo ; akɔki bo pɛ bojeba nongo njea emina , ka enɔi na bopele .
61002022	Mokina mondɛ mosoti mongami na bu bo , Mbwa asɔmbi a mikango minde mɛnɛ ; okasosa ngulube adi bosabilingana a masɛtɛ .
61003001	Baninga , imu modi e dɛye mokanda moMibae mosɔnei mbi no . Namekaka bosisoja bolɛ bonu bopele na bileho a mikanda misusu Mibae ,
61003002	bo otabosani mijɔ Mibala batɔndɔi basɛnɔke eyou , na mobeko moKumu na Moheleja mosɔ no ai babwɛnji banu .
61003003	Mojɔ moboso — toma cingeani bo bato babiloli badi bodoa a masu masuka a mojɔ mobololea .
61003004	Badi bosuma oko posa jibu bɛnɛ ; badi bobala bo , Sako ebodoa bonde edi jɔ ? Mojɔ bo , banga na boyoa bongondo , na ehole egwa basangwa’su , ngando jisusu jidi oko amɛci .
61003005	Ibo bapalaka bodipa miso mabu a mojɔ mu bo , busa bodaka kanga ehele mɛnɛ , na ngondo pongono emana a madiba , na edaka a tei emadiba , cina eebaeli eNjambe .
61003006	Na ngondo yena edaka a ehole emina edinda na pela , na egwa , oko a mojɔ momadiba mamina .
61003007	Busa ko na ngondo yena edi e dɛye jibaneamaka cina eebaeli emina a mojɔ mobotumba ; jihɛngɛmɛ a bo’mba busa boEsambi na bodumba bobato babe .
61003008	Baninga , t’obosaeni oko mojɔ mu ; dusu limɔci libwani na bianga koto emɔci , na bianga koto emɔci bibwani na dusu limɔci , a miso maKumu .
61003009	Kumu Yakputojake nongo sako jinde o alɛkɛ bakina bato . Iyo t’angwake no , mojɔ bo atapalaka bo moto abunge nongo omɔci : apalaka bo bato bahekojae milema mibu kanga basusu mɛnɛ .
61003010	Busa boKumu ko bodoabí o adoaka mobi . Busa bodi-moabí na daka enɛnɛ a ehole emina ; njɔtɔ banangoabí na mosa ; ngondo etumbamabí na mosa , na leka losusu lua lodi ena .
61003011	Oko boa , ajebaka so bo leka lu losusu lodi bonangoa , mida minu Mibwani boda na bosɛnɔ na ejimeli ai Njambe ,
61003012	yana ambaka no bodoa bobusa bua boNjambe na posa enɛnɛ ; mojɔ bo Busa mɛnɛ bodi bongoa na bonangoa , na njɔtɔ badi bonangoa na mosa pongono .
61003013	Njingo esu ko edi oko a Busa boyene na ngondo eyene , o akwa yo sako , na bodongo bodabi ena .
61003014	A mojɔ momina baninga , alɛndɛkɛ no ngando jimina , kɔni na bingi bo yo abolojae no , pɛpɛ nongo litɔnɔ , pɛpɛ nongo mojɔ , oko na bowi .
61003015	Jimani bo Kumu osu ambaka na lingbangba a boheleja . Paulo moninga osu oepaeli asɔnea no boa pongono na bowɛi bosɔ yo .
61003016	Iyo abala a mojɔ mongando jimina , o akɔkɔ yo a mikanda minde misusu . Mikina mijɔ a mikanda minde midi na kpɔkɔsɔ a bocingea . Baya bapeliti bowɛi , na baya baditi bambilimake badukaka cina etongo a mikanda mimina , na basabejaka boa ; bakɔkɔ boa pongono na Misɔnɔ mitongo .
61003017	Ino ko baninga , ajebaka no oko ngando jimina jidoakini , toma nganjamani , bo osaka laboani a mojɔ mobo-kosea bobato babe , na otadani koko bambilimake .
61003018	Hɛni oko na monganji na ejebeli eKumu na Moheleja osu Yesu Masiya . Ekumu ai yo e dɛye oko a ehole yena epeliti suka . Amen .
62001001	Imua modaka kanga a bobanga mɛnɛ , mua moka so , mua monɛ so na miso , mua monja so , mua mobanda so na mɔmɔ , modaka oko Ebaeli ebomɔ .
62001002	Bomɔ bomana a bohu . Iso bonɛ bomɔ bomina , botɔndɔkɔ mojɔ momina . Bwɛnji botɔndɔkɔ so no bodi oko bomɔ bua bodi na bosusu , bua bodaka na Sango , na boboloa ai so .
62001003	Iso botɔndɔkɔ no oko mua monɛ so , na mua moka so , bo okataneni na su ; na bokatana bosu bodi na Sango , na Mwana’nde Yesu Masiya .
62001004	Bosɔneaka no ngando jiji bo sepi enu enɛngɛe oko bonɛngɛ .
62001005	Bwɛnji bosɔ so ai yo , bwɛnji botɔndɔkɔ so no , bodi oko bu ; — Njambe adi bohu . Modidi moditi nongo a tei ende .
62001006	Bokabala bo bodi na nde limbaci yana adalaka so a modidi , bokoseaka ; na mida misu , na mijɔ misoti misangiti nongo mweka .
62001007	Bokadala ko a bohu , o adi yo a bohu , bokatanaka , moto na mina’nde moto , na makia maYesu Mwana’nde masɛnojaka so a bobe bosusu .
62001008	Boka-bala bo boditi na bobe , bosakoseaka So bɛnɛ , na Soti editi a tei esu .
62001009	Bokajima jibe jisu , yo t’akputojake nongo sako , adi bojo , na a yɛ jibe jisu , na âsɛnoja so a bobe bosusu .
62001010	Bokabala bo bokoiti nongo bobe , bomolangaka o mokosei , na ebaeli ende editi a tei esu .
62002001	Bana bambi bakɛkɛ , mbi nasɔneaka no ngando jiji bo otakɔni nongo bobe . Moto ko akakɔ bobe , bodi na mosili a esika eSango , oko Yesu Masiya , yona obodongo .
62002002	Iyo adi lisiko a mojɔ mojibe jisu , te jisu pɛ , oko a mojɔ mojibe jingondo esusu .
62002003	Bokasuma mibeko mide , bodi bojeba na soti bo bomojebaka , oko na mojɔ momina .
62002004	Moto akabala bo , Mbi namojebaka , na moto omina pɛ bosuma mibeko minde , adi oko mokosei , na Soti editi a tei ende .
62002005	Moto ko akasuma ebaeli ende , ngɛnjɔ eNjambe ebɔngi soti a tei ende . Bojebaka bo bodi a tei ende oko na mojɔ momina .
62002006	Moto yona obalaka bo adi a tei ende abwani bodala a njea edalaka yo .
62002007	Baninga , mobeko mosɔnɔkɔ mbi ai no moditi mobeko moyene . Modi oko mobeko moyou mua modaka na nu a bobanga . Mobeko mu moyou modi oko Ebaeli e’ka no .
62002008	Endele ko , mobeko mosɔneaka mbi no modi moyene , modi mobeko mosoti a tei ende na a tei enu . Cina bo modidi mokɛkɛ anɔe , na bohu bosoti bohoi e dɛye .
62002009	Moto akabala bo adi a bohu yana alonaka yo mwangwa’nde , adi oko a modidi .
62002010	Moto yona odi na mwangwa’nde epaeli adi a bohu , na libaku liditi a tei ende .
62002011	Moto ko yona odi na mwangwa’nde soki adi a modidi , na adalaka a modidi ; t’ajebake esika ekɛkɛ yo , mojɔ bo modidi mohindejaka miso mande .
62002012	Nasɔneaka no bana bambi bakɛkɛ , mojɔ bo jibe jinu jikinama a mojɔ mokombe ende .
62002013	Nasɔneaka no basango , mojɔ bo oje-bakani yona odaka oko a bobanga mɛnɛ . Nasɔneaka no menga , mojɔ bo ogbokejami yona Mobe . Nasɔnei no bana bakɛkɛ mojɔ bo oje-bakani Sango .
62002014	Nasɔnei no basango , mojɔ bo ojebakani yona odaka oko a bobanga mɛnɛ . Nasɔnei no menga , mojɔ bo odini na ndangasa , na Ebaeli eNjambe eyeyoaka a tei enu , na ogbokejaini yona mobe .
62002015	T’opalakeni oko ngondo , isa leka lua lodi a ngondo . Isa moto apalaka ngondo , apeliti nongo ngɛnjɔ ai Sango a tei ende .
62002016	Mojɔ bo , ngando jisusu jia jidi a ngondo , na posa emokuku , na posa emiso , na jala emohelo mu , jicingi oko na ngondo pɛ , te nongo na Sango .
62002017	Ngondo ekɛkɛ adimoe , na posa engondo pongono . Moto ko yona okɔkɔ bolulea boNjambe ayeyoaka oko na bosusu .
62002018	Bana bambi , ehole esuka emei . Ino o’kani bo Soki-eMasiya adi bodoa . Soki-jiMasiya badoi banɛnɛ , na badi e dɛye ; oko boa bojebaka bo ehole esuka emei .
62002019	Bahɔtɔnɔ na su oko bobɔtɔnɔ ; baidaka bato basu . Akɔki bo da bato basu ka bayeyoi na su . Bamana ko , na mojɔ momina monejaka bo baditi bato basu , bo basusu mɛnɛ .
62002020	Ino ko osini kpaci ai Yona Mosɛnɔke , na odini na ejebeli , no basusu .
62002021	Mbi nasɔneaka no mojɔ bo ojebakani Soti , na oje-bakani bo Soti etabotaka bokosea . Nitasɔneaka no mojɔ bo otaje-bakani Soti .
62002022	Odi mokosei nda ? Oko yona onganaka bo Yesu adi Masiya . Iyo adi Soki-eMasiya , oko yona onganaka Sango na Mwana .
62002023	Pɛpɛ nongo moto yona onganaka Mwana odi na Sango . Moto ko yona ojimaka Mwana adi na Sango pongono .
62002024	Ino ko , kinani mojɔ modae a tei enu mua moka no a bobanga . Mojɔ moka no a bobanga mokayeyoa a tei enu , odini boyeyoa no bɛnɛ a tei eMwana na a tei eSango .
62002025	Na sako ekinea yo so edi oko bomɔ bua bodi na bosusu .
62002026	Nasɔnei no ngando jimina a mojɔ mobato baya bapalaka bola-boja no .
62002027	Bosopea ko bosɔ nb ai yo boyeyoaka na nu . Mojɔ mua motakaka na nu moditi bo okina otongo akojae no , mojɔ bo bosopea bonde bokojaka no a mojɔ mongando jisusu . Bosopea bomina bodi soti mɛnɛ , te nongo bokosea . A mojɔ momina , yeyoani a tei ende , o akoa no na bosopea bomina .
62002028	E dɛye , bana bambi , yeyoani a tei ende . Oko boa , yo akamana , bodi bo’ma a boso bonde na eci , te nongo na sɔni .
62002029	Isa ojebakani bo yo adi na bodongo , ojebakani bo moto na moto yona odi na ekɔmɛli ebodongo abotami na nde .
62003001	Anjani ngɛnjɔ enɛnɛ epa Njambe so , bo so bodae na kombe jibana baNjambe . Na bodi bana baNjambe . A mojɔ momina , ngondo Pejebake so , mojɔ bo eimojeba yo .
62003002	Baninga , so bodi bana baNjambe oko e dɛye . Bojebakini elimo esu engɔngɔ ; endele ko , bojebaka bo yo akadoa a bohu , so bodabí na elimo ende , mojɔ bo bodi bomonɛ o adi yo .
62003003	Moto na moto yona odi na njingo emina ai yo , asasɛnojaka o adi yo mosɛnɔke .
62003004	Moto na moto yona okɔkɔ bobe asopaka Mibeko . Bobe bosusu bodi oko bosopa boMibeko .
62003005	Ojebakani bo yo adoa a bodongeja jibe . Bobe boditi nongo a tei ende .
62003006	Moto yona oyeyoaka a tei ende t’akɔke bobe . Yona okɔkɔ bobe amonɛkini na amojebakini .
62003007	Bana bambi , T’ojimeni oko bo moto alabojae no . Yona odi na ekɔmɛli ebodongo adi moto obodongo , o adi yo na bodongo .
62003008	Moto yona okɔkɔ bobe adi moto oSatana , mojɔ bo Satana akɔ bobe a bobanga mɛnɛ , na akɔkɔ bobe oko e dɛye . Cina ebodoa boMwana ’ Njambe edi oko bo abejae bilomu biSatana .
62003009	Moto yona obotama na Njambe t’akɔke bobe , mojɔ bo bana baNjambe bayeyoaka a tei ende , na babwaniti bokɔ bobe , mojɔ bo babotama na Njambe .
62003010	Bodi bombetea bana baNjambe na bana baSatana oko na mojɔ momina . Moto amiti da na ekɔmɛli ebodongo aditi moto oNjambe , na moto yona odi na mwangwa’nde soki koko boa .
62003011	Iso bodi bopalana ; bwɛnji bosɔ no a bobanga mɛnɛ oko bu .
62003012	Bobwaniti boda na ekɔmɛli eKaina , yona odaka moto oSatana na awa mwangwa’nde . Na awa mwangwa’nde mojɔ moye ? Mojɔ ke bo bikɔmɛli binde mɛnɛ bidaka bibe , na bia bimwangwa’nde bidaka bipele .
62003013	Baninga , yɛ bokamoani bo ngondo edi na nu soki .
62003014	Iso bojebaka bo bomani a bogwa , na bokwei a bomɔ , cina bo bopalaka baninga . Moto amiti pala , adi oko a tei ebogwa .
62003015	Moto yona odi na mwangwa’nde soki adi mowoi ; na ojebakani bo mowoi apeliti nongo bomɔ bua bodi na bosusu a tei ende .
62003016	Bojebaka ngɛnjɔ oko na mojɔ mu , bo yo apa mohelo monde a mojɔ mosu ; na so hobwani bopa mihelo misu a mojɔ mobaninga .
62003017	Moto akanɛ bo mwangwa’nde adi na taka , yana adi yo mɛnɛ na likonja lingondo , na akadipa molema monde ai yo , ngɛnjɔ eNjambe editi a tei ende .
62003018	Bana bambi , ngɛnjɔ esu ebwaniti boda a bikenge bimonɔkɔ pɛ , oko na ekɔmɛli na soti .
62003019	Oko boa bodi bojeba bo bodi bana basoti , na bodi bohahaneja milema misu a boso bonde , isamilema misu midumbaka so ;
62003020	mojɔ bo , na Njambe na milema misu , Njambe adi boso ; na yo ajebaka ngando jisusu .
62003021	Baninga , isa milema misu mitadumbaka so , boditi nongo na mokakwano a boso boNjambe ,
62003022	na bosɔkɔ ai yo mua mongaka so , cina bo bosumaka Mibeko minde , na bokɔkɔ ngando jia jimosepejaka .
62003023	Mobeko monde modi oko bo bojimee kombe eMwana’nde Yesu Masiya , na bo bopalaneni o apa yo so mobeko .
62003024	Moto yona osumaka Mibeko minde ayeyoaka a tei ende , na yo ayeyoaka a tei emoto omina . Na bojebaka bo ayeyoaka a tei esu oko na Mwembo mopa yo so .
62004001	Baninga , t’ojimeni oko miembo misusu . Sisoani miembo a bojeba isa micingi na Njambe , cina bo batɔndɔi babokosea banɛnɛ banangani a ngondo .
62004002	Odini bombetea Mwembo mo-Njambe oko na mojɔ mu ; miembo misusu mia mijamaka bo Yesu Masiya adoa o moto , micingi na Njambe .
62004003	Miembo misusu mia mijimiti Yesu , micingiti nongo na Njambe . Mwembo mua modi boa modi oko mwembo moSoki-eMasiya ; o’kani bo mwembo momina modi bodoa , na modi a ngondo e dɛye .
62004004	Bana bambi , ino odini bana baNjambe , na ogbokejami miembo mimina , cina bo , na yona odi a tei enu , na yona odi a ngondo , yona odi a tei enu anɔi na ngulu .
62004005	Bato bamina badi bato bangondo ; oko boa ngando jibalaka bo jidi ngando jingondo , na ngondo ebabokeaka .
62004006	Iso ko bodi bato baNjambe . Moto na moto yona ojebaka Njambe ahokeaka so ; na moto na moto yona oditi moto oNjambe t’ahokeake so . Oko boa bombeteaka mwembo mosoti na mwembo molaboake .
62004007	Baninga baepaeli , yɛni bodae na ngɛnjɔ , moto ai mina’nde moto . Mojɔ bo ngɛnjɔ ehulaka ai Njambe , na moto yona odi na ngɛnjɔ abotama na Njambe na ajebaka Njambe .
62004008	Moto yona opeliti ngɛnjɔ t’ajebake Njambe , mojɔ bo Njambe adi ngɛnjɔ .
62004009	Ngɛnjɔ eNjambe eboloa a tei esu oko na mojɔ mu , bo Njambe aloma mwana’nde obotama omɔci a ngondo , bo so bohele a mojɔ monde .
62004010	Iye edi ngɛnjɔ , te bo so bodaka na ngɛnjɔ ai Njambe , oko bo yo adaka na ngɛnjɔ ai so , na aloma Mwana’nde bo adae lisiko a mojɔ mojibe jisu .
62004011	Baninga baepaeli , isa ngɛnjɔ eNjambe ai so edaka boa , iso bobwani boda na ngɛnjɔ pongono , moto ai mina’nde moto .
62004012	Moto anɛkini Njambe , pɛpɛ nongo omɔci . Njambe ko ayeyoaka a tei esu , na ngɛnjɔ ende ebɔngi a tei esu , isa bodi na ngɛnjɔ moto ai mina’nde moto .
62004013	Bojebaka bo bodi a tei ende , na bo yo adi a tei esu , mojɔ bo abopi Mwembo monde .
62004014	Iso bonɛ , na botɔndɔkɔ bo Sango aloma Mwana’nde o Moheleja ongondo .
62004015	Moto na moto yona ojimaka bo Yesu adi Mwana ’ Njambe , Njambe adi a tei ende , na yo mɛnɛ a tei eNjambe .
62004016	Iso bojebaka na bojimaka ngɛnjɔ eNjambe ai so . Njambe adi ngɛnjɔ . Moto yona odi a tei engɛnjɔ adi a tei eNjambe , na Njambe adi a tei ende .
62004017	Ngɛnjɔ ebɔngi ai so bo botada nongo na mokakwano a busa boEsambi mojɔ bo so bodi a ngondo o adi yo .
62004018	Bɔ boditi nongo a ngɛnjɔ . Ngɛnjɔ yena ebɔngi ebenganaka bɔ . Bɔ bodi oko a mojɔ momokindo , na isa moto adi na bɔ , ngɛnjɔ ende ebɔngiti .
62004019	Iso ko bodi na ngɛnjɔ , mojɔ bo yo adaka na ngɛnjɔ ai so boso .
62004020	Moto akabala bo , Mbi nadi na ngɛnjɔ ai Njambe , yana adi yo na mwangwa’nde soki , moto omina adi mokosei . Mojɔ bo isa aditi na ngɛngɔ ai mwangwa’nde yona onɛnɛkɛ na nde , atada nongo na ngɛnjɔ ai Njambe yona odi yo pɛ bonɛ .
62004021	Na so bosɔ mobeko mu ai yo , bo moto yona odi na ngɛnjɔ ai Njambe abwani boda koko na ngɛnjɔ ai mwangwa’nde .
62005001	Moto na moto yona ojimaka bo Yesu adi Masiya abotama na Njambe . Na moto na moto yona odi na ngɛnjɔ ai moboti , adi koko na ngɛnjɔ ai mwana’nde .
62005002	Oko boa bojebaka bo bodi na ngɛnjɔ ai bana baNjambe isa bodi na ngɛnjɔ ai Njambe , na isa bosumaka Mibeko minde .
62005003	Isa ngɛnjɔ ai Njambe edi , lisuma a Mibeko minde lidi koko . Na Mibeko minde miditi na kpɔkɔsɔ .
62005004	Moto na moto yona obotama na Njambe agbokejaka ngondo ; na lilonga lia ligbokejaka ngondo lidi oko ejimeli esu .
62005005	Ogbokejaka ngondo nda ? Oko yona ojimaka bo Yesu adi Mwana ’ Njambe .
62005006	Edi oko yo , Yesu Masiya , yona odoa na madiba na makia ; te na madiba pɛ , oko na madiba na makia pongono .
62005007	Na Mwembo modi motati , mojɔ bo Mwembo modi Soti .
62005008	Batati badi basato , oko Mwembo na madiba na makia ; na tati ebu basato edi oko tati emɔci .
62005009	Bokajima tati ebato , tati eNjambe enɔi tati ebato , mojɔ bo tati eNjambe edi tati a mojɔ moMwana’nde .
62005010	Moto yona ojimaka Mwana ’ Njambe adi na tati emina a tei ende mɛnɛ . Moto yona odi pɛ bojima Njambe , akɔkɔ Njambe mokosei , mojɔ bo atajimaka tati etataka Njambe ai Mwana’nde .
62005011	Na tati emina edi oko ye , bo Njambe apa so bomɔ bua bodi oko na bosusu ; na bomɔ bomina bodi a tei eMwana’nde .
62005012	Moto yona odi na Mwana a tei ende adi na bomɔ . Yona ko opeliti Mwana apeliti bomɔ .
62005013	Mbi nasɔnei no ngando jiji , no baya bajimaka kombe eMwana ’ Njambe , bo ojebeni bo odini na bomɔ bua bodi na bosusu .
62005014	Na ejimeli esu ai yo edi bo boka’nga mokina mojɔ mua mobwani na bolulea bonde , yo adi boka so .
62005015	Na isa bojebaka bo yo ahokeaka mijɔ misusu mingaka so , bojebaka bo bosi mijɔ mingaki so ai yo .
62005016	Moto akajeba bo mwangwa’nde akɔkɔ mokina mojɔ mobe mua mobwamti na bogwa , adi bonga Njambe , na yo adi bomopa bomɔ a mojɔ mobato baya bakɔi bobe bua bobwaniti na bogwa . Bokina bobe bodi oko bobe bobogwa ; nitabalaka bo moto adi bonga a mojɔ mobobe bomina .
62005017	Mijɔ misusu mia miditi mipele midi Mibe ; mokina ko moditi bobe bobogwa .
62005018	Bojebaka bo moto na moto yona obotama na Njambe t’akɔke bobe . Moto yona obotama na Njambe asabaneaka , na yona Mobe atabakea nongo ebɔ ai yo .
62005019	Iso bojebaka bo bodi bana baNjambe , na bo ngondo esusu edi a mɔmɔ mayona Mobe .
62005020	Bojebaka bo Mwana ’ Njambe adoi , na abopi boemgea a bojeba yona oSoti . Na bodi a tei ende yona odi Soti , oko a tei eMwana’nde Yesu Masiya . Iyo adi Njambe oSoti , na bomɔ bua bodi na bosusu .
62005021	Bana bambi , inganjamani a mojɔ mobanjambe babokosea .
63001001	Mbi mosuku oDenga ai Kilia mwali mohɔmɔke na ai bana bawɛ . Mbi napalaka no na soti , na te mbi pɛ , oko basusu batongo baya bajebaka mojɔ mosoti ,
63001002	cina eSoti yena edi a tei esu , na edi boda na su oko na bosusu .
63001003	Monganji na wa na bowi jida na su ; jikahule al Njambe Sango na ai Yesu Masiya , Mwana ’ Sango , a tei eSoti na ngɛnjɔ .
63001004	Mbi nadaka na sepi enɛnɛ yana atana mbi bakina bana bawɛ bakadale a njea esoti , o ama so sɔ mobeko ai Sango .
63001005	Na mojɔ mongaka mbi wɛ e dɛye Kilia , modi bo bodae na epaeli , moto ai mina’nde moto . Nitasɔneaka wɛ mobeko moyene ; modi oko mobeko mosɔ so a bobanga mɛnɛ .
63001006	Ngɛnjɔ edi oko ye , bo bosume Mibeko minde . Mobeko modi oko mu , bo osuseni njea engɛnjɔ , o aka no a bobanga .
63001007	Mojɔ bo bakosei banɛnɛ banangani a ngondo , baya batajimaka bo Yesu Masiya adoa o moto . Yona odi boa adi mokosei , na adi soki-eMasiya .
63001008	Toma nganjamani bo otabungejaeni ndese eelomu enu , na bo osɛni ndese enu esusu .
63001009	Moto yona okinaka njea , pɛ boyeyoa a bokoja boMasiya , aditi na Njambe a tei ende . Yona oyeyoaka a bokoja boMasiya , adi na Sango na Mwana pongono a tei ende .
63001010	Moto akadoa ai no yona oditi na bokoja bomina , pɛ bomosɔni a ndako , pɛ bomobɛjɛni njɛbɛ ;
63001011	mojɔ bo , yona omo-bɛjɛkɛ njɛbɛ akatani na nde a bilomu binde bibe .
63001012	Nadi na ngando jinɛnɛ a bosɔnea no ; napaliti ko bo najisɔne a mokanda , mojɔ bo nadi na njingo bo nadoe a bo’nɛnɛ na nu , na a bobala na nu na monɔkɔ mɛnɛ . Sepi esu edi bobɔngɔ boa .
63001013	Bana bamwangwao mohɔmɔke babɛjɛkɛ wɛ njɛbɛ .
64001001	Mbi mosuku oDenga ai moninga Gayo ; ngɛnjɔ embi ai wɛ na soti .
64001002	Moninga , mbi nangaka Njambe bo mijɔ miwɛ misusu Mibɔnge , na bo odae na mokuku monjilake o adi wɛ na mwembo monjilake .
64001003	Mojɔ bo mbi nadaka na sepi yana amea bakina baninga ya , na babala a mojɔ moSoti yena edi a tei enu , na bo odalakani a njea esoti .
64001004	Mbi naka’ka bo bana bambi badalaka a njea esoti , sepi embi enɔi oko bonɔ .
64001005	Moninga , elomu ekɔkɔ wɛ a mojɔ mobaninga , na a mojɔ momidoa , edi elomu eejimeli mɛnɛ .
64001006	Ibo batati tati a mojɔ mongɛnjɔ ewɛ a boso boDenga . Bopele bo obakɔmejae a mɔngɔ mobu ; mojɔ momina mobwani na elomu eNjambe .
64001007	Mojɔ bo bakɛi a mojɔ mokombe ende , pɛ bosɔ nongo eka ai bapakano .
64001008	Oko boa bobwani bokɔmeja bato bamina , bo bokatane na bu a elomu eSoti .
64001009	Nasɔni mokanda a Denga ; yo ko Diotulepe Yajimake kpaci esu ; apalaka bo asakumejae a tei ebu .
64001010	Oko boa , mbi nakadoa nadi bolɛjɛ bato a mojɔ mobikɔmɛli binde , na bo alɔngɔkɔ so na bibaeli bibe . Te mojɔ momina pɛ , — alonaka bosɔ baninga , na alemoaka na bato baya bapalaka bosɔ baninga , na abamejaka a Denga .
64001011	Baninga , pɛ bokoani na bobe ; ikoanani oko na bopele pɛ . Moto yona okɔkɔ bopele adi moto oNjambe . Moto ko yona okɔkɔ bobe anɛkini Njambe .
64001012	Bato basusu basakoaka Demetulio , na mwako mosoti motataka ai yo pongono . Mbi namosakoaka pongono , na ojebakani bo tati embi edi tati esoti .
64001013	Nadaki na mijɔ minɛnɛ a bosɔnea wɛ ; mtapalaka ko bo namisɔne a mokanda .
64001014	Nadi na njingo bo nanɛnɛe na wɛ ngɔngɔ mweka , na bodi bobalana oko na monɔkɔ .
64001015	Yɛ bowi bodae ai wɛ . Binao babɛjɛkɛ wɛ njɛbɛ . Abɛjɛ bma’su , moto na moto na kombe ende .
65001001	Mbi Yuda , mobuli oYesu Masiya , na mwanange ’ Yakobo , ai baya babeama , baya basɔ ngɛnjɔ eNjambe na baya babaneamaka a mojɔ moYesu Masiya .
65001002	Yɛ monganji na bowi na ngɛnjɔ jinɛngɛe ai no .
65001003	Baninga , adaki mbi na mokano bo nasɔnee no mokanda a mojɔ mobohela hosu na nu , najimi bo nasɔnee no , oko na bonga ai no , a bona na bopipo a mojɔ moejimeli yena epama ai basɛnɔke ehole emɔci pɛ .
65001004	Cina bo bakina bato bakwei a tei enu na poloso , bato babe baya bahekojaka monganji moNjambe a bosambolu , na banga-naka Moswa na Kumu osu omɔci , Yesu Masiya . Mokindo mobato bamina mokoleama ehele .
65001005	Napalaka bolɛjɛ no , nongo ajebaka no ngando ji jisusu , bo Kumu yona oheleja bato a Ejipeto , aweja ngɔngɔ bato baya baijima .
65001006	Na babwɛnji-baDiko koko , baya baidika a bokumu bobu na bakina esika ebu , yo abadeja a minyɔlɔ mimodidi mua modi na bosusu , a bo’mba Esambi ebusa bua bonɛnɛ .
65001007	Sɔdɔmɔ na Gomola koko , na ngando jitongo jia jidaka a esika emina ; mojɔ bo ekɔmɛli ebu edaka oko bɔɔli , na ngando jibosambolu pɛ . Mokindo mobu modi oko mosa mua motadimoa a mojɔ moembete ai so .
65001008	Bato bamina badi koko na ekɔmɛli emina . Babejaka mikuku Mibu na posa jibu . Basɛtojaka kpaci , na baloleaka bato baekumu eDiko .
65001009	Nongo Mikaele , mosuku obabwɛnji-baDiko , yana aswiana yo na Satana a mojɔ momokuku moMose , aipala bomotɔkɔlɔ ; abala oko bo , yɛ Njambe alemoe na wɛ .
65001010	Bato bamina ko baloleaka ngando jidi bo pɛ bocingea . Ejebeli ebu edi oko ejebeli etito , na basabejaka na ejebeli emina .
65001011	Boditigoa ai bato bamina ! Mojɔ bo badalaka a njea edala Kaina . Bakoanaka na libunga liBalama oko na posa elikonja , na bagwaka a mojɔ molipanga o agwa Kole .
65001012	Bato bamina badi mabaku a kola jinu . Bapehti nongo sɔni a mojɔ moma-tanga mabu . Posa jibu jidi oko ai bo bɛnɛ pɛ . Badi biyembi ngasa pɛ madiba , bia bipɛpɛnɛkɛ na pwea ; badi o mele mikakanake miyanga mia midi mitete , Mibikoamake , mia migwi bihole bibae .
65001013	Bamejaka mapuli mabosambolu bobu o ekɔmɛli emula monɛnɛ momadiba-mamukwa . Badi o njɔtɔ balaboake , baya bahɛngɛmɛ a mojɔ momo-didi tuu oko na bosusu .
65001014	Anoka , yona odaka a elulu esambo ngɔngɔ jiAdama , apa koko eseko a mojɔ mobato bamina ; abala bo , Anjani , Kumu akɛkɛ adoe na mandundu mabasɛnɔke bande
65001015	Bo asambejae bato basusu , Na bo adumbe bato basusu babe , A mojɔ mongando jisusu jibe jikɔ bo , Na bibaeli bisusu bibe bibala bato babe a mojɔ monde .
65001016	Bato bamina badi bato babomɛmɛlɛ na bamanungunungu , baya basumaka oko posa jibu bɛnɛ ; bibaeli bibu bidi bibaeli biegbo , na basakoaka bato oko na njingo ebosɔ eka .
65001017	Ino ko baninga , toma salɛjɛni bibaeli bibala babwɛnji baKumu osu Yesu Masiya eyou .
65001018	Babala na nu bo bato babiloli badi bodoa a masu masuka , baya badi bosuma oko posa jibu bɛnɛ pɛ .
65001019	Bato bamina bapengolaka batongo , badi bato babosambolu baya bapeliti Mwembo .
65001020	Ino ko baninga , kinani eyoeli enu edae a diko diejimeli enu esɛnɔke . Ingakani a tei eMwembo Mosɛnɔke .
65001021	Sabaneani a ngɛnjɔ eNjambe , ena ko ombakani monganji moKumu osu Yesu Masiya oko a bomɔ bua bodi na bosusu .
65001022	Dani na wa ai bato baya badi na mokakwano .
65001023	Helejani batongo , bagbulani a mosa . A mojɔ mobatongo , kinani wa enu ai bo edae na bɔ , na gbeseani bisenja bibu bia bibehi na munu .
65001024	Iyo adi na ngulu a bobanea no bo otakwani , na a bomeja no , pɛpɛ nongo litɔnɔ , a boso boekumu ende na sepi ;
65001025	ekumu na bosakoa na bokumu na kpaci ai yo yona odi Njambe omɔci pɛ , Moheleja osu a mojɔ moYesu Masiya Kumu osu , oko ehole eipeta banga , na e dɛye , oko na bosusu . Amen .
66001001	Ibu bodi boboloja boYesu Masiya . Njambe abomopa bo anejae bakɔmɛli bande ngando jia jidi bodoa bokpa ; na yo ajebeja mokɔmɛli onde Yoane mojɔ momina , yana amolomea yo obwɛnji onde .
66001002	Yoane adi motati oEbaeli eNjambe na otati eYesu Masiya , a mojɔ mongando jisusu jinɛ yo .
66001003	Bojongoa ai moto yona olangaka bikenge bieseko ye ; bojongoa ai baya ba’kaka , na baya basumaka ngando jia jisɔnɔmi ena ; mojɔ bo ehole emina edi hulelu .
66001004	Yoane ai Menga sambo maMasiya maya madi a Asia ; Monganji ai no na bowi boYona odi , Yona odaka , na Yona odi na bosusu , na miembo sambo mia midi a boso bongɛndɛ ende ,
66001005	na Yesu Masiya , Motati oejimeli , Mwana-sɔmi a tei ebagwake , Mosuku obakumu bangondo . Iyo apalaka so , na asikoa so a jibe jisu , na makia mande ,
66001006	na akɔ bo bodae bokumu bonganga ai Njambe Sangwa’nde . Ekumu na bokumu ai yo oko na bosusu . Amen .
66001007	Hokeani ; akɛkɛ adoe na biyembi . Miso masusu madi bomonɛ , na baya bamondea pongono . Na makota masusu mangondo mâyea bio a mojɔ monde . Ee , Amen .
66001008	Kumu Njambe abalaka bo , Mbi nadi Alepa na Omega , yona odi , yona odaka , yona odi na bosusu , yona onɔi basusu .
66001009	Mbi Yoane , mwangwa’nu yona okatani na nu a tei eminɔngɔ , na a bokumu , na a eci yena edi a tei eMasiya ; mbi nadaka a mosanga mua modi na kombe Patemo , a mojɔ moEbaeli eNjambe , na a mojɔ motati eYesu .
66001010	Nadaka a Mwembo a busa boKumu , na naka kɔpi epipo a ngɔngɔ jimbi o mondule bo ,
66001011	Sɔnɔ mojɔ monɛkɛ wɛ a mokanda ; moloma a Menga sambo maMasiya , a Ɛpɛsɔ , na Semuluna , na Pelugamona , na Twatila , na Saludi , na Piladelupia , na Laodikia .
66001012	Mbi nahekoa a bonɛ kɔpi yena ebalaka na mbi . Ahekoa mbi , nanɛ paka jiwɔlɔ sambo .
66001013	Okina o Mwana ’ Moto , yona olwaka kasaka eyai adaka a ndanda epaka , na adaka na kamba ewɔlɔ a bupa .
66001014	Molo monde , na swe jinde , jidaka bopu bopɛɛ o makambule . Miso mande mangɛngɛkɛ o mosa .
66001015	Bibota binde bidaka o mboa jipele jia jimana a mosa na bolailai . Kɔpi ende edaka o doi eepela .
66001016	Apeaka njɔtɔ sambo a ebɔ ende ebami , na abɛnɛ onjɛngɔ jibae jipɔlu amanaka a monɔkɔ monde . Boso bonde bodaka o bohu bonɛnɛ bomodika-busa a ngulu ende .
66001017	Yana amonɛ mbi , nakwa a bibota binde o mogwake . Iyo ko abakea ebɔ ende ebami ai mbi , na abala bo , yɛ bobanga . Mbi nadi yona oboso , yona osuka , na yona obomɔ .
66001018	Mbi nagwa ; e dɛye ko nadi mɔ oko na bosusu , na napeli sabe jibogwa na jiesika ebagwake .
66001019	Oko boa , sɔnɔ mijɔ minɛkɛ wɛ , mia midi e dɛye , na mia midi bodoa ngɔndɔ .
66001020	Cina enjɔtɔ sambo bani wɛ a ebɔ embi ebami , na paka jiwɔlɔ sambo edi oko ye ; njɔtɔ sambo badi babwɛnji baMenga sambo , na paka sambo jidi Menga sambo .
66002001	Sɔnea obwɛnji oDenga diƐpɛsɔ bo , Iyona opeaka njɔtɔ sambo a ebɔ ende ebami , yona odalaka a ndanda epaka jiwɔlɔ sambo , abalaka mijɔ mimi .
66002002	Mbi najebaka bikɔmɛli biwɛ , na elomu ewɛ , na lingbangba liwɛ . Najebaka bo bato babe bakɔkɔ wɛ maneene , bo osisoi baya basabeaka babwɛnji na baditi nongo babwɛnji , na onini bo badi bakosei .
66002003	Najebaka bo odi na lingbangba a mojɔ mokombe embi ; ohɔnɔkɔ muna momina na otangwaka .
66002004	Mbi ko nadi na wɛ mojɔ mu ; okini epaeli ewɛ eboso .
66002005	Toma lɛ esika ekwi wɛ ; hekoja molema mowɛ ; kɔ bilomu biboso . Omiti kɔ boa , omiti hekoja molema mowɛ , mbi nadi bodoa ai wɛ , na nâdongeja paka ewɛ .
66002006	Endele ko , odi na mojɔ mu mopele ; olonaka bikɔmɛli biBaNikolaito , o alonaka mbi bikɔmɛli bibu .
66002007	Isa moto adi na matoi , yɛ ahokee mojɔ mobalaka Mwembo na Menga maMasiya . Moto akagbokeja , mbi nâmopa mbuma jimole-mobomɔ mua modi a Paladiso eNjambe bo ayake .
66002008	Sɔnea obwɛnji oDenga diSemuluna bo , Iyona oboso , yona osuka , yona ogwa na ohela koko , abalaka mijɔ mimi .
66002009	Mbi najebaka monɔngɔ mowɛ , na bokwali bowɛ ( nongo adi wɛ na likonja ) . Najebaka mojɔ momasingi mabato baya baba-laka bo badi BaYuda , na baditi BaYuda ; badi oko sinagoge eSatana .
66002010	Boditigoa bokɛkɛ adoe ai wɛ . Yɛ bobanga ko . Hokeani ; Satana akɛkɛ adumbe bakina banu a blɔkɔ a bomeka no , na ôdani na monɔngɔ masu domi . Da ko na lingbangba oko a bogwa , na mbi nâpa wɛ likongo libomɔ .
66002011	Yona odi na matoi , yɛ ahokee mojɔ mobalaka Mwembo na Menga maMasiya . Yona ogbokejaka atadingoa na bogwa bomabae .
66002012	Sɔnea obwɛnji oDenga diPelugamona bo , Iyona odi na abɛnɛ onjɛngɔ jibae jipɔlu abalaka mijɔ mimi .
66002013	Mbi najebaka esika edi ndako ewɛ ; edi oko a esika edi ngɛndɛ eSatana . Opeaka kombe embi boku . Oingana nongo ejimeli embi a masu mawa bo Antipa , motati ombi oejimeli a tei enu , oko a esika eSatana .
66002014	Endele ko , nadi na wɛ mikina mijɔ . Odi na bakwa bato oho baya bajimaka bokoja boBalama , yona okoja Balaka bo asakejae bana baYisalaele libaku , bo bayake masiko maya mapama ai banjambe babokosea , na bo bakɔe mijɔ Mibosambolu .
66002015	Odi koko na bakina baya badi bacinami baBaNikolaito .
66002016	Hekoja molema mowɛ . Omiti hekoja molema , nadi bodoa ai wɛ bokpa , a bona na bato bamina na abɛnɛ omonɔkɔ mombi .
66002017	Yona odi na matoi , yɛ ahokee mojɔ mobalaka Mwembo na Menga maMasiya . Mbi nâpa yona ogbokejaka manna mabombamake . Nâmopa koko litai lipu ; kombe eyene edi bosɔnɔmɔ a litai limina , na pɛpɛ nongo moto oje-baka kombe emina , oko yona oesɔkɔ .
66002018	Sɔnea obwɛnji oDenga diTwatila bo , Mwana ’ Njambe abalaka mijɔ mimi , oko yona odi na miso mamosa mongoake , na bibota binde o mboa jipele jibolailai .
66002019	Mbi najebaka bikɔmɛli biwɛ , epaeli ewɛ , ejimeli ewɛ , elomu ewɛ na lingbangba liwɛ . Na bikɔmɛli biwɛ e dɛye na bikɔmɛli biwɛ biboso , mbi najebaka bo bikɔmɛli biwɛ e dɛye binɔi bikɔmɛli biwɛ biboso .
66002020	Endele ko , nadi na wɛ mojɔ mu ; ojimaka bo Yesabela , mwali yona obalaka bo adi motɔndɔi , akojae na alabojae bakɔmɛli bambi a bokɔ ngando jibosambolu , na a boyaka masiko maya mapama ai banjambe babokosea .
66002021	Namopi ehole bo ahekojae molema monde ; yo ko t’apalake bohekoja molema na bokwa ngando jinde jibosambolu .
66002022	Hokea ; mbi nâmodumba a gbagba eyogo ; na baya bangɛkɛ na nde bɔɔli bamiti hekoja milema Mibu a bikɔmɛli binde , mbi nâbalomea bodingoa bonɛnɛ .
66002023	Nâweja bana bande oko bowa . Na Menga masusu maMasiya madi bojeba bo mbi nadi yona osisoaka bolɛ na molema . Nâpa moto na moto a tei enu ndese yena ebwani na bikɔmɛli binde .
66002024	Ino batongo ko baTwatila baya batajimaka bokoja bomina , na baya baidinda a ngando jibombamake jiSatana , ( ebaeli ebu edi boa ) nabalaka na nu bo nitabakea mokina muna motongo ai no .
66002025	Mojɔ momɔci ko ; peani boku mua mope-lini no , oko a bodoa bombi .
66002026	Iyona ogbokejaka , yona osumaka ngando jimbi oko a suka mɛnɛ , mbi nâmopa kpaci emakota .
66002027	Iyo âkuma makota na tondo eebende , na âmabɛ o abɛkɛ moto teni , mojɔ bo mbi nasi kpaci ai Sangwa’mbi .
66002028	Nâmopa koko monjɔtɔ moelɔngɔ .
66002029	Moto yona odi na matoi , yɛ ahokee mojɔ mobalaka Mwembo na Menga maMasiya .
66003001	Sɔnea obwɛnji oDenga diSaludi bo , Iyona odi na Miembo miNjambe sambo , na njɔtɔ sambo , aba-laka mijɔ mi . Mbi najebaka bikɔmɛli biwɛ . Odi na kombe emoto yona odi mɔ , na odi oko mogwake .
66003002	Sisoa , na pingeja ngando jia jidikai , jia jidi hulelu na bogwa ; mojɔ bo mbi nanɛkɛ bo bikɔmɛli biwɛ bibɔngiti nongo a miso maNjambe ombi .
66003003	Toma lɛ mijɔ misɔ wɛ , na mijɔ mika wɛ . Banea mijɔ mimina , na hekoja molema mowɛ . Omiti nganjama , mbi nâdoa o mobi , na otajeba ehole êdoa mbi ai wɛ .
66003004	Endele ko , odi na bakina bato a Saludi baya baibeja bilwaeli bibu . Ibo badi bodala na mbi na bisenja bipu , mojɔ bo babɔngi .
66003005	Iyona ogbokejaka adi bolwa bisenja bipu boa , na mbi nitahakoa kombe ende a mokanda mobomɔ . Nâjima kombe ende a boso boSangwa’mbi na a boso bobabwɛnji bande baDiko .
66003006	Moto yona odi na matoi , yɛ ahokee mojɔ mobalaka Mwembo na Menga maMasiya .
66003007	Sɔnea obwɛnji oDenga diPiladelupia bo , Iyona mosɛnɔke , yona osoti , yona odi na sabe eDawidi , yona odipoaka na pɛpɛ nongo moto odi bodipa , yona odipaka na pɛpɛ nongo moto odi bodipoa , yo abalaka mijɔ mimi .
66003008	Mbi najebaka bikɔmɛli biwɛ . Hokea ; mbi nakini modipe bwase a boso bowɛ , na pɛpɛ nongo moto Obwani bomodipa . Najebaka bo ngulu ewɛ ehɛhti ; endele ko , osumaka ebaeli embi , na oigana nongo kombe embi .
66003009	Baya badi basinagoge eSatana , baya babalaka bo badi BaYuda na baditi BaYuda , na bakoseaka , mbi nadi bobahuda ai wɛ bo basasunee a boso bobibota biwɛ , bo bajebe bo mbi napalaka wɛ .
66003010	Ehole ebomeka ekɛkɛ adoe a ngondo esusu a bomeka bato bangondo . Mbi ko nadi bobanea wɛ a ehole emina , mojɔ bo obanea ebaeli embi na lingbangba .
66003011	Mbi nakɛkɛ adoe bokpa . Pea boku mua mopeli wɛ , bo moto asaka katoa likongo liwɛ .
66003012	Moto yona odi mogbokoli , mbi nâmokɔ likwe a tempelo eNjambe ombi , na ataya mana . Nâsɔnɔ kombe eNjambe ombi ai yo , na kombe engando eNjambe ombi , oko Yelusalema eyene yena ekahule oho Diko ai Njambe ombi , na kombe embi mɛnɛ eyene pongono .
66003013	Yona odi na matoi , yɛ ahokee mojɔ mobalaka Mwembo na Menga maMasiya .
66003014	Sɔnea obwɛnji oDenga diLaodikia bo , Iyona odi Amen , yona odi motati osoti na oejimeli , yona odi litandei lielomu eNjambe eboyoa , yo abalaka mijɔ mimi .
66003015	Mbi najebaka bikɔmɛli biwɛ . Najebaka bo oditi nongo na pio isa na mosa . Akɔki wɛ da na pio isa na mosa , bopele .
66003016	A mojɔ momina , mbi nâbunja wɛ a monɔkɔ mombi , cina bo odi oko na bodu , pɛpɛ pio , pɛpɛ mosa .
66003017	Obalaka bo , Mbi nadi konji ; nakonji makonja manɛnɛ ; pɛpɛ nongo eka etakaka na mbi . Otajebaka bo odi na esɔpi , na eduku , na bopu , na miso magwake , na bo odi mbundu .
66003018	Mbi nalehaka wɛ bo osombe ai mbi wɔlɔ yena eluama na mosa , bo odae konji soti , na bisenja bipu bo odae na elwaeli , na bo sɔni embundu ewɛ esaka boloa , na sengo a bosuoa ta miso mawɛ bo onɛe .
66003019	Mbi nakapala bato , nabasiaka , na nabatuaka . Oko boa , kɔ na bopipo bo ohekojae molema mowɛ .
66003020	Hokea ; mbi nami mema a modipe , na nabomaka . Moto aka’ka monɔkɔ mombi , na akadipoa modipe , mbi nâkwea ai yo ; nâyaka na nde , na yo âyaka na mbi .
66003021	Mbi nâjima bo yona ogbokejaka adae na mbi a ngɛndɛ embi , o ami mbi gbokeja , na adi mbi na Sangwa’mbi a ngɛndɛ ende .
66003022	Yona odi na matoi , yɛ abokee mojɔ mobalaka Mwembo na Menga maMasiya .
66004001	Yana asia ngando jimina , mbi nanja , na nanɛ bo modipe modi bwase oho Diko . Na kɔpi ema mhi ka boso o ekɔmɛli emondule emi ko bala oko na mbi bo , Doa jɔno diko bo nanejae wɛ ngando jia jikɛkɛ adoe ngɔngɔ .
66004002	Bokpa mɛnɛ , nadaka a Mwembo , na nanɛ ngɛndɛ a tei eDiko na okina a ngɛndɛ emina .
66004003	Yona odaka a ngɛndɛ adaka o litai liyasipi na salali ; na moyama mohika ngɛndɛ o emelaudi .
66004004	Mingbelɛngɔ licinda-na-minɛi mihikaka ngɛndɛ . Basuku licinda-na-banɛi badaka a mingbelɛngɔ baya badaka na bisenja bipu , na makongo mawɔlɔ a melo Mibu .
66004005	Mikalimo , na kɔpi , na bɛi jimana a ngɛndɛ . Mitanda sambo miyoaka a boso bongɛndɛ , mia midi Miembo sambo miNjambe .
66004006	Boso bongɛndɛ bodaka o ekɔmɛli elibale litalatala na kulusutala . Nanɛ koko bato babomɔ banɛi a tei engɛndɛ , na bahikaka ngɛndɛ ; badaka na miso botɔ , saboso na sangɔngɔ .
66004007	Yona obomɔ oboso adaka o gbɔngɔ ; yona obabae adaka o mwana-ngɔmbɔ ; yona obasato adaka na boso bomoto ; yona obanɛi adaka o popo yona opimboaka .
66004008	Bato babomɔ banɛi badaka na mapapulapu masamano-masamano . Badaka na miso botɔ , a sokolu na a tei . Te bakwake bo’mba yembo na bulu na moi bo , Mosɛnɔke ! Mosɛnɔke ! Mosɛnɔke ! Kumu Njambe yona onɔi na ngulu ; Yona odaka , yona odi , na yona odabí na bosusu .
66004009	Bato babomɔ bakumejaka yona odi a ngɛndɛ , bamosakoaka na bamosepejaka , oko yona odi na bomɔ na bosusu .
66004010	Akɔkɔ bo boa , basuku licinda-na-banɛi basadumbaka a boso bonde yona odi a ngɛndɛ , bo bamosakoe yona odi na bomɔ oko na bosusu ; badu-mbaka makongo mabu a boso bongɛndɛ na bambaka yembo bo ,
66004011	Kumu osu na Njambe osu , Wɛ obwani bosɔ ekumu na lisuma na kpaci Mojɔ bo wɛ okɔ leka losusu ; Lodi , na lokɔmɔ oko na bolulea bowɛ .
66005001	Nanɛ koko mokanda a ebɔ ebami ende yona odi a ngɛndɛ , mua modaka na misɔnɔ a tei na a sokolu , na mokandama na bimbete sambo .
66005002	Nanɛ koko obwɛnji oDiko ongulu akabekoe na bopipobo , Obɔngi bo adipoe mokanda na bobuka bimbete sambo nda ?
66005003	pɛpɛ nongo okina ko oho Diko , isa a ngondo , isa a cina jingondo , obwana bodipoa mokanda , isa bonja a tei .
66005004	Mbi nayea bio mojɔ bo pɛpɛ nongo moto oboloa yona obɔngɔ bo adipoe mokanda isa bonja a tei .
66005005	Na okina obasuku abala na mbi bo , YƐ boyea ; anja , Gbɔngɔ ohkota liYuda , obotina boDawidi , agbokejai bo adipoe mokanda na bimbete sambo pongono .
66005006	Mbi nanɛ a sibano engɛndɛ na bato babomɔ banɛi , na a tei ebasuku , nanɛ Mwana-Bata yona odaka ami o yona oma gwa . Adaka na njeka sambo , na miso sambo , maya madi Miembo sambo miNja-mbe mia milomama a ngondo esusu .
66005007	Iyo adoa na atomba mokanda a ebɔ ende ebami yona odaka a ngɛndɛ .
66005008	Ama yo tomba mokanda , bato babomɔ banɛi , na basuku licinda-na-banɛi , ba’mi sadumba oko a boso boMwana-Bata ; moto na moto obu adaka na gongo a ebɔ , na sani jiwɔlɔ jia jiluma na malasi ; malasi mamina madi oko bingeeli bibasɛnɔke .
66005009	Ibo ba’mba yembo ye eyene , bo , Wɛ obɔngi botomba mokanda na bobuka bimbete ; Mojɔ bo wɛ ogwa , na osikoa bato na makia mawɛ mɛnɛ ai Njambe , Bato bamakota masusu , na kɔpi jisusu , na maboti masusu , na tungu jisusu ;
66005010	Okɔ bo badae bokumu na nganga ai Njambe oSu , na bâda na bokumu a ngondo .
66005011	Anja mbi koko , naka kɔpi jimandundu mababwɛnji-baDiko pɛ njɛngi , baya bahikaka ngɛndɛ na bato babomɔ na basuku .
66005012	Babala na kɔpi epipo bo , Mwana-Bata yona ogwa abɔngi bosɔ kpaci , na makonja , na bowɛi na ndangasa , na lisuma , na ekumu , nabojo ngoa .
66005013	Na mbi naka bato basusu baDiko , na bangondo , na cina jingondo , na a madiba , na leka losusu lua lodi ena , bakabale bo , Bojongoa , na lisuma , na ekumu , na kpaci , ai yona odi a ngɛndɛ , na ai Mwana-Bata oko na bosusu .
66005014	Na bato babomɔ banɛi babala bo , Amen . Na basuku basadumba a bosakoa .
66006001	Mbi nanjaka yana adipoa Mwana-Bata embete emɔci ebimbete sambo , na naka okina obato babomɔ banɛi . Iyo abala nakɔpi ebɛi bo , Doa !
66006002	Mbi nanja , na nanɛ punda mopu . Yona odaka abaki a punda adaka na litimbo . Bamopa koko likongo na yo akɛ , mogbokoli a bogbokeja .
66006003	Adipoa yo embete ebibae , naka moto obomɔ obabae akabale bo , Doa !
66006004	Na punda otongo amana , punda mokpetu bosɔɔ . Yona odaka abaki a punda asɔ kpaci a bokatoa bowi a ngondo , bo bato bawane oko bowana ; na asɔ koko abɛnɛ monɛnɛ .
66006005	Adipoa yo embete ebisato , mbi naka moto obomɔ obasato akabale bo , Doa ! Mbi nanja , na nanɛ punda mohindo . Yona odaka abaki a punda apeaka mwɛngi mokilo a ebɔ ende .
66006006	Naka koko kɔpi ekamane a ndanda ebato babomɔ banɛi bo , Kɔpɔ emɔci endongo pata emɔci , na kɔpɔ jisato jilɔsɔ pata emɔci ; pɛ ko bobeja munɛ na vino .
66006007	Adipoa yo embete ebinɛi , mbi naka kɔpi emoto obomɔ obanɛi akabale bo , Doa !
66006008	Mbi nanja , na nanɛ punda mopu . Yona odaka abaki a punda adaka na kombe Bogwa , na esika ebagwake edaka ecini na nde ngɔngɔ . Ibo basɔ kpaci a libondo lingondo libanɛi , a boweja bato na abɛnɛ , na linjale , na mogweli moyogo , na tito babila bangondo .
66006009	Adipoa yo embete ebitano , mbi nanɛ miembo mibato baya bama gwa a mojɔ moEbaeli eNjambe , na a mojɔ motati ema bo tata , cina jihtumbu .
66006010	Babekoa na kɔpi epipo bo , Ee , Kumu mosɛnɔke osoti , enina êda wɛ pɛ bosambeja bato bangondo , na bokunda likundu a mojɔ momakia masu ?
66006011	Basɔ moto na moto kasaka eyai epu , na baka bo badi bohema koko mweka , oko a ehole êbwana etango ebina’bu baelomu na baninga babu , baya badi bogwa o ama bo gwa bo bɛnɛ .
66006012	Nanja yana adipoa yo embete ebisamano , na bojonga bongondo boda bonɛnɛ . Modika-busa mohinda oko bohinda , mohindo tuu . Songe mosusu akindoa o makia .
66006013	Njɔtɔ badiko bakwa nase o asopaka likɔkɔ mbuma , likakumana na pwea epipo .
66006014	Busa mɛnɛ bodonga o abulaka moto ekasa emokanda . Meno misusu minɛnɛnɛ , na sanga jisusu jidonga .
66006015	Bakumu bangondo , na bato banɛnɛnɛ , na bakumu babila , na konji , na bato bapipo , kanga basusu mɛnɛ , na babuli na basɔmi pongono , basabomba a mabɛngɛ mameno na a matai mameno .
66006016	Na babekoa a meno na matai bo , Toma kwani a diko disu ; bombani so a boso bonde yona odi a ngɛndɛ , na a kɛnjɔ eMwana-Bata .
66006017	Mojɔ bo busa bonɛnɛ bolikundu libu bomei ; odi bohɔnɔ husa bomina nda ?
66007001	Ngɔngɔ jimina , nanɛ babwɛnji-baDiko banɛi ; badaka ba’mi a makulu mangondo manɛi a bopea pwea jinɛi jingondo , bo pwea etahwea nongo a ngondo , isa a madiba , isa a mele .
66007002	Nanɛ koko okina obwɛnji-oDiko otongo akamane a dɔngɔ diɛsɛta . Iyo apeaka embete eNjambe obomɔ , na abekoa na kɔpi epipo ai babwɛnji badiko banɛi , baya bama sɔ kpaci a bobeja ngondo na madiba .
66007003	Abala bo , T’obejaeni oko ngondo , isa madiba , isa mele , oko bopetakini bakea embete a maso mabakɔmɛli baNjambe osu .
66007004	Naka etango ebato baya basɔ embete ; badaka koto mokama-na-domi-inɛi na koto jinɛi baya basɔ embete , bamakota masusu maYisalaele .
66007005	Balikota liYuda ; basɔ embete , koto domi-na-jibae . Balikota liLubena , koto domi-na-jibae . Bahkota liGada , koto domi-na-jibae .
66007006	Balikota liAsela , koto domi-na-jibae . Balikota liNepatali , koto domi-na-jibae . Balikota liManase , koto domi-na-jibae .
66007007	Balikota liSimeona , koto domi-na-jibae . Balikota liLewi , koto domi-na-jibae . Balikota liYisakala , koto domi-na-jibae .
66007008	Balikota liSebeuluna , koto domi-na-jibae . Balikota liYosepa , koto domi-na-jibae . Balikota liBenyamina , koto domi-na-jibae .
66007009	Nanja koko , na nanɛ emumu ebato pɛ njɛngi ; pɛpɛ nongo moto obwani bolanga etango emina ; bato bamakota masusu , na tungu jisusu , nambota jisusu , na kɔpi jisusu . Badaka ba’mi a boso bongɛndɛ , na a boso boMwana-Bata . Balwaka kasaka jiyai jipu , na bapeaka mango a mɔmɔ mabu .
66007010	Babekoa na kɔpi epipo bo , Boheleja bodi ai Njambe osu yona odi a ngɛndɛ , na ai Mwana-Bata .
66007011	Na babwɛnji-baDiko basusu baya bahikaka ngɛndɛ , na basuku , na bato babomɔ banɛi , bakwa a maso mabu a boso bongɛndɛ na basakoa Njambe bo ,
66007012	Amen ; bojongoa , na ekumu , na bowɛi na bosakoa , na lisuma , na kpaci , na ngulu , ai Njambe osu oko na bosusu . Amen .
66007013	Okina obasuku abala na mbi ; yo ’ ɛ bo , Ibo banda , baya badi na bisenja bipu ? Bahuli jɔ ?
66007014	Mbi namosɔnibeja bo , Kumu ombi , wɛ ojebi . Iyo abala na mbi bo , Ibaba badi oko baya bamani a bodi-ngoa bua bonɛnɛ ; basosi bisenja bibu , na babipuejai a makia ma-Mwana-Bata .
66007015	A mojɔ momina , badi a boso bongɛndɛ eNjambe , na bamokɔmɛkɛ a tei etempelo ende na bulu na moi . Iyona odi a ngɛndɛ âda etondo ebu bo babolame ena .
66007016	Bataya peka na nja ; bataya da na ekangola emadiba ; batadingoa koko a mojɔ momodika-busa , isa a mojɔ momoi mopipo .
66007017	Mojɔ bo , Mwana-Bata yona Odi a ndanda engɛndɛ âda mobanei obu , na âbaneja njea a melo minjiba jibomɔ ; na Njambe ahakoa mbisoli jisusu a miso mabu .
66008001	Yana adipoa Mwana-Bata embete esambo , mijɔ misusu mi yɛyɔ bowi oho Diko , isa ekenge eheure emɔci .
66008002	Na mbi nanɛ babwɛnji-baDiko sambo baya badi a boso bo-Njambe ; na basɔ mindule sambo .
66008003	Okina obwɛnji-oDiko otongo adoa , na ama a dɔngɔ dilitumbu . Iyo apeaka saani ewɔlɔ a ebɔ , na asɔ leka lolitindi lonɛnɛ a boputoana na bingeeli bibasɛnɔke basusu a diko dilitumbu liwɔlɔ lia lidi a boso bongɛndɛ .
66008004	Modidi moleka lolitindi moputuoana na bingeeli bibasɛnɔke , mokina ebɔ eobwɛnji , na mowea a boso boNjambe .
66008005	Obwɛnji omina atomba saani , aelumeja na mosa molitumbu , na amosopa a ngondo . Ngɔngɔ jimina , jidaka oko bɛi , na daka enɛnɛ , na mikalimo , na bojonga bongondo .
66008006	Babwɛnji sambo , baya badaka na mindule sambo , basɛlingoa a bohuea .
66008007	Obwɛnji oboso ahuea mondule , na mbua akwa a ngondo , oko mbua omatai na mosa maya maputoana na makia . Ekenge ebisato engondo engoa mosa ; ekenge ebisato emele engoa , na njienjie jigwa kanga jisusu mɛnɛ .
66008008	Obwɛnji obabae ahuea mondule , na ekina eka , o mono monɛnɛnɛ mongoake na mosa , edumbama a madiba-mamukwa , na ekenge ebisato emadiba ebongoa makia .
66008009	Tito bamadiba bagwa , libondo limasato ; na masua magwa , libondo limasato .
66008010	Obwɛnji obasato ahuea mondule , na monjɔtɔ monɛnɛ o ekɔmɛli emotanda , adonga oho Diko na akwa nase ; akwa a diko diekenge ebisato edua na njiba .
66008011	Kombe emonjɔtɔ omina edi Abisiniti . Ekenge ebisato emadiba ebongoa abisiniti , na bato bagwa banɛnɛ a mojɔ momadiba mamina , mojɔ bo madaka na boyo .
66008012	Obwɛnji obanɛi ahuea mondule , na ekenge ebisato emodika-busa ebeha , na ekenge ebisato esonge , na ekenge ebisato enjɔtɔ pongono . Ekenge ebisato ebohu bobu ehinda oko bohinda bo ekenge ebisato ebusa etahoa , na ekenge ebisato ebulu pongono .
66008013	Anja mbi koko , nanɛ popo akapimboe oho ta busa , na akabekoe na kɔpi epipo bo , Monɔngɔ , monɔngɔ , monɔngɔ , ai bato baya badi a ngondo , a mojɔ momindule mitongo Mibabwɛnji baya bakɛkɛ ahue .
66009001	Ohwɛnji obatano ahuea mondule , na mbi nanɛ monjɔtɔ yona omadonga Diko na ami kwa oko a ngondo . Iyo asɔ sabe emo-mbɔndɔ monase ,
66009002	na adipoa mombɔndɔ monase . Modidi momana a mombɔndɔ , o modidi momosa monɛnɛ . Modika-busa mohinda , na husa bohinda a mojɔ momodidi momombɔndɔ .
66009003	Bapaala bamana a modidi na banangana a ngondo , na basɔ ngulu yena ebwani na ngulu ekoolo bangondo .
66009004	Basɔ mobeko bo batabeja njienjie jingondo , isa njua , isa mele , oko bato pɛ baya bapeliti embete eNjambe a maso mabu .
66009005	Basɔ kpaci bo babanɔngejae songe batano , te bo babawoe . Na bakeja mwano mwano mokoolo yana akomaka yo moto .
66009006	Masu mamina makadoa , bato badi boduka bogwa , pɛ ko boboloja bogwa . Badi boda na posa ebogwa , na bogwa bodi bobacia oko bocia .
66009007	Bapaala bamina badaka o punda baya badi na mosɛlingo mobila . Badaka na leka a melo Mibu o makongo mawɔlɔ . Maso mabu madaka o maso mabato .
66009008	Swe jibu jidaka o swe jibali , na mino mabu madaka o mino magbɔngɔ .
66009009	Molilo mobu a mupa modaka o nguba jiebende , na epupeli emapapulapu mabu edaka o mokilimo mopunda banɛnɛ baya bapotaka na majangi a bila .
66009010	Mikɔmbɔ mibu midaka o mikɔmbɔ mikoolo , na ngɛngɛ jibu pongono , na ngulu ebu a bodingoja bato songe batano edaka a mikɔmbɔ Mibu .
66009011	Obwɛnji omombɔndɔ monase adi kumu obu ; kombe ende a kɔpi eBaEbele edi Abadona , na edi Apolwona a kɔpi eBaEla .
66009012	Monɔngɔ moboso monɔi . Minɔngɔ mitongo Mibae mikɛkɛ adoe .
66009013	Obwɛnji obasamano ahuea mondule , na mhi naka kɔpi ekamane a njeka jinɛi jilitumbu liwɔlɔ lia lidi a boso boNjambe .
66009014	Kɔpi emina ebala na obwɛnji obasamano yona odaka na mondule bo , Cingoa babwɛnji banɛi baya badi a mbɔci a dua enɛnɛ Pelata .
66009015	Babwɛnji bamina banɛi , baya bama sɛlingoa a mojɔ moehole emina , na busa bomina , na songe omina , na yanga emina , baci-ngoama bo bawoe ekenge ebisato ebato bangondo .
66009016	Etango emandundu mabasoda bapunda edaka mandundu koto licinda , tu lindundu basoda koto domi , na mbi naka etango ebu .
66009017	Anjaka mbi oko bonja , nanɛ punda na baya badaka babaki a punda . Mililo Mibu mimupa midaka mikpetu o mosa , na mihindo , na midaka koko na langi esupulu . Melo mipunda midaka o melo migbɔngɔ , na mosa na modidi mimanaka a minɔkɔ Mibu .
66009018	Ekenge ebisato ebato bangondo egwa a mojɔ momadingoa ma masato , oko a mojɔ momosa , na modidi , na supulu , mia mimanaka a minɔkɔ Mibu .
66009019	Mojɔ bo ngulu epunda edaka a minɔkɔ mibu , na a mikɔmbɔ mibu . Mikɔmbɔ mibu midaka o njɔ na melo minjɔ , na banɔngeja bato oko na melo mimina .
66009020	Bato batongo baya bahela a madingoa mamina bai-hekoja milema mibu a bokina leka lokɔ bo na mɔmɔ ; na baikina bosakoa miembo Mibe , isa bilimo biwɔlɔ , na bilimo bipalata , na bilimo biebende , na bilimo bimatai , na bilimo bimole bia bipeliti nongo njɛnɛ isa njoki , na te bidalake .
66009021	Na baihekoja milema Mibu a bokwa ekɔmɛli ebu ebowa bato , na elomu ebu edemba , na ngando jibu jibosambolu , na liba .
66010001	Nanɛ koko obwɛnji otongo akahule oho Diko , obwɛnji ongulu . Eyembi emohuaka , na moyama modaka a molo monde . Boso bondebodaka o modika-busa , na mako mande madaka o makwe mamosa .
66010002	Adaka na mokanda mokɛkɛ bwase a ebɔ ende . Abakea ebota ende ebami a diko dimadiba-mamukwa , na ebota ende ebali a diko dingondo .
66010003	Abekoa na kɔpi epipo o agbomaka gbɔngɔ . Yana abekoa yo , bɛi sambo bagama oko bogama .
66010004	Yana asia bɛi sambo bogama , mbi nakɔ bo nasɔne ; naka ko kɔpi ekahule oho Diko bo , Kanda na bakea embete a mijɔ Mibali bɛi sambo ; Pojisɔne oko .
66010005	Na obwɛnji onɛkɛ mbi ami a madiba-mamukwa na a ngondo , angɔjɔ ebɔ ende ebami diko ,
66010006	na abɛlɛ bɛli na yona odi na bomɔ oko na bosusu , yona okɔ Diko na leka losusu lua lodi ena , na ngondo pongono , na leka losusu lua lodi ena , na madiba koko , na leka losusu lua lodi ena . Abɛlɛ bɛli na nde bo ehole ebo’mba esii ,
66010007	na bo obwɛnji osambo akahuea mondule , mojɔ mobombamake moNjambe mongame a masu mamina , o ajebeja yo batɔndɔi bakɔmɛli bande .
66010008	Kɔpi eka mbi ekahule Diko ebala na mbi koko bo , Kɛ atombe mokanda mokɛkɛ mua modi bwase a ebɔ eobwɛnji yona odi ami a diko di madiba-mamukwa na a diko dingondo .
66010009	Oko boa mbi nakɛ ai obwɛnji , nabala na nde bo apɛni mokanda mokɛkɛ . Yo abala na mbi bo , Tomba mokanda , moyaka . Môda na boyo a sɔpɔ , a monɔkɔ ko bolɛbulɛbu o pɔki .
66010010	Natomba mokanda mokɛkɛ a ebɔ eobwɛnji , na namomea oko bomea . Modaka na bolɛbulɛbu bopɔki a monɔkɔ mombi ; yana ko amea mbi mokanda , modaka na boyo a sɔpɔ .
66010011	Na abala na mbi bo , Toma pa koko biseko a mojɔ mobato banɛnɛ , na makota , na kɔpi , na bakumu .
66011001	Mbi nasɔ mokɔmbɛ o pango ; na okina abala na mbi bo , Angɔ ; angɛ mwɛngi motempelo eNjambe , na litumbu , na baya basakoaka ena .
66011002	Pɛ bongɛ ko libanda lia lidi a sokolu etempelo . Kina libanda , mojɔ bo lihɛngɛmi ai makota , na badi bodɛhɛ ngando esɛnɔke na bihota bibu songe domi-inɛi na babae .
66011003	Mbi nadi bopa batati bambi babae kpaci a bopa biseko masu koto emɔci mikama Mibae na masu domi-inɛi na badi bolwa oko minyuku pɛ .
66011004	Ibo badi mele mibae miolive na paka jibae , na badi mema a boso boKumu ongondo .
66011005	Okina moto akapala bobanɔngeja , mosa momanaka a minɔkɔ mibu a bowa soki jibu . Moto akapala boba-nɔngeja , adi bogwa boa .
66011006	Ibo badi na kpaci a bokanda busa bo mbua atakwa a masu mabiseko bibu . Na badi na kpaci a bokindoja madiba makia , na a boloma bego bisusu a ngondo yana apalaka bo .
66011007	Bakasieja tati ebu , tito yona omanaka a mombɔndɔ monase adi bona na bu bila , abagbokejabí na abawabí .
66011008	Njemba jibu jidikabí a licilinga lingando yena enɛnɛ ; kombe engando emina edi oko mondɛ , edi Sɔdɔmɔ na Ejipito , esika egwa Kumu a mole-mobokea .
66011009	Bato banjabí njemba jibu masu masato na ekenge , bato bamakota mangondo , na maboti , na kɔpi na tungu jisusu . Na batajimabí bo moto apusee njemba jibu .
66011010	Bato bangondo basepabí na enanga enɛnɛ , na bapanabí leka a mojɔ momina , cina bo batɔndɔi ba babae bama nɔngeja bato bangondo .
66011011	Ama nɔ masu masato na ekenge ko , mohuli mobomɔ mo’mi donga oko ai Njambe , na mokwea a tei ebu , na bama mema . Na bato baya babanɛ baluluma na bɔ .
66011012	Ibo babae baka kɔpi epipo ekahule oho Diko , ekabale na bu bo , Doani jɔno diko ! Na bawea a Diko na eyembi , ena ko soki jibu jibanjaka .
66011013	Ngondo ejonga na bojonga bonɛnɛ a ehole emina , na ekenge edomi engondo egwa oko bogwa . Bato bagwa a mojɔ mobojonga bomina , bato koto sambo . Baya badika badaka na bɔ bonɛnɛ , na basakoa Njambe oDiko .
66011014	Monɔngɔ moMibae mosii ; mua momisato mokɛkɛ adoe .
66011015	Obwɛnji osambo ahuea mondule , na kɔpi jibekoa a Diko bo , Bokumu bongondo bodi e dɛye bokumu boKumu osu na Masiya onde . Iyo adi boda Kumu oko na bosusu .
66011016	Na basuku domi-ibae na banɛi baya badaka a mingbelɛngɔ Mibu a boso boNjambe basadumba nase , oko a maso mabu ,
66011017	na basakoa Njambe bo , Bosakoaka wɛ Kumu Njambe obonɔ , yona odi na yona odaka , Mojɔ bo opei ngulu ewɛ enɛnɛ , na okondi a bokumu bowɛ .
66011018	Makota madaka na kɛlɛ ; likundu liwɛ ko lidoi . Ehole ebosambeja bagwake emei , A bokɔ monganji ai batɔndɔi na ai basɛnɔke , bakɔmɛli bawɛ , Na bato baya basumaka kombe ewɛ , na banɛnɛnɛ na bakɛkɛlɛkɛ , Ehole ehowa likinda haya bahejaka ngondo .
66011019	Tempelo eNjambe oho Diko edipoama , na edejai emokongo monde edaka a bohu a tei etempelo ende . Mikalimo mimana a ehole emina , na daka enɛnɛ , na bɛi , na bojonga bongondo , na mbua monɛnɛ omatai akwa .
66012001	Embete enɛnɛ emana oho Diko , oko mwali yona olwa modika-busa o bisenja . Songe adaka a cina jibibota binde , na adaka na likongo a molo monde , oko njɔtɔ domi-na-babae .
66012002	Mwali omina adaka na demi , na abekoaka a mojɔ mobipeko na mwano mobobota .
66012003	Ekina embete etongo emana oho Diko , oko Dalakona monɛnɛ mokpetu . Iyo adaka na melo sambo na njeka domi , na makongo mabokumu sambo madaka a melo minde .
66012004	Mokɔmbɔ monde mogbula libondo limasato linjɔtɔ badiko , na abadumba nase a ngondo . Dalakona ama a boso bomwali yona opalaka bobota , bo mwali akabota , yo amee mwana oko bomea .
66012005	Mwali abota mwana-momi yona odi boda na kpaci a makota masusu , na tondo ende edi boda tondo eebende . Mwana’nde ko atombama ai Njambe na a ngɛndɛ ende .
66012006	Mwali acia a lisobe , a esika ema sɛlingoa Njambe a mojɔ monde , bo bamobɔkɔe oho masu koto emɔci mikama Mibae na masu macinda masato .
66012007	Bila emana oho Diko . Mikaele na babwɛnji bande bana na Dalakona . Dalakona na babwɛnji bande bana ,
66012008	na bagboka ; na baiboloja koko esika eboda oho Diko .
66012009	Dalakona monɛnɛ akwa , njɔ yona moyou yona odi na kombe Jabalo na Satana , mokosei ongondo esusu . Adumbama a ngondo , na babwɛnji bande badu-mbama na nde pongono .
66012010	Naka koko kɔpi epipo ekabale oho Diko bo , Edɛye , mohelo modoi , na ngulu , na Bokumu boNjambe , na kpaci eMasiya onde . Mojɔ bo yona odumbea baninga basu ebango adumbami nase , oko yona obadumbeaka a boso boNjambe osu na bulu na moi .
66012011	Bamogbokejai a mojɔ momakia maMwana-Bata na a mojɔ moebaeli etati ebu , cina bo baijuma bopa mihelo Mibu , pɛ bobanga bogwa .
66012012	Sepani na mojɔ momina , no baya badi oho Diko , na Diko esusu mɛnɛ . Monɔngɔ ko a ngondo , na a madiba-mamukwa , mojɔ bo Satana atiti ai no na kɛnjɔ enɛnɛ , na ajebaka bo ehole ende edikai mweka pɛ .
66012013	Yana anɛ Dalakona bo adumbama nase a ngondo , yo abengana mwali yona oma bota mwana-momi .
66012014	Mwali ko asɔ mapapulapu mabae mapopo monɛnɛ , a bocia a esika ende a lisobe , bo bamobɔkoe oho yanga emɔci , na bianga bibae , na ekenge eyanga emɔci , bo Njɔ atamonɛe .
