66012015	Njɔ asopa dua emadiba a monɔkɔ monde ngɔngɔ jimwali , bo amocindojae na mopimbola .
66012016	Ngondo ko ekɔmeja mwali ; ngondo edipoa monɔkɔ na emea dua ema sopa Dalakona a monɔkɔ monde .
66012017	Dalakona akɛnjɔ na mwali bou mɛnɛ , na akɛ a bona bila na bana bande batongo baya basumaka mibeko mi-Njambe , na baya batataka tati ai Yesu .
66013001	Na ama a mbongu emadiba-mamukwa . Nanɛ koko Tito akamane a madiba-mamukwa . Adaka na njeka domi , na melo sambo . Makongo mabokumu domi madaka a njeka jinde , na kombe jibosambolu jidaka a melo minde .
66013002	Tito onɛ mbi adaka o swa . Makaka mande madaka o makaka matito kombe ours , na monɔkɔ monde modaka o monɔkɔ mogbɔngɔ . Dalakona amopa ngulu ende mɛnɛ na ngɛndɛ ende , na kpaci ende enɛnɛ .
66013003	Nanɛ bo mokina molo monde modi na pola ebogwa . Iyo ko ahela a pola ende ebogwa , na ngondo esusu ecingama na Tito na bokamoa .
66013004	Bato basakoa Dalakona mojɔ bo yo ama pa kpaci ende a Tito . Basakoa koko Tito na ebaeli ye ; Obwani na Tito nda ? Odi na ngulu a bona na nde nda ?
66013005	Tito adaka na monɔkɔ a bobala bikenge biegbo , na bikenge bibosambolu ; na asɔ kpaci bo akɔe o apalaka yo songe domi-inɛi na babae .
66013006	Adipoa monɔkɔ monde a botangola Njambe , na kombe ende , na ngando ende , na baya badi oho Diko .
66013007	Adaka na kpaci a bona bila na basɛnɔke na bo abagbokejae . Asɔ koko kpaci a makota masusu , na tungu jisusu , na kɔpi jisusu , na maboti masusu .
66013008	Bato basusu bangondo badi bomosakoa , oko baya baditi na kombe jibu a mokanda moMwana-Bata yona ogwa , kombe jia jisɔnɔmɔ ena oko a libangake lingondo .
66013009	Isa moto adi na matoi , yɛ ahokee .
66013010	Moto yona opeaka masungu âpeama lisungu yo mɛnɛ . Moto akawa na abɛnɛ , adi bogwa na abɛnɛ yo mɛnɛ . Cina elingbangba libasɛnɔke na ejimeli ebu oko yena .
66013011	Nanɛ koko okina Tito otongo . Iyo amana a ngondo , na adaka na njeka jibae , njeka jimwana-bata ; ebaeli ende ko edaka ebaeli eDalakona .
66013012	Iyo adaka na kpaci esusu eTito oboso a ngando ende , na akɔ bo bato basusu bangondo , ngondo esusu mɛnɛ , basakoe Tito yona oboso , yona oma hela a pola ende ehogwa .
66013013	Akɔ koko mindumba minɛnɛ , na akɔ bo mosa modonge obo Diko na motite nase a boso bobato .
66013014	Na alɛngɛ bato bangondo cina emindumba mikɔkɔ yo a esika eTito , na abatɔndɔ bo bakɔe elimo eTito yona oma hela a pola eabɛnɛ .
66013015	Asɔ koko kpaci bo apɛ mohuli a elimo eTito , bo elimo eTito ebale , na bo awejae bato basusu baya balona bosakoa elimo eTito .
66013016	Na akɔ bo bato kanga basusu mɛnɛ basɛ embete a ebɔ ebami isa a boso , na bakɛkɛ na banɛnɛnɛ , na bato balikonja na bato babokwali , na sɔmi na babuli pongono ,
66013017	bo , moto amiti da na embete emina , oko kombe eTito , isa etango ekombe ende , atahɔnɔ bosomba eka , isa bongɛjɛ eka .
66013018	Mojɔ momina modi mojɔ mobowɛi . Isa moto adi na bocingea , yɛ alange etango eTito . Mojɔ bo etango emina edi etango emoto , na etango ende edi Mikama misamano domi-isamano na isamano .
66014001	Nanja koko , na nanɛ Mwana-Bata ami a Mono moSiona . Bato badaka na nde koto mokama domi-inɛi-na-inɛi , na badaka na kombe ende , na kombe eSangwa’nde , a maso mabu .
66014002	Naka kɔpi ekahule Diko ; edaka na molunju moepeela enɛnɛ , o ekɔmɛli ebɛi ; kɔpi eka mbi ebwana na doi libato babibumba baya babomaka bibumba bibu .
66014003	Ba’mba yembo eyene a boso bongɛndɛ , na a boso bobasuku , na a boso bobato babomɔ banɛi . Pɛpɛ nongo okina otongo obwana bokoa yembo emina , oko bato bamina , bato koto mokama domi-inɛi-na-inɛi baya bama sikoama a ngondo .
66014004	Ibo badi oko baya baisabeja na bali , mojɔ bo batajebaka mojɔ momwali . Bacingamaka na Mwana-Bata bisika bisusu bikɛkɛ yo . Basikoama a tei ebato bo badae mbuma jiboso ai Njambe , na ai Mwana-Bata .
66014005	Bokosea boditi nongo a minɔkɔ mibu , mojɔ bo bapeliti nongo litɔnɔ .
66014006	Nanɛ koko okina obwɛnji otongo akapimboe a tei ebusa . Iyo adaka na Mwako Mopele mua modi na bosusu , bo atɔndɔe bato bangondo , makota na makota , tungu na tungu , kɔpi na kɔpi , maboti na maboti .
66014007	Abala na kɔpi epipo bo , Bangani Njambe ; mokumejani yo , mojɔ bo ehole ende ebosambeja emei . Mosakoani yo , yona oyoa Diko na nase , na madiba-mamukwa , na njiba .
66014008	Okina otongo , obwɛnji obabae adoa , na abala bo , Ekwi ! Babilo ekwi , ngando yena enɛnɛ ! mwali yona okɔ bo makota masusu malangoe na vino eposa elisɔngi linde .
66014009	Okina otongo , obwɛnji obasato adoa , na abekoa bo , Moto akasakoa Tito na elimo ende , na akasɔ embete ende a licinga limbanda , isa a ebɔ ,
66014010	moto omina adi bomwaka vino elikundu li-Njambeyena esɛlingoamaa kɔpɔ ekɛlɛ ende , pɛpɛ nongo bombɛjɛ ; na adi bodingoa na mosa na supulu a boso bobabwɛnji basɛnɔke , na a boso boMwana-Bata .
66014011	Modidi momosa mobodingoa bobu moweaka diko oko na bosusu ; baditi nongo na bowi , isa na bulu isa na moi , basakoi bamina baTito na elimo ende , na baya basɔ embete ekombe ende .
66014012	A mojɔ momina , baya basumaka Mibeko mi-Njambe na ejimeli eYesu , babwani boda na lingbangba .
66014013	Naka koko kɔpi ekabale oho Diko bo , Sɔnɔ mojɔ mu ; Bagwake baya bagwaka a tei eKumu badi na bojongoa , e dɛye , oko na bosusu . Mwembo mobalaka bo , Ee badi na bojongoa , bo baheme a minɔngɔ Mibu , mojɔ bo bilomu bibu bibasusaka .
66014014	Anja mbi koko , nanɛ eyembi epu . Okina adaka abaki a eyembi o moto . Adaka na likongo liwɔlɔ a molo monde , na mombimbi mopɔlu a ebɔ ende .
66014015	Okwa obwɛnji otongo amana a tempelo , na abekoa na bopipo ai yona odaka abaki a eyembi bo , Tomba mombimbi mowɛ na kɛsɛ , mojɔ bo ehole ebojua emei . Bojua bongondo bobwani oko bobwana .
66014016	Oko boa , yona odaka abaki a eyembi ameja mombimbi monde a diko dingondo , na ajua ngondo oko bojua .
66014017	Okina obwɛnji otongo amana a tempelo oho Diko , na yo adaka na mombimbi mopɔlu pongono .
66014018	Na okina obwɛnji otongo koko amana a litumbu . Iyo adaka na kpaci a mojɔ momosa , na abekoa na bopipo ai yona odaka na mombimbi mopɔlu ; abekoa bo , Imeja mombimbi mowɛ mopɔlu ; kɛsɛ bililo bimbuma jivine engondo , mojɔ bo mbuma jingondo jikpeti .
66014019	Obwɛnji omina ameja mombimbi monde a diko dingondo , akɛsɛ mbuma jivine engondo , na adumba jisusu a eboka enɛnɛ ekɛnjɔ eNjambe .
66014020	Eboka emina edaka a sokolu engando . Yana asieja bo bo’nda mbuma , makia mamana a eboka , na makɛlɛ bohali , oko a kilometa mikama misato na domi-isamano ; na madaka na ndinda oko a kamba emolo mo-punda .
66015001	Nanɛ koko ekina embete etongo oho Diko , embete enɛnɛ ebokamoa , oko babwɛnji sambo baya bapeli minɔngɔ sambo , minɔngɔ misuka , mojɔ bo kɛnjɔ eNjambe edi bosia na minɔngɔ mimina .
66015002	Nanɛ koko ekina eka yena edaka o libale litalatala lia liputoana na mosa . Baya bama gbokeja Tito , na elimo ende , na embete ekombe ende , badaka ba’mi a mbongu elibale litalatala , na badaka na bibumba biNjambe a mɔmɔ mabu .
66015003	Ibo ba’mbaka yembo eMose mokɔmɛli oNjambe , na yembo eMwana-Bata bo , Ee , Kumu Njambe obonɔ ! Bilomu biwɛ bidi binɛnɛnɛ , bidi na bokamoa . Ee , Kumu omakota ! Njea jiwɛ jidi jitangboake , njea jisoti .
66015004	Ee Kumu ; odi pɛ bosuma , pɛ bokumeja kombe ewɛ nda ? Mojɔ bo , odi mosɛnɔke oko wɛ pɛ . Makota masusu madi bodoa a bosakoa wɛ , Mojɔ bo masambeja mawɛ maboloi a bohu .
66015005	Ngɔngɔ jimina , nanja koko , na tempelo eEtondo ebotata oho Diko edipoama .
66015006	Babwɛnji sambo baya badaka na minɔngɔ sambo bamana a tempelo . Badaka na bisenja bipu bopɛ , na kamba jiwɔlɔ jidaka a mupa mabu .
66015007	Okina obato babomɔ apa babwɛnji sambo kɔpɔ jiwɔlɔ sambo jia jiluma na likundu liNjambe yona odi na bosusu .
66015008	Na tempelo eluma na ekumu , na ngulu eNjambe , o ekɔmɛli emodidi momosa . Pɛpɛ nongo moto obwani bokwea a tempelo oko adi minɔngɔ sambo Mibabwɛnji sambo pɛ bopeta sia .
66016001	Nakakokokɔpi epipo ekamane a tempelo , ekabale nababwɛnji sambo bo , Kɛni asope kɔpɔ sambo jilikundu liNjambe a ngondo .
66016002	Obwɛnji oboso akɛ na asopa kɔpɔ ende a ngondo . Na bato baya badaka na embete eTito , na baya basakoaka elimo ende badingoa na pola jibe jisaya .
66016003	Obwɛnji obabae asopa kɔpɔ ende a madiba-mamukwa , na madiba makindoa makia , o makia manjemba emoto . Na leka losusu lua lodaka mɔ a madiba logwa oko bogwa .
66016004	Obwɛnji obasato asopa kɔpɔ ende a dua na njiba , na jikindoa makia .
66016005	Na naka obwɛnji omadiba akabale bo , Ee , wɛ Mosɛnɔke yona odi , na yona odaka , Wɛ olongi na bisambi biwɛ ;
66016006	Mojɔ bo bato basopa makia mabasɛnɔke na mabatɔndɔi , Na wɛ obanusi makia . Mokindo mobu mobwani .
66016007	Naka koko litumbu likabale bo , Ee , Kumu Njambe obonɔ , Bisambi biwɛ bibɔngi , bidi bongbebongbe .
66016008	Obwɛnji obanɛi asopa kɔpɔ ende a modika-busa , na modika-busa mosɔ kpaci a bonɔngeja bato na mosa .
66016009	Bato bakɛloa na moi mopipo , na basinga kombe eNjambe yona odaka na kpaci a minɔngɔ mimina , na baibekoja nongo milema Mibu bo bakumejae Njambe .
66016010	Obwɛnji obatano asopa kɔpɔ ende a ngɛndɛ eTito . Bokumu boTito bohinda na modidi . Bato bakokala biemi bibu a mojɔ momwano ,
66016011	na basinga Njambe a mojɔ momwano mobu na pola jibu , na baihekoja nongo milema Mibu a bokina bikɔmɛli bibu .
66016012	Obwɛnji obasamano asopa kɔpɔ ende a Pelata , dua yena enɛnɛ . Madiba madua emina makoka oko bokoka , a bosɛlingoa njea ebakumu baɛsɛta .
66016013	Nanɛ koko miembo Mibe misato mia midaka o magbɔsɔ , mikamane a monɔkɔ moDalakona , na a monɔkɔ moTito , na a monɔkɔ moMotɔndɔi obokosea .
66016014	Miembo mimina midi miembo Mibajabolo ; mikɔkɔ mindumba , na mikɛkɛ ai bakumu bangondo esusu bo Mibabolee a mojɔ mobila a busa bua bonɛnɛ boNjambe obonɔ .
66016015	( Hokeani ; mbi nadoaka na mbɛmbɛ emobi . Bojongoa ai moto yona odi mosu , yona obaneaka bisenja binde bo atamana mbundu na sɔni a boso bobato . )
66016016	Na Mibabolea a esika yena edi na kombe Alamagedo a kɔpi eBaEbele .
66016017	Obwɛnji osambo asopa kɔpɔ ende a pwea . Kɔpi epipo emana a tempelo ; kɔpi emina edonga a ngɛndɛ na ebala bo , Mojɔ mosii !
66016018	Mikalimo mimana na daka enɛnɛ , na bɛi , na bojonga bongondo bonɛnɛ . Bojonga bomina bodaka bonɛnɛ mɛnɛ ; ehole edi bato a ngondo , baipaka nɛ bojonga bongondo bonɛnɛ boa .
66016019	Ngando yena enɛnɛ ekabama , mabondo masato , na ngando jimakota jigwa . Njambe aibosa Babilo , ngando yena enɛnɛ ; amonusa kɔpɔ elikundu linde ligbasoake .
66016020	Sanga jisusu jicia bohali , na meno miiboloa koko .
66016021	Mbua monɛnɛ omatai adonga Diko , na makwa a diko dibato . Matai mamina madaka na manji , kilo domi-itano , kilo domi-itano , na bato basinga Njambe a mojɔ momogweli momatai cina bo mogweli momina modaka mojɔ monɛnɛ mɛnɛ .
66017001	Okina obabwɛnji sambo baya badaka na kɔpɔ sambo , adoa na abala na mbi bo , Doa bo nanejae wɛ esambi emwali obɔɔli yona monɛnɛ , yona odi na edie ende a diko didua jinɛnɛ .
66017002	Bakumu bangondo bangɛkɛ na nde bɔɔli , na bato bangondo balangoi na vino elisɔngi linde .
66017003	Obwɛnji omina atomba mbi a mwembo a lisobe , na nanɛ okwa mwali oho . Adaka abaki a Tito mokpetu bosɔɔ yona odaka na kombe jinɛnɛ jibosambolu a mokuku monde , na adaka na melo sambo , na njeka domi .
66017004	Mwali omina alwaka bisenja bikpetu na bikpetu bosɔɔ ; mohlo monde modaka molilo mowɔlɔ , na matai mayumu , na mayaka mayumu enɛnɛ . Adaka na kɔpɔ a ebɔ ende , kɔpɔ ewɔlɔ , yena eluma botɔ na ngando jinde jibosambolu , na lisɔngi linde , na ndukeli jinde .
66017005	Ekina kombe esɔnɔmɔ a licinga limbanda , na cina ekombe emina edi mojɔ mobombamake ; BABILO MONƐNƐ , NANGE ’ BATO BABƆƆLI NA NGANDO JIBOSAMBOLU JINGONDO .
66017006	Mbi nanɛ mwali omina yona oma langoa na makia mabasɛnɔke , na makia mabatati baYesu . Yana anɛ mbi mwali omina , nakamoa na bokamoa bonɛnɛ .
66017007	Obwɛnji ko abala na mbi bo , Okamoaka mojɔ moye ? Mbi nadi boboloja ai wɛ mojɔ mobombamake momwali omina , na Tito yona omotombaka , yona odi na melo sambo na njeka domi .
66017008	Tito onɛki wɛ adaka , na aditi . Adi bomana ko a mombɔndɔ monase , na adi bonɔ oko a bodimoa . Na bato bangondo , oko baya badi pɛ bosɔnɔmɔ kombe a mokanda mobomɔ a bobanga bongondo , badi bokamoa yana anɛkɛ bo Tito yona odaka , yona oditi , na yona odi bodoa koko .
66017009	Mojɔ mu mobwani na bocingea bomoto obowɛi . Melo sambo midi meno sambo , na edie emwali edi a meno mimina .
66017010	Melo mimina midi koko bakumu sambo . Batano babu bakwi ; okina adi oko ; yona otongo adoakini ; na yo akadoa , atayeyoa nongo ekoka .
66017011	Tito yona odaka , na aditi e dɛye , adi kumu obomwambe ; acingi na bakumu sambo , na akɛkɛ a bodimoa .
66017012	Njeka domi jinɛki wɛ jidi bakumu domi baya basɔkini bokumu ; badi bosɔ kpaci ebakumu , na Tito pongono , heure emɔci .
66017013	Ibo basusu badi na mokano momɔci , na bapaka ngulu ebu na kpaci ebu a Tito .
66017014	Badi bona bila na Mwana-Bata , na Mwana-Bata adi bobagbokeja , mojɔ bo yo adi Kumu obakumu , na Koi obaroi ; na baya bacingi na nde babeama , babɔmɔ , na badi bato baejimeli .
66017015	Abala na mbi koko bo , Dua jinɛki wɛ , oho adi mwali obɔɔli na mobondo , jidi oko makota , na makumu , na bato , na kɔpi .
66017016	Njeka domi jinɛki wɛ , njeka jimina na Tito pongono , — ibo badi boda na mwali obɔɔli oko soki ; bamobejabi , bamokinabi mbundu , bayakabí mimi minde na bamotumbabi na mosa .
66017017	Mojɔ bo Njambe asi mojɔ momina a milema Mibu bo bakɔe mokano monde na molema momɔci , na bo bapɛ Tito kpaci ebu ebakumu oko adi bibaeli bi-Njambe pɛ bopeta ngama .
66017018	Na mwali onɛki wɛ adi oko ngando enɛnɛnɛ , yena edi na kpaci ai bakumu bangondo .
66018001	Yana asia ngando jimina , nanɛ okina obwɛnji otongo akahule oho Diko . Iyo adaka na kpaci enɛnɛ , na ngondo esusu ehoa na bolailai boekumu ende .
66018002	Abekoa na kɔpi epipo bo , Ekwi ! Babilo , ngando yena enɛnɛ ekwi ; Edi oko ekokolo ebajabolo , Esika emiembo misusu Mibe , Esika embulu basusu babosɔtɔ na bamaneene .
66018003	Mojɔ bo makota masusu malangoi na vino elisɔngi linde ; Bakumu bangondo ba’ngi na nde bɔɔli , Na bato babwasa bangondo bahɛjɛ likonja libu linɛnɛ a mojɔ mobikɔmɛli binde binɛnɛ bibosambolu .
66018004	Naka koko kɔpi etongo ekahule Diko na ekabale bo , Bato bambi , imanani , mokinani yo , osaka cingamani na nde a jibe jinde , osaka katanani na nde a madingoa mande .
66018005	Mojɔ bo jibe jinde jidi o mono monɛnɛ mua momeaka a Diko , Na Njambe alɛi mojɔ mojibe jinde .
66018006	Sɔmbejani ai yo oko na mwɛngi mopaka yo mɛnɛ , Na nɛngejani mokindo monde a mojɔ mobikɔmɛli binde ; Lumejani kɔpɔ enusa yo na bato batongo bihole bibae , a mojɔ monde mɛnɛ .
66018007	O asakumejaka yo , na adaka yo na bikɔmɛli bibosambolu , Oko boa mopani yo molɔbɔ na bio oko na mwɛngi momina . Mojɔ bo abalaka a molema monde bo , Mbi nadi a ngɛndɛ ekumu , Naditi nongo mwali-obogwa , nitada nongo na mokwea .
66018008	A mojɔ momina , madingoa mande madi bodoa ai yo a busa bomɔci , mogweli , mokwea , na linjale . Na atumbama na mosa , Mojɔ bo Kumu Njambe yona omosambejaka adi mopipo .
66018009	Bakumu bangondo baya bangɛ na nde bɔɔli na bakatana na nde a bikɔmɛli binde bibosambolu , bakanɛ modidi mobotumba bonde , badi bomoyea kɔndɔ .
66018010	Badi bo’ma bohali a mojɔ mobɔ bobodi-ngoa bonde . Badi bobala bo , Monɔngɔ ! Monɔngɔ ! Wɛ ngando enɛnɛnɛ ! Wɛ Babilo ngando epipo ! Likundu liwɛ limei bundumo .
66018011	Bato babwasa bangondo bayeaka mbisoli na bamoyeaka kɔndɔ , mojɔ bo bato te bayake somba na bu leka lobwasa ,
66018012	leka lowɔlɔ , na palata , matai mayumu , na mayaka mayumu , bisenja bibotɛlɛtɛlɛ bikpetu na bikpetu bosɔɔ , soa ekpetu , na mele misusu miyumu , leka longɔlu jimbongo , na leka losusu lua lokɔmɔ na mele na matai , na leka lua loluama na ebende na mboa ,
66018013	sinamona , na lihengako , na midikadika , na malasi , na male , na vino , na minɛ , na mitɛkɛ mipele , na ndongo , na ngɔmbɔ , na bata , na punda , na mituka , na mikuku na milema mibato .
66018014	Molema mowɛ modaka na posa embuma jikpetu , na jicia wɛ bohali . Leka lowɛ losusu loyumu , na leka lowɛ losusu loekumu lobungi na wɛ , na bato bata-loboloja koko .
66018015	Bato baya bakɔ masa na leka lomina , baya badiba likonja linɛnɛ a mojɔ monde , badi bo’ma bohali oko na bio na bolɛbɛ , na bɔ pongono , a mojɔ mobodingoa bonde , na badi bobala bo ,
66018016	Monɔngɔ ! monɔngɔ ! ngando yena enɛnɛnɛ ! yena elwaka oko bisenja bibotɛlɛtɛlɛ bikpetu na bikpetu bosɔɔ , yena edaka na molilo mowɔlɔ , na matai mayumu , na mayaka mayumu ,
66018017	Makonja ma manɛnɛ mɛnɛ manami na heure emoɔci pɛ . Bakapitɛni bamasua , na bato bamasua masusu , na bato basusu bamadiba , na bato basusu baya bakɔkɔ elomu ebu a madiba , ba’ma oko bohali .
66018018	Banja modidi mobotumba bonde na babekoa bo , Ngando yena ebwani na ngando ye enɛnɛnɛ nda ?
66018019	Basopa dutu a melo mibu ; bayea , balɛbɛ na babekoa bo , Monɔngɔ ! monɔngɔ ! ngandoye enɛnɛnɛ ! Bato basusu baya badaka na masua a madiba-mamukwa badiha likonja linɛnɛ a mojɔ molituna linde . Edikai o mopɔtu na heure emɔci pɛ .
66018020	Sepani oho Diko a mojɔ mongando emina ; Ino basɛnɔke , na babwɛnji-baDiko , na batɔndɔi , sepani koko , Mojɔ bo Njambe alongejai no na amodumbi yo .
66018021	Ngɔngɔ jimina , okina obwɛnji mopipo atomba litai linɛnɛnɛ , alidumba a madiba-mamukwa na abala bo , Babilo , ngando yena enɛnɛnɛ , êdumbama nase na bopipo boa , na etaboloa koko .
66018022	Bato bata’ka koko doi egongo , na bibumba , na poolo na mindule , a tei ewɛ . Pɛpɛ nongo moto yona okɔkɔ ekina elomu odi boboloa koko a tei ewɛ . Bata’ka koko a tei ewɛ doi libon’nda ndongo .
66018023	Eyoi epaka etaya hoja modidi a tei ewɛ . Bata’ka koko a tei ewɛ kɔpi emomi na mwali obolongana , Mojɔ bo bato bawɛ bamasa badaka bakumu bangondo , Na wɛ osela makota masusu na male mawɛ .
66018024	Makia mabatɔndɔi na mabasɛnɔke maboloi a tei ende , Na makia mabato basusu baya bawama a ngondo .
66019001	Yana asia ngando jimina , naka doi linɛnɛ lia lidaka o kɔpi elindundu libato banɛnɛ oho Diko haya babekoa bo , Aleluya ! Boheleja , na ekumu , na ngulu , jidi ai Njambe osu ;
66019002	Mojɔ bo yo asambejaka na soti na bongbebongbe . Asambejai mwali obɔɔli yona monɛnɛ , yona obeja ngondo na bɔɔli bonde . Njambe akundi likundu limakia mabakɔmɛli bande .
66019003	Babekoa koko bo , Aleluya ! Modidi mobotumba bonde moweaka diko na bosusu .
66019004	Basuku domi-ibae na banɛi , na bato babomɔ banɛi , basumana a bosakoa Njambe yona odi a ngɛndɛ . Babala bo , Amen . Aleluya !
66019005	Ekina kɔpi emana a ngɛndɛ bo , Sakoani Njambe osu , ino bakɔmɛli bande basusu , Ino baya bamosumaka , banɛnɛnɛ na bakɛkɛlɛkɛ .
66019006	Naka koko doi likɔpi elindundu libato banɛnɛ . Edaka o molunjo moepeela enɛnɛ na ebwana na bɛi mɛnɛ . Babala bo , Aleluya ! Mojɔ bo Kumu Njambe osu yona onɔi , akumaka .
66019007	Kinani bosepe na enanga enɛnɛ , na bomokumejae , Mojɔ bo ehole ebolongana boMwana-Bata emei , Na mwali onde obolongana alwai molilo monde ,
66019008	Mojɔ bo asi kpaci bo alwae bisenja bibotɛlɛtɛlɛ bipu bopɛɛ . Bisenja bimina bibotɛlɛtɛlɛ bidi oko bikɔmɛli bibodongo bibasɛnɔke .
66019009	Obwɛnji abala koko na mbi bo , Sɔnɔ mojɔ mu ; Bojongoa ai bato baya babeami a libonje libolongana boMwana-Bata . Na abala na mbi bo , Bikenge bimina bidi bikenge biNjambe na soti mɛnɛ .
66019010	Mbi nasadumba a bibota binde bo namosakoe . Iyo ko abala na mbi bo , yɛ bokɔ boa ! Mbi nadi oko mokɔmɛli pɛ , o adi wɛ mɛnɛ , na baninga bawɛ baya babaneaka tati eYesu . Sakoa oko Njambe . Mojɔ bo tati eYesu edi mwembo moeseko .
66019011	Nanɛ bo Diko didi bwase , na nanɛ punda mopu . Okina adaka abaki a punda yona odi na kombe ji , Yona oejimeli , Yona osoti . Iyo asambejaka , na anaka bila oko na bodongo .
66019012	Miso mande madaka o mosa mɛnɛ . Adaka na makongo manɛnɛ mabokumu a molo monde . Adaka na kombe yena esɔnɔmɔ ; pɛpɛ nongo moto ko ojebaka kombe emina , oko yo mɛnɛ pɛ .
66019013	Aiwaka kasaka eyai yena edaka na matɔnɔ mamakia , na kombe ende edi Ebaeli eNjambe .
66019014	Mandundu mabasoda baDiko mamosusaka , madaka mabaki a punda bapu , na malwaka bisenja bibobuno bipu bopɛɛ .
66019015	Abɛnɛ monɛnɛ amanaka a monɔkɔ monde a bokwɛlɛ makota mangondo . Tondo ende ebokumu edi tondo eebende a mojɔ mobu . Iyo adi bonda eboka evino ekɛlɛ egbasoake eNjambe obonɔ .
66019016	Adaka koko na kombe a kasaka ende na a ebɛ ende bo , Koi obaroi , na Kumu obakumu .
66019017	Nanɛ koko okina obwɛnji yona odaka ami a modika-busa . Iyo abea mbulu basusu baya bahombaka diko na kɔpi epipo bo , Doani ; titanani a mojɔ molibonje linɛnɛ liNjambe ,
66019018	a boyaka mini Mibakmuu , na mini Mibakapitɛni , na mini Mibato banɛnɛnɛ , na mini mipunda , na mini mibasoda bapunda , na mini Mibato basusu mɛnɛ , basɔmi na babuli , banɛnɛnɛ na bakɛkɛ .
66019019	Nanɛ Tito , na bakumu bangondo , na mandundu mabasoda babu , baya bama titana a bona bila , na yona odaka abaki a punda , na lindundu libasoda bande .
66019020	Bapea Tito na motɔndɔi obokosea yona okɔkɔ mindumba , oko yona okosea bato na mindumba mimina , bato baya bama sɔ embete eTito , na baya bama sakoa elimo ende . Ibo basusu babae badumbama yana adaka bo mɔ , a libale limosa mosupulu .
66019021	Yona odaka abaki a punda awa basusu batongo na abɛnɛ onde , oko abɛnɛ yona omanaka a monɔkɔ monde . Na mbulu basusu bagola na mini mibu .
66020001	Nanɛ okwa obwɛnji akahule oho Diko . Iyo apeaka sabe emombɔndɔ monase na mokina monyɔlɔ monɛnɛ a ebɔ ende .
66020002	Apea Dalakona , oko njɔ yona moyou , yona odi Jabalo na Satana , na amo’sa ta mbɔci bo adae ena bianga koto emɔci .
66020003	Amodumba a mombɔndɔ monase , adipa modipe , na abakea embete a modipe bo atakosea koko makota mangondo , oko a suka ebianga koto emɔci . Ehole emina ekasia adi bocingoama mweka .
66020004	Nanɛ koko mingbɛlɛngɔ , na baya badaka a mingbɛlɛngɔ mimina basɔ kpaci a bosambeja . Nanɛ koko miembo Mibato baya bama tɛndɔmɔ melo a mojɔ motati ebu ai Yesu , na a mojɔ moEbaeli eNjambe , na miembo Mibato baya balona bosakoa Tito na elimo ende , na baisɔ embete ende a maso mabu , isa a mɔmɔ mabu . Ibo basɔ koko bomɔ , na bakuma na Yesu bianga koto emɔci .
66020005	Bagwake batongo basɔ koko bomɔ , oko a suka ebianga koto emɔci ; bongɔ boboso a bogwa oko bu .
66020006	Yona odi a libondo libato baya badi bongɔ a bogwa a bongɔ boboso , adi na bojongoa na bosɛnɔ . Bogwa bomabae boditi nongo na kpaci ai bo ; badi boda nganga baNjambe na nganga baMasiya , na badi bokatana na nde a bokumu bonde bianga koto emɔci .
66020007	Bianga koto emɔci bikasia , Satana adi bocingoama a blɔkɔ ende .
66020008	Adi bomana a bokosea makota mangondo , oko a suka engondo mɛnɛ , oko Gogo na Magogo , bo ababolee a mojɔ mobila . Etango ebu edi o mbume jimbongu .
66020009	Badonga a bisika bisusu bingondo na bahika ngando ebasɛnɔke na ngando eepaeli . Mosa ko modonga oho Diko ai Njambe , na mobatumba kanga basusu mɛnɛ .
66020010	Satana , mokosei obu , adumbama a libale lomosa na lisupulu , esika edi Tito na motɔndɔi obokosea , na badi bodingoa oho mabulu na mei oko na bosusu mɛnɛ .
66020011	Nanɛ ngɛndɛ enɛnɛ epu , na yona odaka a ngɛndɛ . Ngondo na busa bacia boso bonde , na baibo loa koko .
66020012	Nanɛ koko bagwake , banɛnɛnɛ na bakɛkɛlɛkɛ ; badaka ba’mi a boso bongɛndɛ . Mikanda midipoama . Na mokina mokanda motongo modipoama , oko mokanda mobomɔ . Na bagwake basamba a mojɔ mobikɔmɛli bibu bia bisɔnɔmɔ a mikanda .
66020013	Madiba-mamukwa mahuleja bagwake baya badaka ena . Bogwa na Seolo bahuleja koko bagwake baya badaka ena , na basusu basamba a mojɔ mongando jima bo kɔ .
66020014	Ngɔngɔ jimina , Bogwa na Seolo badumbama a libale limosa ; bogwa bomabae oko bu , bua bolibale limosa .
66020015	Isa kombe emoto eiboloa , pɛ bosɔnɔmɔ a mokanda mobomɔ , moto omina adumbama a libale limosa .
66021001	Ngɔngɔ jimina , nanɛ Diko diyene na ngondo eyene , mojɔ bo Diko diboso dima dimoa , na ngondo eboso pongono , na madiba-mamukwa maditi koko .
66021002	Na nanɛ ngando yena esɛnɔke , Yelusalema eyene , ekadonge oho Diko ai Njambe , na mosɛlingo momwali-obolongana yona olwa molilo monde a mojɔ momuma’nde .
66021003	Naka koko kɔpi epipo ekamane a ngɛndɛ bo , Anjani ; etondo eNjambe edi a tei ebato . Iyo adi boda na bu . Ibo badi boda bato bande , na Njambe yo mɛnɛ adi boda na bu .
66021004	Iyo adi bohakoa mbisoli jisusu a miso mabu . Bogwa botada koko na ikina . Batayea koko kɔndɔ na ikina , pɛpɛ koko bio isa mwano , mojɔ bo ngando jiboso jisia oko bosia .
66021005	Iyona odaka a ngɛndɛ abala bo , Anjani ; mbi nakɔkɔ leka losusu loyene . Abala koko bo , Sɔnɔ mojɔ mu , cina bo bikenge bimina bidi soti , bitakputoa nongo .
66021006	Na abala na mbi bo , Mojɔ mosii ! Mbi nadi Alepa na Omega , libangake na suka . Isa moto adi na ekangola emadiba , mbi nadi bomonusa madiba mamolo momadiba mabomɔ ; nadi bomopa oko bopa , pɛpɛ bongɛjɛ .
66021007	Moto akagbokeja , adi bosangoa likwa . Mbi nadi boda Njambe onde , na yo adi boda mwana’mbi .
66021008	A mojɔ mobimɛli ko , na baya bapeliti ejimeli , na bato babosambolu , na bawoi , na bato babɔɔli , na bato bademba , na basakoi babilimo , na bakosei basusu , — libondo libu lidi oko a libale limosa na supulu ; bogwa bomina bodi bogwa bomabae .
66021009	Okina obabwɛnji sambo baya badaka na kɔpɔ sambo jia jiluma na madingoa masuka Sambo , adoa na abala na mbi bo , Doa nanejae wɛ Mwali-obolongana , yona odi mwali oMwana-Bata .
66021010	Iyo atomba mbi a mwembo a diko dimono monɛnɛ , na anejani Yelusalema , ngando esɛnɔkɛ , ekadonge oho Diko ai Njambe na ekatite nase .
66021011	Edaka na ekumu eNjambe . Langilangi engando edaka o litai liyumu , oko litai liyasepi , na bosangesange o talatala .
66021012	Edaka na mongba , mongba monɛnɛnɛ moyai , mua modaka na midipe domi-na-Mibae . Babwɛnji-baDiko domi-na-babae badaka a midipe , na kombe jimakota domi-na-babae mabana baYisalaele jisɔnɔmɔ a midipe .
66021013	Midipe minɛi midaka a dɔngɔ diɛsɛta , midipe minɛi a dɔngɔ dinɔdɔ , midipe minɛi a dɔngɔ disudo , na midipe minɛi a dɔngɔ diwɛsɛta .
66021014	Mongba mongando modaka na eyoeli-ecina , mboba domi-na-jibae , na kombe jibabwɛnji domi-na-babae ba-Mwana-Bata jidaka a mboba jimina .
66021015	Obwɛnji yona obalaka na mbi adaka na mongendu-momwɛngi a bongɛ ngando , na midipe , na mongba .
66021016	Ngando edaka mɔngɔ masusu manɛi oko amɛci , boyai na sasa oko amɛci . Angɛ ngando na mongendu , na angɛ kilometa koto jibae na mikama minɛi , boyai na sasa na diko oko amɛci .
66021017	Angɛ mwɛngi momongba pongono , mako mokama momɔci na macinda mabae na mako manɛi na bongɛ bomoto na bongɛ boobwɛnji pongono .
66021018	Mongba moyoama na yasepi . Ngando mɛnɛ eyoama na wɔlɔ esoti , na edaka na bosangesange botalatala .
66021019	Eyoeli-ecina engando edaka na matai mayumu tungu jisusu . Mboba eboso eyoama na yasepi ; yena ejibae sapili ;
66021020	yena ejisato kalekedona ; yena ejinɛi emelaudi ; yena ejitano saladonike ; yena ejisamano saludi ; yena esambo kulusoliti ; yena ebomwambe beluli ; yena elibwa topasi ; yena edomi kulusopalo ; yena edomi-na-emɔci yakinto ; yena edomi-na-jibae ametusiti .
66021021	Midipe domi-na-Mibae midaka mayaka mayumu domi-na-mabae , tu modipe liyaka liyumu limɔci . Licilinga lingando lidaka licilinga liwɔlɔ esoti , na lidaka na bosa-ngesange botalatala .
66021022	Nainɛ nongo tempelo a ngando , mojɔ bo tempelo engando edi oko Kumu Njambe yona onɔi , na Mwana-Bata .
66021023	Ngando ebwanaka , pɛpɛ nongo modika-busa isa songe a boboja ngando , mojɔ bo ekumu eNjambe edi bobu bongando , na paka engando edi Mwana-Bata .
66021024	Bato bamakota masusu badi bodala a bohu bomina ; bakumu bangondo badi bodoa na ngbemeani na ekumu ebu a ngando emina .
66021025	Midipe mingando mitadipama nongo a ehole emose na bosusu , mojɔ bo bulu botada nongo oho .
66021026	Badi bokwea ena na ekumu na lisuma limakota mangondo .
66021027	Pɛpɛ nongo eka epita ko edi bokwea ena , pɛpɛ nongo moto yona okɔkɔ ngando jibosambolu isa bokosea . Badi bokwea ena oko baya basɔnɔmɔ kombe a mokanda mobomɔ moMwana-Bata .
66022001	Anejani koko dua emadiba mabomɔ ekamane a ngɛndɛ eNjambe na eMwana-Bata ; madaka na bosangesange bota-latala , na makɛlɛkɛ a ndanda elicilinga lingando .
66022002	Mole mobomɔ modaka a mɔngɔ masusu mabae madua , mua mobotaka mbuma , tungu domi-na-jibae , tu songe ekina tungu . Na kasa jimole jidaka a mojɔ mosengo emakota mangondo .
66022003	Ndakeja etaya da . Ngɛndɛ eNjambe na eMwana-Bata edabi ena , na bakɔmɛli bandɛ bamo-kɔmɛbí .
66022004	Ibo banɛbí boso bonde , na kombe ende edabí a maso mabu .
66022005	Na bulu botaya dabí ; paka editi koko na elomu oho , isa modika-busa , mojɔ bo Kumu Njambe abapabi bohu , na bakumabi oko na bosusu .
66022006	Abala na mbi bo , Bikenge bimina bidi soti , bitakputoa nongo . Na Kumu , Njambe omiembo na obatɔndɔi , alomi obwɛnji onde bo anejae bakɔmɛli bande ngando jia jidi bodoa ngɔngɔ mweka .
66022007	Hokea ; mbi nâdoa bokpa . Bojongoa ai moto yona osumaka bikenge bieseko emokanda mu .
66022008	Mbi Yoane naka , na nanɛ ngando jimina . Yana aka mbi , na yana anɛ mbi ngando jimina , nasadumba nase a bibota biobwɛnji yona ojinejani bo namosakoe .
66022009	Iyo ko abala na mbi bo , yɛ bokɔ boa ! Mbi nadi oko mokɔmɛli pɛ , o adi wɛ mɛnɛ , na batɔndɔi baninga bawɛ , na bato basusu baya basumaka bikenge bimokanda mu . Sakoa oko Njambe .
66022010	Abala na mbi koko bo , T’obombe oko bikenge bieseko emo-kanda mu , mojɔ bo ehole eba’i mea .
66022011	Yona odi mobe , yɛ akɔe oko bobe ; yona odi na mbindo , yɛ adae oko na mbindo ; yona odi na bodongo , yɛ akɔe oko ngando jibodongo ; yona odi mosɛnɔkɛ , yɛ adae oko mosɛnɔkɛ .
66022012	Hokea ; mbi nadi bodoa bokpa . Nadi bodoa na ndese embi , bo napɛ moto na moto ndese yena ebwani na bikɔmɛli binde .
66022013	Mbi nadi Alepa na Omega , yona oboso na yona osuka , libangake na suka .
66022014	Bojongoa ai bato baya basosaka bisenja bibu , bo badae na njea ebodoa a mole mobomɔ , na njea ebokwea a midipe mingando .
66022015	Sokolu ko , oko mbwa , na bato bademba , na bato babɔɔli , na bawoi , na basakoi babilimo , na basusu baya bapalaka na bakɔkɔ bokosea .
66022016	Mbi Yesu nalomi obwɛnji ombi bo ajebejae no ngando jiji a mojɔ moMenga . Mbi nadi monjeli oDawidi na ombota ende ; nadi monjɔtɔ yona odi na eyoeli enɛnɛ a elɔngɔ .
66022017	Mwembo , na Mwali obolongana babalaka bo , Doa . Isa moto a’kaka , yɛ abale bo , Doa . Yona odi na ekangola , yɛ adoe ; yɛ moto na moto yona opalaka , aloke madiba mabomɔ oko boloka , pɛpɛ nongo bosomba .
66022018	Mbi nalehaka bato basusu baya ba’kaka bikenge bieseko emokanda mu . Moto akaputana bikenge bitongo a bikenge bimina , Njambe adi bobakea ai yo madingoa maya masɔnɔmi a mokanda mu .
66022019	Na moto akakatoa bikenge bimokanda moeseko ye , Njambe adi bokatoa libondo linde a mole mobomɔ , na a ngando esɛnɔkɛ , o adi misɔnɔ mimokanda mu .
66022020	Yona odi motati ongando jimina abalaka bo , Soti , mbi nadoaka bokpa . Amen . Kumu Yesu , doa .
66022021	Yɛ monganji moKumu Yeslu modae na basɛnɔkɛ basusu . Amen .
